.o namo gaṇapataye| śrīpaśupataye namaḥ |

yo 'ajasraṃ hi rasādibhiśca bhagavāṃstasmai namaḥ śambhave|| 1 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

munīśvara prasādāt te śrutaṃ meroḥ praśaṃsanam|
bhūyaśca śrotum icchāmo māhātmyaṃ himavadgireḥ|| 2 ||

tatra tapaḥkṛtānāṃ yaddevānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ|
māhātmyaṃ tacca tīrthānāṃ śṛṅgāṇāṃ vada no vibho|| 3 ||

lomaharṣaṇa uvāca |

śṛṇudhvaṃ vipraśārdūlā yadvṛttāntaṃ purābhavat|
tayormitho hi saṃvādam agastyaskandayorgirau|| 4 ||

māhātmyaṃ caiva tīrthānāṃ harātmajaṃ mahāvibhum|
papraccha khalu senānīṃ kulaśaile ghaṭodbhavaḥ|| 5 ||

agastya uvāca |

pradiṣṭaṃ bhavatā yadyacchrutaṃ devīśayormukhāt|
bhavān sarvajña evārya sarvajñāt tvadbhavo yataḥ|| 6 ||

pītvā tava mukhāmbhojānniḥsṛtaṃ vāṅmayāmṛtam|
na tṛpyāmi tathā skanda gharmārtaḥ salilaṃ yathā|| 7 ||
 vāṅmayo .amṛtaṃ B

pramāṇaṃ ca sumerorhi tacchṛṅgāṇāṃ praśaṃsanam|
adhiṣṭhānāni devānāṃ tvatprasādācchrutaṃ mayā|| 8 ||

bhūdharāṇāṃ yathotpattiṃ tīrthānāṃ teṣu janminām|
himālayasya māhātmyaṃ vada me śaṃkarapriya|| 9 ||

skanda uvāa |

īśvareṇaiva me proktaṃ maṇimayaśiloccaye|
tat sarvaṃ te pravakṣyāmi samāsena ghaṭodbhava|| 10 ||

bhūdharāṇāṃ dharāyāśca yadvṛttāntam abhūt purā|
tadvakṣyāmyadhunā sarvaṃ śṛṇu mattaḥ samāhitaḥ|| 11 ||

abhaktāya ca dambhāya piśunāya hi pāpine|
naiva kathyam idaṃ dhīra yadīcchet phalam ātmanaḥ|| 12 ||

āsīdekārṇave ghore sarvasattvāvasānake|
viṣvaksenastamaḥplutya jalaśāyī sunirjanaḥ|| 13 ||

sarvalokāṃśca saṃhṛtya nakṣatrāṇīndubhāskarau|
jalenātmānam āchādya ekaḥ śete ciraṃ vibhuḥ|| 14 ||

avyaktavigraho devastejomayavapurmune|
kalpaṃ vyāpya ciraṃ viṣṇuḥ praśete brahmaṇaḥ kṣaye|| 15 ||

īkṣaṇasthā mahāmāyā māyāchāditavigrahaḥ|
brahmāṇḍe jyotiṣāṃ puñjastasyeśvaraḥ svayaṃ sthitaḥ|| 16 ||

kalpānte brahmaṇo 'agastya daśa diśi tamaḥplute|
tasya nābhau samudbhūte sahasrapattrapuṣkare|| 17 ||

dhātā jajāpa tanmadhye lokānugrahakārakaḥ|
tato 'adbhuto 'aniśaṃ dhyeyaṃ saṃcintya hṛdi śaṃkaram|| 18 ||

tato nārāyaṇo devaḥ karṇābhyāṃ ca malaṃ mune|
aṅgulībhyāṃ kaniṣṭhābhyām ādāyākṣipadambhasi|| 19 ||

samudbhūtau tato daityau tasmādambhasi bhīṣaṇau|
madhukaiṭabhasaṃjñau tau jalamadhye vyavasthitau|| 20 ||

tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrau malodbhūtau tasmāddaityātmakau mune|
divyānām ayutābdānte vardhamānau prakopinau|| 21 ||

ceratustasya tau pārśve tadā karṇamalodbhavau|
karālavadanau bhīmau mahākāyau mahābalau|| 22 ||

nāgāyutabalopetau pīnapādabhujottamau|
sarvayuddhaviśālau tau śyāmāṅgau cakralocanau|| 23 ||

yuddhāyāsphālya hastau tau karatālaṃ pracakratuḥ|
avalokya diśaḥ sarvāḥ kṛtveti ko 'api tiṣṭhati|| 24 ||

adṛṣṭau kaṃ ca saṃcintya kurvāvaḥ kim atho sakṛt|
tato dadṛśatuḥ padmaṃ dīrghanālaṃ mahojjvalam|| 25 ||

gatvā tadantikaṃ daityau durātmānau prakopinau|
ruruhatuḥ sunālaṃ tau padmaṃ kiñjalkabhūṣitam|| 26 ||

tatra dṛṣṭau mahātmānaṃ padmayoniṃ mahāprabham|
japantaṃ dhyāyamānaṃ vai pañcavaktraṃ caturbhujam|| 27 ||

akṣamālādharaṃ śāntam īṣatprahasitānanam|
hiraṇyagarbham ādyaṃ taṃ svatejobhiḥ prasāritam|| 28 ||

pitāmahaṃ ca lokānāṃ taptakāñcanasaṃnibham|
divyāmbaradharaṃ prājñaṃ divyābharaṇabhūṣitam|| 29 ||

vyācaṣṭaturvacastasmai tau madhukaiṭabhau mune|
pitāmahāya vīrau ca prakṛtyā kopinau tadā|| 30 ||

madhukaiṭabhaūcatuḥ |

ko bhavānatra kiṃ kāryaṃ kiṃ karoṣi kim adbhutam|
kasmādāgatya sustho 'asi kasya kiṃ vātra kathyatām|| 31 ||

śūnye cāmbhomaye bhīṣme avyakte ca diśāṃ tathā|
japtavān vai kathaṃ padme bahvāsya nau vada dhruvam|| 32 ||

brahmovāca |

dhyānastho 'ahaṃ sukhaṃ vīrau sarvabhūtadayākaram|
jananāya ca bhūtānāṃ bhūteśvaraṃ parāt param|| 33 ||

brahmāhaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ kartā cāsmi mahābalau|
īśvaraṃ dhyāyamāno hi jagadānandarūpiṇam|| 34 ||

na sthātavyaṃ ciraṃ kālaṃ yathāgatau hi gacchatam|
yo gacchati rahasthāne prāpnoti cāpadaṃ mahat|| 35 ||

madhukaiṭabhaūcatuḥ |

sthātuṃ naivātra lokeśa āgatau yuddhakāṅkṣayā|
kaṇḍūyanti āvayorhastā yuddhalālasino 'adhunā|| 36 ||

yuyutsavau viddhi cāvām atrāgatau tvadantikam|
ataśca nau mahābrahman yuddhaṃ tvaṃ dehi sāmpratam|| 37 ||

dadāsi yuddhaṃ khalu no 'adhunā tvam upasthite ca tvayi cejjayeva|
pravardhayāvaḥ savarairbhavantaṃ vyatikrame cenna tu tiṣṭha jīvan|| 38 ||

no ceddadāsi yuddhaṃ bho āvayorhi yuyutsavoḥ|
utpāṭyābjodbhavaṃ kṣipraṃ tvāṃ padmaṃ luṇṭhayāvahe|| 39 ||

skanda uvāca |

vaco niśamya sāṃgrāmyaṃ vipralāpaṃ pitāmahaḥ|
manasā dūyamāno 'asau tūṣṇīm āsīt tadā mune|| 40 ||

kiṃ karomi kva gacchāmi kuto muñcāmi sāmpratam|
nidrayā chādito viṣṇuḥ kathaṃ jāgarti viśvajit|| 41 ||

iti saṃcintya viśvātmā prabodhāya hareḥ punaḥ|
stavaṃ cakre hi nidrāyai sarvalokopakāriṇam|| 42 ||

brahmovāca |

saṃhṛtya sakalā/llokān samplutyātmāmbhasā jagat|
ekāśeta harernetre mohayantī hariṃ śive|| 43 ||

namastasyai vimohinyai jagatāṃ yā pramohinī|
antasthā moharūpeṇa śarmakartrī vivekinī|| 44 ||

vaiṣṇavī viśvarūpiṇyai viśveśvari namo 'astu te|
vyomasthe vyomarūpāyai tejorūpe namo 'astu te|| 45 ||

mohinyai viśvamohinyai maṅgalāyai namo namaḥ|
śivāyai śivarūpiṇyai māyāyai te namo namaḥ|| 46 ||

megharūpe rasaklinne kṣitirūpe namo 'astu te|
bījakartryai nibījāyai bhaiṣajyāyai namo 'astu te|| 47 ||

pañcānām ātmarūpiṇyai bhoktriṇyai bhojyarūpiṇi|
koṣasthe buddhirūpiṇyai citsvarūpe namo 'astu te|| 48 ||
 °rūpiṇī Y

abhimānasvarūpiṇyai hṛdrūpāyai namo 'astu te|
dhairyāyai samadhairyāyai vivekinyai namo namaḥ|| 49 ||

mātaḥ kṣetrajñarūpāyai jīvarūpe namo 'astu te|
medhyāyai śabdarūpiṇyai mātṛkāyai namo namaḥ|| 50 ||

ekamātre dvimātrāyai bahumātre namo 'astu te|
ardhamātrāsvarūpāyai trisvarāyai namo namaḥ|| 51 ||

triguṇātmakarūpiṇyai guṇātīte namo namaḥ|
icchājñānakriyāśaktitrividhāyai namo namaḥ|| 52 ||

mahāmāye mahājihve mahādaṃṣṭre namo namaḥ|
kālarūpe mahādevi kālarātri namo 'astu te|| 53 ||

rakṣa rakṣāmbike māṃ tvaṃ daityapāpagrahārtinam|
nidre 'alakṣe jaganmātarjagatkope namo 'astu te|| 54 ||

nidrāstavaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ saṃkaṭastho 'api vā paṭhet|
sarvapāpairvinirmukto labheta varam īpsitam|| 55 ||

nityaiśvaryam avāpnoti rujaḥ śāntiṃ grahodbhavam|
dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ sutāñjāyāṃ kālarātryāḥ prasādataḥ|| 56 ||
 sutān jāyāṃ B

śrādhakāle paṭhet tṛptāḥ pitaro yānti samāyutam|
dāne 'akṣayam avāpnoti saṃgrāme vijayaṃ labhet|| 57 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ yā saṃstutā nidrā brahmaṇāmitatejasā|
saṃtuṣṭā sā tadā devī saṃjahre viṣṇum avyayam|| 58 ||

prabudhyāsau mahāviṣṇurmāyātyaktakalevaraḥ|
saṃdadarśa mahātmānau garjamānau prakopinau|| 59 ||

anyonyaṃ paribhāṣantau padmam ucchettum udyatau|
padmoparisthitau daityau brahmāṇaṃ hantum udyatau|| 60 ||

uvāca vacanaṃ viṣṇurasurau madhukaiṭabhau|
bho bho daityau durātmānau atrāgatya kim ucyatām|| 61 ||

iti śrutvā vaco daityau viṣṇunā paribhāṣitam|
krodhāviṣṭau mahākāyau kaṭukaṃ karṇavipriyam|| 62 ||

tato visṛjya dhātāraṃ dudruvaturmahāvibhum|
yuddhe kaṇḍūyamānau tau mahāmāyāvimohitau|| 63 ||

teṣāṃ yuddhaṃ mahaccāsīt sarvasattvabhayaṃkaram|
anyonyaṃ parisaṃjaghnustalairmuṣṭiprahārakaiḥ|| 64 ||

bāhuyuddhaṃ tato 'agastya cakrurmadhye 'ambhasāṃ hi te|
divyavarṣasahasrāṇi pañca vai lomaharṣaṇam|| 65 ||

kṛtvā yuddhaṃ tato viṣṇuruvāca vacanaṃ tadā|
bho bho yuddhaviśālau vāṃ nānāyuddhaparākramaiḥ|| 66 ||

saṃtuṣṭo 'ahaṃ mahābāhū dāsyāmyadya yadīpsitam|
vāṃ sarvadaṃ hi matvā māṃ yāceyāthāṃ yuvāṃ varam|| 67 ||
 mabhyā B

madhukaiṭabhaūcatuḥ |

āvāṃ daityau mahābāhau tvāṃ kathaṃ yācayāvahe|
āvāṃ te sampradāsyāvo varaṃ vṛṇīṣva cāvayoḥ|| 68 ||
 °vāho B

skanda uvāca |

niśamyeti vaco viṣṇuḥ sarvabhūtodbhavāya vai|
yayāce tau jagaddhetostayorvadhaṃ varaṃ purā|| 69 ||

yadi dattaṃ varaṃ mahyaṃ sarvalokopakārakam|
yuvayornidhanaṃ vīrau tanme dattha idaṃ dhruvam|| 70 ||

madhukaiṭabhaūcatuḥ |

evam astu tathā viṣṇo yathā vadasi tat tathā|
vyomni jale na hantavyau sthale vāvāṃ viśeṣataḥ|| 71 ||

skanda uvāca |

evam astu pratiśrutya bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ|
gṛhītvorau samāropya cakreṇāśu jaghāna tau|| 72 ||

nihatyaivaṃ mahākāyau bahuyojanavistṛtau|
jale cikṣepa tanmāṃsaṃ chittvā cakreṇa vigrahau|| 73 ||
 vigraho B

tato 'arṇā māṃsayogena tanmedasā samāplutā|
tasmādbhūmiḥ samudbhūtā divyakoṭisamāgate|| 74 ||

sā divyāyutavarṣānte bhavedgāḍhatarā guruḥ|
nānāmṛdgrāvasaṃkīrṇā āchannasalilācalā|| 75 ||

tato varāhena dhṛtā hi sā yā sthireti dhīraiḥ kathitā ca śaśvat|
tanmedasaḥ saṃcaraṇena tasyā bhūyaśca nāma dvija medinīti|| 76 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe puṣkaraprādurbhāvo nāma prathamo adhyāyaḥ|| 1 ||

agastya uvāca |

kathaṃ samudbhūtā bhūmirvarāheṇāmitaujasā|
prajāpate mahaccitraṃ tanme svānte ṣaḍānana|| 1 ||

adbhuto hi varāho 'asau utpattiṃ tasya me vada|
tasyām adrīn kathaṃ dhātā sasarja sarvajīvinaḥ|| 2 ||

lomaharṣaṇa uvāca |

ityeva pṛcchyamāno 'asau kumbhajena dvijottamāḥ|
vyācaṣṭa bhagavān skandastasmai taddhetukaṃ vacaḥ|| 3 ||

sudṛḍhāṃ medinīṃ prekṣya tāṃ nimnoccavivarjitām|
vistīrṇāṃ viśikhāṃ mṛtsnāṃ mumoda sa prajāpatiḥ|| 4 ||

etasyāṃ varamedinyāṃ kathaṃ sṛṣṭirbhaviṣyati|
vinā kṛpāṃ maheśasya sṛṣṭisthitiharātmanaḥ|| 5 ||

tato brahmā jagaddhātā sarvalokopakārakaḥ|
saṃsṛṣṭyai sarvalokānāṃ stavaṃ cakāra śūlinaḥ|| 6 ||

praṇamya śirasā rudraṃ vāṅmanovigrahairnaman|
mūrdhnyañjaliṃ prabaddhyāsau parikramya punaḥ punaḥ|| 7 ||

brahmovāca |

.o, |

namo 'astu vyomakeśāya tārakākhyāya vai namaḥ|
tārakeśāya devāya tārakasthāya vai namaḥ|| 8 ||

nama ānandarūpāya nityānandāya vai namaḥ|
pūrṇānandāya nandāya nirañjanāya śūline|| 9 ||

namo mānyāya mokṣāya maṅgalāya ca mānine|
hṛdbuddhicittarūpāya paramāya parātmane|| 10 ||

namaḥ śarvāya bhīmāya śambhave sthāṇave namaḥ|
śivāya śitikaṇṭhāya śaṃkarāya mahātmane|| 11 ||

namo vāyuśarīrāya pañcāṅgāya namo namaḥ|
vāmadevāya viśvāya vyomarūpāya vai namaḥ|| 12 ||

namo yogāya yajñāya yajñarūpāya yogine|
yogeśvarāya yogāya yogācārya namo namaḥ|| 13 ||

namo bhavāya bhavyāya bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ|
bhūtātmane vibhūtāya bhūtodbhūtāya bhūtine|| 14 ||

namaḥ parāya pārāya paramāya parātmane|
parāparapratītāya parāparamayāyine|| 15 ||

namaḥ sadasadaṃśāya haṃsarūpāya vai namaḥ|
saṃsārasārarūpāya sate 'asate namo namaḥ|| 16 ||

sūkṣmāya samasūkṣmāya sūkṣmātītāya saṃśine|
sthūlāya sthūlagātrāya sthūlātītāya vai namaḥ|| 17 ||

namo jyotiḥsvarūpāya jyotiṣāṃ pataye namaḥ|
tejaḥpuñjāya rudrāya alakṣyāya namo namaḥ|| 18 ||

.o, |

namo jalasvarūpāya kṣitirūpāya vāyave|
agnaye vyomarūpāya sūryāyābjāya cātmane|| 19 ||

skanda uvāca |

śrutvā stavaṃ mahadbhadraṃ brahmaṇā paribhāṣitam|
harṣotphullaprakāśāṅgo vyomni devo mahāvibhuḥ|| 20 ||

saṃsārasārarūpo yaḥ saṃsārodbhavakāraṇam|
pracakrame varaṃ dātuṃ bhaktāya bhaktavatsalaḥ|| 21 ||

jyotirūpeśvara uvāca |

brahmaṃstava mukhāmbhojasambhūtavāṅmayāmṛtam|
pītvā karṇena tuṣṭo 'ahaṃ sarvalokopakārakam|| 22 ||

ya idaṃ paṭhate brahman sarvainobhiḥ pramucyate|
asādhyaṃ sādhayet sarvaṃ stavarājaprapāṭhataḥ|| 23 ||

idānīṃ te pradāsyāmi sarvaṃ varam anuttamam|
tvatstavānandamūḍhāṅgo varaṃ varaya viśvasṛk|| 24 ||

brahmovāca |

alakṣa sarvalokeśa tejorūpa mahāvibho|
sarvatejomayeśāna sarvabhūtānukampaka|| 25 ||

yadi tuṣṭo 'asi me nātha saṃsārasthitaye satām|
kriyatāṃ hi mahādeva prādurbhāvaṃ varaṃ mayi|| 26 ||

prekṣya me medinīṃ śūnyāṃ koṭisamāyutādhikaiḥ|
sraṣṭuṃ carācarānasyāṃ vāñchāmyahaṃ prabho 'adhunā|| 27 ||

yāce 'ahaṃ tvāṃ varaṃ ceti jagatsarjanakāraṇam|
sṛjyamānāṃśca srakṣyāmi jantūn bhavatprasādataḥ|| 28 ||

jyotirūpa uvāca |

suraśreṣṭha yat tvaṃ vadasi tat tathā|
sṛjyantāṃ mātmanā sarvam adyaprabhṛti jantavaḥ|| 29 ||

viṣṇo prapālanāya tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ca jīvinām|
carācarātmanāṃ śastā duṣṭānāṃ pāpakarmaṇām|| 30 ||

svalpāyuṣāṃ bhaviṣyāmi kālarūpastvahaṃ vidhe|
saṃhariṣyāmi tān sarvān kāle kāle hi pāpinaḥ|| 31 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ labdhavaro dhātā sarvaṃ sraṣṭuṃ mano dadhe|
īśvarasya prasādādvai prādurbhāvāya jīvinām|| 32 ||

tato dhātā kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā tūṣṇīm āsīt tam avyayam|
aṇḍaṃ sasarja medinyāṃ rasātmanā hi saṃyutam|| 33 ||

divyavarṣasahasraṃ taṃ dhṛtvā yogī karātmanau|
aprameyamahāṇḍaṃ vai sarvabhūtodbhavāruṇam|| 34 ||

alakṣavarṇam ādyaṃ tam avyaktaṃ samagocaram|
mahāṇḍaṃ viśvajanmānaṃ kiṃciddīrghaṃ suvartulam|| 35 ||

bahuyojanavistāraṃ bahuyojanavartulam|
dhāturlomaikarandhre taṃ nimagnaṃ tatpramāṇitam|| 36 ||

svakīyāṃ brahmaṇo mūrtiṃ taptakārtasvaraprabhām|
jagadādhāram ādyaṃ taṃ jagadgarbhanidānakam|| 37 ||

tato yugasahasrānte bibhedordhvamukhaṃ vidhiḥ|
sajjananāya lokānāṃ bibhedādhomukhaṃ punaḥ|| 38 ||

bhūyo 'aṣṭadhā bibhedāṇḍaṃ sarvabhūtopakārakaḥ|
cakārātra vibhāgaṃ tajjagataḥ kāraṇaṃ punaḥ|| 39 ||

tacchidram ūrdhvam ākāśaṃ dharmiṣṭhānāṃ parā gatiḥ|
kṛtavān viśvayoniḥ sa yadadhastadrasātalam|| 40 ||

pūrvaṃ bibheda yaccāṇḍaṃ svargaṃ sukṛtināṃ gṛham|
samantādaṣṭadhā yogī chidrāṇi kṛtavān punaḥ|| 41 ||

vidiśaśca diśaḥ sarvā manasaiva tathā punaḥ|
sasarja siddhatoyāni svarṇaratnākṛtāni ca|| 42 ||

nānācitrāṇi varṇāni yāni kāni kalāni tat|
bahuvarṇadharā meghā babhūvustatprasādataḥ|| 43 ||

yadaṇḍamadhye skannaṃ tadrasam āsīt samāhitam|
jātarūpaṃ samabhavat tat sarvaṃ medinītale|| 44 ||

tasya kledārṇavaughena prāchādyanta samantataḥ|
medinī nikhilāgastya sarvabhūtopakāriṇī|| 45 ||

yadaṇḍam akarodūrdhvaṃ devalokacikīrṣayā|
tatra yat salilaṃ klinnaṃ so 'abhavat kāñcano giriḥ|| 46 ||

tenāmbhasā pramathitāḥ sarvā diśaścopadiśaśca hi|
antarikṣaṃ ca nākaṃ ca yaccānyat kiṃcidantaram|| 47 ||

yatra yatra jalaṃ skannaṃ tatra tatrotthito giriḥ|
bahuśailaghanā devī medinī viṣamābhavat|| 48 ||

parvatairbahubhistoyaiḥ pīḍitā medinī mune|
nārāyaṇātmakaṃ divyaṃ tejomayaṃ hiraṇmayam|| 49 ||

dhārayitum aśaktārṇam adhastāt prāviśadrasā|
pīḍyamānā jalaiḥ śailairvyathitā medinī bhṛśam|
stavaṃ cakāra devāya svātmoddhāraṇam eva ca|| 50 ||

medinyuvāca |

namo 'acyutāya devāya vaikuṇṭhāya ca viṣṇave|
vyaktāya vyaktarūpāya vyaktāvyaktavibhūtine|| 51 ||

viṣvaksenāya kṛṣṇāya caturbhujāya śārṅgine|
nārāyaṇāya kālāya nārākhaṭvopaśāyine|| 52 ||

puṇḍarīpattranetrāya daityāraye suparvine|
adhokṣajāya devāya śrīpataye namo namaḥ|| 53 ||

viśvāya viśvarūpāya bahurūpāya rūpiṇe|
ekarūpavirūpāya arūpāya namo namaḥ|| 54 ||

ekavaktradvivaktrāya bahuvaktrāya te namaḥ|
ekajihvadvijihvāya dvijihvaśāyine namaḥ|| 55 ||

bhavodbhūtakadehāya bhavarūpāya vai namaḥ|
pravibhavāya bhūtānāṃ haraye bhūtibhūṣaṇe|| 56 ||

anantāyāprameyāya māyine gatamāyine|
nityāyānityarūpāya ānandāya namo namaḥ|| 57 ||

nārodbhavāya nārāya nārādhārāya nandine|
nārodbhavodbhavārcāya nāyakāya namo namaḥ|| 58 ||

nirañjanāya śāntāya nirvikalpāya sūcine|
akhaṇḍāya nirodhāya sadānandāya śāśvate|| 59 ||

matsyarūpāya kūrmāya varāhāya nṛsiṃhine|
vāmanāya trirāmāya namo buddhāya kalkine|| 60 ||

skanda uvāca |

ityetat stavam ākarṇya karṇapeyaṃ sukhāvaham|
viṣṇustutoṣa tejasvī sa medinyai ghaṭodbhava|| 61 ||

stavaiḥ saṃtoṣito devaḥ pūrṇānandastadā vibhuḥ|
tasyā vāñchāvaraṃ dātum āvirbhūto mahābalaḥ|| 62 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

varaṃ varaya kalyāṇi lokānugrahakārakam|
adya dāsyāmi vāñchārthaṃ yat te manasi vidyate|| 63 ||

medinyuvāca |

yadi dadāsi me pūrvaṃ varam āvrīyatāṃ prabho|
tataścarācaraṃ sarvaṃ dhāryate bhavatā saha|| 64 ||

vinā tava varaṃ dhāryaṃ pīḍitāhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ|
śaktā tavaujasā yuktā carācarairgarīyasī|| 65 ||

dātavyam iti me deva patitvaṃ ca varottamam|
bhūyaḥ stavasya me nātha phalaṃ phalaya sāmpratam|| 66 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

evam astu dhare devi yat tvaṃ vāñchasi tat tathā|
mākāle mriyatāṃ martyo mābhibhūyāt parābhavaiḥ|| 67 ||

putravāñchaktivān bhūyānna pāpairlipyate tathā|
śatravo vilayaṃ yāntu medinīstutipāṭhataḥ|| 68 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ tasyai varaṃ datvā medinyai sa mahāvibhuḥ|
chandobhirakṣarairmantraiḥ śrutibhiḥ samalaṃkṛtam|| 69 ||

varāhaṃ tanum āsthāya sarvayajñamayaṃ vibhuḥ|
daṃṣṭrayā gāṃ samudrasthām ujjahāra mahābalaḥ|| 70 ||

samudrairgiribhiryuktām adyāpi sacarācaram|
daṃṣṭrāyāṃ dhārayāmāsa varāho medinīṃ mune|| 71 ||

agastya uvāca |

yajñarūpo varāho 'asau tvayokto me camūpate|
pramāṇaṃ vapuṣastasya kiṃ varṇaṃ vada me 'adhunā|| 72 ||

skanda uvāca |

rūpaṃ dadhāra vārāhaṃ sarvadaityabhayāvaham|
tisraḥ koṭyardhakoṭīnāṃ lomatīrthaiḥ pavitrakam|| 73 ||

koṭiyojanavistāraṃ taddviguṇaṃ samucchritam|
varāho 'asau mahākāyo divyarūpaḥ śrutistutaḥ|| 74 ||

nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśaḥ kṣayagarjitaniḥsvanaḥ|
śvetadīptogradaṃṣṭrī ca śailasaṃkāśavigrahaḥ|| 75 ||

vidyudagniprakāśākṣa ādityābhāsamaprabhaḥ|
pīnavṛttāyataskandhastvaṣṭaśārdūlavikramaḥ|| 76 ||

pīnonnatakaṭīsthānaṃ vṛṣalakṣaṇacihnitaḥ|
vedarāvo yūpadaṃṣṭraḥ kratuhastaścitīmukhaḥ|| 77 ||

agnijihvo darbharomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥ|
ahorātrekṣaṇaḥ śaśvadvedāṅgaḥ śrutibhūṣaṇaḥ|| 78 ||

ājyanāsaḥ śruvastuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvaro mahān|
satyadharmamayaḥ sākṣāt satyavikramasatkṛtaḥ|
chāyāśaktirmahāyogī svarṇaśaila ivocchritaḥ|| 79 ||

evaṃ vārāham āsthāya tanuṃ yajñamayaṃ vibhuḥ|
sāmuddhartuṃ rasāṃ gurvīṃ praviveśa rasātalam|| 80 ||

adbhiḥ saṃchāditām ūrvīṃ rasātalatale gatām|
daṃṣṭrayā gāṃ samudrasthām ujjahāra mahābalaḥ|| 81 ||

samudrairgiribhiryuktām adyāpi sacarācaram|
daṃṣṭrāyāṃ dhārayāmāsa lokahitāya viśvajit|| 82 ||

pṛthivīpravibhāgāya manaścakre mahāvibhuḥ|
ājñāpayat tadāgastya brahmāṇaṃ tacca janmane|| 83 ||

tasyāṃ vidhātā sakalāṃśca jantūn pañcātmakairvipra sasarja nityam|
lakṣāṇi jānīhi bahūni tāni māyāpraśaktāni bhṛśaṃ babhūvuḥ|| 84 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe medinyuddhāraṇaṃ nāma dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

tasyāṃ dhātā ghaṭodbhūta saptadvīpānakalpayat|
jambūdvīpaṃ tataḥ plakṣaṃ śālmalīkaṃ kuśaṃ tathā|| 1 ||

krauñcadvīpaṃ punaḥ śākaṃ puṣkaram asṛjat prabhuḥ|
jambūdvīpaṃ tato madhye teṣāṃ kramāt samasṛjat|| 2 ||

pañcāśatkoṭivistāro yojanānāṃ navāntaraḥ|
jambūdvīpapramāṇo 'ayaṃ bhūyasteṣāṃ vadāmi te|| 3 ||

kṣārodaṃ dviguṇaṃ jñeyaṃ jambūdvīpasya kumbhaja|
kṣārasya dviguṇaṃ plakṣaṃ plakṣasya dviguṇaṃ tathā|| 4 ||

ikṣuṃ taddviguṇaṃ cānyaṃ śālmalīdviguṇaṃ tathā|
śālmalyāśca surābdhiṃ vai surāyā dviguṇaṃ kuśam|| 5 ||

kuśasya dviguṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ ghṛtaṃ taddviguṇaṃ mune|
krauñcaṃ taddviguṇaṃ jñeyaṃ dadhi taddviguṇaṃ tathā|| 6 ||

śākaṃ śākasya ca kṣīraṃ dviguṇaṃ tasya puṣkaram|
sarvadvīpasamudrāṇāṃ dviguṇāddviguṇottaram|| 7 ||

pramāṇaṃ vistaraṃ jñeyaṃ saptadvīpaṃ saritpatim|
dvīpānāṃ madhyato 'agastya jambūdvīpo virājate|| 8 ||

jambūdvīpāntare madhye caturasre suśobhane|
meruṃ cakāra viśvātmā sarvaśailottamottamam|| 9 ||

jāmbūnadamayaṃ śailaṃ sarvatejomayaṃ param|
ayutārkapratīkāśaṃ jyotīrūpam aharniśam|| 10 ||

yojanaṃ caturāśītilakṣāṇāṃ saṃkhyayā mune|
merostuṅgaśca vistāram adhaśca tādṛśastathā|| 11 ||

ṣoḍaśānāṃ ca lakṣāṇāṃ yojanānāṃ ca saṃkhyayā|
catuḥśṛṅgaṃ suvistāraṃ meroryena pṛthak kṛtam|| 12 ||

vidikṣu tādṛśaṃ dhātrā kṛtaṃ sānuṃ punaḥ pṛthak|
yojanaṃ pañcalakṣāṇāṃ prāmaṇena suvistṛtam|| 13 ||

prācyaṃ śṛṅgaṃ ca sauvarṇam avācyaṃ śṛṅgam āyasam|
prātīcyaṃ rājataṃ śṛṅgam udīcyaṃ tāmrakaṃ tathā|| 14 ||

pravālamayam ekaṃ ca śṛṅgaṃ ratnamayaṃ tathā|
sauvarṇaspāṭikaṃ dhātā tadvidikṣu cakāra vai|| 15 ||

prācyasthānaṃ mahendrasya avācye śamanasya ca|
pratīcye vāruṇaṃ jñeyam udīcye dhanadasya ca|| 16 ||

vahnikarbūravāyūnāṃ devānāṃ hi yathākramāt|
sthānaṃ vidikṣu jānīyāt kumbhayone svakaṃ svakam|| 17 ||

koṭiśṛṅgaiḥ samāyuktaṃ gaṅgāpātairmahojjvalam|
caturdaśaṃ dadhānaṃ ca bhuvanaṃ taṃ surālayam|| 18 ||

jāmbūnadamayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ sahasre rājitaṃ param|
indranīlamayaiḥ śṛṅgairvaidūryamayakoṭibhiḥ|| 19 ||

mārakatamayodbhūtaiścandrakāntimayodbhavaiḥ|
sūryakāntimayagrāvai raupyakāntimayaistathā|| 20 ||

puṣparāgamayairdivyairnīlāñjanamayodbhavaiḥ|
sphāṭikairmaṇibhirdivyaiḥ śekharairupaśobhitam|| 21 ||

pañcaratnamayaiḥ śṛṅgairbahuratnamayaiḥ kvacit|
nānauṣadhisutejobhistejomayasamudbhavaiḥ|| 22 ||

mauktikodbhavasaṃyuktaiḥ pravālāṅkurasambhavaiḥ|
śrīmadvjarasamudbhūtaiḥ sarvaratnamayojjvalaiḥ|| 23 ||

sahasrasānubhiryuktaṃ nānāratnaprakuṭṭimaiḥ|
siddharasasamutkīrṇairhiraṇyavṛkṣasayutaiḥ|| 24 ||

hiraṇyavetrasaṃyuktairhiraṇyapadmasambhavaiḥ|
cintāmaṇidrumodbhūtairhiraṇyakusumojjvalaiḥ|| 25 ||

kāñcanābhiḥ śilābhiśca guhābhiśca vibhūṣitam|
nānāpuṣpayutaiḥ kuñjaiḥ sarvakālaphalairdrumaiḥ|| 26 ||

jāmbūnadamayairveśmairvividharatnabhūṣitaiḥ|
hiraṇyāchāditaiḥ śubhraiḥ savajrakalaśairyutaiḥ|| 27 ||

vāpībhiramṛtotpannaiḥ praṇālībhiḥ suśobhanaiḥ|
bahucitradhvajābhiśca patākāyaṣṭiśobhanaiḥ|| 28 ||

gaṅgāpātaiścaturbhiśca caturdigbhyaḥ sunirjharaiḥ|
virājate hi śailendraḥ kūṭodbhūtaiḥ sunirmalaiḥ|| 29 ||

prācīkūṭodbhavenāśu javaprapatanena ca|
raktābhena jalenārya patākayeva pūjitam|| 30 ||

yāmyakūṭodbhavenāśu vegaprapatanena vai|
añjanābhena toyena patākayeva sundaram|| 31 ||

pratīcīkūṭasambhūtanirjhareṇa suveginā|
raupyābhena jalenaivaṃ patākayeva śobhitam|| 32 ||

udīcīkūṭasambhūtanirjhareṇa suveginā|
hiraṇyābhajalenaiva patākayeva sundaram|| 33 ||

koṭibhirjaladhārābhirnirjharairjalapātibhiḥ|
rājitaṃ girirājendraṃ sarvatejobhisārakam|| 34 ||

jāmbūnadajayā nadyā āvartinyā mahodayām|
anavyayāścaturdikṣu tadadho hi susaṃvṛtam|| 35 ||

tatprāntare 'acalaiścānyaiḥ sarvadhātumayairvṛtam|
ityetat kathito 'agastya sarvadevāśrayo giriḥ|| 36 ||

bhūyo 'ahaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikāgramānasaḥ|
tataḥ prācīdiśaṃ gatvā cakārodayaparvatam|| 37 ||

lakṣayojanavistāraṃ tadardhaṃ ca samucchritam|
ṛṣabhaṃ nāma ca brahmā prathitaṃ bhuvi durlabham|| 38 ||

hemarajatavṛkṣāḍhyaṃ puṣparatnopaśobhitam|
śatayojanavistāraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam|| 39 ||

jātarūpamayaiḥ śṛṅgai rājitaṃ sānubhirbhṛśam|
bhūyaścakāra dhātāsau bahuratnopalairmune|| 40 ||

mahendram atha śailendraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam|
jātarūpamayaiḥ śṛṅgairbālakādityasaṃnibhaiḥ|| 41 ||

rājitaṃ taṃ mahāśailaṃ sarvadhātuvibhūṣitam|
sarvadrumalatopetaṃ sarvapuṣpopaśobhitam|| 42 ||

bahurasaphalopetaṃ trividhairjantubhiścitam|
parvatāṃśca bahūṃstatra cakāra ca pitāmahaḥ|
sānumān dhātumāñchailān sapakṣan bahuśo bahūn|| 43 ||
 dhātumān śailān Y

nadyastatra prajāyante girigahvarasānutaḥ|
dyau ārohaṇahetukyo mokṣakāmaphalapradāḥ|| 44 ||

dakṣiṇāsyāṃ diśi dhātā gatvā vindhyaṃ cakāra saḥ|
sāhasraśikharairdivyairvividhadrumalatāvṛtam|| 45 ||

tadyāmye sa samāgatya sasarja bahuśo 'acalān|
nānādrumalatākīrṇān bahudhātuvibhūṣaṇān|| 46 ||

malayaṃ ca giriśreṣṭhaṃ sasarja punarātmabhūḥ|
merupratimarūpeṇa kiraṇena sadārcitam|| 47 ||

nānāratnasamākīrṇaṃ nānādrumasamākulam|
divyagandhamahollāsaṃ divyacandanavṛkṣakam|| 48 ||

sāhasrairyojanāyāmaṃ tadardhena samucchritam|
svarṇaraupyākarai ratnaiḥ śobhitaṃ paramācalam|| 49 ||

nadyaśca vipulā vṛttāḥ pulinadrumaśobhitāḥ|
vetralatādrumairyuktāḥ sasarja trividhā bahūḥ|| 50 ||

sānuśikharajā dhātā vaitaraṇī tathā punaḥ|
nānātīrthāni jāyante saṃgame vividhāni ca|| 51 ||

pratīcyāṃ diśi gatvāsau bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ|
sasarja parvataṃ ramyam ardhakāñcanarājitam|| 52 ||

ardhaṃ ca sūryasaṃkāśam ekataścandrasaṃnibham|
tejobhyāṃ yugapadvyāptaṃ sūryācandramasoriva|| 53 ||

sānumantaṃ giriśreṣṭham aśvamantaṃ suśobhanam|
bahuyojanavistāraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam|| 54 ||

sarvakāmaphalairdivyairvṛtaṃ manoramaṃ drumaiḥ|
sarvataḥ kāñcanaṃ gehaṃ sarvataḥ svarṇavedikam|| 55 ||

kāñcanaraupyavṛkṣāḍhyaṃ puṣpahāsaiḥ samṛddhitam|
astācalaṃ mahāśailam ṛṣabhaṃ nāma cocchritam|| 56 ||

mahendram aparaṃ śailaṃ śatayojanam ucchritam|
jātarūpodbhavaiḥ śṛṅgairbahudhātusamāyutam|| 57 ||

cakārāgastya medinyāṃ prajākṣobham ivācalam|
nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ sarvapuṣpopaśobhitam|| 58 ||

tataḥ sasarja śailendraṃ sarvatejaḥpraśobhanam|
dhātuśilāsamāyuktaṃ bahudrumalatāyutam|| 59 ||

śobhitaṃ taṃ mahāśṛṅgairjātarūpamayairdrumaiḥ|
sānūdbhūtaiśca dhārābhirbahupuṣpopaśobhanaiḥ|| 60 ||

sarvauṣadhisamudbhūtaṃ sasarja gandhamādanam|
auṣadhīnāṃ ca dhātūnāṃ tejobhiśca samujjvalam|| 61 ||

ṣaṣṭiṃ girisahasrāṇi paścime saṃniveśayat|
sarvaphalodbhavairvṛkṣaiḥ sarvapuṣpoparājitaiḥ|| 62 ||

nāvyā pārā apārā hi nadyastebhyo visusruvuḥ|
pāvinyaḥ kāmadāgastya bahusaṃgamasaṃyutāḥ|| 63 ||

gatvodīcyāṃ diśi sraṣṭā ratnakūṭaṃ suśobhanam|
bahudhātusamāyuktaṃ vaidūryamaṇirājitam|| 64 ||

jātarūpaprabhaiḥ śṛṅgairhemavṛkṣalatāḍhyakaiḥ|
jāmbūnadarasotpannairjalaiḥ kūṭaprapātanaiḥ|| 65 ||

hemaraupyagṛhairyuktaṃ guhādarisamāyutam|
vividharatnacitrāḍhyaṃ sasarja girim uttamam|| 66 ||

śatayojanavistāraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam|
divi sthānaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ harṣajanakam aṅginām|| 67 ||

mandaraṃ ca tapaścakre hemaraupyaśilāmayam|
bahudhātusamāyuktaṃ bahutejaḥsamākulam|| 68 ||

citrasānuṃ susānuṃ ca bahusānuṃ tathāparam|
maṇisānuṃ taḍidvantaṃ jyotiṣsānuṃ dharottamam|| 69 ||

puṣpaphalalatotpannaṃ hemalatāsamāvṛtam|
bahuvṛkṣauṣadhīyuktaṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam|| 70 ||

viṃśayojanavistāraṃ daśayojanam ucchritam|
catvāriṃśat tathā triṃśat pañcāśacca tathāparam|| 71 ||

ṣaṣṭiṃ ca saptamaṃ caiva cāśītinavatistathā|
yojanānāṃ ca keṣāmcidvistāram ucchritaṃ tathā|| 72 ||

bahuśailāṃstathā cakre sarvadrumavibhūṣitān|
nānākarasamāyuktān bahudhāturasodbhavān|| 73 ||

nadyo visusruvustebhyo hemavālūjjvalā varāḥ|
hemavetravalatpatrā hemapuṣpopaśobhitāḥ|| 74 ||

hiraṇyāśmataraṅgiṇyo hiraṇyodakasaṃyutāḥ|
bahusaṃgamasaṃyuktāḥ pāvinyo 'atibhramākulāḥ|| 75 ||

tato vidhātā diśi cottarasyāṃ cakāra gatvā hi girīn sa bhūyaḥ|
tatprāntareṣvevam alaṃ digadrīn kṛtvā vidhijño giriśaprasādāt|| 76 ||

meroruttarabhāge 'asau suvarṇādriṃ cakāra ca|
bahuyojanavistāraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam|| 77 ||

bahudhātusamāyuktaṃ bahuratnamayaṃ dharam|
svarṇapuṣpapraphullāḍhyaṃ svarṇavṛkṣasamākulam|| 78 ||

hiraṇyapadmaphullāḍhyaṃ nikuñjaiḥ svarṇasambhavaiḥ|
rājitaṃ svarṇapākhaṇḍairguhādarisamāyutam|| 79 ||

praṇālībhiśca vāpībhiḥ sānubhiśca manoramaiḥ|
siddhirasojjharairdivyaiḥ svarṇajalaprapātanaiḥ|| 80 ||

tatra svāṃśaṃ ca herambaṃ pratiṣṭhāpyādhikaṃ mune|
ityevaṃ kṛtya taṃ sraṣṭā pūrvadiśi samāvrajat|| 81 ||

gatvā prācīṃ diśaṃ sraṣṭā cakāra girim uttamam|
citrasānuṃ tathā bhūyaḥ sarvonnatena nirmitam|| 82 ||

nānādhātusamāyuktairbahugairikasambhavaiḥ|
sarvaratnasamāyuktaiḥ sarvatejobhisārakaiḥ|| 83 ||

bahukāñcanasambhūtairbahupuṣpopaśobhanaiḥ|
raktotpalasamākīrṇaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ|| 84 ||

ramyavedīsamāyuktaiḥ sānubhiḥ samalaṃkṛtaiḥ|
haritālaiḥ suraṅgaiśca manaḥśilāmanoramaiḥ|| 85 ||

raktavṛkṣasamāyuktai raktavetralatodbhavaiḥ|
raktatejomayaṃ śailaṃ raktābhajalanirjharaiḥ|| 86 ||

bahuyojanavistāraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam|
agamyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvasāramayaṃ śubham|| 87 ||

āryāprekṣasamāgatya śailarāje samāviśat|
catuḥṣaṣṭigaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ yoginīkoṭibhirmudā|| 88 ||

citrasānuṃ vidhiḥ kṛtvā vidhātā lokabhāvanaḥ|
bhūyaḥ kartuṃ giriṃ dhīrāvācīṃ diśaṃ tathāgamat|| 89 ||

samāgatya tato brahmā cakāra girim uttamam|
kailāsaṃ sumahākūṭaṃ sarvatejomayaṃ śivam|| 90 ||

raupyābhaṃ rājitaṃ śailaṃ nānādhātusamudbhavaiḥ|
pāṣāṇai rājitairdivyai rājatābhamahādrumaiḥ|| 91 ||

rājitaṃ sānubhirbhavyai rājatodbhavavetrakaiḥ|
rājatodbhavarājībhii rājatakusumaistathā|| 92 ||

rājatābhajalairyuktaiḥ sarobhii rājodbhavaiḥ|
rājatotpannavallībhiḥ śvetaphullanikuñjakaiḥ|| 93 ||

rājatābhajalotpannaiḥ sarvatejomayaiḥ śubhaiḥ|
rājatābhāsudhābhūtāgaṅgādhārānipātanaiḥ|| 94 ||

nānārasaphalotpannaiḥ ṣaḍṛtujairmanoharaiḥ|
triguṇairvāyubhiryuktaṃ sarvasattvānukāmpakam|| 95 ||

bahuyojanavistāraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam|
raupyatāmramayāgāraṃ guhāḍhyaṃ ratnasaṃyutam|| 96 ||

jāmbūnadarasodbhūtaṃ pārijātaṃ sukhāvaham|
mahataḥ parvatasyāgre puṣpahāsaṃ nyaveśayat|| 97 ||

ekayojanavistāram ekayojanam ucchritam|
siddhirasarasopetaṃ manovāñchāphalapradam|| 98 ||

sphāṭikāḍhyaṃ mahollāsaṃ maṇimayaṃ manoramam|
sadānandaṃ mahāśailaṃ sarvatejobhihāriṇam|| 99 ||

tam īḍyaḥ śaṃkaro devaḥ samadhyaniṣṭhadīśvaraḥ|
catuḥṣaṣṭigaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ girirāje nirantaram|| 100 ||

trikūṭaṃ ca tathā kṛtvā bhinnāñjanacayopamam|
yāmyāṃ diśaṃ punardhātā prayayau hi yadṛcchayā|| 101 ||

tato dhyātvā maheśānaṃ sarvadevamaheśvaram|
pracakāra vidhānajño himavantaṃ nageśvaram|| 102 ||

sahasrakūṭam āścaryaḥ sarvonnatāḍhyasundaraḥ|
sarvātiriktasāreṇa himairgirirvirājate|| 103 ||

himarūpairvidhirdharmaṃ saṃsṛjya tvaritaṃ mudā|
dharmarūpairhimaistaiśca dhātrā vibhūṣito giriḥ|| 104 ||

puṇyasthānaṃ mahāśṛṅgaḥ sarvaśailottamottamaḥ|
raupyābho vividhākāro 'abhralehī sureśvaraḥ|| 105 ||

nānāratnamayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ sāhasrairupasevitaḥ|
tuṣārabhūṣitaiḥ śṛṅgai rājatābhairvirājitaḥ|| 106 ||

puṇyatīrthaiśca sāhasraiḥ koṭyudbhavasunirjharaiḥ|
sāhasraiḥ sānubhiryuktaiḥ sāhasrapādasambhavaiḥ|| 107 ||

kvacijjātamayaiḥ śṛṅgairvaidūryamaṇisambhavaiḥ|
pravālāṅkurasambhūtairvidrumāḍhyaṃ virājitaiḥ|| 108 ||

puṣparāgamayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ sphaṭikāḍhyaṃ sunirmalaiḥ|
kvacinmārakasambhūtairindranīlamayaiḥ kvacit|| 109 ||

kvacidvajramayaiḥ śṛṅgaiścandrakāntamayaistathā|
sūryakāntamayirdivyairnīlāñjanacayopamaiḥ|| 110 ||

tāmramayairmahāśṛṅgairlohamayaistathāparaiḥ|
trapusīsamayaiḥ śṛṅgairbahudhātumayaistathā|| 111 ||

haritālamayaiḥ śṛṅgairmanaḥśilāmanoharaiḥ|
gairikamayasambhūtairañjanācalamecakaiḥ|| 112 ||

vividhaiḥ sānubhirnityaṃ bhūṣito giribhūṣaṇaḥ|
jāmbūnadamayodbhūtakuṭṭimottamasundaraiḥ|| 113 ||

rājatāḍhyamayodbhūtacandraśālāmahojjvalaiḥ|
sutejāmayavajrāḍhyacandraśālāvirājitaiḥ|| 114 ||

vaidūryamayanirmāṇacandraśālāvibhūṣitaiḥ|
indranīlamayodbhūtakuṭṭimojjvalasundaraiḥ|| 115 ||

puṣparāgamayodbhūtakuṭṭimairgaurakāntibhiḥ|
mārakatamayanirmāṇacandraśālāharitprabhaiḥ|| 116 ||

nīlāñjanopalodbhūtakuṭṭimaśyāmalaprabhaiḥ|
candrakāntamayodbhūtacandraśālārjunojjvalaiḥ|| 117 ||

sūryakāntamayodbhūtakuṭṭimairlohitaprabhaiḥ|
sphaṭikopalanirmāṇacandraśālārjunaprabhaiḥ|| 118 ||

padmarāgamayodbhūtakuṭṭimaśoṇasundaraiḥ|
pravālāḍhyasunirmāṇacandraśālāruṇaprabhaiḥ|| 119 ||

nānāratnāḍhyanirmāṇakuṭṭimakurburojjvalaiḥ|
itthaṃbhūtairmahāśṛṅgairvirājitaṃ himālayam|| 120 ||

jāmbūnadamayairvṛkṣai rājatodbhavapādapaiḥ|
trapusīsodbhavairvṛkṣai rājatodbhavaśākhibhiḥ|| 121 ||

kanakodbhavavallībhiḥ svaccharājatasambhavaiḥ|
hiraṇyakusumairbhavyaiḥ prasūnairbahuraṅgajaiḥ|| 122 ||

bahulatodbhavaiḥ kuñjairdarbhāṅkuraistathāvidhaiḥ|
hiraṇyanalinairdivyai rājatodbhavapuṣkaraiḥ|| 123 ||

vāpībhirvividhākhātairguhābhiḥ kandaraistathā|
bhṛgubhirnirjharaiḥ kūṭāgaṇḍaśailairmahādbhutaiḥ|| 124 ||

śuśubhe girirājendraḥ śikharairbahunāmabhiḥ|
bhṛgupātairnadībhiśca bahutīrthaistadā mune|| 125 ||

kedārabadrikāphāryatriśīrṣaśikharaistathā|
viṣṇvāśramamahākūṭakūrmādriśikharaiḥ punaḥ|| 126 ||

raupyaśikharijaṃbadribrahmaśikharakoṭibhiḥ|
agniśṛṅgaikaśṛṅgomāparvataśekharaistathā|| 127 ||

yatraiva bhagavān dharmo dravībhūto 'atra hetutaḥ|
tathāvidho 'apyadharmo hi dharmatīrthena ke tathā|| 128 ||

dharmakūṭābhralehībhiḥ siddhāśramanagottamaiḥ|
gaṇḍādrimuktipāṇḍvadriśyāmalaśikharaistathā|| 129 ||

vṛttāhāryatriśūlādrimuñjavatśikharaiḥ punaḥ|
buddhāśramādriviṣṇvadrigauryadriśikharairvaraiḥ|| 130 ||

kuśaparvatakāmādrinīlādriśikharairvaraiḥ|
agniśekharabhasmādrikāmādrisundarādribhiḥ|| 131 ||

rājitaṃ girirājendram etaiḥ kāraṇam ādibhiḥ|
pūrvato dakṣiṇe śṛṅge prekṣyācyuto himālayam|| 132 ||

harṣaṃ nyavīviśadviṣṇurbadrikādrigaṇaiḥ saha|
koṭiyojanavistāraṃ lakṣayojanam ucchritam|| 133 ||

pūrvāparārṇavaṃ vyāptaṃ tadadhaśca tathāvidham|
koṭisānusamāyuktaṃ koṭikoṭyanvitārcitam|| 134 ||

koṭyātmajaiḥ samaṃ pātrairhimālayo virājate|
merupratimasaṃkāśaṃ himabhūṣaṇabhūṣitam|| 135 ||

yāvatyaḥ prodbhavā nadyastāvatyaḥ kāmadāniśam|
pāvinyaḥ sarvalokānāṃ vimocanti hi kilbiṣān|| 136 ||

brahmaputrapravāhena haimavatyā ca gaṅgayā|
bhadrayālakanandākhyarevayā śatarudrayā|| 137 ||

kauśikīgaṇḍakībhiśca vāgmatyā parayā tathā|
śiprāvātādibhirdhīro himavān rājate 'aniśam|| 138 ||

kṛtvāccharūpiṇaḥ śailān sapakṣān vividhāṃścaran|
pavitrakān punardhātā sasarja bahuśo dharān|| 139 ||

tato brahmā manaścakre jantūn sraṣṭuṃ rasātalam|
sarvalokahitātmāsau sthitaye sarvajanminām|| 140 ||

tato girīṇāṃ ca tadā didṛkṣurdṛptaujaso matyarādhahetoḥ|
ciccheda śakraḥ kuliśena pakṣāñchailāṃścirāt sthāvaratāṃ gatāste|| 141 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe sarvācalotpattirnāma tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ|| 3 ||

skanda uvāca |

tato dhātā kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā trinetraṃ śaṃkaraṃ vibhum|
stutiṃ cakāra dharmātmā sarvabhūtodbhavāya ca|
vidhāya svāñjaliṃ mūrdhni sanatirbhagavān prabhuḥ|| 1 ||

brahmovāca |

.o, |

namo 'astu devadevāya sarvabhūtāya bhūtine|
bhūtodbhavāya bhavyāya bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ|| 2 ||

sṛṣṭisthitisvarūpāya sarvajñāya vivekine|
viśvātmane maheśāya viśvavyāpakarūpiṇe|| 3 ||

alakṣāya niraṃśāya nirvikārāya nandine|
apramāṇāya mānāya gamyāyāgamyadehine|| 4 ||

mānāpamānaghāriṇe māyine 'amāyine namaḥ|
sārāya sāradevāya saṃsārasaṃhatātmane|| 5 ||

alakṣyāyākṣarāṅgāya kṣaṇarūpāya śūline|
antodbhavāya jīvāya antaḥsthitāya śāśvate|| 6 ||

tejorūpāya tāpāya tryambakāya namo namaḥ|
varadāya jagatkartre jagatāṃ cakṣuṣe namaḥ|| 7 ||

pañcātmakodbhaveśāya pañcātmakavibhūtine|
dhātusthāya vidhātāya jagat sarvaṃ vidhāyine|
saṃsāradāya rudrāya saṃsārarūpiṇe namaḥ|| 8 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti stavaṃ samākarṇya jyotirūpī mahāvibhuḥ|
saṃtuṣṭavān vidhātre ca varaṃ dātuṃ pracakrame|| 9 ||

vyaktaṃ kṛtya svam ātmānaṃ sarvatejomayo vibhuḥ|
svatejobhiḥ saharṣaṃ ca udyotayan diśo vidik|| 10 ||

jyotirūpa uvāca |

tuṣṭo haṃ te stavenārya sarvabhūtopakāriṇā|
varaṃ varaya lokeśa yat te vāñchasi sāmpratam|| 11 ||

dāsyāmīdam ahaṃ sarvaṃ jaṅgamasthāvarātmakam|
jñātvā māṃ kāmadaṃ dhātarupakārāya jīvinām|| 12 ||

stavaṃ yaḥ prapaṭhelloke tava vaktrādvinirgatam|
sarvapātakanirmuktaḥ sarvakāmaphalaṃ labhet|| 13 ||

brahmovāca |

tvatprasādādahaṃ deva kṛtavān bhūdharān dharān|
idānīṃ sraṣṭum icchāmi sarvabhūtāni śaṃkara|| 14 ||

andhībhūtaṃ jagat sarvaṃ kathaṃ sthāsyanti jīvinaḥ|
udyotavyaṃ samāṃśena yadi prema mayi prabho|| 15 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya vaco dhāturlokānugrahakārakam|
cintayāmāsa devo 'asau kṣaṇaṃ tadā ghaṭodbhava|| 16 ||

tato dakṣekṣaṇāṃśaṃ sa ādāya pāṇinā vibhuḥ|
sasarjādau purā devaṃ jyotīrūpaṃ mahāvibhum|| 17 ||

tejorūpaṃ jagannetram aprameyam agocaram|
jagatsākṣiṇam ābhāḍhyam ādidevaṃ sanātanam|| 18 ||

dvihaste padmasaṃyuktam ekāsyaṃ tīkṣṇadīdhitim|
trinetraṃ lohitāṅgaṃ taṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam|| 19 ||

bhūyaḥ sasarja bhūteśo bhūtānāṃ patiravyayam|
vāmanetrāṃśam ādāya sarvalokahite ratam|| 20 ||

āhlādanaṃ mahākāntiṃ sudhāṃśuṃ śītadhṛṣṇayam|
divyarūpaṃ mahābhūtiṃ sarvādhārasvarūpiṇam|| 21 ||

somaṃ ca saumyamūrtiṃ ca raupyābhaṃ sukalevaram|
trinetraṃ dvibhujaṃ śāntam ekasyam upakāriṇam|| 22 ||

bhūyaḥ sasarja tejasvī sarvatejomayaṃ suram|
ūrdhvanetraṃ samādāya pāṇinā divyarūpiṇā|| 23 ||

saptānanaṃ mahāraudram aurvaṃ tīkṣṇakalevaram|
ekaviṃśekṣaṇairyuktaṃ caturdaśabhujaistathā|| 24 ||

saṃsṛjya trisurān rudra uvāca vacanaṃ tadā|
pitāmahāya vipreśa prādurbhāvasya hetukam|| 25 ||

īśvara uvāca |

mama rūpo harirjñeyo viṣṇoḥ rūpastvahaṃ tathā|
tava rūpo harirbrahman viṣṇoḥ rūpastvam ātmanaḥ|| 26 ||

mama mūrtistathā tvaṃ ca tava mūrtirahaṃ punaḥ|
tena tasya na bhedatvaṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmyaham|| 27 ||

tathā no mūrtayo devāḥ sūryacandrānalāmbhasaḥ|
kṣitivyomānilā devī yajamānastathā dvijāḥ|| 28 ||

bhedābhedaṃ na kartavyam iti ājñā te mayā kṛtā|
no mūrtayo mahāprājña sarvabhāvena bhūtinā|| 29 ||

skanda uvāca |

vyaktīkṛtya tadātmānaṃ sambodhyaivaṃ pitāmaham|
bhāsayaṃśca diśo bhābhiryayau kailāsam īśvaraḥ|| 30 ||

ityetadvacanaṃ śrutvā rudrasya paramātmanaḥ|
bhūyaḥ stavaṃ tadāgastya cakāra sa pitāmahaḥ|| 31 ||

brahmovāca |

.o, |

śivāya viṣṇurūpāya viṣṇave śivarūpiṇe|
namo devādhidevāya viśveśvarāya bhūtine|| 32 ||

namaḥ sudhāṃśubhālāya namastilakacarcine|
trinetrāya dvinetrāya dvidoṣṇe bahubāhave|| 33 ||

namo nāgendrakaṇṭhāya namaḥ kaustubhakaṇṭhine|
bhasmāṅgarāgaśobhāya ghanasārāṅgarāgiṇe|| 34 ||

vyāghrāmbarāya bhargāya pītāmbarāya viṣṇave|
kailāsavāsine 'ajāya vaikuṇṭhavāsine namaḥ|| 35 ||

vividhadeharūpāya nānākāyavidhāyine|
kālātītāya kālāya kāmakāntāya śauraye|| 36 ||

namo viśvesvarāryāya namo viśvambharāya ca|
vāmadeva namastubhyaṃ vāsudeva namo 'astu te|| 37 ||

śivāya jalarūpāya kṣitirūpāya viṣṇave|
rudrāya vyomarūpāya haraye vāyumūrtaye|| 38 ||

īśāya ravirūpāya kṛṣṇāya somamūrtaye|
ugrāya yajñarūpāya vahnirūpāya śārṅgiṇe|| 39 ||

namo bhavāya mantrāya vedāṅgāya namo namaḥ|
yajamānasvarūpāya śruvarūpāya vai namaḥ|| 40 ||

namo ghṛtātmane 'ajāya namo haviḥsvarūpiṇe|
namo bhoktre ca bhojyāya sukhāyānandaśāśvate|| 41 ||

tṛptaye tṛptirūpāya tuṣṭirūpāya vai namaḥ|
jīveśvarāya rudrāya caitanyāya namo namaḥ|| 42 ||

skanda uvāca |

niśamyeti stavaṃ viṣṇurdivyaṃ hariharātmakam|
prahṛṣṭavāṃstadā tasmai brahmaṇe brahmasambhavaḥ|| 43 ||

tato varapradānāya vyaktaṃ kṛtya kalevaram|
saṃtuṣṭavān haristasmai uvāca vacanaṃ mune|| 44 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

tuṣṭo 'ahaṃ stutibhirbrahman bhavadvaktrādviniḥsṛtaiḥ|
dāsye 'adhunā varaṃ tubhyaṃ śṛṇuṣva naḥ samāhitaḥ|| 45 ||
 vinissṛtaiḥ Y

sṛjatāṃ sarvalokān vai yadṛcchayā rasātale|
sṛjāmi ca tvayā sārdhaṃ bahunetra pitāmaha|| 46 ||

yaḥ paṭhiṣyati martyo vā stavaṃ hariharātmakam|
asmatpriyakaraṃ brahman sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate|| 47 ||

dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ yaśaścāyurlabdhvā pīḍāvivarjitaḥ|
asādhyaṃ sādhayet kṣipraṃ sarvaśatruṃ vimardyatām|| 48 ||

bhūtvā ca vedavidvipro bhuktā bhogān yathepsitān|
caturvargaphalaṃ prāpto mayyante sa viliṣyati|| 49 ||

skanda uvāca |

samākarṇya tato dhātā vacanaṃ viṣṇubhāṣitam|
mene svam iti kartāraṃ romāñcanaḥ prahṛṣṭavān|| 50 ||

tataḥ sasarja sarvātmā om ityekākṣaraṃ param|
tasmāt svarāḥ prajāyante mātrā varṇāstataḥ param|| 51 ||

vyāhṛtī ca mahādevī caturviṃśākṣarātmikā|
jāyate tatpadaṃ divyaṃ catuḥpādasamāyutam|| 52 ||

tato nādāśca chandāṃsi vaṣaṭkāraḥ prajāyate|
ṛksāmātharvayajuṣo jāyante śrutayastathā|| 53 ||

viṣṇuḥ sasarja devarṣīn saṃsārasthitihetave|
nārāyaṇo narātmāno manasaivaṃ purā mune|| 54 ||

sanacca bhagavān ādyaḥ sanakaśca mahāvibhuḥ|
sanātanaśca viśvātmā sanandako varapradaḥ|| 55 ||

sanatkumāra evārya brahmā ca kapilastathā|
ete yogina ādyāśca viṣṇormanasi sambhavāḥ|| 56 ||

dharmiṣṭhāste vratasthāśca munayo dharmadeśikāḥ|
ete viśvaṃ hi yogīśā dhārayanti carācaram|| 57 ||

tato brahmā sasarjādau saptarṣīṃśca dvijottamān|
manasaiva tadāgastya sarvabhūtodbhavāya ca|| 58 ||

marīciṃ varam atriṃ ca pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum|
bhṛgum aṅgirasaṃ caivam etān munivarān mune|| 59 ||

jaigīṣavyaṃ manuṃ bhūyo 'asitaṃ devalaṃ tathā|
pitṛṃśca sarvabhūtānāṃ nṛdevāsurarakṣasām|| 60 ||

saptarṣibhyaśca tebhyo vai jajñire sacarācarāḥ|
devāsurāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ|| 61 ||

kiṃnarā guhyakāścaiva vidyādharāpsarogaṇāḥ|
sādhyānilāḥ piśācāśca ete 'agastya surodbhavāḥ|| 62 ||

agastya uvāca |

dehināṃ sarvabhūtānām utpattiśca kathaṃ bhavet|
saṃsārasāradehānāṃ vinā śaktiṃ ca sarvavit|| 63 ||

śivaśaktyātmakaṃ proktaṃ jagacca sacarācaram|
iti naḥ saṃśayo jāto vismayo 'atra mahān bhavet|| 64 ||

skanda uvāca |

sthityutpattinirodhānāṃ devānāṃ caritaṃ hitam|
saṃśayaśca na kartavyo 'adbhutaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ|| 65 ||

sarvabhūtopakārasya brahmaṇā śrutibhiḥ stutam|
devasya caritaṃ vakṣye tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu|| 66 ||

brahmaṇo 'agastya kalpānte niḥśeṣānte suradruhām|
paraṃ śivaṃ harirdadhyau lokajananahetunā|| 67 ||

sargaṃ cintayato viṣṇorvaktrāt praniḥsṛtaḥ purā|
puruṣaḥ khalu devāṃśaḥ kiṃ karomītyupasthitaḥ|| 68 ||

saṃsṛjātmānam ityuktvā tirodhānaṃ gato 'acyutaḥ|
tataḥ sa puruṣaḥ sraṣṭuṃ dhyātavān hi śarīriṇas|| 69 ||

puruṣasya tato 'agastya dhyānavatastatastadā|
salilaṃ jāyate tasmādbhūmiḥ prajāyate punaḥ|| 70 ||

tataḥ śailāḥ prajāyante tasmādoṣadhayastathā|
candramā manaso jātaścakṣvoḥ sūryo vyajāyata|| 71 ||

śrotrābhyāṃ janayadvāyuṃ mukhādagnirajāyata|
nāsābhyāṃ jāyate vyoma āsīddyauḥ śīrṣam avyayam|| 72 ||

daśa diśaśca pādāgraṃ dakṣāṅguṣṭhādajasya vai|
ajāyata ghaṭodbhūta dakṣo nāma prajāpatiḥ|| 73 ||

vāmāṅguṣṭhācca hastasya dākṣāyaṇī vyajāyata|
bhāryā dakṣasya jānīhi asyāḥ kanyā ajāyata|| 74 ||

brāhmaṇāstasya mūrdhno vai bāhubhyāṃ kṣatriyāḥ punaḥ|
ūrubhyāṃ ca tathā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ padbhyāṃ tathāvidhāḥ|| 75 ||

nadādimṛttikāḥ sarvāḥ pūtā bhavanti bhūtale|
tajjalāni ca sarvāṇi tīrthā eva na saṃśayaḥ|| 76 ||

tato dākṣāyaṇī dhīra ṣaṣṭiṃ kanyā ajījanat|
pradadau daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa|| 77 ||

saptaviṃśacca somāya manave ca trayodaśa|
satīm ekāṃ dadau dakṣaḥ śaṃkarāya mahātmane|| 78 ||

adityāṃ jajñire devā bhāryāyāṃ kaśyapasya vai|
indropendrādayo devāḥ koṭikoṭisahasraśaḥ|| 79 ||

dvitīyāyāṃ ca bhāryāyāṃ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ|
dityāṃ ca jajñire daityā mahāśūrā mahābalāḥ|| 80 ||

hiraṇyakaśipurnāma hiraṇyākṣastathā punaḥ|
śumbhastathā niśumbhaśca andhakaśca mahāsuraḥ|| 81 ||

eteṣāṃ devadaityānāṃ koṭikoṭisurāsurāḥ|
ajāyanta mahāprājña sutāstīvraparākramāḥ|| 82 ||

devānāṃ ca surāṇāṃ ca kālānte ca parasparam|
virodhaśca mahān āsīdbhṛśaṃ mitho jayaiṣiṇām|| 83 ||

durvāsanāmna āryasya śāpāt teṣām abhūddvija|
tataḥ prabhṛtiranyeṣāṃ virodham aparādhataḥ|| 84 ||

himavati varaśaile vāñchitārthaprade te anupamaphalalabdhā devadevaprasādāt|
atisulalitalokān prāpnuyurdevadaityā dvijavara tava hārdrāt te mayoktaṃ hi sargam|| 85 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe lokasargo nāma caturtho adhyāyaḥ|| 4 ||

agastya uvāca |

pātālānāṃ pramāṇaṃ yat kathaṃ svarṇācalaṃ dhṛtam|
balinaḥ ke ca saptānāṃ dhārakāsteṣu vāsinaḥ|| 1 ||

vareṇa toṣitaḥ kena himavān bhūdhareśvaraḥ|
vivāhitā kathaṃ kanyā kasyātmajā vada prabho|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

śṛṇudhvam abhidhāsyāmi maṇimaye 'acalottame|
pureśena yaduktaṃ me tat sarvaṃ nikhilena ca|| 3 ||

koṭiyojanavistāraṃ tadardhaṃ ca samucchritam|
tvagasthisaṃvṛtaṃ dehaṃ kūrmarūpaṃ dadhāra saḥ|| 4 ||

tasyopari varāho 'asau sthito mahākalevaraḥ|
sthitaye bhuvanānāṃ ca dvisaptānāṃ ghaṭodbhava|| 5 ||

tasya pṛṣṭhe mahāpadme koṭiyojanavistṛte|
sakeśare mahacchubhre karṇikāyāṃ ca bhāsvati|| 6 ||

ābrahmalokaparyantaṃ sthāpayenmerum ātmabhūḥ|
diggajaiśca samāyuktaṃ sāhasrairyojanairmune|| 7 ||

tatpramāṇaiścaturbhiśca caturdikṣu kramāt punaḥ|
bhuvanāni dvisaptāni dhārayantaṃ mahojjvalam|| 8 ||

teṣāṃ madhye sthito gāḍhaṃ jambūdvīpaḥ saparvataḥ|
pramāṇaṃ tasya pūrvoktaṃ śeṣāṇāṃ ca vadāmyaham|| 9 ||

dvīpaprānte ca śeṣāhivalayākṛtiśobhanaḥ|
adhobhāge sthito 'ajasraṃ pātālaṃ nāma saptamaḥ|| 10 ||

padmākāraṃ sakiñjalkaṃ dhvānte ratnamahojjvalam|
caturdikṣu sthitaṃ vyāpya ratnasānoḥ suśobhanam|| 11 ||

yojanānāṃ ca koṭīnāṃ tatpañcāśatpramāṇataḥ|
pātālasya ca vistāraṃ daśalakṣaṃ samucchritam|| 12 ||

vāsukistatra nāgendro vasan nityaṃ gaṇaiḥ saha|
pūjayaṃśca maheśānaṃ virājate nirantaram|| 13 ||

sitena dehena virājate 'aniśaṃ suratnahārārcitakandharottamaḥ|
sahasrabhogāḍhyaphaṇīndravāsukiḥ śivārcanāsaktakarāravindakaḥ|| 14 ||

dadhāra pṛthvīṃ valayākṛtirvai ahīśvaraḥ prāntarataśca tasyāḥ|
sahasrabhogairlalajihvatīkṣṇaiḥ supuṇyapāpocchvasitottamāṅgaḥ|| 15 ||

dhārayaṃśca mahīṃ sarvāṃ sabhāmadhye virājate|
yadā devadvijān gāśca nārcayanti ca mānavāḥ|| 16 ||

medinī ca guruḥ pāpādatiśayo bhavedbhṛśam|
tadbhāreṇa samākrānto bahūcchvasiti vāsukiḥ|
saṃjāyate hi tacchvāsādbhūmikampaḥ saparvataḥ|| 17 ||

śaṃsati ca tadā nṛṇāṃ kampaḥ svalpāyuṣastataḥ|
pūjayantyatha vā martyā dīrghāyuṣo na saṃśayaḥ|| 18 ||

tatra cādhipatirdaityo vairocanirmahābalī|
rājate viṣṇunā yukto dānavaiḥ saha nityaśaḥ|| 19 ||

vipradoṣaistathā śrādhe vākyadoṣairamedhyataḥ|
pitṛṇāṃ yannarairdattaṃ tat sarvaṃ harate balī|| 20 ||

pūjayaṃśca mahādevaṃ mudā yukto varottamam|
himavatparvate labdhvā śaṃkarasya prasādataḥ|| 21 ||

tato rasātalaṃ nāma śilāsaṃghātabhūmikam|
śvetakāntisamāyuktaṃ bhavedratnāṃśubhirmune|| 22 ||

koṭīnāṃ yojanānāṃ ca tat pūrvoktaṃ pramāṇataḥ|
rasātalasya vistāraṃ paṅktilakṣasamucchritam|| 23 ||

mahāpadmaśca nāgendro bahunāgaiḥ susevitaḥ|
sitaratnamaye gehe avasacca nirantaram|| 24 ||

hemādrikāntyuttamavigraho vai hāraprabhākāntitasundaraśca|
śūlābjaśaṅkhāṅkitamastako 'asau strībhistriśīrṣaiḥ pravirājamānaḥ|| 25 ||

valayākṛtināgendro dadhāra phāṇibhii rasām|
mahāpadmo mahānāgo harapādārcane rataḥ|
pātālaṃ dhārayaṃstatra pūjayati maheśvaram|| 26 ||

yadā dharmopavāsāṃśca na kurvanti mahītale|
gurutā ca bhavedbhūmergāḍhapāpādanāratam|| 27 ||

tadbhāreṇa bhṛśaṃ krāntaḥ procchvāsayati nāgarāṭ|
nāgocchvāsodgatādvāyorbhūmikampaḥ prajāyate|| 28 ||

nṛṇāṃ śaṃsati tatkampo nānārogāṃstadā punaḥ|
prakurvanti narāstāṃśca vyādhināśaprasūcakāḥ|| 29 ||

sulomā tatra daityendraḥ suvarṇābhapure śubhe|
virājate 'asuraiḥ sārdhaṃ pūjayan īśvaraṃ tadā|| 30 ||

keśadūṣaṇam annaṃ ca velātīte ca bhojanam|
aśraddhayā ca yaddattaṃ tat sarvaṃ bhuñjate 'asuraḥ|| 31 ||

himavacchikhare puṇye labdhavaro mahāsuraḥ|
divyavarṣasahasreṇa tepa īśaprasādataḥ|| 32 ||

tadadhaḥ sutalaṃ nāma pītābhaṃ nāgabhūṣitam|
pītaratnamayaṃ divyaṃ pītaratnasutejasam|| 33 ||

pañcāśatkoṭimānena yojanānāṃ kramāt punaḥ|
daśalakṣasamutsedhaṃ yojanaṃ ca tathāvidham|| 34 ||

bahunāgagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhavane tatra śobhane|
takṣako bhāsate nāgo dhārayaṃśca rasātalam|| 35 ||

supītadehena subhogabhoginā virājamāno hi gaṇaiśca takṣakaḥ|
ratnābhasusvastikamastakopamaścāhīndrakanyāgaṇasaṃyuto 'aniśam|| 36 ||

nāgarāṭ takṣakaḥ śrīmān nāgakoṭyā samanvitaḥ|
tatra nityaṃ mahādevaṃ prastūyati mahotsavaiḥ|| 37 ||

yadā dānāni kurvanti na mānavā mahītale|
atibhārā bhavet kṣoṇī teṣāṃ pāpātmanāṃ spṛśāt|| 38 ||

tadbhāreṇa dṛḍhākrānta ucchvasati ca takṣakaḥ|
tacchvāsodgatavāyośca bhūmikampaḥ prajāyate|| 39 ||

nṛṇāṃ śaṃsati tatkampo dāridraṃ ca tadā punaḥ|
kartāraścennarāstāni lakṣmīvantaḥ prasūcitāḥ|| 40 ||

tasya cādhipatirdaityaḥ kālanemirmahābalaḥ|
taptacāmikaraprakhye bhavane hi virājate|| 41 ||

bahukoṭyasurairyuktaḥ koṭikoṭisusevitaḥ|
nānāratnamaye divye saṃsadi pravirājate|| 42 ||

aprakṣālya karau pādau karoti karma bhojanam|
martyo gṛhṇati tat sarvaṃ kālanemiḥ suniścitam|| 43 ||

divyavarṣasahasreṇa tapaseśaprasādataḥ|
labdhvā varaṃ mahādaityaḥ pūjayaṃśca maheśvaram|| 44 ||

tatastalātalaṃ nāma śarkarācitabhūmikam|
haritābhairdiśodyotaṃ marakatamaṇiprabham|| 45 ||

talātalasya vistāraṃ pañcāśatkoṭimānataḥ|
daśalakṣasamutsedhaṃ divyapurarasāyutam|| 46 ||

mahāmarakatairdyote bhuvane divyaśobhane|
koṭināgagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ karkoṭako virājate|| 47 ||

hemādrīśādvaraṃ prāpya mahābalaparākramaḥ|
dadhāra sutalaṃ bhūmiṃ śirasā bahubhārabhṛt|| 48 ||

kṛṣṇābhadehena virājamānaḥ karkoṭako 'asau lilihan dvijihvaḥ|
kaṇṭhāptarekhātrayabhūṣito 'asau daṃṣṭrākarālāṅkitanāgakanyaḥ|| 49 ||

karkoṭako mahānāgo viṣadarpabalānvitaḥ|
sampūjayati vai tatra sadākālaṃ sadāśivam|| 50 ||

snānayajñotsavairdāyairvarjitā mānavā yadi|
gāḍhabhārā bhavet kṣoṇī tatpāpaiśca pralepitā|| 51 ||

tadbhāreṇa parākrāntaḥ karkoṭako hi nāgarāṭ|
ucchvasati mahocchvāsaṃ sarvasattvabhayaṃkaram|| 52 ||

tacchvāsodgatavāyośca bhūmikampaḥ prajāyate|
śubhāśubhāni sattvānāṃ praśaṃsati ca vepathuḥ|| 53 ||

tathetītītanāvṛṣṭīn durbhikṣāṃśca praśaṃsati|
kartāro yadi tān martyā viparītāśca sarvaśaḥ|| 54 ||

bahuratnamaye divye bhavane citraśobhite|
hiraṇyākṣo 'asuraiḥ sārdhaṃ virājate hi tatra vai|| 55 ||

hiraṇyakaśipuścaiva sarvadaityapitāmahaḥ|
nānāratnamaye gehe virājate 'asuraiḥ samam|| 56 ||

adharmopārjitārthena yaddharmaḥ kriyate naraiḥ|
tat sarvaṃ ca pragṛhṇāti hiraṇyākṣo mahābalaḥ|| 57 ||

labdhavaro mahādevāddhimālayanagottame|
divyavarṣasahasreṇa tapasā pūjayan haram|| 58 ||

tadadho nitalaṃ nāma pātālaṃ raktabhūtalam|
bahuratnakarairdyotaṃ padmākāraṃ sadotsavam|| 59 ||

nitalasyaiva vistāraṃ pañcāśayojanakramāt|
daśalakṣasamutsedhaṃ prāntaraṃ ghaṭasambhava|| 60 ||

vividharatnagehaiśca nānāprabhākarottamaiḥ|
dūrīgataḥ khalu dhvānto vidyotave hyaharniśam|| 61 ||

śaṅkhapālo mahānāgo bahubhṛtyaiḥ samāyutaḥ|
vibhāti satataṃ tatra svaratnairdyotayan diśaḥ|| 62 ||

sukṛṣṇakāntyā ruruce ha īśvaraḥ suratnakāntyaikagalaikalekhayā|
dvijihvaleḍhī viṣadarpapauruṣaṃ cāhīndrakanyāṅkitavāmavigrahaḥ|| 63 ||

śaṅkhapālaḥ śriyā dīptaḥ śivapādābjapūjakaḥ|
caturtho dhārayan bhūmiṃ samarhati maheśvaram|| 64 ||

yadā prajāḥ suparvāṇo lehayanti nṛpān dvijān|
apaharanti gobhūmiṃ dānadharmairvivarjitāḥ|| 65 ||

tatpāpāni samudvoḍhum asamarthā bhavet mahī|
tato gurutarāgastya sapātālākramat punaḥ|| 66 ||

tadbhāreṇa dṛḍhākrāntaḥ śaṅkhapālaḥ phaṇīśvaraḥ|
ucchvasati mahāśabdaṃ bahubhāravyathodbhavam|| 67 ||

tacchvāsodgatavāyośca bhūmikampaḥ prajāyate|
bhittvā caturthakaṃ bhūmiṃ sarvasattvabhayāvaham|| 68 ||

nityaṃ śaṃsati tatkampa utpātān kṣīṇagorasān|
alpasasyān kṣitau gulmān hīnabuddhiṃ ca jīvinām|| 69 ||

yadyarcayanti tān mānyān mānuṣāḥ susukhaiṣiṇaḥ|
bahukṣīraṃ mahā sasyā bhaveddhi sukhasampadaḥ|| 70 ||

tatraivādhipatirdaityaścānuhlādo mahābalī|
bahukoṭyasuraiḥ sārdhaṃ sabhāmadhye virājate|| 71 ||

devebhyaśca dvijebhyaśca gobhyo 'anivedya bhojanam|
annapānādikaṃ sarvaṃ khādantikaṃ narādhamāḥ|| 72 ||

tat sarvaṃ ca samādāya nitale ca mahītalāt|
prabhunakti sukhaṃ tatra anuhlādo mahāsuraḥ|| 73 ||

himālaye varaṃ labdhvā daitya īśaprasādataḥ|
divyavarṣasahasreṇa tapaseśaṃ samarhayan|| 74 ||

tadadhaśca talaṃ nāma śuklakṣitiṃ mahojjvalam|
candrārkakāntiratnābhairvidyotate hi nityaśaḥ|| 75 ||

yojanānāṃ ca koṭīnāṃ pañcāśat kramaśaḥ kṣitim|
daśalakṣasamutsedhaṃ talasyaitat pramāṇataḥ|| 76 ||

śvetaratnamaye gehe divyopakaraṇairyute|
padmākhyo nāgarājo 'asau bahubhṛtyairvirājate|| 77 ||

supuṇḍarīkābhakalevaro babhau supuṇḍarīkākṣavilolasṛkkā|
sabindupañcāsyasuhārabhūṣito bhujaṃgakanyāṅkitadehabhīṣaṇaḥ|| 78 ||

khyātaḥ padmo mahānāgo harapādārcane rataḥ|
virājate tale madhye dhārayan pañcabhūmikam|| 79 ||

yadā rudanti viprāśca nṛpāttasvahṛdādbhayāt|
patantyaśrūṇi tadbhūmau tena bhārā bhavedrasā|| 80 ||

anyāyairyacca daṇḍanti avicārya prajā nṛpāḥ|
tatpāpācca bhavedbhūmirgariṣṭhā ca saparvatā|| 81 ||

avamānāt piturmāturguroścaiva mahātmanaḥ|
tatkilbiṣādgariṣṭhā sā bhavet kṣoṇī samantataḥ|| 82 ||

tadbhāreṇa dṛḍhākrāntaḥ padmanāmā phaṇīśvaraḥ|
ucchvasati mahacchabdaṃ gāḍhabhāravyathoditam|| 83 ||

nāgocchāsodgatādvāyorbhūmikampaḥ prajāyate|
bhittvā pañcarasāṃ gāḍhaṃ sarvaprāṇivijṛmbhakaḥ|| 84 ||

nityaṃ śaṃsati tatkampaḥ sthānabhraṣṭaḥ prajākṣayaḥ|
rājyanāśo mahākaṣṭaṃ bhaviṣyatīti bhūbhujām|| 85 ||

tasyādhipo bhavennityaṃ prahlādo daityarāṭ sukham|
bahukoṭyasuraiḥ sārdhaṃ ratnālaye ca rājate|| 86 ||

asaṃkalpena dharmāṇi yat karoti narādhamaḥ|
tat sarvaṃ ca pragṛhṇāti prahlādo dānaveśvaraḥ|| 87 ||

labhdvā varaṃ hi māhārya tapasā toṣayañchivam|
divyavarṣasahasreṇa rudrārādhanatatparaḥ|| 88 ||

tato mahātalo nāma sarvādho nalinākṛtiḥ|
pañcaraṅgamaṇijvālairvidyotate hi nityaśaḥ|| 89 ||

yojanānāṃ ca koṭīnāṃ pañcāśat kramaśastathā|
daśalakṣasamutsedhaṃ mahātalasya mānataḥ|| 90 ||

tatrānantaḥ phaṇī svāmī rājate saha pannagaiḥ|
sarvaratnamaye gehe devāsuranamaskṛtaḥ|| 91 ||

suratnakāntyāktatanūttamaḥ phaṇī suraktanetrādharasundarānanaḥ|
mahotpalābhāṅkitacārumastakaḥ sahasramūrdhā ramaṇīpriyo babhau|| 92 ||

ananto nāgarājendraḥ śivapādārcane rataḥ|
dadhāra ṣaṣṭhapātālaṃ pūjayañchivam avyayam|| 93 ||

pāpāṅkitā yadā martyā dānadharmairvivarjitāḥ|
mithyābhājo bhaveyuste gariṣṭhā ca bhavenmahī|| 94 ||

agamyagamane niṣṭhāḥ paradārāvimardakāḥ|
piśunāśca bhaveyuste gurutarā bhavenmahī|| 95 ||

gobrāhmaṇāmarān martyā nindanti śāstrasajjanān|
mantraṃ dharmopavāsaṃ ca sadā guru bhavenmahī|| 96 ||

adharmiṣṭhāśca rājāno nītidharmavivarjitāḥ|
na rakṣanti prajādharmāṃstadā gururbhavet kṣitiḥ|| 97 ||

prajāḥ samyaṅna sevante gāśca dvijān surān nṛpān|
tasmādgururbhavet kṣoṇī svasvakarmavivarjitāḥ|| 98 ||

yadā viprā na kurvanti snānādikarmavarjitāḥ|
japahomārcanairdānaṃ devadharmaparāṅmukhāḥ|| 99 ||

asatpratigrahe niṣṭhā bhaveyurbrahmarākṣasāḥ|
abhakṣabhakṣakāstasmādatigururbhavet kṣitiḥ|| 100 ||

tāḍayanti dvijān gāśca tatsvaṃ luṇṭhanti bhaumikāḥ|
nārakāśca bhaveyuste tato gurus bhaveddharā|| 101 ||

godvijavedabhūmyo hi hriyante yena pāpinā|
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ teṣāṃ pāpadgururmahī|| 102 ||

tatkilbiṣāṇi saṃvoḍhum asamarthā bhavet kṣitiḥ|
tataścātiguruḥ kṣoṇī bhaveccaiva kramāt kramāt|| 103 ||

ye haranti kṣitau sasyān bhūmisvāmīṃ pravañcayan|
api tatkṣetrakartāro hyalpasasyo bhaveddhi sā|| 104 ||

tadbhāreṇa dṛḍhākrānto hyananto nāgarāṇmune|
ucchvasati mahāgāḍhaṃ sarvabhāravyathodbhavam|| 105 ||

bahūchvāsodgatādvāyorbhūmikampaḥ prajāyate|
bhittvā ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca pātālaṃ bahuprāṇibhayāvahaḥ|| 106 ||

sūcayati vepathurnityaṃ mahāmārīṃ mahābhayam|
saṃvartako mahāmūrtirjagadgrasati kumbhaja|| 107 ||

arcanti devagoviprān dānadharmaratā nṛpāḥ|
prajāśca sukhino 'ajasraṃ bhaviṣyanti rasātalam|| 108 ||

brāhmaṇāśca taponiṣṭhā vedādhyayanatatparāḥ|
japopavāsaniṣṭhāścet sarvadā kurbhaviṣyati|
evaṃ śaṃsati tatkampaḥ sarvebhyo medinītale|| 109 ||

tasya cādhipatirdaityo hayagrīvo mahānabhūt|
koṭikoṭyasurairyukto 'apūpujacca śaṃkaram|| 110 ||

nikumbhāndhakasuhlādaiḥ kālena madhunā samam|
virājate sabhāyāṃ sa niśumbhena tathāparaiḥ|| 111 ||

daityapatnyo mahābhāgā daityānāṃ kanyakāḥ śubhāḥ|
kumārāścaiva daityānāṃ virājante mithastataḥ|| 112 ||

asadvṛttyā ca yad dravyān saṃcayanti narādhamāḥ|
tatkriyādharmadānādīṃstat sarvaṃ harate 'asuraḥ|| 113 ||

himālaye giriśreṣṭhe labhdvā varaṃ ca śaṃkarāt|
divyavarṣasahasreṇa tapasātoṣayaddharam|| 114 ||

pātālānāṃ ca saptānām adhobhāge tamaḥsu ca|
santi narakakuṇḍāni gṛhāṇi vṛjinātmanām|| 115 ||

aṣṭāviṃśatirevādhaḥ kṣiternarakakoṭayaḥ|
saptamasya talasyāte ghoratamasi saṃsthitāḥ|| 116 ||

ghorākhyā prathamā koṭiḥ sughorā tadadhaḥ sthitā|
atighorā mahāghorā ghorarūpā tu pañcamī|| 117 ||

ṣaṣṭhī taralatārākhyā saptamī ca bhayānakā|
aṣṭamī kālarārtriśca navamī ca bhayotkaṭā|| 118 ||

daśamī tadadhaścaṇḍā mahācaṇḍā tato 'apyadhaḥ|
caṇḍakolāhalā caṇḍā pracaṇḍā navanāyikā|| 119 ||

padmā padmavatī bhīmā bhīṣabhīṣaṇanāyikā|
karālā vikarālā ca vajrā viṃśatimāḥ smṛtāḥ|| 120 ||

trikoṇā pañcakoṇā ca sudīrghā parivartulā|
saptabhaumā ca bhaumā ca dīptā māyeti cāṣṭamī|| 121 ||

tā nāmataḥ samuddiṣṭā ghorā narakakoṭayaḥ|
aṣṭāviṃśatirevaitāḥ pāpināṃ yātanātmikāḥ|| 122 ||

āsāṃ krameṇa vijñeyāḥ pañca pañcaiva nāyikāḥ|
pratyekaṃ sarvakoṭīnāṃ nāmatastān nibodhata|| 123 ||

rauravaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ rudante yatra dehinaḥ|
mahārauravapīḍābhirmahānto 'api rudanti hi|| 124 ||

tamaḥ śītaṃ tathā coṣṇaḥ pañcādyā nāyakāḥ smṛtāḥ|
raurāvādyam avīracyantaṃ narakāṇāṃ śataṃ smṛtam|| 125 ||

catvāriṃśat samadhikaṃ mahānarakamaṇḍalam|
eṣu pāpāḥ prapacyante narāḥ pāpānurūpataḥ|| 126 ||

yātanābhirvicitrābhirnarāḥ karmakṣayā bhṛśam|
āmalaprakṣayādvadvad agnau dhāmyanti dhāvakāḥ|| 127 ||

tathā pāpakṣayāt pāpāḥ śodhyante narakāgniṣu|
sugāḍhaṃ hastayorbaddhvā tapaśṛṅkhalayā narāḥ|| 128 ||

mahāvṛkṣāgraśākhāsu lambyante yamakiṃkaraiḥ|
dolantaścātivegena niḥsaṃjñāṃ yānti yojanam|| 129 ||

antarīkṣasthitānāṃ tu lauhabhāradvayaṃ naraḥ|
pādayorbadhyate teṣāṃ yamadūtairmahābalaiḥ|| 130 ||

tena bhāreṇa mahatā bhṛśam ānāmitā narāḥ|
dyāyantaḥ svāni karmāṇi tūṣṇīṃ tiṣṭhanti niścalāḥ|| 131 ||

tataḥ keśairagnikalpairlohadaṇḍaiḥ sakaṇṭakaiḥ|
hanyante kiṃkarairghoraiḥ samantāt pāpakāriṇaḥ|| 132 ||

tataḥ kṣāreṇa dīptena vahnerapi viśeṣataḥ|
samantataḥ pralipyante kṣatāṅgā jarjarīkṛtāḥ|| 133 ||

punarvidārya cāṅgeṣu śirasaḥ prabhṛti kramāt|
vṛntākavat prapacyante taptatailakaṭāhitāḥ|| 134 ||

viṣṭhācūrṇe tataḥ kūpe kṛmīṇāṃ nicaye tataḥ|
medosṛkpūyapūrṇāyāṃ vāpyāṃ kṣipanti tān punaḥ|| 135 ||

bhakṣyante kṛmibhistīkṣṇairlohatuṇḍaiśca vāyasaiḥ|
śvabhirdaṃśairvṛkairvyāghrai raudraiśca vikṛtānanaiḥ|
pacyante matsyavadvāpyāṃ vividhanarakeṣu tān|| 136 ||

etatpramāṇaṃ kathitaṃ mayā te pātālapātraṃ nilayasya sūkṣmam|
bhūyo rasādeḥ kathayāmi kīrtiṃ tatsaptalokasya śṛṇuṣva mattaḥ|| 137 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe pātālakīrtanaṃ nāma pañcamo adhyāyaḥ|| 5 ||

skanda uvāca |

pātālānāṃ ca saptānām upari saṃsthitā mahī|
tasyā eva pramāṇaṃ ca vakṣyāmi śṛṇu vistaram|| 1 ||

koṭikoṭisuvistāraṃ yojanānāṃ samantataḥ|
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśaivordhvaṃ samucchritam|| 2 ||

bhūrloka iti vikhyātaḥ sarvalokottamottamaḥ|
gandharvayakṣarakṣobhiḥ piśācaiśca niṣevitaḥ|| 3 ||

manuṣyaiḥ paśubhiścaiva mṛgaiḥ pakṣisarīsṛpaiḥ|
sthāvarairvividhākārairbhūtairetaistu ṣaḍvidhaiḥ|| 4 ||

dvīpānāṃ caiva saptānāṃ bhūrlokamadhyato mune|
jambūdvīpa iti khyātaścārdhacandrākṛtiḥ kvacit|| 5 ||

hemavacchikhare ramye prottuṅge śikharottame|
jambūvṛkṣo mahān āsīdagmaye sarvajantubhiḥ|| 6 ||

yojanaikaṃ suvistāraṃ tadevam ucchritaṃ śubham|
phalati ṣaḍṛtūn vyāpya bahujambūphalāni tat|| 7 ||

yadyat pakvaphalāni ārya patanti giriśekhare|
tasmānmune rasaklinnāt sambhūtā hi nadī varā|| 8 ||

ekadā sūryaputrīyaṃ tasyāṃ chanditum āgatā|
yamunā śāpitā seti durvāsasā dravībhava|| 9 ||

saṃgatena vavāhāryā taddravībhūtayāniśam|
yamuneti samākhyātā dvayoḥ saṃgācca sā nadī|| 10 ||

brahmaṇā ṛṣibhiḥ snātvā sūryeṇa ca pavitritā|
jambūvṛkṣasya nāmnaiva kṣārodaḥ prāntarastataḥ|| 11 ||

jambūdvīpa iti khyātaḥ sarvadvīpāntare sthire|
pañcāśatkoṭivistāro yojanānāṃ virājate|| 12 ||

jambūdvīpo mahādvīpaḥ sarvadvīpottamottamaḥ|
jāyante karmabhistatra sukhaduḥkhānvitā narāḥ|| 13 ||

jambūdvīpe kṛtaṃ yadyadbhuñjate taṃ tam ātmanā|
karmadvīpa iti khyātaḥ puṇyabhūmyaśca karmadaḥ|| 14 ||

yaṃ yaṃ karoti martyastaṃ tebhyaḥ phalati tatra tam|
dharmādharmaṃ mahat karma yat kṛtaṃ jīvibhirmune|
tat sarvaṃ prāpyate nūnaṃ jambūdvīpe hi karmade|| 15 ||

tanmadhye girirājendro himālayo virājate|
merordakṣiṇabhāge ca dvitīyo merusaṃjñitaḥ|| 16 ||

plakṣavṛkṣaḥ sthito yatra plakṣadvīpastato 'abhavat|
śālmalīśākhinā reje śālmalīdvīpa āśrutaḥ|| 17 ||

kuśena rājate yasmāt kuśadvīpo vicakṣate|
krauñcācalena yo reje krauñcadvīpa iti śrutaḥ|
śākādriṇā hi yo reje śākadvīpo bhavenmune|| 18 ||

puṣkareṇa samaṃ reje yaddvīpo hyacyutātmanā|
puṣkaradvīpa iti ākhyaḥ sarvadvīpottamottamaḥ|| 19 ||

bhūrlokato bhuvarloko yāvadādityamaṇḍalam|
antike tāvat santyasmin vasurudrāḥ sabhāskarāḥ|| 20 ||

ādityamaṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ proktaṃ svarlokam ādhruvāt|
vimānakoṭayastasminnaṣṭāviṃśatirāsate|| 21 ||

meḍhībhūto vimānānāṃ sarveṣām upari dhruvaḥ|
calanti yatra vaddhāni krameṇānilamaṇḍale|| 22 ||

yojanānāṃ mahīpṛṣṭhādūrdhvaṃ pañcadaśe dhruvaḥ|
niyatāścānilaskandhāḥ saptāsminnuttare sthitāḥ|| 23 ||

pṛthivyāṃ prathamaskandhaḥ sthita āmeghamaṇḍalāt|
āvaho nāma meghānāṃ vyūhanāvāhanādikṛt|| 24 ||

dvitīyaḥ pravaho nāma vibaddhaḥ sūryamaṇḍale|
tṛtīya udvaho vāyuskandha induṃ prati sthitaḥ|| 25 ||

caturthaḥ saṃvahaskandhaḥ sthito nakṣatramaṇḍale|
graheṣu pañcamaḥ so 'api vivahaḥ parikīrtitaḥ|| 26 ||

skandhaḥ parāvahaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sthitaḥ saptarṣimaṇḍale|
vāyuḥ parivaho nāma nibaddhaḥ saptamo dhruve|| 27 ||

karotyutplavanādīni varṣaṇādīni cāvahaḥ|
upariṣṭhāt sthitaḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ vimānodvahanakriyām|| 28 ||

yojanānāṃ dhruvāt koṭirmaharlokaḥ samucchritaḥ|
vinivṛttādhikārāṇām adhivāso mahātmanām|| 29 ||

viṃśatikoṭayo 'aṣṭau ca surāṇām adhikāriṇām|
janāḥ svarlokam āgatya niyogāt padmajanmanaḥ|| 30 ||

sthitvā manvantaraṃ tatra svavyāpārāvasāyite|
ārohanti maharlokam āgacchantyapare janāḥ|| 31 ||

brahmaṇo divasenetthaṃ devavargāścaturdaśa|
krameṇa kṛtvā karmāṇi maharloke vasanti te|| 32 ||

koṭidvayaṃ maharlokājjanalokaḥ samucchritaḥ|
sādhyā nāma surāstasmin vasanti sukhinaḥ sadā|| 33 ||

yojanānāṃ tapoloke catasraḥ koṭiyojanāḥ|
prajānāṃ patayastatra mānasā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ|| 34 ||

satyalokastapolokāt koṭayaḥ ṣaṭsamucchritaḥ|
indranīlapratīkāśaṃ mahābhogairalaṃkṛtam|| 35 ||

viṣṇusthānāt paraṃ lokaṃ mama loko ghaṭodbhava|
svacchamauktikasaṃkāśaṃ varabhogasamanvitam|| 36 ||

mama sthānāt paraṃ sthānam umādevyāḥ prakīrtitam|
taptacāmīkaraprakhyam aśeṣaguṇasaṃyutam|| 37 ||

umāsthānācca parataḥ sthānam ādyam umāpateḥ|
viṣṇulokācca parataḥ śrīmacchivapuraṃ mahat|| 38 ||

dvātriṃśatkoṭivistīrṇaṃ tadardhena samucchritam|
mahāprabhāvasaṃyuktaiḥ sūryāyutasamaprabhaiḥ|| 39 ||

gaṇairapyuṣitaṃ sthānam asaṃkhyairyogatatparaiḥ|
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaiḥ sarvavādyasamanvitaiḥ|| 40 ||

gītanṛtyarasopetairaprameyaguṇānvitaiḥ|
manojavairasaṃkhyaiśca parivāraiḥ samanvitaiḥ|| 41 ||

vimānaiḥ sarvato vyāptaṃ tārakābhirivāmbaram|
kvaciddolāgṛhai ramyaiḥ kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitaiḥ|| 42 ||

agamyaṃ sarvadevānāṃ dhyāyamānaṃ surāsuraiḥ|
vikārendriyaṣaḍvargairmāyābhiśca vivarjitaiḥ|| 43 ||

agocaraṃ hi pāpānāṃ manasā karmaṇā satām|
yato vāco nivartante pāpātmanāṃ ca dehinām|| 44 ||

sarvaratnamaye tatra tejomayagṛhottame|
virājate mahādeva umayā sahito 'aniśam|| 45 ||

akhaṇḍānandam ādyeśaṃ tattvānandam ajaṃ śivam|
sahajānandam ātmānaṃ kaivalyānandam īśvaram|| 46 ||

pūrṇānandam ajānandaṃ vyāpakānandam arcitam|
gaṇairnityaṃ sadānandaṃ bhaktibhistrividhairmune|| 47 ||

mokṣārthibhirgaṇaiḥ sarvairlabdhavarairhimālaye|
mahādevaprasādācca labdhaṃ hi tatpadaṃ mudā|| 48 ||

na jāyante punaryonau na dhvaṃsanti tathā ca te|
ye tatra rudraloke ca tiṣṭhantīśātmakā mune|| 49 ||

ye 'apīśayogino martyā jīvanmuktā na saṃśayaḥ|
tatra yogālayaṃ yānti janmāni ca vihāya te|| 50 ||

pratapyate yena śivātmanā vai sampūjya rudraṃ himavadgirau tataḥ|
pralabhyate tena girīśaloko 'anūpamaḥ sarvasukhānvito yaḥ|| 51 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe lokānukīrtanaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ|| 6 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ saṃsṛjya dhātrādrīn kumbhayone himālayam|
tatpāṇipīḍanāyājastat kālānte mano dadhe|| 1 ||

vyācaṣṭa vacanaṃ brahmā pūrvaṃ pitṛgaṇaṃ dhruvam|
ātmajānāṃ vivāhāya merorhimavato mune|| 2 ||

pitṛgaṇasutā yūyaṃ kanye dve ca sulakṣaṇe|
saṃsṛjantu ca divyāṅge mānasairajarāmṛte|| 3 ||

ākarṇya vacanaṃ dhātuḥ pitṛgaṇā hi mānasaiḥ|
om iti ca pratiśrutya sasṛjuḥ kanyakā varāḥ|| 4 ||

tāsāṃ madhye ca divyāṅge divyāmene sulakṣaṇe|
sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇe āstāṃ pitṛsute purā|| 5 ||

kaścitkālāntare 'agastya te kanyake vavardhatuḥ|
krīḍyamāne vayobhiśca saptavarṣavayo 'anvite|| 6 ||

tataśca nāradaḥ pautraṃ brahmaṇo vacanādyayau|
vyācaṣṭa kila saṃdeśaṃ pitṛbhyo hetukaṃ vacaḥ|| 7 ||

nārada uvāca |

namo 'astu pitaro vo hi maṅgalaṃ varṣmasu dhruvam|
avyayātmanadehebhyo natirastu tanurmama|| 8 ||

atrāgato hi deho 'ayaṃ tadbījaṃ śṛṇuta prabho|
tadvacanam ahaṃ yena preṣitaḥ parameṣṭhinā|| 9 ||

dve kanye vo hi vidyete sarvāsāṃ jyeṣṭhile vibho|
varābhyāṃ yujyatāṃ sadyo divyāmenābhidhānake|| 10 ||

merave dīyatāṃ divyā menā himavate khalu|
evaṃ matsammataṃ bhadram ityuktaṃ brahmaṇo hi vaḥ|| 11 ||

skanda uvāca |

niśamya vacanaṃ tasya pitaro yātamarṣiṇaḥ|
añjo nirvyañcanāmarṣāḥ praṇamyocustam ādṛtam|| 12 ||

pitara ūcuḥ |

svāgataṃ bho muniśreṣṭha kuśalaṃ te 'asti varṣmasu|
yenotsṛṣṭaṃ jagat sarvaṃ tasmai dhātre namo namaḥ|| 13 ||

aho jātaṃ mahat kaṣṭaṃ vidhāturvacanāddhi naḥ|
kathaṃ dāsye sute tābhyāṃ sthāvarābhyāṃ munīśvara|| 14 ||

sthāvaro niścalaḥ kuṣṭhī kāṇaḥ khañjo rujānvitaḥ|
badhiro guṇahīnaśca mūko napuṃsakastathā|| 15 ||

piṅgākṣaḥ kekaro mūḍho nyūnādhikāṅginau punaḥ|
parajātirajātiśca svagotrī piśunastathā|| 16 ||

ebhyaḥ kanyā na dātavyā dhīmatā bhadralipsunā|
aniṣedhānmahadvākyādbrahmaṇo vacanādapi|| 17 ||

naiva dāsye sute tābhyāṃ pratiyātu munīśvara|
kṣamasvādya mamāgāṃsi dhātre mudeti varṇyatām|| 18 ||

skanda uvāca |

pitṛṇāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā pratyāgatya vidheḥ padam|
avarṇayaddhi tadvārtāṃ nārado brahmaṇe naman|| 19 ||

samākarṇya tato brahmā nāradamukhasambhavam|
pitṛṇāṃ tacca vṛttāntaṃ cukopa tān prati prabhuḥ|| 20 ||

antaḥkopaṃ samādhāya sailaṃ prati vrajan vidhiḥ|
pakṣāṇi ca sasarjājo nagānāṃ sahasā ruṣā|| 21 ||

himālayasya saṃsṛjya sumeroścāntikaṃ yayau|
sṛjyamāne vidhau pakṣaṃ merostatrāyayuḥ surāḥ|| 22 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

vibhunā maiva kartavyaṃ pakṣaṃ gireḥ kadāpi na|
lokā bhraṃśyanti caitasmāt sapakṣacalanādyadi|| 23 ||

nimajjiṣyati bhūyo 'asau vibho yatnodbhavā rasā|
saṃcarati yadā tatra ratnasānuritastataḥ|| 24 ||

skanda uvāca |

devaṣīṇāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā satyātmā hi mudānvitaḥ|
nivavṛte vidhirmeroḥ pakṣau sraṣṭuṃ tadā mune|| 25 ||

ālokya tādṛśaṃ tāta pakṣasṛṣṭinivartitam|
ratnasānurnipatyāśu duḥkhātmājam uvāca ha|| 26 ||

meruruvāca |

matpakṣasthānabhit tāta katham ayaṃ pravañcitaḥ|
duṣṭātmanāṃ surarṣīṇāṃ matvā tathyaṃ vaco 'adhunā|| 27 ||

yadyevaṃ madvipakṣāste pātayiṣyāmi sarvaśaḥ|
mama sānvojaso lokānadya te 'aja śape tvami|| 28 ||

brahmovāca |

maivaṃ duḥkhaya śailendra pakṣahetoḥ kadācana|
anena sthūladehena sthāvarastvaṃ bhavāṅga vai|| 29 ||

sūkṣmadehena te mero saṃcarānena sarvadā|
bhraṃśahetośca lokānāṃ sthūlāṅgaṃ te niṣedhitam|| 30 ||

ato hetorvaraṃ dāsye ratnasāno hi te śṛṇu|
ye ca tvām avamanyanti ta eva kilbiṣānvitāḥ|| 31 ||

mūrtayorāvayoḥ putra na bhedo 'asti kadācana|
karoti yo viśeṣaṃ ca madaṅgaghātako bhavet|| 32 ||

kulaśaila iti jñātvā bhuvanādhāra ādrayan|
praṇamanti sma ratnāṅgam uddhariṣyāmi tāṃstvayi|| 33 ||

tapasvino 'arcakā rudrāṃ dānadharmopavāsakāḥ|
nābhaktinaśca dharmiṣṭhāstīrthasnānavikilbiṣāḥ|| 34 ||

satyadharmaparāḥ śāntā dayādānotsukāḥ sadā|
devyā ye bhaktino viṣṇoḥ rudrasya ca viśeṣataḥ|| 35 ||

ta eva tvayi tiṣṭhantu anubhuñjan sukhāni ca|
tāṃstvaṃ prapālayājasraṃ nānāsukhāni bhāvayan|| 36 ||

kṣīṇasukṛtino ye ca kilbiṣāṅkitadehinaḥ|
tāneva putra te sānoḥ pātayāśu sunirdayam|| 37 ||

dhṛtaliṅgaśarīreṇa pitṛloke vrajan dhruvam|
udvāhyatāṃ hi tatkanyāṃ gaccha putrādhunānagha|| 38 ||

skanda uvāca |

niśamya vacanaṃ dhāturmerurmene kṛtārthatām|
naradehaṃ samāsthāya yayau paitraṃ vivāhitum|| 39 ||

śrutvā dhāturvaraṃ labdhaṃ sumeruṇā himālayaḥ|
atoṣayadvidhiṃ bhaktyā tasmāllabdhavaraḥ punaḥ|| 40 ||

himavānuvāca |

guṇātītāya devāya .o namaste triguṇātmane|
prapañcāntarasaṃrūḍha prapañcasṛṣṭine namaḥ|| 41 ||

anugrahāmṛtāsāraistadvarairmāṃ prasiñcaya|
liṅgakalevaraṃ naśca meroryathā pradīyatām|| 42 ||

brahmovāca |

evam astu hi te putra yathā vadasi tat tathā|
bhavatāt kāmarūpī tvaṃ yatrecchāsaṃcaras bhava|| 43 ||

kanyām udvāhyatāṃ putra pitṛṇāṃ kulasambhavām|
te 'api dāsyanti te putrīṃ tallokaṃ vraja niścitam|| 44 ||

skanda uvāca |

ākarṇya vacanaṃ dhāturhimavān harṣasaṃyutaḥ|
samāhvayan munīñchailān naradehabhṛtastadā|| 45 ||

nāradapramukhairlokairhimavān giribhiḥ saha|
pitṛlokaṃ yayau śīghram udvāhituṃ mudānvitaḥ|| 46 ||

māghasitārdhamāsasya ekādaśīyute gurau|
dṛgārke śubhayoge ca pitaro hi śubhagrahe|| 47 ||

daduḥ svarṇādraye kanyāṃ divyāṃ nāmnā sulakṣaṇām|
tām ādāya saharṣātmā pratyāyayau svam ālayam|| 48 ||

rādhaśuklārdhamāsasya trayodaśyāṃ gurau dine|
revatyāṃ śobhane yoge gurugrahoccasaṃsthite|| 49 ||

saṃkalpya vidhivat kanyāṃ menākhyāṃ pitaraḥ purā|
dadurhimavate 'agastya sadhenusvarṇadakṣiṇām|| 50 ||

śataṃ pāriṣadaḥ kanyāḥ sumukhyaḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ|
svāṅgajāyai dadau dātā dāyasvarṇapalāyutam|| 51 ||

pradaduḥ pitaro 'agastya jāmātre svāśiṣaṃ punaḥ|
tanmūrdhānaṃ karaiḥ spṛṣṭvā trividhoktaṃ ca saṃsadi|| 52 ||

pitara ūcuḥ |

ciraṃ jīvyāt sukhaṃ putra yāvadasti ca medinī|
śailarājo mahābāhurlokadayānidhirbhava|| 53 ||

sarvalokāśrayo vatsa saralokārcito bhava|
yāvat prasravitaṃ toyaṃ tvattastīrthaṃ bhaviṣyatu|| 54 ||

sthāsyanti tvayi yāvaddhi jīvino hi caturvidhāḥ|
sarvainobhirvinirmuktā yāsyantyante parāṃ gatim|| 55 ||

ye narāstvayi tiṣṭhanti api jñānairvivarjitāḥ|
labhiṣyanti parāṃ muktim amutra yogadurlabhāṃ || 56 ||

avidhavā bhavārye tvaṃ patyuḥ supreyasī bhava|
bahuputravatī bhūyā ajarā cāmṛtā bhava|| 57 ||

devarṣivanditā mānyā bhaveśvareṇa vanditā|
sarvalokadayātmā tvaṃ tadrakṣakā bhavāniśam|| 58 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti dattvāśiṣaṃ tābhyāṃ pitaraścādriyan bahu|
prāsthāpayet svalokārtau pārṣadaiḥ saha bhojayan|| 59 ||

ādāya himavān patnīṃ pārṣadaiḥ saha harṣayan|
pratyāyayau svakaṃ sthānaṃ vyomakūṭaṃ sumaṅgalaiḥ|| 60 ||

anvabhuktaṃ sukhaṃ tau hi varavadhūdbhavaṃ muhuḥ|
ratikrīḍārasairyuktau tau āstāṃ dampatī mune|| 61 ||

divyapañcadaśābdānte pratyāyayau pitṛgṛhe|
vyācaṣṭa vacanaṃ menā pitṛbhyaḥ priyaceṣṭitam|| 62 ||

menovāca |

pitaro māṃ prarakṣadhvaṃ patinā rahitāṃ muhuḥ|
vo 'aṅghripadmāni saṃsevya sthāsyāmyaham amutra vai|| 63 ||

mayyekānte priyastāta na tiṣṭhati manāgapi|
saharṣeṇa mamāsyaṃ ca na prekṣati bhayākulaḥ|| 64 ||

premā bhavet sa dāsīnāṃ tasya priyatamā hi tāḥ|
na muñcati kṣaṇaṃ tāśca kramaśaḥ khalvaharniśam|| 65 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya vaco 'agastya duhituḥ pitarastadā|
amarṣaiḥ pūritāḥ sadyaḥ śaptum ārebhire girim|| 66 ||

pitara ūcuḥ |

dāsyo bhūtvā sute te tvām avamānanti tā yataḥ|
tāsāṃ yavat prasūtiśca sthāvarā ca bhaviṣyati|| 67 ||

bhaviṣyantu ca te dāsyaḥ svaprasūtisamākulāḥ|
na labhiṣyantu bhadraṃ tāḥ priyeṇāpi kṣaṇaṃ samam|| 68 ||

yadyapi duhitā jātāstā nadyo bhavitāra u|
bhaviṣyantu ca te dāsyaḥ śīrṇā duhitṛbhiryataḥ|| 69 ||

śreṣṭhaputraprasūtā tvaṃ bhavitāsi tathāparāḥ|
lokavandyā bhaviṣyantu tisraḥ putryaḥ sumadhyamāḥ|| 70 ||

pratiyātu gṛhaṃ putri yathāgatāsi tat tathā|
na striyaḥ svagṛhe stheyaṃ patinā tāḍitāpi ca|| 71 ||

sahyamānā sadāgāṃsi patyustiṣṭheta tadgṛhe|
gotraṃ vasu yaśaḥ kīrtiṃ pralabhitā na saṃśayaḥ|| 72 ||

śivayā sahitaṃ rudraṃ sampūjayāniśaṃ sute|
tattithīṣu vratopoṣyaiḥ saubhāgyaṃ lapsyasi dhruvam|| 73 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ādeśaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā piturmenā hitoditam|
pratyāyayau gṛhaṃ patyuḥ sakhībhiḥ saha satvarā|| 74 ||

ādeśena piturmenā upoṣya vratam ācarat|
sampūjya śaṃkaraṃ bhaktyā kaścitkālaṃ vyatikramat|| 75 ||

evaṃ puṇyaprabhāvāt sā saṃreme patinā saha|
bhuktvā rājyaṃ sukhaṃ bhojyaṃ kaṃcit kālaṃ praṇīyatī|| 76 ||

suṣuve sā ca mainākaṃ kīrtimantaṃ sutottamam|
tasyāṃ kālāvasāne ca tisraḥ kanyāśca jajñire|| 77 ||

aparṇā caikaparṇā ca tathaikapāṭalā punaḥ|
tyaktaparṇā hyaparṇā sā ekaparṇāśanāparā|| 78 ||

ekapuṣpāśanā cānyā tathaikapāṭalā smṛtā|
mahogratapasā yuktā vrateṣu tāstathā vidhim|| 79 ||

dadau manmātaraṃ pūrvaṃ śūline himavān kila|
asitāyaikaparṇāṃ tāṃ jaigīṣavyāya cāparām|| 80 ||

tāḥ suṣuvuḥ śataṃ dāsyaḥ sahasrāṇi kramāt sutān|
mātṛbhiḥ sthāpitā yatra tatraiva sthiratāṃ gatāḥ|| 81 ||

prasuṣuvuśca tāḥ putryaḥ kālānte ca kramānmuhuḥ|
srotovatyo 'adravañchailāt sarvā nadyo jalākulāḥ|| 82 ||

tāḍayantyastarjayantyo garhayantyo muhurmuhuḥ|
pāvinyastāniśaṃ sarvā brahmaṇo vacanānmune|
pitṛṇāṃ vacanānnityaṃ caturvargaphalapradāḥ|| 83 ||

dāsyo 'avadaṃśca putrebhyaḥ svāntaduḥkhāṅkitā muhuḥ|
tāḍayantyastarjayantyo garhayantyo muhurmuhuḥ|| 84 ||

samuccaratha putrāśca naikasmiṃstiṣṭhathāniśam|
saṃcārāllabhate sarvaṃ varaṃ mānyaṃ ca sāhasam|| 85 ||

evaṃ sambodhitāḥ putrā noccaritāstathāpi te|
na śaktirvidyate procuścarituṃ tāśca mātaraḥ|| 86 ||

samprekṣya tādṛśān putrān dravībhūtā duhitṛkāḥ|
dāsyo 'abhūvaṃśca duḥkhārtāḥ patyau cāvarṇayaddhi tat|| 87 ||

niśamya vacanaṃ prājñaḥ priyāyā himavāṃstadā|
āśvāsayadvadhūṃ prājño vacanairmadhuroktibhiḥ|| 88 ||

tato yugaśatānte cābhavaddevāsuraṃ mṛdham|
kaśipurgirim āmantryāyodhayaṃśca suraiḥ saha|| 89 ||

sa himavāṃstadā pakṣī pakṣatibhyāṃ samāvṛṇot|
prahantuṃ devasainyaṃ yat sthagitāmbarapakṣatiḥ|| 90 ||

ālokya devasainyastaṃ tādṛśādriṃ bhayāturaḥ|
trāhi trāhīti samprocya tadviṣṇoḥ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ|| 91 ||

dhātaḥ pālaka viṣṇvīśa sraṣṭaḥ saṃhārakācyuta|
rakṣa rakṣeśa naḥ pāpāt kaśipoḥ parvatādvibho|| 92 ||

sa śrutvā vacanaṃ teṣām uttīrṇaḥ kṣīrasāgarāt|
prodyamya pauṣaṇaṃ cakraṃ provāca tridaśān hariḥ|| 93 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

mā bhīyatāṃ surāstasmāt pratikāro bhaviṣyati|
praśāmyati hyayaṃ duṣṭaḥ svavarga iva nāyakaḥ|| 94 ||

duṣṭānāṃ śāsanāyāhaṃ sādhūnāṃ rakṣaṇāya ca|
pṛthak pṛthak ca dehena avatāraṃ karomyaham|| 95 ||

skanda uvāca |

ityuktvā prayayau śīghraṃ pakṣau chettuṃ ghaṭodbhava|
nārāyaṇo 'amaraiḥ sārdhaṃ yatrāsīt kaśipuśca saḥ|| 96 ||

ālokya kaśipuḥ śailo viṣṇuṃ suraiḥ sahāgatam|
dudruvaturhi cakrāktaṃ kṛtāntam iva jīvinaḥ|| 97 ||

avīviśat svakaṃ sthānaṃ kaśipuṃ himavān bhayāt|
trāhi trāhīti ca proktvā vibhordhātaḥ pitāmahaḥ|| 98 ||

śatrupakṣagato yo hi kṛcchraṃ tu svakṛtaṃ ca yat|
himavate tadetyuktvā viṣṇuścukopa kumbhaja|| 99 ||

kṣīrārṇavam abhidrutya pakṣāvuddiśya bhūbhṛtaḥ|
cikṣepa sahasā cakraṃ viṣṇuu roṣānvito bhṛśam|| 100 ||

ciccheda tvarayā pakṣau himavataḥ sudarśanaḥ|
suniḥśeṣaṃ hi tat kṛtvā viṣṇoḥ karaṃ samāvrajat|| 101 ||

stūyamāno 'amarairviṣṇuḥ svadhāma paramaṃ yayau|
tyaktvā cāyodhanaṃ devāḥ svaṃ svaṃ lokaṃ yayuḥ punaḥ|| 102 ||

pakṣalūno hi kṛcchrāṅgo brahmāṇaṃ himavān yayau|
tat sarvaṃ varṇayāmāsa brahmaṇe prekṣayaṃstanum|| 103 ||

niśamya vacanaṃ tasya prekṣya śailaṃ vyathāṅkitam|
provāca taṃ samāśvāsya dhātā madhurayā girā|| 104 ||

tam evārādhayāśu tvaṃ himavadbhaktivatsalam|
pradāsyati sa bhaktebhyaḥ svāntepsitaṃ na saṃśayaḥ|| 105 ||

śrutvā vaco vidhātuḥ sa yayau yatra hariḥ sthitaḥ|
siddharatnaṃ samādāya pārśvasthaiḥ saha dehadhṛk|| 106 ||

nyasyopahārakaṃ viṣṇoḥ purato himavān mune|
parikramyānamat pādau bhaktyā stuvan muhurmuhuḥ|| 107 ||

namo nārāyaṇājāya divyānāṃ pataye namaḥ|
nārāśrayāya nandāya lokanāyaka te namaḥ|| 108 ||

pakṣābhāvādahaṃ tāta jaṅgamairnindito 'acalaḥ|
kāmarūpaḥ kṛto dhātrā me kṛpayasi tadvaram|| 109 ||

prekṣya bhaktiyutaṃ śailaṃ namram abhyarthanepsitam|
provāca bhagavāṃstasmai varaṃ dātuṃ svabhaktine|| 110 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

vatsa te sthūladeho 'asau bhavati sthāvaraściram|
lokānāṃ bhayado 'ajasraṃ yatra kutrāpi saṃcarāt|| 111 ||

mā dūyatāṃ gire tasmāllokānāṃ rakṣako bhava|
anenāṅgena vatsa tvaṃ kāmarūpī bhavāniśam|| 112 ||

śṛṇu dāsye varaṃ tubhyaṃ sarvaṃ varam anuttamam|
bhava bhūdhararājendra adyādi lokavandanaḥ|| 113 ||

tvayi tiṣṭhāmyahaṃ nityaṃ svagaṇaistridaśaiḥ saha|
vidhātā śaṃkaraḥ siddhā gaṇarṣibhiśca tiṣṭhati|| 114 ||

digīśāḥ khalu sevante yakṣagandharvadānavāḥ|
tvayi tiṣṭhan mudājasram apsarasaḥ svavṛttikāḥ|| 115 ||

dharmeṇa bhūṣitaḥ śailastvam īśvareṇa sarvadā|
nādharmairanvabhuṅktastvaṃ sarvadevāśramo yataḥ|| 116 ||

tvaddarśanaṃ maddarśanaṃ na bhedo 'asti kadāpi ca|
mūḍhaḥ karoti yo bhedaṃ madaṅgahā bhaveddhi saḥ|| 117 ||

sarvāśramo giristvaṃ ca sarvadevamayo hyaham|
tulyena mānyate yena sa yāti paramaṃ padam|| 118 ||

gaccha bhūdhararājendra taptuṃ sānau svake śive|
ārādhaya maheśānaṃ sa dāsyatīpsitaṃ hṛdā|| 119 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti dattvā varaṃ viṣṇurhimavate ghaṭodbhava|
antardadhe punastasminnavātsīt sa nirantaram|| 120 ||

chinnagrīvo mahāviṣṇurhiraṇyaśekhare girau|
devāsurārcito 'ajasraṃ pitṛlokairviśeṣataḥ|| 121 ||

labdhavaro girīndro 'asau pratyāyayau himālayaḥ|
sarvalokaiḥ prasevante tatsānuṣu vasan muhuḥ|| 122 ||

divyavarṣaśatānte ca labdhavaro 'abhavanmahān|
paśupateḥ prasādādvai divyāśramaparācalaḥ|| 123 ||

tadādyanantādharamaṇḍano 'abhūt tapomayo lokaphalaprado 'asau|
himācālaḥ sarvasurāśramaśca kilāśutoṣāptavibhūtirāryaḥ|| 124 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe himālayavarapradānaṃ nāma saptamo adhyāyaḥ|| 7 ||

agastya uvāca |

sarvavit pārvatīnanda bhavellabdhavaro giriḥ|
tapasā toṣayan rudraṃ tasmai dattaṃ varaṃ ca kim|| 1 ||

skanda uvāca |

īśvareṇa varaṃ dattaṃ himavate purā mune|
tat sarvaṃ varṇayiṣyāmi samāhitamanāḥ śṛṇu|| 2 ||

tapobhiḥ sukaṭhoraiḥ sa toṣayāmāsa śaṃkaram|
vyācaṣṭa vacanaṃ caiva himavate maheśvaraḥ|| 3 ||

paśupatiruvāca |

akṣayyo bhava himādre yāvadbrahmā na saṃśayaḥ|
tāvat sthiraściraṃ bhūyā merutulyo bhavācala|| 4 ||

yāvanna tapyate lokaistvayi haimācale tapaḥ|
na sthāsyanti ca tāvanto merau cāpi vikilbiṣāḥ|| 5 ||

tiṣṭhāmyahaṃ pṛthagbhūtvā liṅgātmā tvayi hemabhṛt|
vidhātā tridaśā viṣṇurdikpāstiṣṭhanti saṃtatam|| 6 ||

tiṣṭhanti matpriyā vandyā bahurūpā gaṇaiḥ saha|
tvatsānuṣu pṛthagbhūtvā sarvalokavarapradāḥ|| 7 ||

gandharvāpsarasaḥ siddhā devarṣayastapasvinaḥ|
tava sānuṣu tiṣṭhanti yakṣā rakṣāṃsi dānavāḥ|| 8 ||

sthāsyanti mānuṣā nityaṃ tvatsānuṣu himālaya|
phalamūlāśanairdhānyaiḥ poṣayaṃstān prarakṣasi|| 9 ||

saṃtataṃ tvayi ye martyāḥ pratiṣṭhanti gṛhaujasaḥ|
upatyakāsu sānau vā kūṭeṣu śikhareṣu vā|| 10 ||

sthāsyanti tridive saukhye parivāraiḥ samanvitāḥ|
tvayi pravrajitā yāvat tatsaṃkhyayānusārataḥ|| 11 ||

ye cārohanti te sānum api jñānairvivarjitāḥ|
pade pade phalaprāptā vājapeyāśvamedhayoḥ|| 12 ||

ye tapāṃsi prakurvanti tvatsānuṣu vasan muhuḥ|
te dhīrairna pralīyante vihāya kaṣṭasaṃsṛtim|| 13 ||

japārcanaratān dhīrāḥ kacāti tvayi naḥ prati|
uddhariṣyāmi tāvat sa utsarjayan hi saṃsṛtim|| 14 ||

tvatprasūtāsu yo martyaḥ snāyate himavan sakṛt|
ājanmārjitapāpāni tyaktvāṅgaṃ tridivaṃ vrajet|| 15 ||

yāsu kāsu prasūtāsu tvatta upatyakādapi|
snātā parvasu te tyaktāḥ saptajanmārjitainasā|| 16 ||

dūrāt paśyanti ye ca tvāṃ himahemavibhūṣitam|
ekābdārjitapāpaiste vimucyante na saṃśayaḥ|| 17 ||

tvatsānuśikhare 'arhanti kadācit pravasaṃśca naḥ|
abhaktinaḥ sakṛccāpi uddhariṣyāmi tān gire|| 18 ||

śaityā cālakanandā ca bhadrā haimavatī tathā|
gaṇḍakī śatarudrā ca bhāgīrathī ca vāgmatī|| 19 ||

haimavatī tathā bhadrā satyagaṅgā ca kauśikī|
śatarudrā tathā śaityā tretāyāṃ ca varapradāḥ|| 20 ||

bhāgīrathyalakānandā dvāpare kalipūrvataḥ|
vāgvatī kalimadhye ca taccheṣe gaṇḍakī punaḥ|| 21 ||

bhaviṣyanti ca tā nadyo lokepsitavarapradāḥ|
tajjīvibhyaḥ pradāsyanti manasthaṃ martyamaṇḍale|| 22 ||

etābhirbhūṣitastvaṃ ca satataṃ ca pavitritaḥ|
śaktyāvataraṇībhirmatsamāṣṭabhirvibhūtibhiḥ|| 23 ||

gaccha bhūdhararājendra bahuputrayuto bhava|
bhaviṣyati ca no hetuḥ sambandhaṃ tvayi matkulam|| 24 ||

evaṃ labdhavaro rudrāt pūjyo 'asau himavān sadā|
sarvairdevādibhiḥ sattvaiḥ prayatātmā girīśvaraḥ|| 25 ||

agastya uvāca |

devairadhyāsyamāno 'asau himavān bhūdhareśvaraḥ|
varaiḥ samphalitaḥ samyagbrahmaviṣṇumaheśvaraiḥ|| 26 ||

himavatyacale skanda tacchekaraujaso narāḥ|
vimuktā iha saṃsāraiḥ prāptaphalāśca ke vada|| 27 ||

skanda uvāca |

ākarṇaya ghaṭodbhūta vimuktā mānuṣāḥ purā|
tadvṛttāntaṃ pravakṣyāmi himavadacalaujasaḥ|| 28 ||

kaścidākarajīvī ca karaṅgo nāma viśrutaḥ|
parivārānvito mleccho bhramati smācalaṃ prati|| 29 ||

dhātūnanveṣayañchaśvaddhimavantaṃ samāyayau|
ājanmakilbiṣātmāsau dānadharmavivarjitaḥ|| 30 ||

yatrodbhūtā yaśodhārā nīlakaṇṭhāddhi paścime|
triyojanaṃ vidūre sa hemakūṭagiriṃ yayau|| 31 ||

yatra dravyeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ kuṇḍamadhye virājitam|
śuddhasphaṭikaliṅgeśaṃ gharmaklinnadravāplavam|| 32 ||

gaṇenārādhitaṃ pūrvaṃ tapastena mamerṣayā|
tasmāllabdhagaṇādhyakṣaṃ devarṣidaityavandanam|| 33 ||

payodhārājalaṃ mlecchastṛṣārto hi muhuḥ papau|
dhautakarānanāṅghriśca mūrdhni siñcyāśu tajjalaiḥ|| 34 ||

ajahādbhuvi ṭaṅkāni kṣīṇaraudrapariśramaḥ|
nadītīre kṣaṇaṃ śrāmya nirjharotpātane hi tat|| 35 ||

adriṃ hiraṇmayaṃ prekṣya bhṛtyānavocadāśu saḥ|
harṣajaḍāṅgamoho 'asau vacanairgadgadoktibhiḥ|| 36 ||

śrāvaṇe sitapakṣasya caturdaśyāṃ kṣudhāturaḥ|
pūrvāhne śītaduḥkhārto 'annābhāvādghaṭodbhava|| 37 ||

karaṅga uvāca |

aho bhrātaḥ priye putra paśyata purato naman|
hiraṇmayaṃ ca śailendraṃ paropakāriṇaṃ varam|| 38 ||

aho bhāgyam anāthānāṃ no 'adyaiva tat pradarśanāt|
adyaiva saphalaṃ janma bahupāpajuṣāṃ khalu|| 39 ||

adattaṃ naḥ priye vipre sakṛddāyaṃ vasuṃ purā|
tasmāddhi nirdhanaiḥ kliṣṭāstallobhairbhramitā iha|| 40 ||

bahujanmani tallabdhaṃ kaṣṭaṃ suduḥsahaṃ mayā|
kaṣṭāt taṃ bhramitaṃ prekṣya īśvarānugrahāddhi naḥ|| 41 ||

asyāḥ prabhāvataścāhaṃ nidhūlitaḥ kṛto jalaiḥ|
prāṅmanāgavaśiṣṭena dharmeṇehātra cāgataḥ|| 42 ||

yaṃ yaṃ ca vayam icchāmo rājyaṃ vā yogināṃ padam|
samudravalayāṃ kṣoṇīm īśvareṇa pradarśitām|| 43 ||

paśya putra priye bhrātastejonidhim imaṃ girim|
tatpaścimeṣu pūrveṣu cottareṣu tathāvidham|| 44 ||

yeṣūdbhūtāḥ purā nadyaḥ kauśikyo devamānitāḥ|
yeṣūdbhūtāśca gaṇḍakyastāni kūṭāni paśyata|| 45 ||

sarvaṃ svarṇamayaṃ śailaṃ sahasraśīrṣaṃ jātajam|
nānāratnaiḥ pradīptaṃ vai paśya paśyāgrato naman|| 46 ||

bhṛtyā ūcuḥ |

naivāsmābhiśca śailendro dṛṣṭaḥ svarṇamayo vibho|
vṛkṣagulmopalaiḥ śītairvibhūṣito 'acaleśvaraḥ|| 47 ||

karaṅga uvāca |

etaiḥ pūtairjalairnetre mānyāt sammārjyatāṃ naman|
tataḥ pītvā payaḥ putra paśyasi hāṭakācalam|| 48 ||

skanda uvāca |

gaṇakuṇḍodbhavaistoyairalepat pāṇibhiśca taiḥ|
pītvārṇa bhaktito 'agastya adrākṣuḥ purato 'acalān|| 49 ||

sarvaṃ jātamayaṃ śailaṃ sahasraśīrṣam agrataḥ|
maṇirtanāṃśubhirdyotam āścaryairupaśobhitam|| 50 ||

praṇemustvaritaṃ śailaṃ subhaktyā daṇḍavanmuhuḥ|
payodhārātaṭe mlecchāḥ kṛtārthaṃ menire hṛdā|| 51 ||

bhṛtyāṃṣṭaṅkāni saṃtyajya eka evāruroha saḥ|
jātamayaṃ giriṃ sākṣāt kṣīṇo viśrāmya sānuṣu|| 52 ||

ādhāya hṛdi cetyevaṃ nītvaitairhāṭakai rasām|
sārvabhaumo bhaviṣyāmi jitvāśu kṣatriyān kṣitau|| 53 ||

āruhya girisānuṃ sa gaṇakuṇḍaṃ prāptavān mune|
adarśadīśvaraṃ kuṇḍe ambhasthaṃ sphāṭikaṃ vidheḥ|| 54 ||

tato 'amaragaṇaṃ tatra jaleśvaraprasevinam|
apaśyannartayantaṃ sa gītavādyamahotsavaiḥ|| 55 ||

nartayantaṃ samaṃ devairlambodaraṃ mahotsavaiḥ|
apsarogīyamānaṃ ca vṛṣaketuṃ sa padmajaiḥ|| 56 ||

kuṇḍaprānte 'amale tasmin mlecche prāpte hi rodhasi|
papāta puṣpavṛṣṭiśca vyomni nādaṃ nanāda ca|| 57 ||

āyayustatra śaivāśca vimānapāṇayo 'ambarāt|
prodyotayaṃścaturdikṣu vaimānikai raviprabhaiḥ|| 58 ||

tam āsthāya vimāne te śaivā vyomani śāṃkaram|
cāmarairdhūyamānaṃ ca rudrakanyākareritais|| 59 ||

ninyuḥ śivapuraṃ sadyo gītavādyamahotsavaiḥ|
sadehaṃ dyotayan dikṣu vimānabhānubhirmune|| 60 ||

tādṛśaṃ tadgaṇā vyomno ninyurbhṛtyān pṛthak puram|
śatayugaṃ sukhaṃ vyāpya śāṃkaraṃ bubhujurhi te|| 61 ||

so 'abhavaddhi pṛthagrājā rasāṃ sarvāṃ śaśāsa saḥ|
kṛtvātmasān nṛpāṃstasyāṃ gaṇakuṇḍaprabhāvataḥ|| 62 ||

tatrasthā sā śilādarśadbhṛtyāṃśca tādṛśān bhayāt|
nirjanā caraṇāśaktā nadī ruroda nirbharam|| 63 ||

krandanaṃ ravam ākarṇya gaṇarṣistatra cāyayau|
upagamya jaṭī saumyo brāhmaṇīṃ tām avocayat|| 64 ||

jaigīṣavya uvāca |

mā rodīḥ putri dāridri prākpāpaistvaṃ prapīḍitā|
taddhetoḥ pāpinīśīle prāgadānaiḥ sunirdhanā|| 65 ||

kathaṃ rodiṣi pāpiṣṭhe svakṛtaiḥ karṣitādhunā|
idānīm api dharmaṃ hi saṃsṛtitārakaṃ kuru|| 66 ||

śilovāca |

ekākinī tvaśaktāhaṃ patiputrairvivarjitā|
kva gacchāmīha hā kaṣṭaṃ māṃ tyajya kva gatāśca te|| 67 ||

śūnye 'araṇye nadītīre jalajhaṃkāranisvane|
jantupakṣisamāyukte patitā nirjanā vibho|| 68 ||

kilbiṣaiḥ karṣitāhaṃ kairbahukṛtaiḥ purā kṛtaiḥ|
bhṛtyānāṃ doṣajairvāpi yathārthaṃ vada me dvija|| 69 ||

jagīṣavya uvāca |

kṛṣikartuḥ priyāsi tvaṃ dānadharmairvivarjitā|
tasmādaśrī ca dāridrī abhūjjanmani janmani|| 70 ||

yasmai kasmai na dattaṃ prāk śākamūlaphalaṃ ca yat|
svakukṣiṃ kevalaṃ bhartrī annakaṇā manāgapi|| 71 ||

bhūtvāvasacchile kṣetraṃ kalāvaphalarakṣikā|
patriṇo varitāścāpi jantavo laguḍena ca|| 72 ||

tvayi tadrakṣamānāyāṃ kākaḥ koṣaikam agrahīt|
