tvayā saptaṃ phalāyāśu amedhyaiḥ pūryatām iti|| 73 ||

tatkoṣaṃ pradadau kākaścitraguptāya saṃcitum|
tena tat saṃcitaṃ samyagdātum ante punarhi tat|| 74 ||

tvaddehānte praṇītāyāṃ saṃyamanīṃ yamānugāḥ|
tṛṣārtāhaṃ kṣudhārtāham arodīreva nirbharam|| 75 ||

bhuṅksveti dattavāṃstubhyaṃ tatkoṣāni yamo 'agrataḥ|
koṭiguṇaṃ cayaṃ kṛtvā ato nītāni kiṃkaraiḥ|| 76 ||

bhakṣitaṃ prekṣitaṃ tāni nakhābhyāṃ bhindya tat pṛthak|
amedhyaistatra pūrṇāni adrākṣīdduḥkhitā bhṛśam|| 77 ||

kṣutpipāsāpradagdhāṅgā magnā narakasadmasu|
lakṣābdānte punarjanma sarvayoṇiṣu te pṛthak|| 78 ||

lakṣābdānte punarjātā narayonyām iyaṃ tanuḥ|
gaṅgātaṭe mṛtāt puṇyādbhṛtyāsta eva te khalu|| 79 ||

te 'api labdhvā varaṃ puṇyānmattīrthādriprabhāvataḥ|
adānāṃ tvāṃ ca saṃtyajya ārohaṇāddhimālayam|| 80 ||

mattīrthe 'asmin dhruvaṃ snātvā āruhyatām ayaṃ giriḥ|
tatpadavīṃ suniḥpāpāṃ bhṛtyān prāpsyasi tāṃ śile|| 81 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ sambodhya tāṃ vipra puṇyamārgaṃ pradarśayan|
jaigīṣavyo yayau taptuṃ varāhārṣisarovaram|| 82 ||

yatra taptaṃ varāheṇa muniśṛṅgeṇa vai purā|
adyāpi tāṃ na muñcanti siddhā devarṣayo 'aniśam|| 83 ||

siddhakūṭaṃ samāruhya gantā pāpairvimucyate|
hradadarśanamātreṇa aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet|| 84 ||

kacādiddaivayogena snānaṃ karoti mānavaḥ|
saptajanmakṛtaiḥ pāpaiḥ sa mukto nātra saṃśayaḥ|| 85 ||

samākarṇya śilāgastya jaigīṣavyavacastathā|
kṛtvā tathyaṃ hṛdā tatra tattīrthaṃ prayayau śanaiḥ|| 86 ||

jaigīṣavyo jale sasnau yāmbūrasaiśca saṃyute|
gaṇḍatīrthaśilāgastya aruhadgiriśekharam|| 87 ||

sāṅgā sāpi yayau śaivaṃ yānena sūryavarcasā|
evaṃ ca bahavo muktāstattīrthādriprabhāvataḥ|| 88 ||

koṭimartyagaṇo nityaṃ dvikoṭipaśavastathā|
trikoṭayaḥ pragacchanti catvāraḥ kṛmayaḥ param|| 89 ||

api vivarjitā jñānairhemabhṛcchekharaujasaḥ|
aruhaṃstadgiriṃ ye ye trividhotpattayo mune|| 90 ||

sahasrābdaṃ tathāgastya tatraujasaśca jīvinaḥ|
svarge tiṣṭhan mudā vyāpya bhuñjan mahat sukhaṃ purā|| 91 ||

muktā lakṣaṃ purābdhīśe bhasmapaṅkeśvare tathā|
muktāḥ kāleśvare lakṣaṃ lakṣam aiśānakeśvare|| 92 ||

abhratuṅgeśvare lakṣaṃ ratnakoṭīśvare tathā|
kāmeśvare tathā lakṣaṃ vāgmatīśe tathā punaḥ|| 93 ||

kāmarūpe ca bhasmeśe saundaryādrau tathā mune|
jaleśvare mahāliṅge hayagrīve ca lakṣakam|| 94 ||

bahurūpeśvare lakṣaṃ pretāsane tathā punaḥ|
vidyāliṅge mahākūṭe viśvambhareśvare tathā|| 95 ||

vārāhe śaṃkare lakṣaṃ mleccharūpeśvare tathā|
svarṇaliṅge mune lakṣaṃ ratnaliṅge ca lakṣakam|| 96 ||

chinnagrīve mahāviṣṇau lakṣaṃ devapureśvare|
pārvatīśe tathā lakṣaṃ dugdhasteyeśvare punaḥ|| 97 ||

nīlakaṇṭheśvare lakṣaṃ pāśupateṣu lakṣakam|
paśupatau dvilakṣaṃ syādvimuktāste savigrahāḥ|| 98 ||

cakratīrthe ca śūleśe harikṣetre ca lakṣakam|
devaghaṭṭe tathā lakṣaṃ prabhātīrthe ca lakṣakam|| 99 ||

dharmakūṭe tathā lakṣaṃ dharmanadī yatodbhavā|
śaśāpājaḥ purā dharma dravībhaveti cādyataḥ|| 100 ||

abhrakūṭe girīśāne svarṇaśṛṅge trilakṣakam|
halotkhāte tathā lakṣaṃ keśave lakṣakaḥ punaḥ|| 101 ||

svarṇanābhamahākūṭe svarṇagarbhācale trayam|
dvilakṣaṃ badrikāśaile kedāre lakṣakaṃ dvayam|| 102 ||

viśvakūṭe mahāpanthe svarṇadvāre pṛthak trayam|
dvilakṣaṃ bhairavīśaile dvilakṣaṃ triyugīśvare|| 103 ||

mānassare trayaṃ lakṣaṃ bhadrāyāṃ ca trilakṣakam|
lakṣam alakanandāyāṃ bhāgirathyāṃ tathā trayam|| 104 ||

lakṣaṃ karṇaprayāge dve lakṣaṃ viṣṇuprayāgake|
lakṣaṃ rudraprayāge dve dvayaṃ brahmaprayāgake|| 105 ||

lakṣe devaprayāge dve vyāsasaṃgāhvaye tathā|
lomāśraye mahāliṅge jvālāmukhīgirau trayam|| 106 ||

viśvambhareśvare lakṣaṃ gaṅgākānteśvare tathā|
trikūṭe vimale lakṣaṃ viśvaketau ca lakṣakam|| 107 ||

jambūśaile tathā lakṣaṃ śrīśekhare ca lakṣakam|
sūryādrau candraśaile dve agnidīpte ca lakṣakam|| 108 ||

maṇibhūmau dvayaṃ lakṣaṃ dvilakṣaṃ candraśekhare|
abdhikūṭeśvare lakṣaṃ ratnakūṭeśvare trayam|
taptācale trayaṃ lakṣaṃ lakṣaṃ bhuvanaśekhare|| 109 ||

koṭikoṭinarairvyāptaṃ bhūrlokaṃ ca ghaṭodbhava|
bhuvarlokaṃ tathā svargaṃ munilokaṃ kṛtāntakam|| 110 ||

vyāptaṃ nairṛtyakaṃ martyairvāruṇaṃ vāyumandiram|
kauberaṃ ca tathaiśānaṃ sūryalokaṃ himāṃśukam|| 111 ||

nākṣatraṃ ca maharlokaṃ janalokaṃ tapastathā|
satyalokaṃ puno brāhmaṃ viṣṇulokaṃ ca yat tathā|| 112 ||

samprekṣya tridaśā martyairvyāptaṃ lokaṃ svakaṃ svakam|
brahmādayaśca sambhūya duḥkhāt paśupatiṃ yayuḥ|| 113 ||

brahmovāca |

prāgdattaṃ bhavatā no yadvyarthayatno bhavediha|
janako jīvināṃ cāhaṃ pālako 'ayam iti prabho|| 114 ||

sadehaiḥ pūritaṃ martyaiḥ surasadmāni sarvaśaḥ|
snānadānārcanairhīnaiḥ paśupakṣimṛgādibhiḥ|| 115 ||

lakṣābdaṃ no bhavedadya evaṃ martyamayo giriḥ|
bhavanti jñānino muktāḥ pāmaraisteṣu pūritam|| 116 ||

paśupatiruvāca |

avaśyaṃ prāpyate devāstapasvibhiḥ phalaṃ hi yat|
labdhavarācalasparśāt samlapsyanti ālayāni vaḥ|| 117 ||

mā dūyatāṃ hare tasmāt pratīkāro bhaviṣyati|
avaśyaṃ te prayacchanti himavacchikhare janāḥ|| 118 ||

saṃtyajya vigrahāṇi āśu pāmarāḥ snātakā api|
tapasvino himaśaile tat sānuṣu sakṛt tvayi|
uddhariṣye sadehāṃstān nirvāṇena vinā kalim|| 119 ||

skanda uvāca |

paśupatervacaḥ śrutvā harṣaiḥ prapūritāḥ surāḥ|
jyotirliṅgaṃ naman bhaktyā parikramya yayuḥ svakam|| 120 ||

tadādi jīvinaḥ śaile saṃtyajya vigrahāṇi te|
nirvāṇaiḥ prayayuḥ svargaṃ kṛtaṃ vinā ghaṭodbhava|| 121 ||

śṛṇvanti dhīrā himavanmahātmyaṃ prāpyātikīrtiṃ suyaśo 'anvayante|
dhānyaṃ dhanāni āyuṣam āśu bhūmau haimācale yat sukṛtaṃ vrajet tat|| 122 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe himālayamāhātmyaṃ nāma aṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ|| 8 ||

skanda uvāca |

lokam aṣṭādaśaṃ kṣubdhaṃ mlecchaputraiḥ purā mune|
badrikeśaprasādādvai kedārānugrahāt tathā|| 1 ||

nāradasyopadeśāt tairgaṅgāyāṃ mokṣam āpnuyuḥ|
labdhaṃ nirvāṇamāhātmyam etaddhimavati mune|| 2 ||

agastya uvāca |

kathaṃ saṃkṣobhitaṃ mlecchairdevalokaṃ camūpate|
pratoṣitau kathaṃ devau kedārabadrikeśvarau|| 3 ||

kathaṃ labdhaṃ hi gaṅgāyāṃ sunirvāṇaṃ ca pāmaraiḥ|
nāradasyopadeśena mlecchāstadudbhavaṃ vada|| 4 ||

lomaharṣaṇa uvāca |

kumbhayonervacaḥ śrutvā munayaḥ pārvatīsutaḥ|
vyājahāra vacastasmai pūrvodbhūtakathottaram|| 5 ||

skanda uvāca |

cyavanāśramatīrthe 'aṅga cyavane tapasi sthite|
yayau ānāyadhṛk tatra vaṅgunāma ca dhīvaraḥ|| 6 ||

matysāṃścikṣepa jālaṃ sa samuddiśya vadhāya ca|
avadhīt katicinmatsyānavamatya janānṛṣīn|| 7 ||

ṛṣiniṣedhitaṃ śaśvadaśrutvā vacanaṃ hi tat|
ruṣāviṣṭaḥ śaśāpāśu śūkaro bhava pāpakṛt|| 8 ||

sa kolaḥ satyaśeṣe ca bhramati sma vanādvanam|
śatābdānte 'agamacchailaṃ himavatsānusundaram|| 9 ||

tatrāvātsīt sukhaṃ kolastāmrakūṭanidhānake|
pañcayojanadūre ca devaghaṭṭottare diśi|| 10 ||

bhādrasya pūrṇimāyāṃ sa pūrvābhādrarkṣasaṃyute|
saumye prātardine 'agastya hradottamaṃ dadarśa saḥ|| 11 ||

śailakūṭe hrade kolaḥ prapapau jīvanaṃ sakṛt|
māsānte daivayogāddhi khādan mūlaphalāni ca|| 12 ||

pītamātreṇa tat toyaṃ so 'ajahat kolavigraham|
avātsīt tadgirau mlecchaḥ kaṃcit kālaṃ hi sānvayaḥ|| 13 ||

badrikādāyayau kaścidbhikṣārthī tadgṛhe jaṭī|
dattvā spṛśaddhi tatpādau nīvārānnaṃ sa dhīvaraḥ|| 14 ||

tadbadrikārohaṇapūtapādau saṃsparśadūrīgatakilbiṣo 'asau|
adyādyahaṃ tatpadavīṃ vraje vai saṃkalpam ādyaṃ kṛtavān hṛdeti|| 15 ||

putrā yūyaṃ prarakṣadhvaṃ bhṛtyān sarvān gṛhāśramam|
vrajāmyahaṃ tapaḥ sthātuṃ vṛddho 'ayaṃ yātanābhayāt|| 16 ||

jīvino bahavaḥ putrā mayā hatāḥ sunirdayam|
tatpāpairliptadeho 'ahaṃ yāmyaṃ yāsyati niścitam|| 17 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ sambodhya putrān sa saṃtyajya viṃśatiṃ niśi|
prayayau himavacchaile tadvāruṇottare diśi|| 18 ||

nirjanaḥ prayayau saumya udāsīkeśavātmakaḥ|
parvatān sa samuttīrya badrikāśramam āptavān|| 19 ||

siddheśvarātmako mleccho badrikācalam āruhat|
taptakuṇḍe mudā snātvā udakuṇḍodakaṃ papau|| 20 ||

vaiśākhapūrṇimāyāṃ ca so 'adrākṣīt parameśvaram|
anamaddaṇḍavat kṛtvā trividhairbhaktito mune|| 21 ||

vimohito 'ayaṃ jana īśa māyayā nimagnasaṃsāragabhīrasāgare|
na sevate tvāṃ paramauṣadhīrasaṃ tathāpi mūḍho bhavatā prarakṣyate|| 22 ||

nārāyaṇāya devāya siddheśvarāya śāśvate|
parameśāya nandāya paramāya namo namaḥ|| 23 ||

paraṃ brahmarūpaṃ paraṃ śaṃkareśaṃ śarīraprarūḍhollasaddvandvabhāvam|
manobhirvacobhistanūbhiḥ sadāhaṃ nato 'asmīśvaraṃ taṃ bhaje 'ahaṃ pareśam|| 24 ||

evaṃ saṃstūyamānaṃ vai ninyuryānena taṃ gaṇāḥ|
viṣṇulokaṃ sadehaṃ ca dhārayaṃścaturāyudham|| 25 ||

pituranvagaman sadyo 'anurodhituṃ hi tatsutāḥ|
hā tāteti ca saṃkrandya sambhūya pathi te yayuḥ|| 26 ||

bhrātaro 'aṣṭādaśa śailānuttīrya prayayurvanāt|
prāptā rudraprayāgaṃ tu tīrthe tvaharniśaṃ vasan|| 27 ||

sitāṣṭamyāṃ ca rādhasya sasnuḥ pītajalottamāḥ|
te 'api jagṛhurgṛhasthānāṃ pratyāgamanam ālayam|| 28 ||

prāptavanto hi kedāraṃ vrajantaste śanaiḥ śanaiḥ|
rudrakuṇḍajalaṃ spṛṣṭvā te jahuḥ pūrvakilbiṣam|| 29 ||

apaśyan paramaṃ liṅgaṃ jyotīrūpaṃ mahādbhutam|
mithaḥ procustadā mlecchā bhrātarastyaktaśaṃkaram|
no gṛhaṃ na gamiṣyāmaḥ seviṣyāmaḥ śam atra vai|| 30 ||

praṇamya daṇḍavadbhaktyā kedāreśaṃ ca dhīvarāḥ|
tuṣṭuvurharṣitā devaṃ vāgbhirgadgadavāditaiḥ|| 31 ||

dhīvarā ūcuḥ |

natāḥ smo maheśaṃ trinetraṃ trirūpaṃ bhujaṃgāvalībhūṣitāṅgaṃ pareśam|
vibhūtiprabhūtipralepaṃ pratīkaṃ jaṭājūṭarociṣṇuśīrṣaṃ bhaje 'aham|| 32 ||

trilokaprayāṇātaraṅgojjvalāṅgam avalakṣyendukhṇḍāṅkitākalpabhālam|
vṛṣaṃ vyāghracarmādināgendrahāraṃ triśūlaṃ dadhānaṃ ca maḍḍuṃ bhaje 'aham|| 33 ||

ravīndvarkanetraiśca vibhrājamānaṃ vṛṣavyañjanaṃ saumyarūpaṃ smitāsyam|
himādryātmajāliṅganārdhapratīkaṃ sadānandarūpaṃ paraṃ jyotirūpam|| 34 ||

hṛdi dyāyamānaṃ satāṃ yogināṃ śaṃ girīndrātmajāsyekṣaṇprollasantam|
tuṣārāṃśukāntiprakāṇḍapratīkaṃ prapañcāntarālollasaccittavṛttim|| 35 ||

sadānanda uvāca |

cidānandarūpaṃ vikārojjhiteśaṃ nirastāndhapāpābdhimagnodbhavantam|
ṣaḍādhārapadmollasajjīvarūpaṃ śarīrāntarojjṛmbhitotpatticittam|| 36 ||

anirliptam ādyeśaṃhoviluptam iḍāpiṅgalāsuṣumṇāmadhyavṛttim|
prapañcāṅgacatvārarūpollasantaṃ sadīśaṃ mudā taṃ bhaje 'ahaṃ bhaje 'aham|| 37 ||

sadā dhyāyamānaṃ manaḥpadmamadhye satāṃ yogarūpaṃ ca kaivalyanātham|
prakāśekṣaṇendvarkavahniprabhṛtiṃ maheśaṃ sureśaṃ deneśasvarūpam|| 38 ||

yadaṃśaprabhusvargalokaprapālam abhivyaktatejonirastāndhakāram|
jaḍābuddhamūrkhājñamokṣāyaneśaṃ namaste kṛpāsāgeśāṣṭamūrte|| 39 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ parikramya muhurmuhuḥ|
vaiśākhapūrṇimāyāṃ te bhaktyānarcuśca pañcabhiḥ|| 40 ||

rudrānuśāsanastho 'asau nandī tatpurato 'agamat|
varadānāya tebhyo yadvyājahāra vaco mudā|| 41 ||

nandyuvāca |

bhaktito yācyatāṃ māṃ yat svāntepsitāni vaḥ khalu|
yūyaṃ vikilbiṣāścādya bhaveyuu rudradarśanāt|| 42 ||

iha loke varasthānaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca sudurlabham|
sudurlabhāṃ vibhūtiṃ vā suraloke 'api vā param|| 43 ||

dhīvarā ūcuḥ |

na yācayāmahe tāṃ tvām iha loke 'api tāṃ sthitam|
kāṅkṣāmaḥ svargalokeṣu pṛthak sthānaṃ dadasva naḥ|| 44 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya vacasteṣāṃ svīkāraṃ kṛtavān suraḥ|
tān ādadhyurgaṇā raudrā vimāne sārvakāmike|| 45 ||

ninyurvyomnaśca yānasthān pramathā devasadmasu|
saṃsthāpitā gaṇai raudrairdevalokeṣu tān pṛthak|| 46 ||

maivātra tiṣṭha śakrācca yatrepsitaṃ vrajāśu tat|
naścenniḥsārayāmyadya yuddhaṃ cet tvāṃ prahantyaham|| 47 ||

evaṃ taistāḍyamānāśca vāgasibhirdivaukasaḥ|
amarṣaiḥ pūritāḥ sadyo babhūvurudyatā yudhi|| 48 ||

yuyudhustridaśaiḥ sārdhaṃ dhīvarā varadarpiṇaḥ|
tatsthānāni sunirjitya devāṃstasthurvareṣu te|| 49 ||

ātmasāt kṛtavantaste śakralokapuraḥsarān|
bubhujire sukhāni ārya teṣu rudraprasādataḥ|| 50 ||

āsīt sahasravarṣānte sambhūyāsan surā yayuḥ|
dikpālālokinaḥ sarve śakrādayo ghaṭodbhava|| 51 ||

ākarṇya vacanaṃ teṣāṃ brahmāṇḍe tridaśaiḥ samam|
viṣṇulokaṃ yayau sadyo 'avocadvyasanaṃ hi tat|| 52 ||

vaco niśamya viṣṇuśca brahmādibhiḥ samaṃ punaḥ|
rudralokaṃ yayau taddhi avocadvyasanaṃ tadā|| 53 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

rakṣa rakṣa vibho no vaḥ kiṃkarān sthānacālataḥ|
dhīvaropaplavārtāṃstvaṃ namaḥ sarvārtihāriṇe|| 54 ||

rudra uvāca |

avaśyaṃ bhuñjate devāḥ kṛtaṃ karma śubhoditam|
dhīvaraistaiḥ suniḥpāpaiḥ pratoṣitastapobalaiḥ|| 55 ||

ato datto varaṃ tebhyo bhaktitoṣeṇa connatam|
kālaṃ na yācitairmāṃ tairbhoktāro lakṣavatsaram|| 56 ||

skanda uvāca |

rudragiraṃ ca gīrvāṇāḥ śrutvā lokaṃ svakaṃ yayuḥ|
bubhujire sukhaṃ teṣu lakṣābdaikasahasrakam|| 57 ||

bhuvaḥsvarjanalokāni mahastapo harermama|
aṣṭau lokāni divyānāṃ sūryendroḍḍagaṇasya ca|| 58 ||

ekadā sammato viṣṇornāradaḥ paryaṭan mahīm|
dhīvareṇārcito bhaktyā brahmāṅgajeti saṃnaman|| 59 ||

vaṅguruvāca |

aho bhāgyaṃ mamaivādya yato bhavānihāgataḥ|
pravṛttijña pravṛttirno lokānāṃ vada me vibho|| 60 ||

nārada uvāca |

vatseha lokapo bhūtvā na jāgarṣi kathaṃ dhruvam|
sahasrottaralakṣābdaṃ dattaṃ rudreṇa vaḥ sthitim|| 61 ||

tadante samato yūyaṃ bhraśiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ|
yathāpūrvaṃ kṣitau śaśvat svavṛttiṃ kārakāḥ punaḥ|| 62 ||

vaṅguruvāca |

tapāṃsyatra kariṣyāmi ārādhayan vibhuṃ śivam|
mokṣe devyaciraṃ bhūyo bhrātarastādṛśāḥ punaḥ|| 63 ||

nārada uvāca |

maivaṃ martye hi vaktavyaṃ manasāpi kadā budha|
atrodbhūtastapovṛkṣaḥ phalati na phalāni tat|| 64 ||

vinā himālaye puṇye samudbhūtatapodrumam|
pūrvaṃ himālaye vatsa etatkālatapaḥ kṛtām|| 65 ||

vaṅguruvāca |

kiyadvarṣam iha sthāne saṃsthātavyaṃ mayā vibho|
bhrātṛṇāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa vada me sarvavit punaḥ|| 66 ||

nārada uvāca |

ekābdaṃ vidyate śeṣaṃ svargabhogyaṃ ca vaḥ kila|
patiṣyanti dhruvaṃ svargādbhrātarastvaṃ ca sarvataḥ|| 67 ||

yāvat saukhyaṃ ca tāvaddhi duḥkham eva bhaviṣyati|
sukhaduḥkhānvitā bhūtirdhīmadbhistyajyate hi tat|| 68 ||

nirvāṇam eva saukhyaṃ syāt sarvaduḥkhairvivarjitam|
ata evārya dhīmadbhirmokṣaṃ prārthyaṃ yataḥ śive|| 69 ||

vaṅguruvāca |

avaśyam eva kāṅkṣāmo nirvāṇaṃ nārada dhruvam|
upadeṣāmṛtairmāṃ tān prasiñcayāśu dharmavit|| 70 ||

bhrātṛṇām agrataḥ satyam etadvārtāṃ ca varṇyatām|
avaśyaṃ tatra yāsyāmastapasthānaṃ punastviti|| 71 ||

nārada uvāca |

gacchāśu bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ tapaḥsānau himālaye|
lomaśādupadeśaṃ yadgṛhya tatra tapasyatām|| 72 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ādiśya yayau dānto nārado dhīvarān mune|
sarvalokaṃ samāgamya vārtāṃstebhya uvāca tat|| 73 ||

nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā sammīlya mantrayaṃstadā|
sarvalokāni saṃtyajya prayayurhimavadgirim|| 74 ||

tapasthaṃ lomaśaṃ dāntaṃ prekṣya tadāśramaṃ yayuḥ|
praṇamya vidhivadbhaktyā procuḥ samantato hi te|| 75 ||

dhīvarā ūcuḥ |

dharmairvivarjitā jñeyāḥ svargaprabhraṃśino vayam|
teṣu bahu sukhaṃ bhuktvā daivena preritā iha|| 76 ||

kva yāsyāmaḥ kva tiṣṭhāmo nirvāṇaṃ lipsato vayam|
tadupadiśyatāṃ no vai bhavān sarvavidātmavit|| 77 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya vacasteṣāṃ lomaśo harṣavān mune|
svāgatān yogarūḍhāṃstānavocadvacanaṃ tadā|| 78 ||

lomaśa uvāca |

sādhu sādhu naraśreṣṭhā īdṛgdhīrdhāritā yataḥ|
kṣudrasvapnasukhaṃ svargaṃ te suduḥkhaparāṅmukhāḥ|| 79 ||

haraśīrṣārcitā nadyāḥ saṃgame 'alakanandayā|
dharmakūṭe tridhā snātvā rudrāśramaṃ pragacchata|| 80 ||

pañcākṣaraṃ hṛdā dhāyam ārādhayata śaṃkaram|
namaścādyaṃ caturthantaṃ tadrūpaṃ mokṣadaṃ śivam|| 81 ||

dhīvarā ūcuḥ |

praṣṭum icchāmahe kiṃcidbhavantaṃ bhavataḥ prabhoḥ|
kiyanto vatsaraṃ nītaṃ tapaḥsthasyātra varṇinaḥ|| 82 ||

skanda uvāca |

śrutvā tadvacanaṃ dānto vihasyāryaḥ smitānanaḥ|
vyājahāra vacastebhyaściraṃjīvanātmakaḥ|| 83 ||

lomaśa uvāca |

aciraṃ jīvino me yat paśyatvatorasyalomaśam|
mudrānumitam ādyaṃ tallomabhirvarjitaṃ dhruvam|| 84 ||

manvantarāt tadekaikaṃ lomedaṃ bhraṃsyati dhruvam|
etatpramāṇato yātā manvantarāṇi dhīvarāḥ|| 85 ||

skanda uvāca |

niśamya vacanaṃ tasya dhīvarā jātavismayāḥ|
svātmānaṃ khalu dhik kṛtvā tannamannagamaddharam|| 86 ||

śukraśuklaśadabhyānte sasnurdevaprayāgake|
saṃkrame pūrṇimāyāṃ ca trivāraṃ vidhivanmudā|| 87 ||

rudrāśramaṃ samāruhya taptavantaściraṃ girau|
tanmanaskāsaṃmekābdaṃ sampūjyāharniśaṃ muhuḥ|| 88 ||

saṃtyajya vigrahāṇi āśu jyotīrūpam ca śaṃkaram|
tadā te viviśurdhīrā himādritapasaḥ phalam|| 89 ||

śṛṇoti dhīro himabhṛnmahātmyaṃ bhaktiprayukto varacittavṛttiḥ|
devaprayāge salilāplavaṃ yallabhet phalaṃ pūtayaśāṃsi nākam|| 90 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe himālayamāhātmyaṃ nāma navamo adhyāyaḥ|| 9 ||

agastya uvāca |

bhūyo 'ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi tvatto brahmavidāṃ vara|
devānāṃ cāsurāṇāṃ ca tapo 'anyeṣāṃ ca yat kṛtam|| 1 ||

deva kena prakāreṇa tapaścakāra kaḥ kadā|
vidhinā kena kaḥ kasmin sthāne dhyeyaṃ himālaye|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

śṛṇu mune hi vakṣyāmi yat pṛṣṭaṃ bhavatā ca mām|
brahmakarma tapo jñānam ādau manaḥsamāhitaḥ|| 3 ||

brāhme muhūrte cotthāya saṃsmaret pūrvam īśvaram|
tato dharāṃ namaskṛtya svāsānukramato nyaset|| 4 ||

samudravalaye devi parvatastanamaṇḍale|
viṣṇupatni namastubhyaṃ pādasparśaṃ kṣamasva me|| 5 ||

iti stutvā padaṃ nyasya bahirvrajedvicakṣaṇaḥ|
nairṛtyāṃ diśi saṃvrajya malamocanam ācaret|| 6 ||

malamūtrasamutsargaṃ divā kuryādudaṅmukhaḥ|
dakṣiṇābhimukho rātrau sandhayostu yathā divā|| 7 ||

yajñasūtraṃ śrave kṛtvā maunī bhūtvā vicakṣaṇaḥ|
evaṃ kṛtvā ca śaucārthe jalāśayaṃ samāvrajet|| 8 ||

uddhṛtodakam ādāya mṛttikāṃ caiva vāgyataḥ|
udaṅmukho divā kuryādrātrau ceddakṣiṇāmukhaḥ|| 9 ||

ekā ca liṅge ca gude ca tisraḥ savye ca haste ca daśastathā ca|
kartavyam evaṃ hyubhayostu sapta mṛcchuddhirāryeṇa śucau budhena|| 10 ||

śaucaṃ vipra vidhāyaivaṃ tisrastisraśca pādayoḥ|
śuddham udakam ādāya ācamecca punaḥ punaḥ|| 11 ||

tataḥ sūryaṃ nirīkṣedvai gāṃ vāgastya dvijaṃ tathā|
ālokanāddhi saṃśuddhim āpnuyāt taṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ|| 12 ||

mukhaṃ prakṣālya pāṇī dvau prakuryāddantadhāvanam|
śuddhakāṣṭhaṃ samādāya kṣīriṇaṃ kaṇṭasaṃyutam|| 13 ||

sarvaṃ kaṇṭakiṇaṃ puṇyaṃ pramāṇaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam|
parijapya ca mantreṇa prāṅmukhaḥ sa udaṅmukhaḥ|| 14 ||

āyurbalaṃ yaśo varcaḥ prajāḥ paśuvasūni ca|
brahma prajñāṃ ca medhāṃ ca tanno dehi vanaspate|| 15 ||

mukhaṃ prakṣālya hastau ca tathā pādau samāhitaḥ|
maunī bhūtvā dvijaśreṣṭha ācamanaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ|| 16 ||

brahmatīrthena hastena manuṃ smaran dhiyā sudhīḥ|
ṛjukāyaḥ samāsīnaḥ prāṅmukho vāpyudaṅmukhaḥ|| 17 ||

aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ ca śrotrabandhaṃ tataḥ smṛtam|
mukhe ca nāsayorghrāṇe cakṣuṣoḥ karṇayostathā|
bāhvorurvostathāgastya sarvāṅgāni tataḥ spṛśet|| 18 ||

.o vāṅme āsye 'astu .o nāsayorme proṇo 'astu |

.o akṣṇorme cakṣurastu .o karṇayorme śrotram astu |

.o bāhvorme balam astu .o ūrvo me ojo 'astu |

.o ariṣṭāni me 'aṅgāni santu .o tanustanvā me saho 'astu|| 19 |

etanmanuṃ smaran vipraḥ sarvāṅgāni spṛśet sudhīḥ|
tatastīrthaṃ samāgatya snānaṃ ca vidhivat punaḥ|| 20 ||

prakṣālya hastau pādau ca jihvām ācamanaṃ saha|
prāṇāyāmaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā śikhāṃ mantreṇa bandhayet|| 21 ||

tatastīrthaṃ samāvāhya manuṃ smaraṃśca cetasā|
adyādyasminnahaṃ tīrthe prītyarthaṃ vā hṛdīpsitam|| 22 ||

snānam ahaṃ kariṣye vā kāmenaivaṃ yathā punaḥ|
gaṅgābhāvena tīrthajñaḥ pronmajjet kuśahastakaḥ|| 23 ||

nadoṣā pūtasalilā haramūrthirnamo 'astu te|
ādau sūryāya devāya apāñjaliṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ|| 24 ||

dadyānmantraṃ smaran dhīro mṛttikāsnānam ācaret|
mṛttike hara me pāpaṃ yanmayā duḥkṛtaṃ kṛtam|| 25 ||

tvathāhṛtena pāpena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate|
iti paṭhan sakṛddhīraḥ kuryāt sarvāṅgalepanam|| 26 ||

praṇavena tato mantrī āvartayet trathaṃjale|
tataḥ suvimale tīrthe sarvapāpahare śubhe|| 27 ||

mano nirmalyabhāvena smaran mantraṃ dhiyā sudhīḥ|
sarvāṅgagharṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā pronmajya ca punaḥ punaḥ|| 28 ||

nimajjanatrayaṃ kuryāddevasnānaṃ paraṃ matam|
ātmānaṃ mārjayeddhīro drupadādi ṛcaṃ paṭhan|| 29 ||

kuśodakaṃ samādāya prāṅmukhaṃ ca muhurmuhuḥ|
āpohiṣṭheti japtena karasampuṭayojitam|| 30 ||

mūrdhni kuryājjalaṃ bhūyastriḥsaptapañcadhā tathā|
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā gāyatrīṃ prajapeddaśa|| 31 ||

kumbhākāreṇa pāṇyośca mūrdhni triḥ prakṣitet punaḥ|
evaṃ snānavidhiṃ kṛtvā tūttīrya parivāya vai|
vāsasī cottarīyaṃ vai tatastarpaṇam ācaret|| 32 ||

ambhastho vā sthalastho vā tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ|
tarpayet tu yathākāmam apsu sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam|| 33 ||

āpo devagaṇāḥ sarve āpaḥ pitṛgaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ|
tasmājjale jalaṃ deyaṃ pitṛbhyo dattam akṣayam|| 34 ||

tridaśānāṃ pitṛṇāṃ ca jale dadyājjalāñjalim|
asaṃskṛtapramītānāṃ sthale dadyājjalāñjalim|| 35 ||

tarpaṇaṃ tu śuciḥ kuryāt pratyahaṃ snātako dvijaḥ|
devebhyaśca ṛṣibhyaśca pitṛbhyaśca yathākramam|| 36 ||

devāśca pitaraścaiva vāñchanti salilaṃ prati|
adatte tu nirāśāste pratīyānti yathāgatam|| 37 ||

tasmāt sarvaprayatnena tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ|
tarpaṇāt siddhim āpnoti pratyavāyam atarpaṇāt|| 38 ||

tat tarpaṇavidhiṃ kṛtvā paridhānadhṛto yatī|
ācamya ca trayaṃ maunī sandhyāṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ|| 39 ||

brahmatīrthena hastasya manuṃ smaran dhiyā sudhīḥ|
ṛjukāyaḥ samāsīnaḥ prāṅmukhī vāpyudaṅmukhaḥ|| 40 ||

śucau deśe samāgatya sthānaśuddhiṃ vicārayet|
gṛhe tvekaguṇaṃ kṛtyaṃ nadyāṃ daśaguṇaṃ smṛtam|| 41 ||

gavāṃ goṣṭhe śataguṇaṃ magnyāgāre śatādhikam|
siddhakṣetreṣu tīrtheṣu devatānāṃ ca saṃnidhau|| 42 ||

sahasraśatakoṭīnām anantaṃ śivasaṃnidhau|
girikūṭe mahātuṅge kiṃśuke ca tathāvidham|| 43 ||

koṭikoṭiguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ tatra kṛtyaṃ pralabhyate|
sānuṣu himaśailasya tapasām arbudaṃ guṇam|| 44 ||

tuṣāradarśane kūṭe kṛtaṃ daśaguṇaṃ phalam|
himakaṇṭāṅkite kūṭe kharvaguṇaṃ phalaṃ labhet|| 45 ||

upatyakāsu śītādrernikharvaṃ madhyataḥ punaḥ|
himasaṃhatikūṭeṣu mahāpadmaguṇaṃ kramāt|| 46 ||

āsanaṃ ca tato dhīmān prakalpayedvidhānataḥ|
sarvasiddhyai vyāghracarma jñānasiddhyai mṛgājinam|| 47 ||

vastraṃ rogaharaṃ viddhi vetrajaṃ śrīpravardhanam|
kauśeyaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ jñeyaṃ kāmbalaṃ duḥkhamocakam|| 48 ||

yathokte cāsane dhīmānṛjukāyaḥ praveśayet|
svastike caiva padmākhyaṃ saṃvidhāya vicakṣaṇaḥ|| 49 ||

jānūrvorantare samyak kṛtvā pādatale śubhe|
ṛjukāyaḥ samāsīnaḥ svastikaṃ tu mahāsanam|| 50 ||

vidhāyetthaṃ mahāprājñaḥ prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ tataḥ|
ṛṣīn ādau ca saṃsmṛtya maunī nimilitekṣaṇaḥ|| 51 ||

vidhāya pūrakaṃ kumbhaṃ recakaṃ ca tataḥ param|
triṣu sthāneṣu dhyeyaṃ vai śyāmaṃ raktaṃ tathā sitam|| 52 ||

nābhau hṛdi lalāṭe ca pūrake kumbhake tathā|
recake ca mahāprājño jñeyaṃ kramāt kramaṃ dvija|| 53 ||

aṅgeṣu sparśanaṃ kuryāt ṣaṭsu sthāneṣu mantravit|
hṛllalāte śiraskandhacakṣuṣpāṇiṣu saṃnyaset|| 54 ||

arghyaṃ dadyāt sudhīḥ pūrvaṃ sūryāya puṣpasaṃyutam|
āpohiṣṭheti mantreṇa manuṃ smaraṃstu cetasā|| 55 ||

tato mālāṃ samādāya yathoktamaṇisambhavām|
japaṃ kuryāddhiyā mantrī dhyānasthaḥ sujitendriyaḥ|| 56 ||

rudrākṣairnirmitā mālā sarvakāmaprasādhanī|
sphāṭikairnirmitā mālā sarvasiddhipradāyinī|| 57 ||

mauktikaiḥ sambhavā mālā saubhāgyaśrīprasādhanī|
mantrapratyakṣadā cānyā padmarāgodbhavā tathā|
sauvarṇī rājatī mālā sarvān kāmān prayacchati|| 58 ||

saṃkhyāṃ kuryāt tato bāhye yajjaptaṃ saphalaṃ bhavet|
asaṃkhyātaṃ ca yajjaptaṃ tat sarvaṃ niḥphalaṃ bhavet|| 59 ||

tasmādyatnena kartavyā saṃkhyā japasya dhīmatā|
tato japaṃ samarpyārghaṃ dadyāddevāya mantravit|| 60 ||

stotraṃ kuryāt tato mantrī sarvakāmārthasiddhaye|
gṛhasthānām ayaṃ dharmo yoginām anya īritaḥ|| 61 ||

gṛheṣu yaddharmakṛtaṃ sudhīraiḥ samīritaṃ taddhi gṛhasthadharmam|
pīṭhe ca tīrthe giriśekhare vai tadyogadharmaṃ varayogibhiryat|| 62 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe gṛhasthadharmaṃ nāma daśamo adhyāyaḥ|| 10 ||

skanda uvāca |

atha dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi yogināṃ ca viśeṣataḥ|
brāhme cotthāya yogīśaḥ smaran vai gurum īśvaram|| 1 ||

śaucaṃ kṛtvā tato yogī siddhakṣetre samāsane|
ṛjukāyaḥ samāsīnaḥ prāṅmukho vā udaṅmukhaḥ|| 2 ||

ekaṃ pādam athaikasmin vinyasyoruṇi saṃsthitam|
itarasmiṃstathā corvoryogāsanam udāhṛtam|| 3 ||

vibhūtiṃ ca samādāya mantrayan mantravidbudhaḥ|
tarpayecca guruṃ devam ātmānaṃ vai pralepayet|| 4 ||

brahmarandhre sadā pūrvaṃ lalāṭe ca tripuṇḍrakam|
kaṇṭhe caiva kaṭau deśe hṛdaye skandhayostathā|| 5 ||

nābhau pṛṣṭhe tathāgastya kūrparayostathāpare|
maṇibandhanayoryogī nitambakaṭideśayoḥ|| 6 ||

ābrahmarandhrapādāntaṃ yoginām āplavaṃ matam|
nābherūrdhvaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ ca viśeṣaṇam|| 7 ||

evaṃ snātvā mahāyogī rudrākṣān dhārayet tataḥ|
ātmānam ātmanā yogī dhyāyet tam īśvaraṃ param|| 8 ||

hṛtpadme vasupattrairvai karṇikāyāṃ sukeśare|
praṇavarūpam ādyantam aṅguṣṭhamātram īśvaram|| 9 ||

prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kuryāt tato yogī suniścalaḥ|
pūrayediḍayā vāyuṃ piṅgalayā ca kumbhayet|| 10 ||

recayecca tayā nūnaṃ brahmarandhraṃ suṣumṇayā|
nirālambastadā yogī paraṃ yogam avāpnuyāt|| 11 ||

snāpayenmānaseneśaṃ mānasena prapūjayet|
kṣaumaiśca mānasodbhūtairmānasādyaiśca candanaiḥ|| 12 ||

mānasotphullapuṣpaistaṃ dhūpairdīpaiśca mānasaiḥ|
naivedyairmānasotpannairmānasaiḥ pravarairjapaiḥ|| 13 ||

ṣaṇṇāṃ sthānodbhavairvarṇai rakṣagaṇaiśca mantravit|
kramavyatikramairdhīro japenmantraṃ dhiyā mune|| 14 ||

tārapūrvo namaścāntaḥ śivāyeti tataḥ param|
mumukṣuḥ prajapenmantraṃ duḥkhasaṃsāratārakam|| 15 ||

śivaśaktyā samāyuktaṃ mantraṃ ṣaḍakṣaraṃ param|
ṣaṭsvaraiḥ saṃyutaṃ bījaṃ satārakaṃ japedbudhaḥ|| 16 ||

iti yogaṃ paraṃ viddhi yogināṃ paramātmanām|
evaṃ yaḥ kurute yogī jīvanmukto na saṃśayaḥ|| 17 ||

ṣaḍṛtūnāṃ yathāyogyaṃ mānasasambhavairmune|
pūjayedupacāraistaṃ kāle kāle yathodbhavaiḥ|| 18 ||

agastya uvāca |

adbhutaṃ bhavatoktaṃ me sarveṣāṃ jīvināṃ tathā|
yogināṃ śaktidhṛk snānaṃ praśastaṃ ca vibhūtibhiḥ|| 19 ||

kasmācca tat samudbhūtaṃ phalaṃ ca kīdṛśaṃ bhavet|
bhasmasnāyī ca ko muktaḥ skanda tadvada me 'adhunā|| 20 ||

skanda uvāca |

śṛṇu kumbhaja vakṣyāmi pṛṣṭaṃ yadbhavatā hi mām|
tasya śravaṇamātreṇa bhasmasnānaphalaṃ labhet|| 21 ||

trailokyaṃ bhīmarudreṇa prakṣānalena cakṣuṣā|
yadā dagdhīkṛtaṃ kalpe tasmādbhasma pracakṣate|| 22 ||

tadbhasma ca samādāya rudreṇāṅgaṃ pralepitam|
dūrīkṛtaṃ jalasnānaṃ tasmādbhasma praśasyate|| 23 ||

devarṣiyogisiddhāśca samāplāvya ca bhasmabhiḥ|
prāpnuvanti paraṃ kṣipraṃ pūtai rudrekṣaṇodbhavaiḥ|| 24 ||

nāsti bhasmāt paraṃ snānaṃ mokṣaṃ ca bhasmanaḥ param|
nāsti bhasmāsanāt stheyaṃ nāsti bhasmārcanāt param|| 25 ||

na pāpairlipyate dhīro bhasmasnāyī śivātmakaḥ|
pātakaiḥ pañcabhiścāpi brahmahatyādibhistathā|| 26 ||

abhakṣyabhakṣako martyo bhasmasnāyī bhavedyadi|
tatpāpairlipyate naivam agamyāgamanādapi|| 27 ||

mithyākhyānodbhavaiḥ pāpairnindodbhavaiśca vācanaiḥ|
asatyairmarmasaṃspṛgbhirninhavaiḥ sa na lipyate|| 28 ||

āsīt kaściddvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sarvavidyāsu pāragaḥ|
viṣṇubhakta iti khyātaścāntarvedipurottame|| 29 ||

ṣaṭkarmanirato vipro vedapāṭhe hi tatparaḥ|
satyaśīlastapaḥkliṣṭo dāntaśca sarvajantuṣu|| 30 ||

havyakavyakriyācārāt kṛtavānarcane rataḥ|
dānaśīlo 'abhavacchaśvadatithīṃśca priyaṃkaraḥ|| 31 ||

tasya putro dvijaśreṣṭho viṣṇudāsa iti śrutaḥ|
vidyāhīno mahatkaṣṭī pañcatve ca pitaryabhūt|| 32 ||

sarvācāraḥ sadā lokaiḥ sarvabhakṣī viḍambanaḥ|
parayoṣitpriyo 'ajasraṃ paradravyāpahārakaḥ|| 33 ||

niśācāro divāsupto veśyāgamanatatparaḥ|
sarvajanaiḥ sagotraiśca vivarjito ghaṭodbhava|| 34 ||

mlecchaḥ śaṭho mṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ vāgmatīsutaṭe mune|
tatpuṇyato 'abhavadvipra śrotriyaḥ karmanindakaḥ|| 35 ||

ekadā divase vipro bahukṣudhāprapīḍitaḥ|
bāhyadeśe 'api cauryeṇa kutrāpyannam alabdhavān|| 36 ||

yācitavāṃstadā rātrau bhāryāṃ pratyaśanaṃ dvijaḥ|
paribhramya niśāyāṃ sa deśaṃ grāmaṃ gṛhaṃ prati|| 37 ||

viṣṇudāsa uvāca |

priye he sutape sādhvi dehyannaṃ me ca sāmpratam|
tīkṣṇakṣudhānalārto 'ahaṃ yena jīvaṃ pradhāraye|| 38 ||

vātyābhyantaram āgāraṃ bhramitaṃ bahu rāṣṭrakam|
kutrāpyannaṃ na labdhaṃ ca pariśramāturaḥ priye|| 39 ||

sumukhyuvāca |

satyam uktaṃ priyenādya pīḍito 'asi kṣudhānalaiḥ|
bhraman pariśramādduḥkhī prabho tvaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ|| 40 ||

mayā sahodayāpyadya nānnaṃ bhuktaṃ śape priya|
nāsti kim annam āgāre kiṃ dāsye te kṣamasva me|| 41 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya vaco vipraḥ sutathyam apyatathyabhāk|
bhāryayā madhuroktāyāḥ krodhena mūrchito bhṛśam|| 42 ||

kṣudhā prapīḍitaḥ krodhī bhāryāṃ madhurabhāṣiṇīm|
kukṣim uddiśya pādena bhartsayaṃśca jaghāna tām|| 43 ||

mṛtāṃ bhāryāṃ sagarbhāṃ tāṃ gṛhe tyaktvā ca sāmpratam|
niryayau sa puradvārāt pāpiṣṭhaśca tato bahiḥ|| 44 ||

bhramati sma tato bhraṣṭo deśāddeśāntaraṃ bahu|
taskaravṛttim āsthāya kaṃcidabdaṃ ca nītavān|| 45 ||

ekadā nagare pāpī kṛtavān steyam arthakam|
dhṛtvā lokāḥ prabandhyāśu tāḍayanti sma taṃ bahu|| 46 ||

tato rātrau pramucyāśu daśanai rajjukaṃ rahaḥ|
pradudrāva bahiḥ pāpī sthānaṃ cintitavān vane|| 47 ||

tato vaneṣu pāpiṣṭha uvāsa sa nirantaram|
nihatya pathikāṃstatra kāṃścinmāsān nināya saḥ|| 48 ||

alabdhvaikadine martyān gāṃ caiva hatavān punaḥ|
anivedya ca paitre tanmāṃsaṃ jaghāsa pāpavān|| 49 ||

bhramati sma tataḥ pāpī unmattavadvanādvanam|
kṣudhānalakṛśāṅgaśca tṛṣāturaśca kuṣṭhavān|| 50 ||

tata ekākinaṃ vipraṃ pathi yāntaṃ dadarśa saḥ|
bhikṣārthinaṃ mahādīnaṃ niḥsvaṃ tathaikavāsasam|| 51 ||

dūrācchareṇa pāpiṣṭho jaghāna pathikaṃ vane|
hatvā tatastadaṃṣuṅge anveṣayan vasūni ca|| 52 ||

bhraṣṭaḥ kṛtvā kim astīti kim apyadarśitaṃ vasu|
tato dadarśa rudrākṣaṃ mūrdhanyekādaśānanam|| 53 ||

taṃ samādāya rudrākṣaṃ svamūrdhni ca babandha saḥ|
pātakaiḥ pañcabhiryukta unmattavadbhraman mahīm|| 54 ||

tato 'agamaddhimādreḥ sa sānau girivilaṅghitaḥ|
tatra kuśeśvaro liṅgaḥ svayambhūstejasāṃ paraḥ|| 55 ||

tatra pravahatī svacchā kauśikī ca saridvarā|
saṃgame indravatyāśca ādiliṅgo virājate|| 56 ||

prāptavān kauśikītīram abhramya sa vanādvanam|
pañcapāpairniṣedhātmā kuṣṭhavraṇī savepathuḥ|| 57 ||

taddadarśa mahāliṅgaṃ pūjitaṃ muninā mudā|
phalamūlopahāraiśca saha pañcopacārakaiḥ|| 58 ||

tapo 'asite mune pakṣe trayodaśyāṃ mahāniśi|
ṛṣiṇā kuśanāmnā vai vinidreṇa ca pūjitam|| 59 ||

tatra sa cintayāmāsa steyī tam upacārakam|
kathaṃ gṛhṇāmi bhakṣyāṃstāṃstatrāhaṃ bhojanāya ca|| 60 ||

ekākī snātakastatra caikākinaṃ hi māṃ tathā|
tāḍiṣyati sakopaṃ cet sahyo bhokṣyāmi tān balāt|| 61 ||

kṣudhayā pīḍitaṃ māṃ ca tāḍiṣyati bhṛśaṃ yadi|
dīnaṃ prekṣyātha vā nāsau na mokṣyāmi tathā ca tān|| 62 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ vimṛṣyamāṇo 'asau bhraṣṭaḥ svāntena kumbhaja|
vepamānaḥ kṛśāṅgaśca abhyagamat tadantikam|| 63 ||

dhyātavati munau rātrau japacintāparāyaṇe|
liṅgāntikaṃ śanairgatvā sa jahāra balīn balāt|| 64 ||

tato munerbhayādbhraṣṭaḥ kampayukto vyaloḍayat|
liṅgopari lalāṭaṃ tadgharṣitavāṃstadā dvijaḥ|| 65 ||

liṅgasparśena tadbhāle tadvibhūtyā pralepitaḥ|
śanairutthāya kampātmā bhayākulaḥ suvihvalaḥ|| 66 ||

saṃsparśya maṇibandhābhyāṃ liṅgādbhasmāṅkitau karau|
balīn ānīya pāpiṣṭho bahirāgatya bhuktavān|| 67 ||

śivakṣetraparoddeśe saṃsthitāḥ pañcapātakāḥ|
samprekṣya tādṛśaṃ taṃ ca vañcayituṃ samāvrajan|| 68 ||

tataste māyayā divyaṃ cānnaṃ bahurasaṃ ca tam|
lobhayituṃ ca saṃdarśya tam ārūḍhā yayatnire|| 69 ||

pāpā ūcuḥ |

re re bhraṣṭādhunā tubhyaṃ divyam annam idam varam|
samānītam ihāsmābhistvatsnehācca prapaśyatām|| 70 ||

kṣudhayā pīḍito vipra kṛśāṅgī ca vraṇī tathā|
te sahāyā bhavāmo vai jñātvānītam iti dhruvam|| 71 ||

kuru snānaṃ jale vipra lalāṭe bhasma dhautya ca|
tvacchiraḥsthaṃ ca rudrākṣaṃ prakṣipyatāṃ jale 'adhunā|| 72 ||

kṛtvaivaṃ vipra śaucaṃ tvaṃ bhasmarudrākṣavarjitaḥ|
bhuṅkṣva yathepsitaṃ cānnaṃ priyasakhe gṛhāṇa vai|| 73 ||

bhraṣṭa uvāca |

nāhaṃ bhuñjāmi cādyānnaṃ yadi caturvidhaṃ varam|
samānītaṃ ca yuṣmābhirmatsnehādapi bhoḥ sakhāḥ|| 74 ||

phalāsanaṃ mayānītaṃ nānāvidharasottamam|
bhūteśvaraprasādaṃ tadṛṣeranugrahāt tathā|| 75 ||

vraṇī kampī kṛśāṅgī ca nāhaṃ snātuṃ ca śaktavān|
na tyajāmi ca rudrākṣaṃ bhasma dhautaṃ na śaktavān|| 76 ||

rātrau bhuktaṃ sukhaṃ pūrṇam atastṛptaḥ phalāni tat|
śvo yaddadāti bhūteśo bhokṣyāmi tanna saṃśayaḥ|| 77 ||

skanda uvāca |

bhasmarudrākṣasaṃsparśācchivaliṅgaṃ tathā hi saḥ|
niṣpāpo jñānavān bhraṣṭaḥ śaṃkarātmā babhūva hi|| 78 ||

tataḥ śrutva vacastasya nirāśāste pracakrame|
tasmin sthātuṃ mune bhraṣṭe na śekuḥ sparśituṃ ca tam|| 79 ||

bhasmeśākṣakam aṅgeṣu prekṣya bhraṣṭasya pātakāḥ|
tatraiva bhuvi saṃlīnā babhūvuste bhayākulāḥ|| 80 ||

tataḥ so 'api dvijo bhraṣṭaḥ pañcatvaṃ prāptavān niśi|
kauśikītīram āsādya bahuśītaiḥ prapīḍitaḥ|| 81 ||

tatkṣaṇe yamadūtāste himālayādrigahvare|
samāgatāstam ānetuṃ babandhuu rajjubhistataḥ|| 82 ||

tatraiva śivadūtāśca samāyayuśca tatkṣaṇe|
sūryāyutapratīkāśe vimāne samadhiṣṭhitāḥ|| 83 ||

garhayan yamadūtāṃste protkṣipya rajjum āśu tat|
rudrakanyānvite yāne taṃ samāropayan mudā|| 84 ||

āropitaṃ vimāne taṃ śivadūtaiḥ suniścitam|
gaṇā ninyurhi taṃ śaivaṃ yānena sūryavarcasā|| 85 ||

saṃtyajya vigrahaṃ sadyaḥ paraṃ mokṣaṃ sa labdhavān|
prekṣya teṣāṃ ca ceṣṭāṃ te cintayanti sma duḥkhitāḥ|| 86 ||

tata uvāca kālo 'asau tebhyo hi yamakiṃkarāḥ|
vimarṣyādau mitho vipra jñātvā śivabalānvitān|| 87 ||

kāla uvāca |

bho bhoḥ śivaparā bhaktā enaṃ nārakiṇaṃ dvijam|
katham āropitaṃ yāne yuṣmābhiravivekayan|| 88 ||

pātakaiḥ pañcabhirgrastaṃ bhraṣṭaṃ svācārajātitaḥ|
goghnaṃ brahmahaṇaṃ strīghnaṃ bālaghnaṃ narahaṃ tathā|| 89 ||

anena na kṛtaṃ snānaṃ japapūjādikaṃ tathā|
dānaṃ śaucaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ satkarma ca kriyā vibho|| 90 ||

itthaṃ pāpāṅkitaṃ bhraṣṭaṃ yāne svāropitaṃ śubhe|
vihāya nārakaṃ tasmai yātanā duḥsahaṃ vibho|| 91 ||

ādiṣṭāścitraguptena vayam atra samāgatāḥ|
ānīya taṃ dvijaṃ bhraṣṭaṃ kṣipyatāṃ narakeṣu ca|| 92 ||

iti ādeśaṃ samādāya prabhuṇā preritā vayam|
atrāgatāḥ śivātmaṃste kiṃ kurvāmaśca kiṃkarāḥ|| 93 ||

śivadūtā ūcuḥ |

na vaktavyaṃ ca yuṣmābhiḥ kutsitam asya ceṣṭitam|
dūrīkṛtāśca tatpāpā īśvareṇa hi sarvataḥ|| 94 ||

anekabahupāpāni kṛtaṃ yadyapi sarvadā|
niṣpāpo 'asau bhavadyāmyāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ tasya hetukam|| 95 ||

anena sparśitaṃ liṅgam enaṃ kuśeśvaraṃ param|
hastābhyāṃ śirasā vatsā ajñānato 'api pūyate|| 96 ||

anena dhāritaṃ mūrdhni rudrākṣaṃ ca nirantaram|
lalāṭe hi vibhūtiṃ ca tasyāṅge taddhi paśyatām|| 97 ||

ājñā dattā śivenāśu mahyaṃ loke mama dhruvam|
bhraṣṭaścānīyatāṃ ceti vayam atrāgatā ataḥ|| 98 ||

idānīṃ nīyate 'asmābhiḥ śivalokam ayaṃ dvijaḥ|
yūyaṃ gacchata yāmyaṃ ca mā dūyantāṃ yathāgatāḥ|| 99 ||

skanda uvāca |

ityuktvā śivadūtāste yāmyebhyaḥ khalu sāmpratam|
tam āsthāya vimāne hi codayadyānavāhanān|| 100 ||

sūryāyutapratīkāśe kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍite|
gītavādyaravopete bhraṣṭo yāne virājate|| 101 ||

rudrakanyākaroddhūtaiścāmaraiḥ sa niṣevyate|
gandharvaiḥ sevakairbhraṣṭa upahāraiḥ prapūjitaḥ|| 102 ||

tato 'agamadvimānena bhraṣṭaścoddhṛtaduṣkṛtaḥ|
sarvalokān samālokya devānāṃ śivalokakam|| 103 ||

sarvalokoṣitān devān sādhu sādhviti vādayan|
mudā yukto 'agamacchaivaṃ dvitīya iva śaṃkaraḥ|| 104 ||

tatra śivapure divye sarvasukhānvite pare|
yugakoṭisahasrāṇi bhraṣṭo gaṇairmahīyate|| 105 ||

tato bhraṣṭaśca medinyāṃ janitaḥ sa mahīpatiḥ|
jambūdvīpe dvijaśreṣṭha sārvabhaumo hyabhūdasau|| 106 ||

tato bhraṣṭaḥ sa medinyāṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān|
devarājastvabhūdbhūyastyaktvā svaṃ ca kalevaram|| 107 ||

himavati vare śaile taporjitaphalottame|
ityetat kathitaṃ dhīman viṣṇudāsena yat kṛtam|| 108 ||

bhūyo vakṣye vibhūtīnāṃ phalottamaṃ viśeṣataḥ|
bhasmasnānayutaṃ vipra jalasnānanivāraṇam|| 109 ||

jalena bhasmanā snānam antaraṃ bahu cāntaram|
sarvatīrthamayaṃ bhasma sarvadevamayaḥ śivaḥ|| 110 ||

bhasmasnāyī ca rudrākṣī sa rudro nātra saṃśayaḥ|
bhasmasnāyī ca rudrākṣī rudrajāpī viśeṣataḥ|
na paśyati tathā yāmyaṃ paraṃ prāpnoti bhāvataḥ|| 111 ||

sarvatīrtheṣu yat puṇyaṃ sarvayajñeṣu yat phalam|
bhasmasnānācca rudrākṣī śivamantrasamāyutaḥ|
tat phalaṃ labhate amntrī rudrākṣadhāraṇāt kila|| 112 ||

sarvadāneṣu yat puṇyaṃ sarvadharmeṣu yat phalam|
bhāle tripuṇḍrakaṃ kṛtvā śivadhyānasamāhitaḥ|| 113 ||

rudrākṣān dhārayeddhīmān sthāne sthāne vicakṣaṇaḥ|
śikhāyāṃ keśavṛnde ca grīvāyāṃ caiva hastayoḥ|| 114 ||

prakoṣṭe kurpare dve ca maṇibandhe tathāpare|
vakṣasi karṇayordhīmān sa rudras nātra saṃśayaḥ|
agamyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ draṣṭuṃ ca hiṃsituṃ kutaḥ|| 115 ||

te varṇitaṃ bhasmavidhāraṇasya rudrākṣasaṃdhāraṇataśca yat phalam|
atyadbhutaṃ kumbhaja vipra bhūyaḥ kim icchasi tvaṃ hi paraṃ paraṃtapa|| 116 ||

te varṇitaṃ bhasmavidhāraṇasya ajñānato yaccaritaṃ mayā vai|
stokaṃ namerośca phalottamānāṃ śrotuṃ punarvāñchasi kiṃ dvije 'adya|| 117 ||

agastya uvāca |

rudrākṣāṇāṃ mahat puṇyaṃ bhavatoktaṃ ca me vibho|
tuṣṭo 'ahaṃ śravaṇāt tasya atyadbhutaṃ paraṃtapa|| 118 ||

ko devaḥ kīdṛśaṃ rūpaṃ kati phalaṃ ca dhāraṇāt|
kathaṃ saṃtuṣṭavān rudro rudrākṣeṇa vada prabho|| 119 ||

skanda uvāca |

yaduktaṃ me purāgastya śaṃkareṇācale hi me|
rudrākṣāṇāṃ phalaṃ caiva rūpaṃ teṣāṃ yathāvidhi|| 120 ||

manmūrtayo hi rudrākṣāścaturvargaphalapradāḥ|
yaduktam eva rudreṇa tat sarvaṃ vacmi te śṛṇu|| 121 ||

pādapānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ nameruruttamo bhavet|
tatphalāni ca jānīhi rudrākṣān rudravigrahān|| 122 ||

saṃsārapādapeśānaḥ saṃphalati ca bhūrasān|
lokoddhāraṇahetūṃstāṃstathaiva tanmayaṃ jagat|| 123 ||

devādayo narāḥ sarve dhāraṇādrudravigrahāḥ|
yaṃ yam icchanti te 'agastya prāpnuvanti na saṃśayaḥ|| 124 ||

rudrākṣaṃ mokṣadaṃ viddhi śrīsādhanaṃ ca kāmadam|
rudrākṣaṃ pāpadāhaṃ ca duḥkhadāridyaghātakam|| 125 ||

haste pramāṇabandhena rudrākṣān mokṣam āpnuyāt|
bhuktimuktipradaṃ sākṣāt sa rudro nātra saṃśayaḥ|| 126 ||

śirasā dhāraṇāddhīmān koṭiguṇaṃ phalaṃ labhet|
karṇayordaśakoṭiḥ syāt kaṇṭhe koṭisahasraśaḥ|| 127 ||

anantaṃ syācchikhāyāṃ ca tathaiva bāhumūlayoḥ|
vakṣasi daśalakṣaṃ syādaṅgeṣu dhāraṇāt phalam|| 128 ||

japadhyānavihīno 'api rudrākṣaṃ dhārayan dvijaḥ|
devānām asurāṇāṃ ca vandanīyo yatheśvaraḥ|| 129 ||

sarvapāpairvinirmuktaḥ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim|
anyāsāṃ caiva mālānāṃ daśaguṇaṃ japāllabhet|| 130 ||

karasthacālanāccaiva sahasraṃ manusaṃyutān|
triśūnyaṃ manujaptena sahasreṇaiva lakṣakam|| 131 ||

lakṣajaptena koṭiḥ syāt koṭijaptena sarvadṛk|
koṭikoṭiguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ rudrākṣamālayā tataḥ|| 132 ||

vācikena tathā caivam upāṃśunā punardvija|
cetasā ca mahāprājña koṭikoṭiguṇaṃ labhet|| 133 ||

dhyānayogena cittena anantaṃ phalam āpnuyāt|
vaktrāṇāṃ ca phalaṃ vacmi rudrākṣāṇāṃ pṛthak pṛthak|| 134 ||

ekavaktraḥ śivaḥ sākṣādbrahmahatyāṃ vyapohati|
dvivaktro devadevo 'asau gohatyāṃ nāśayeddhruvam|| 135 ||

trivaktraścāgnirūpaḥ syāt strīhatyāṃ harate kṣaṇāt|
caturvaktraḥ svayaṃ brahmā narahatyāṃ vyapohati|| 136 ||

pañcavaktrastathā rudraḥ kālāgnirnāma bhīṣaṇaḥ|
pañcavaktrasya māhātmyaṃ śṛṇu mune samāhitaḥ|| 137 ||

agamyagamanāccaiva abhakṣyabhakṣaṇāt tathā|
adṛśyadarśanāccaiva avācyabhāṣaṇāt tataḥ|
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ pañcavaktrasya dhāraṇāt|| 138 ||

ṣaḍvaktro mama mūrtiḥ syāddhāraṇāt sarvadā mune|
dakṣiṇe hastamūle ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate|| 139 ||

saṃgrāme jayam āpnoti mucyate pātakairbhayaiḥ|
ṣaḍvaktraḥ karayoḥ kaṇṭhe dhāraṇācca phalaṃ śṛṇu|
avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ rudravadvicaredbhuvi|| 140 ||

saptavaktraśca rudrākṣo hyananto nāma nāgarāṭ|
taddhāraṇena saubhāgyaḥ suvarṇāḍhyaḥ sukhī bhavet|
ripunāśastathārogī balavān vigatajvaraḥ|| 141 ||

rudrākṣo 'aṣṭānano devaḥ śūlapāṇiśca nāmataḥ|
tasyāṣṭāsyasya māhātmyam avadhāraya kumbhaja|
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ dhāraṇācca svayaṃ samaḥ|| 142 ||

navavaktraśca rudrākṣo devo 'asau bhairavo mune|
dhārayedvāmahastena atulaṃ balavān bhavet|| 143 ||

navagrahaistathā bhūtaiḥ piśācairḍākinīgaṇaiḥ|
anyaiśca vividhairdevairna bādhyate kadāpi ca|| 144 ||

lakṣakoṭisahasrāṇi pañcahatyāṃ karoti yaḥ|
vinaśyati hi tat sarvaṃ navavaktrasya dhāraṇāt|| 145 ||

rudrākṣo daśavaktro 'asau svayaṃ devo janārdanaḥ|
taddhāraṇānmahāprājña vakṣyāmi tat phalaṃ śṛṇu|| 146 ||

grahāḥ sarve piśācāśca vetālā brahmarākṣasāḥ|
pannagāśca vinaśyanti daśavaktrasya dhāraṇāt|| 147 ||

ekādaśāsyarudrākṣam aṃśairekādaśairmune|
īśvarasya samāyuktaḥ śambhurnāma mahāvibhuḥ|| 148 ||

śikhāyāṃ dhārayennityaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu|
aśvamedhasahasrāṇi vājapeyaśatāni ca|
tat phalaṃ labhate nityaṃ tadrudrākṣasya dhāraṇāt|| 149 ||

dvādaśāsyaśca rudrākṣaḥ sūryo nāma mahādyutiḥ|
saṃyukto dvādaśairaṃśairādityasya ghaṭodbhava|| 150 ||

taddhāraṇānmahātejā bhaveccaiva nirantaram|
keśānte dhāraṇānnityaṃ sūryatulyo na saṃśayaḥ|| 151 ||

na pīḍyate mahāghorairādityādinavagrahaiḥ|
gomedhasya vratānāṃ ca yat phalaṃ parikīrtitam|| 152 ||

yat phalam upavāsānāṃ tat phalaṃ labhate dhruvam|
pīḍābhirmucyate rogī saubhāgyaṃ yāti durbhagaḥ|| 153 ||

trayodaśāsyarudrākṣaḥ kāmadevo hi nāmataḥ|
kaṇṭhe ca dhāryate yena sa rudro nātra saṃśayaḥ|| 154 ||

dvitīyaḥ kāmadevo 'asau strīṇāṃ saṃkṣobhako bhavet|
sarvakāmam avāpnoti sarvasaubhāgyasampadam|
sarvakāryaṃ ca siddhiṃ ca bhāgyahīno 'api saṃlabhet|| 155 ||

caturdaśyāsyarudrākṣaḥ paraṃbrahma sanātanam|
dhārayet satataṃ mūrdhni sarvatejomayaṃ vibhum|| 156 ||

mūrtiścaturdaśānāṃ ca bhuvanānāṃ na saṃśayaḥ|
tasmāccaturdaśo vaktraḥ sarveṣām uttamaḥ smṛtaḥ|| 157 ||

dhāryate yaiśca rudrākṣaṃ caturdaśānanaṃ tathā|
mūrdhni tena dhṛtaṃ sarvaṃ bhuvanānāṃ caturdaśa|| 158 ||

yāvatyo mūrtayaḥ santi pātālatridivaukasām|
sthāvaraṃ jīvitānāṃ syāt tāvatyo rudramūrtayaḥ|
tāvatyo mūrtayaḥ sarvāstiṣṭhanti bhuvaneṣu ca|| 159 ||

tatrudrākṣo dhṛto yena tena dhṛto hi māṃ mune|
yena dhṛtaṃ sadā mūrdhni caturdaśānanaṃ vibhum|| 160 ||

pravakṣyāmi ca te snehāt tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu|
sarvasiddhiśca taddhaste tiṣṭhati ca nirantaram|| 161 ||

mahatkaṣṭena tallabhyaṃ siddho bhavet tathāparaḥ|
sarvapāpaharo nityaṃ mahatpuṇyena labhyate|| 162 ||

tadrudrākṣo dhṛto yena pātakaiśca na lipyate|
medinyāṃ yāni dattāni mahādānāni sarvaśaḥ|| 163 ||

prāpnoti tat phalaṃ martyastadrudrākṣasya dhāraṇāt|
sarvatīrtheṣu yat puṇyaṃ sarvayajñeṣu yat phalam|| 164 ||

pūjopavāsadharmeṣu tat phalaṃ labhate 'aniśam|
devavanmānuṣo bhūtvā bhunakti sakalaṃ sukham|
sarvakāmāṃściraṃ bhuktvā gacchati paramaṃ padam|| 165 ||

pañcadaśānanādīnāṃ rudrākṣāṇāṃ ca dhāraṇāt|
sādhāraṇaphalaṃ jñeyaṃ mālodbhavaṃ yathorasi|| 166 ||

ityetat kathitaṃ te vai yaduktaṃ giriśena me|
rudrākṣāṇāṃ phalāni ārya saṃsāratāraṇāni ca|| 167 ||

devāśca pūrvaṃ himavadgirau hi tapaḥ pracakruḥ sukaṭhorapuṇyam|
rudrākṣabhasmāni vidhāya kāye prāpuśca dikpālavarān maheśāt|| 168 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe vibhūtirudrākṣamāhātmyaṃ nāmaikādaśo adhyāyaḥ|| 11 ||

agastya uvāca |

devadevātmaja skanda tvatprasādācchrutaṃ mayā|
anuṣṭhānaṃ dvijātīnāṃ bhūtirudrākṣayostathā|| 1 ||

idānīṃ śrotum icchāmi tvatto brahmavidāṃ varāt|
himavato mahādreśca śṛṅgeṣu sumahatsu ca|| 2 ||

ke gīrvāṇāstapaścakrurvada me lokaśaṃkara|
nāmadheyaṃ ca śṛṅgānāṃ tīrthānāṃ ca viśeṣaṇam|| 3 ||

yeṣu snātvā phalāni āśu labdhavantaḥ surottamāḥ|
teṣāṃ nāma ca tīrthānāṃ vada me deva sarvaśaḥ|| 4 ||

skanda uvāca |

āsīt pūrvaṃ mahātejāḥ kaśyapo nāma satyavāk|
devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ trividhānāṃ pitāmahaḥ|| 5 ||

satyavādī sadā dānto medhāvī suvicakṣaṇaḥ|
samadṛṣṭiśca bhūteṣu sarvaśāstreṣu pāragaḥ|| 6 ||

śivārcane rato nityaṃ śivamantraparāyaṇaḥ|
nirvikāraḥ sadānandaḥ śivadhyāne ca tatparaḥ|| 7 ||

ukteṣvaṅgeṣu rudrākṣān dadhāno bhūtilepanam|
nityaṃ deheṣu bhāleṣu tripuṇḍrakaṃ dadhāra vai|| 8 ||

tasyātmajo mahātejāḥ śakro nāma ghaṭodbhava|
tīkṣṇabuddhirmahāprājñaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ|| 9 ||

kaścitkāle mahatkṣetre sarvatīrthottamottame|
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye pāvane lokapāvane|| 10 ||

aśvamedhaśataṃ śakraḥ sāṅgaṃ pūrṇaṃ cakāra vai|
vedavedāṅgatattvajñairṛṣibhiḥ sapurohitaiḥ|| 11 ||

yajñāṅgairvividhaiḥ sārdhaṃ havyakavyaiśca pūjanaiḥ|
viprān sambhojayan nityaṃ dadau haimān sadakṣiṇān|| 12 ||

saṃtuṣṭāśca tato viprā devāścaiva tathāvidhāḥ|
tato yajñāvasāne vai abhiṣekaṃ daduḥ surāḥ|| 13 ||

tasmai mahātmane siddhā hotāra ṛṣayastathā|
rājatvam amarāvatyāḥ śakraṃ cakrustataśca te|| 14 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

adyaprabhṛti cāsmākaṃ rājatvaṃ bhavatu prabho|
nāke hartā ca kartā tvaṃ dātā tvaṃ rakṣako hi naḥ|
hantā śāstā ca śatrūṇāṃ naḥ pāpako 'aniśaṃ prabhuḥ|| 15 ||

śakra uvāca |

anugrahaḥ kṛto mahyaṃ bhavadbhiśca surottamaiḥ|
ṛṣibhiśca tathā mānyān yuṣmānadya prapūjaye|| 16 ||

skanda uvāca |

tataḥ śakro munīn devān ānarca vividhārhaṇaiḥ|
stavairbahuvidhairviprānatithīṃśca pradakṣiṇaiḥ|| 17 ||

bṛhaspatistadā prājña avadat tān prati dhruvam|
ādāya vidhivat pūjāṃ sabhāmadhye bhaviṣyati|| 18 ||

bṛhaspatiruvāca |

bho bho devāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ me vacanaṃ tathyabhāṣaṇam|
na sthātavyaṃ ciraṃ cātra tyaktvā svargaṃ divaukasaḥ|| 19 ||

asmi/lloke 'amarāḥ śaśvadbahavaḥ santyupadravāḥ|
svargasthānepsayā loko 'avaśyaṃ copadraviṣyati|| 20 ||

devala uvāca |

aho ṛtaṃ gurorvākyaṃ sattvānāṃ ca hitoditam|
yaduktaṃ guruṇā tathyaṃ yuṣmākaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ|| 21 ||

gacchadhvaṃ tridaśā yūyam atyājyastridivaḥ khalu|
tadvākyaṃ na bhavenmithyā api tadvelayoditam|| 22 ||

skanda uvāca |

jīvadevalayorvākyaṃ tathyaṃ kṛtvāmarāstadā|
gantuṃ pracakrire nākaṃ purodhāyāśu kāśyapam|| 23 ||

tatkāle tejasāṃ puñjo 'antarikṣāduvāca ca|
prasthitānāṃ ca tacceṣṭāṃ samprekṣya tridivaṃ prati|| 24 ||

jyotirūpa uvāca |

mā nīyatāṃ surāḥ śakrastapohīnaṃ tripiṣṭapam|
na labhyate divaḥ pūjyaṃ tapobhiḥ kaṭhinairvinā|| 25 ||

asti cedamarāvatyāṃ kartuṃ rājye sukhottamam|
tapyatāṃ pratapaḥ śakra himavacchikharottame|| 26 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya mahāvākyaṃ sutejorūpiṇo vibhoḥ|
citreṇa manasā śakraḥ samadrākṣīdgurormukham|| 27 ||

guruṇokte ṛte vākye namaskṛtya guruṃ śivam|
tapaḥ kartuṃ yayau śakro himavacchikharottame|| 28 ||

prācīṃ diśaṃ samāgatya darbhavati śiloccaye|
tapaścakāra śakro vai trividhaiḥ susamāhitaḥ|| 29 ||

agastya uvāca |

pītvāhaṃ lālasībhūtastvanmukhāmbhojaniḥsṛtām|
sudhām anupamāṃ pātuṃ mādhuryaiḥ preritaḥ punaḥ|| 30 ||

viśākha vidhinā kena prakāreṇa himācale|
tapaścakre tadā śakro vada me tadyathāvidhi|| 31 ||

skanda uvāca |

brahmaputro nadaḥ śreṣṭha āryā nāma parā nadī|
tayośca saṃgame tīrthaṃ śakrasyodāhṛtaṃ mune|| 32 ||

gaṅgāyāṃ śatadhā snātvā dattvā dāyāṃstathaiva ca|
sakṛdyaḥ snāyate tatra sa śakro nātra saṃśayaḥ|| 33 ||

bhādrakṛṣṇatrayodaśyāṃ pūrvabhādrarkṣasaṃyute|
gurormantropadiṣṭo 'asau himādriṃ prayayau mudā|| 34 ||

kuśodakaṃ samādāya dhautāsyāṅghrikaro hi saḥ|
tiṅsubantacayairvākyaiḥ saṃkalpate 'adyapūrvataḥ|| 35 ||

sasnau śakro mahattīrthe hṛdepsitaprade śubhe|
vilipya bhasmanā gātram āpādatalamastakam|| 36 ||

rudrākṣāṃśca dadhāno 'asau yukte sthāne tathāvidhān|
tripuṇḍrakaṃ lalāṭe ca kṛtvā śakraḥ surottamaḥ|| 37 ||

dadau dānāni viprebhya ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ|
āruroha tataḥ śakro ratnakoṭiṃ himācalam|| 38 ||

himaiḥ prabhūṣite kūṭe babandhāsanam ādṛtaḥ|
padmarāgamayaṃ liṅgaṃ saṃsthāpya vidhivadvṛṣāḥ|| 39 ||

divyāsanaṃ samāsīno bhaktyārcanairapūpujat|
tato gandhaiḥ prasūnaiśca dhūpairdīpairbalī varaiḥ|| 40 ||

bhūtvā sunirjanaḥ śakro 'aṣṭaparvasu caiva hi|
samutsṛjya ca ṣaḍvargān prasannavadanaḥ śuciḥ|
mohakañcukam utsṛjya jñānakañcukasaṃvṛtaḥ|| 41 ||

pūrvoktayogam āsthāya sarvaṃ mānasasambhavam|
tapaścakāra yogīśo yogadharmaṃ samāśritaḥ|| 42 ||

dhyātvā jyotiḥparaṃ rudraṃ liṅgaṃ svātmani cātmanā|
divyavarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ śakro manuṃ jajāpa hi|| 43 ||

tato varṣaśatānte tadbhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ|
āvirbabhūva deveśaḥ sarvatejomayo vibhuḥ|| 44 ||

varaṃ dātuṃ tato liṅgādvyaktīkṛtya kalevaram|
sudṛṣṭavāṃstam ālokya japantaṃ nirjanaṃ mudā|| 45 ||

dadarśa bhagavantaṃ sa devaṃ tribhuvaneśvaram|
vyaktarūpaṃ mahādevaṃ sarvatejomayaṃ śivam|| 46 ||

trinetraṃ dvikaraṃ śāntaṃ muṇḍamālāvibhūṣitam|
khaṭvāṅgaṃ ca triśūlaṃ ca pradadhānaṃ vibhuṃ mune|| 47 ||

devyāliṅganahastābjam ajaṃ guhyajanārcitam|
nāgabhūṣaṇabhūṣāḍhyam īṣatprahasitānanam|| 48 ||

gaṅgojjvalajaṭāśīrṣaṃ śakalenduvibhūṣaṇam|
candrānanaṃ śivaṃ saumyaṃ bhūtibhūṣaṇadehakam|| 49 ||

taṃ parikramya hṛṣṭo 'asau daṇḍavannamya śūlinam|
stutiṃ cakre tadā bhaktyā vākkāyamānasairmudā|| 50 ||

śakra uvāca |

.o, |

namastriśūlahastāya rudrāya paramātmane|
sṛṣṭisthitivināśāya kapāline namo namaḥ|| 51 ||

brahmāṇḍabhāṇḍarūpāya jagaddhātre mahātmane|
vibhūtibhūṣitāṅgāya trilocana namo 'astu te|| 52 ||

khaṭvāṅgadhāriṇe tubhyaṃ kapālamāline mṛḍa|
śipiviṣṭāya bhīmāya vyomakeśa namo 'astu te|| 53 ||

bhaktavatsalarūpāya śāntāya śāntirūpiṇe|
ātmane deharūpāya cakṣurūpa namo 'astu te|| 54 ||

ghrāṇasthāya ca nāsāya śrotrasthāya ca vāyave|
jihvāya rasarūpāya kaṇṭharūpa namo 'astu te|| 55 ||

nābhisthāya samīrāya prāṇāpānasvarūpiṇe|
samānodānarūpāya vyāpine janmine namaḥ|| 56 ||

jaṭharasyāgnirūpāya agnirūpāya śambhave|
bhoktre ca bhojyarūpāya poṣakartre namo namaḥ|| 57 ||

prajñāya cittarūpāya mānasāya bhayāya ca|
krodhāya māṃsine 'ajāya parameśa namo 'astu te|| 58 ||

caitanyāya ca jīvāya māyāsvarūpiṇe hara|
parāparātmarūpāya parātītāya te namaḥ|| 59 ||

alakṣāya ca lakṣāya bhāvarūpāya bhāvine|
bhaktavatsalamātā tvam aṣṭaiśvaryapitā bhavān|| 60 ||

kṣāntavyaṃ mama nātheśa sarvabhūtahite rata|
aparādhasahasrāṇi durātmāno hyajānataḥ|| 61 ||

skanda uvāca |

ākarṇyeti stavaṃ divyaṃ prahṛṣṭavān maheśvaraḥ|
saṃstutaḥ kila śakreṇa trividhairbhaktipūrvakam|| 62 ||

tapasthāya ca śakrāya prekṣya cograṃ ca tattapaḥ|
varaṃ dātuṃ tadā rudra uvāca vacanaṃ mune|| 63 ||

śrīśvara uvāca |

aho vatsa tvayā taptaṃ suduścaraṃ mahātapaḥ|
amānuṣyam idaṃ karma svātmoddhāraṇahetukam|| 64 ||

ato darśayituṃ tvaṃ ca vyaktarūpaṃ himācale|
kevalaṃ ca prasīdāmi himādrau yat phalaṃ viduḥ|| 65 ||

varaṃ varaya dharmajña yat tvaṃ vāñchasi sāmpratam|
jñātvā kāmadughaṃ māṃ tvam iti tapaḥparāyaṇaḥ|| 66 ||

maghavaṃste stavaṃ divyaṃ yaḥ paṭhiṣyati mānavaḥ|
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sa yāsyati ca te purīm|| 67 ||

śatravo vilayaṃ yānti tasya vaktrāvalokanāt|
paṭhiṣyati stavaṃ śakra rogaśokabhayāpaham|| 68 ||

asādhyaṃ sādhayet kāryaṃ tvatstavaṃ pāṭhako budhaḥ|
medinyāṃ jāyate yarhi tava tulyo na saṃśayaḥ|| 69 ||

tataḥ śakro mudā yukta ākarṇya śītalaṃ vacaḥ|
prārthitavān mahādevaṃ vākyaṃ gadgadayā girā|| 70 ||

vidhāya svāñjaliṃ mūrdhni pradakṣiṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ|
tato nanāma deveśaṃ varaṃ dātuṃ samāgatam|| 71 ||

śakra uvāca |

nāhaṃ varaṃ samutsehe anyaṃ varaṃ varaprada|
vibudhairme hi yaddattaṃ yāce bhavantam īśa tat|| 72 ||

īśvara uvāca |

vatsādyaprabhṛti tvaṃ ca indro bhava surārcakaḥ|
yajñānām ādyabhoktā tvaṃ vibudhānāṃ kramāt prabhuḥ|| 73 ||

tvacchāsane ratā devāḥ prabhaviṣyanti nānyathā|
adhīśastvamarāvatyām aiśvaryatvaṃ dadāmi te|| 74 ||

bhūyo dadāmi te śakra prācīdiśaśca pālanam|
meroḥ prāgbhāgataḥ śṛṅge tava sthānaṃ bhaviṣyati|| 75 ||

prācīnabarhiṣo nāma tava loko bhaviṣyati|
tasmāt prācyān sadā śāstā kartā hartā bhaviṣyati|| 76 ||

gaccha śakrāmarāvatyāḥ palāyituṃ diśaṃ ca tat|
vibudhānām abhiṣekam ādāya taiḥ samaṃ dhruvam|| 77 ||

skanda uvāca |

varaṃ yathepsitaṃ dattvā sarvavaram anuttamam|
tapasā nandito yayau tvantarhitaṃ divi|| 78 ||

devāḥ samāgatya tato 'antarīkṣādālokya śakraṃ tapasā prayuktam|
harṣaṃ pracakruḥ suvaraṃ girīśāt saṃsparśya hastaiḥ samaharṣakampaiḥ|| 79 ||

tato devagaṇāḥ sarve prācyāṃ sānuṃ yayurgireḥ|
bṛhaspatismukhā viprāḥ kṛtvā śakraṃ purastadā|| 80 ||

marīciśca tathā cātriḥ pulastyo munisattamaḥ|
pulahaśca kratuścaiva bhṛguraṅgirasastathā|| 81 ||

brahmā ca nāradaścaiva siddhāśca munisattamāḥ|
mārkaṇḍeyaścirāyuśca dadhīcirmunisattamaḥ|| 82 ||

sanak ca sanakaścaiva sanātanaḥ sanandakaḥ|
sanatkumāro dharmiṣṭho brahmā ca kapilastathā|| 83 ||

gandharvāśca tathā cānye vasavaścāpsarogaṇāḥ|
sūryaśca candramā ṛkṣā viṣṇuścaiva tathāpare|| 84 ||

tasmai dattvābhiṣekaṃ yadāryātīrthoddhṛtairjalaiḥ|
prācīsānau sumerostaṃ sthāpitenaiva ādritāḥ|| 85 ||

agastya uvāca |

skanda kathaṃ dadurdevā abhiṣekaṃ mahātmane|
devarṣayaśca gandharvāstathā cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ|| 86 ||

kasmin sthāne mahāśṛṅge siddhāśca munisattamāḥ|
śrotum icchāmi caitaddhi vada me sarvavidvibho|| 87 ||

skanda uvāca |

himādre ratnakoṭyāṃ tam ānīya vidhivat tadā|
ratnasiṃhāsane divye praviśyodaṅmukhaṃ mune|| 88 ||

śakratīrthajalaṃ puṇyam ānīya vidhipūrvakam|
abhiṣekaṃ dadustasmai suvarṇakalaśoddhṛtaiḥ|| 89 ||

dadau brahmā paṭhan vedān bṛhaspatistathā vidhiḥ|
saptarṣaya ṛcābhiścābhiṣekaṃ pradadurmuhuḥ|| 90 ||

stuvan devāstathā cānye siddhā mantragaṇaistathā|
gandharvā gītavādyaiśca nṛtyairapsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ|| 91 ||

guruṇā cārcitaḥ paścāccandanairvividhairmudā|
dadau brahmā punastasmai sarvaiśvaryasurādhipam|| 92 ||

dadau sūryaḥ punastasmai abhiṣekaṃ varottamam|
ripūṇām asahaṃ tāpaṃ sahasrāṃśaṃ svatejasām|| 93 ||

dadau ca candramāstasmai abhiṣekaṃ punarvaram|
devānāṃ sukhadaṃ divyaṃ śītalaṃ ca mahojjvalam|| 94 ||

viṣṇuścaiva dadau bhūyo 'abhiṣekaṃ varottamam|
ripūṇāṃ bhayadaṃ krodhaṃ daityaśatruvimardakam|| 95 ||

pulomā ca dadau kanyāṃ śacīṃ nāmnīṃ mahāsatīm|
upayeme yayā śakro vidhivaddvijasattamaiḥ|| 96 ||

vādyaṃ cakrurdivisthāśca dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāṃstato mudā|
bherīśca dundubhīn kāṃsyān mṛdaṅgāṃśca tathāparān|| 97 ||

devakanyā jagustatra vavarṣuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭayaḥ|
nanṛtuścāpsarovṛndā āśiṣo munayo daduḥ|| 98 ||

jayaśabdastato bhūyo 'abhūt tatra samantataḥ|
ānarcuśca tato 'agastya devarṣayastathāpare|| 99 ||

tato devagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ yayau śakro 'amarāvatīm|
gandharvaiścāpsarobhiśca vimānastho mudānvitaḥ|| 100 ||

tato 'amarāvatīṃ rājyaṃ rakṣāṃ cakāra nirjarān|
tadāprabhṛti cādyāpi sa dikpālo 'abhavadvṛṣā|| 101 ||

ratnakoṭigiriṃ tasmādārohati suniścayaḥ|
āryatīrthajalāplāvya śakraloke vasecciram|| 102 ||

tataśca vahniḥ sutapo himādrau cakāra nūnaṃ sahajaḥ sutejāḥ|
śrutvā ca śakreṇa phalaṃ pralabdhaṃ so 'abhūdvidikpālaka ārya bhūyaḥ|| 103 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe śakrābhiṣeko nāma dvādaśo adhyāyaḥ|| 12 ||

lomaharṣaṇa uvāca |

niśamya ghaṭayonistat purāṇaṃ skandavaktrajam|
bhṛśaṃ mumoda viprāryāḥ punaḥ śrotumanā abhūt|| 1 ||

śṛṇudhvaṃ muniśārdūlā yat pṛṣṭaṃ kumbhayoninā|
pārvatīnandanaṃ bhaktyā hutabhujaścaritrakam|| 2 ||

agastya uvāca |

bhūyaḥ śrotumanā deva jano 'ayaṃ śaṃkarātmaja|
sarvajñe tvayi tadvārtāṃ kṛśānutapa{}udbhavām|| 3 ||

himavacchikhare kasmin snātvā tīrthe tathā punaḥ|
kathaṃ cakre tapo vahniḥ kenopadeśito vibho|
devasenāgraṇīḥ skanda tat phalaṃ prāptavān kutaḥ|| 4 ||

skanda uvāca |

āsīdaṅgiraso vipro mānaso yaḥ purā vidheḥ|
tasyātmajo mahātejā agnirnāma triṣu śrutaḥ|| 5 ||

mahābalī mahāprājñaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ|
rudrabhaktirato 'ajasraṃ rudrasmaraṇabhāvitaḥ|| 6 ||

kvacit sa śrutavān kāle ṛṣibhyo dahano mune|
indreṇa caritaṃ yacca labdhā ca tridiveśatā|| 7 ||

ekadā divase vahniḥ papraccha janakaṃ mudā|
śakreṇa caritāṃ vārtām ānamya pitaraṃ muhuḥ|| 8 ||

agniruvāca |

pūjyāya pitṛdevāya janmadātre namo namaḥ|
tāta kathaṃ ca śakreṇa tapastaptaṃ suduścaram|| 9 ||

mamaivaṃ vartate kāmastapastaptuṃ tathāvidham|
kasmin sthāne mahāprājña kṛpābhirupadiśyatām|| 10 ||

aṅgirā uvāca |

brahmaputro nadaśreṣṭho brahmajvālā nadī varā|
tayoḥ susaṃgame tīrthe brahmatvaṃ prāpyate suta|| 11 ||

himavato mahāśṛṅge sarvapuṇyaphalaprade|
nānāratnasamākīrṇe bahutuṣārabhūṣite|| 12 ||

prācīdakṣiṇayormadhye jyotiḥkūṭasya śekhare|
uttarataśca bhasmādrestejonāmaśiloccaye|| 13 ||

tasmiṃstīrthe suta snātvā tejovacchekhare punaḥ|
saṃsthāpya vidhivalliṅgam ekacittena japyatām|| 14 ||

tārapūrvaṃ namaścānte sampradānapadaṃ tataḥ|
saṃsāratārakaṃ mantraṃ sevyādbhuktīpsitapradam|| 15 ||

skanda uvāca |

tato vaiśvānaro vipra ākarṇya vacanaṃ pituḥ|
ekacittaṃ samādhāya himavantaṃ yayau mudā|| 16 ||

tasmiṃstīrthe samāplāvya vibhūtyā lepitastanuḥ|
bhāle tripuṇḍrakaṃ kṛtvā rudrākṣān dhārayet punaḥ|| 17 ||

samāruhya tataḥ śailaṃ tejovantaṃ suśekharam|
kūṭottame maṇijvāle pavitre hi samāviśet|| 18 ||

yogāsane samāsīna ṛjukāya udaṅmukhaḥ|
vicintya vidhivaddevaṃ sarvadehaguhāśayam|| 19 ||

liṅgaṃ ratnamayaṃ sthāpya vidhipūrvaṃ dvijottamaḥ|
sampūjayet tato bhaktyā trividhairmānasaiḥ punaḥ|| 20 ||

divyavarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ jajāpa mantram uttamam|
āvirbhūtastato devo vyomnastejaḥkalevaraḥ|| 21 ||

tataścādarśayadrudro bhaktāya svaṃ kalevaram|
vyaktarūpaṃ samāsthāya caikākine tapasvine|| 22 ||

so 'api dadarśa deveśaṃ bhūteśvaraṃ mahāvibhum|
varaṃ dātuṃ tapasthāne avatarantam ambarāt|| 23 ||

sampradarśya mahādevaṃ vyaktarūpaṃ smitānanam|
dvibhujaṃ ca vṛṣārūḍhaṃ harṣitastu tadā śuciḥ|| 24 ||

parikramya tato devam aṣṭāṅgairhi nanāma saḥ|
vācā madhurayā rudraṃ harṣagadgadayā tadā|| 25 ||

lomāñcitaḥ samādhāya karapuṭaṃ ca mūrdhani|
trividhairbhāvayuktaḥ sa stutiṃ cakāra śūline|| 26 ||

agniruvāca |

śaṃkareśa mahādeva jagajjīvana janyaka|
jīveśvara mahadbrahmaṃścaitanyaka namo 'astu te|| 27 ||

tejorūpa virūpākṣa gaṅgādhara trilocana|
viśvambhara virāṭeśa saṃsārasāra te namaḥ|| 28 ||

bhaktibhāvya vibhāveśa bhāvābhavāvigocara|
bhavābhayada bhūteśa bhaveśvara namo 'astu te|| 29 ||

vedavedāntatattvajñairalakṣyo 'asi mahāprabho|
sarvadeveśa vāgīśa vāgrūpa te namo namaḥ|| 30 ||

bhavaśārdūlasaṃkrīḍāmohitajīvanoddhṛta|
bhavāndhatamaopāyaprodbhūtārka namo 'astu te|| 31 ||

saṃvartake bhavāpāyavilokanāgnibhālaka|
icchāprodbhūtasaṃsāra svecchārūpa namo 'astu te|| 32 ||

kālarūpa kalātīta kāmeśvara ca kāmada|
kaṅkāla kālarūpāja kāladeva namo 'astu te|| 33 ||

vibhūtibhūṣaṇogreśa aṣṭaiśvaryaphalaprada|
bahurūpadhara sthāṇo viśvarūpa namo 'astu te|| 34 ||

kailāsaśikhare vāsin tuṣārabhūtibhūṣite|
gaṅgojjvalajaṭāśīrṣe sūryendvagnīkṣaṇe namaḥ|| 35 ||

vyāghrājinapidhānāṅga muṇḍamālāgalāvṛtaḥ|
khaṭvāṅgaṃ ca triśūlaṃ ca dadhānaṃ te namo namaḥ|| 36 ||

vimohito 'ahaṃ tava deva māyayā bhramāmi na tvāṃ vibhavāḍhyagarvitaḥ|
kadāpi vācā tanunā hṛdā ca me kṣamasva deveśa mamāparādhakam|| 37 ||

skanda uvāca |

tato maheśvaro 'agastya samākarṇya stavottamam|
harṣitavāṃstadā tasmai protphullalocano bhṛśam|| 38 ||

babhāṣe vacanaṃ bhūyo vahnaye stutiharṣitaḥ|
tapasvine mahātejā varaṃ dātuṃ ghaṭodbhava|| 39 ||

īśvara uvāca |

stuto 'ahaṃ stutibhirvipra tvanmukhānnisṛtottamaiḥ|
prekṣya tapaḥ kaṭhoraṃ te suduṣkaraṃ surairapi|| 40 ||

idānīṃ te varaṃ dāsye bhaktāya ca tapasvine|
varaṃ varaya dharmajña yat tvaṃ vāñchasi sāmpratam|| 41 ||

agniruvāca |

yadi dāsyasi me deva sarvavaram anuttamam|
tava bhaktiratiṃ nityaṃ tvāṃ pūjaye suniścalam|| 42 ||

tvatsmaraṇe suniṣṭhā ca cihnāyāste stavottame|
idam eva varaṃ kāṅkṣe tanme kṛpaya bho vibho|| 43 ||

rudra uvāca |

bahubhaktiratāyādya dadāmīdaṃ varaṃ śṛṇu|
bhavatu te mahāśaktirbhūyādaiśvaryam āryatā|| 44 ||

bhavitā lokasākṣī tvaṃ sarvabhuk saṃtataṃ punaḥ|
vinā tvāṃ sarvakarmaṇyaṃ lokānāṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet|| 45 ||

tvanmūrtibhirayaṃ heturlokadagdho bhaviṣyati|
havirbhuk kraturūpastvaṃ sarvakarmaprasādhakaḥ|| 46 ||

sarvadevamayo bhūyāḥ sarvepsitaphalapradaḥ|
prācīdakṣiṇayormadhye meroḥ sānau pratiṣṭhasi|| 47 ||

adyaprabhṛti agne tvaṃ vatsa bhava digīśvaraḥ|
diśaṃ pālaya nityaṃ vai sarvakartā ca śāśvataḥ|| 48 ||

yaḥ paṭhati śucirbhūtvā divyam agnistavaṃ sadā|
sarvapāpairvimukto 'asau tava lokaṃ pragacchati|| 49 ||

pīḍāyāṃ saṃkaṭe vāpi krūrogragrahapīḍane|
saṃgrāme te bhayodbhūte tvaṃ taṃ rakṣasi pāṭhakam|| 50 ||

yaḥ paṭhet satataṃ dhīraḥ stavarājaṃ manoharam|
sarvapāpairvinirmuktastava loke mahīyate|| 51 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ mahadvaraṃ dattvā nirjanāya tapasvine|
kumbhayone mahādevastirodhānaṃ gato 'ambare|| 52 ||

tato devagaṇāḥ sarve gandharvāpsaraso gaṇāḥ|
devarṣayastathā siddhā nāradaśca bṛhaspatiḥ|| 53 ||

samāgatya mahākūṭe tejonāmaśiloccaye|
mumuduśca tam ālokya varalabdhaṃ tapasvinam|| 54 ||

bṛhaspatimukhā devāḥ siṣicurdahanaṃ mudā|
brahmajvālāsutīrthasya prādāya jalam uttamam|| 55 ||

hiraṇyakalaśairvipra mantrajapte pavitrakaiḥ|
vāsobhiḥ paridhāyaivaṃ guruṇā carcitastathā|| 56 ||

nedurvyomni ca nādāśca gandharvapatayo jaguḥ|
devyaśca cikṣipurlājān vavarṣuḥ kusumāni ca|| 57 ||

agnaye ca tadā patnīṃ svāhānāmnīṃ ghaṭodbhava|
dadurdevāstato vāhnistām udvahe yathāvidhi|| 58 ||

tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ purodhāyāgnidaivatam|
prācīdakṣiṇayormadhye merorjagmuśca satvaram|| 59 ||

agniṃ saṃsthāpya lokeśastatkūṭe kumbhasambhava|
sambodhya vidhivat pautraṃ brahmalokaṃ yayau mudā|| 60 ||

tathāvidhaṃ sagandharvā devā jagmuḥ svakaṃ svakam|
sthānaṃ vahniṃ ca sampūjya vidhivat taṃ muhurmuhuḥ|| 61 ||

snāyate cāgnitīrthe yaḥ sakṛdapi ghaṭodbhava|
agniṣṭomaphalaṃ prāpya agniloke mahīyate|| 62 ||

tadādi vahnirmumude tathāvidho yathaiva śakrasya bhavet pramodaḥ|
yamaḥ samākarṇya śucestapo vai cakāra tat so 'api kaṭhoracetasā|| 63 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe agnidikpālasiddhisnāma trayodaśo adhyāyaḥ|| 13 ||

agastya uvāca |

proktaṃ me duścaraṃ taptaṃ tapo yamena rudraja|
kasmiṃstīrthe ca śṛṅge vā ko 'asau yamo mahābalaḥ|| 1 ||

tepe purā mahāsena yamaścāsau kathaṃ punaḥ|
śrotum icchāmyahaṃ tvattastat sarvaṃ kathayasva me|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

rudratejomahābhānuḥ pūrvoktaste mahāvibhuḥ|
tasyāpatyaṃ trayo devā manuryamaḥ śanaiścaraḥ|| 3 ||

śaivaḥ sarvavidāryaśca sarvaśāstreṣu pāragaḥ|
sarvadharmarato 'ajasram adharmeṣu parāṅmukhaḥ|| 4 ||

saṃyamaḥ sarvakarmasu tasmādyama iti śrutaḥ|
nirdvandvo nispṛho dānto nirvikāraḥ sadā śuciḥ|| 5 ||

tasmāllokairyamaḥ proktaḥ samadṛṣṭiśca jīviṣu|
satyavādī ca kālajño dharmādharmeṣu nirmitaḥ|| 6 ||

viṣṇubhaktirato nityaṃ śivapūjanatatparaḥ|
advaitavādī madhuvāgyajñaniṣṭhaśca dāyakaḥ|
sūryabhaktirato 'agastya atithipūjakastathā|| 7 ||

kadāciddivase vārtāṃ pṛcchati sma raviṃ yamaḥ|
agninā yat tapastaptaṃ śrutvā devamukhānmune|| 8 ||

yama uvāca |

tāta kathaṃ tapastaptam agninā ca mahātmanā|
mamāpi vidyate kāmastapastaptuṃ suniścitam|| 9 ||

lokasākṣin mahātejo 'anujñāṃ hi prayaccha me|
yasmācca prāpyate siddhirnājñāṃ vina care tava|| 10 ||

sūrya uvāca |

agninā yat tapastaptaṃ tanmayā kathyate 'adhunā|
śṛṇu putra mahājñānaṃ yasmāt saṃlabhyate param|| 11 ||

upadeśaṃ samādāya pituryayau himālayam|
bhasmoddhūlanadeho 'asau rudrākṣāṃśca dadhāra ca|| 12 ||

tapaścakāra dharmajñastato vaiśvānaro 'amaraḥ|
taponte suvaraṃ labdhvā dikpālaścābhavaddhruvam|| 13 ||

tathāvidhaṃ tvayā vatsa tapyatāṃ duścaraṃ tapaḥ|
yadīcchedātmanaḥ siddhiṃ himavaddakṣiṇe diśi|| 14 ||

nīlakaṇṭhasya pūrvasmādumāyāḥ kuṇḍadakṣiṇe|
siddhakūṭa iti khyātastatra vai tapyatāṃ suta|| 15 ||

ṣaḍakṣaraṃ mahāmantraṃ tārapūrvaṃ prajapyatām|
saṃsthāpya vidhivalliṅgaṃ bhaktyā cārādhayeśvaram|| 16 ||

siddharasā nadīśreṣṭhā umākuṇḍodbhavāpagā|
tayoryoge siddhatīrthe snātvādrau ca giriṃ vrajet|| 17 ||

tatra snātvā divaṃ yāti sadeho nātra saṃśayaḥ|
umākuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā siddho bhavati tatkṣaṇāt|| 18 ||

skanda uvāca |

śrutvā pathyaṃ piturvākyaṃ sarvavāguttamottamam|
praharṣito mahāprājñaḥ sarvāṅgalomaharṣaṇaḥ|| 19 ||

vācā gadgadayā vijñaḥ stutiṃ cakāra bhāsvate|
vidhāya cāñjaliṃ mūrdhni parikramya punaḥ punaḥ|| 20 ||

.o namo bhānave 'ajāya jagatāṃ locanāya vai|
sṛṣṭisthitisvarūpāya saṃhāraka namo 'astu te|| 21 ||

jñānāya jñānarūpāya jñānaprade ca śāśvate|
jyotirūpāya devāya jyotiṣāṃ pataye namaḥ|| 22 ||

evaṃ stutvā sa dharmajñaḥ pitaraṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ|
praṇamya śirasā devaṃ himavacchikharaṃ yayau|| 23 ||

tato yamaḥ samāgatya siddhatīrthe jalottame|
siddhaiḥ prasevite 'agastya snānaṃ cakre yathāvidhi|| 24 ||

tataḥ snātvā yamaḥ svaccho bhūtyā dehe pralepitaḥ|
lalāṭe saṃvidhāyādyaṃ tripuṇḍrakaṃ suśobhanam|
rudrākṣān dhārayedvidvān deśe deśe yathāvidhi|| 25 ||

dadau dāyaṃ munibhyaśca yathāvibhavavistaram|
dattvā dayāṃstataḥ saurī ruroha siddhaparvatam|| 26 ||

tatra śṛṅge mahāpuṇye siddhalokaprasevite|
tuṣārasaṃkule divye sarvadevamanohare|| 27 ||

bahuratnasamākīrṇe siddharasasamudbhave|
divyāsane samāsīna ṛjukāya udaṅmukhaḥ|| 28 ||

vicintya jyotiṣāṃ puñjaṃ manaḥpadme sakeśare|
vaidūryamaṇisambhūtaṃ liṅgaṃ saṃsthāpya vai yamaḥ|| 29 ||

nirmite vedike divye pañcasūtraiḥ sunirmitam|
tīrthatoyaiḥ susaṃsthāpya vibhūtibhiḥ pṛthak tataḥ|| 30 ||

gandhottamairdukūlaiśca dhūpairdīpaistathāśanaiḥ|
ananyabhāvasaṃyukta ekacittaśca mantravit|| 31 ||

tato 'apūpujadādyeśaṃ sarvabhūtaguhāśayam|
jajāpa manasā nūnaṃ manuṃ yamo mahāmatiḥ|| 32 ||

ādhāya śaṃkaraṃ devaṃ nāsāgre taṃ nirīkṣya vai|
divyavarṣaśataṃ sāgram ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ|| 33 ||

tato varṣāvasāne vai āvirbhūto mahāvibhuḥ|
jyotirbhūto mahātejastejasā bhāsayan diśaḥ|
varaṃ dātuṃ svabhaktāya avatatāra puṣkarāt|| 34 ||

vilokya tapasā pūrṇaṃ kliśyamānaṃ ca mauninam|
divyarūpaṃ samādhāya darśayāmāsa taṃ svakam|| 35 ||

prahṛṣṭavān mahādevastapasā tasya mauninaḥ|
pravyaktarūpavān bhūtvā sarvatejomayo vibhuḥ|| 36 ||

tato dadarśa bhūteśaṃ tejasāṃ param īśvaram|
trilocanaṃ caturbāhuṃ candrabhālaṃ kapālinam|| 37 ||

prasannavadanaṃ rudraṃ harṣapūrṇaṃ ca śūlinam|
dadhānaṃ ḍamaruṃ mālāṃ vyāghracarmottarīyakam|| 38 ||

samprekṣya devadeveśaṃ vividhaiḥ sa nanāma ca|
stavaṃ cakāra dharmātmā kṛtapradakṣiṇo mudā|| 39 ||

yama uvāca |

.o, |

namaḥ śivāya devāya śāntāyomeśvarāya ca|
jyotiṣāṃ puñjadehāya tejorūpāya vai namaḥ|| 40 ||

alakṣāya ca lakṣāya mṛgalāñchanamauline|
trinetrāya caturdoṣṇe śūlahastāya vai namaḥ|| 41 ||

khaṭvāṅgaṃ ḍamaruṃ mālāṃ dadhānāya namo namaḥ|
namo bhasmāṅgarāgāya rudrākṣamāline namaḥ|| 42 ||

bahurūpāya rudrāya anantarūpiṇe namaḥ|
anantaśaktisaṃgāya anantaphaladāya ca|| 43 ||

namo dayānidhānāya dayārūpāya te namaḥ|
dāntāya dānarūpāya dāyakāya namo namaḥ|| 44 ||

sarvabhūteśadevāya dambhahantre harāya ca|
anādidevadevāya śaṃkarāya namo namaḥ|| 45 ||

paśupāśavimuktāya trirūpāya namo namaḥ|
jñānapradāya bhavyāya mṛtyuṃjayāya vai namaḥ|| 46 ||

anūpamaśarīrāya viśvarūpāya vai namaḥ|
viśveśvarāya bhīmāya dehasthāya namo namaḥ|| 47 ||

nīlakaṇṭhāya śarvāya piṅgalanetracārave|
nirdhūtamalapaṅkāya śāśvatāya namo namaḥ|| 48 ||

mahābhogīndrahārāya ajāyāmitamūrtaye|
parāya parameśāya sarvapraṇata te namaḥ|| 49 ||

bhaktavatsala deveśa bhaktihīnasya dehinaḥ|
kṣantavyo me 'aparādhaśca vāgvibhavodbhavaṃ stavam|| 50 ||

skanda uvāca |

etat stotraṃ samākarṇya devadevo mahāvibhuḥ|
umayā sahito harṣaṃ vilokya tasya ceṣṭitam|| 51 ||

uvāca vacanaṃ tasmai varadānāya sāmpratam|
mahādevaḥ svabhaktāya nirjanāya tapasvine|| 52 ||

īśvara uvāca |

varaṃ varaya vatsa tvaṃ svāntepsitam anuttamam|
dadāmi te mahābāho bhuktimuktipradaṃ param|| 53 ||

sutaporajjunā baddhām ānītāṃ gāṃ tvayā srutām|
stutivatsatarīṃ kāmaṃ duhyatāṃ te yadṛcchayā|| 54 ||

yama uvāca |

adyaivaṃ bhavatā tanme dīyate lokanandana|
trailokyeśa sadā mahyaṃ kṛpayā tāṃ varottamaḥ|| 55 ||

yathāgnaye purā datto dikpālatvaṃ nirantaram|
mamāpi vartate kāmastathā tanme 'aja dīyatām|| 56 ||

īśvara uvāca |

bhakta yama mahāprājña yaduktaṃ ca tvayādhunā|
datte bhavatu kāmaṃ ca dikpālyaṃ pūṣaṇātmaja|| 57 ||

sānau dakṣiṇato meroḥ kūṭe tiṣṭha nirantaram|
adyaprabhṛti cārya tvaṃ tasyāṃ dikpālako bhava|| 58 ||

tato lokā vadiṣyanti yāmyā digiti ca śrutiḥ|
bhuyo dāsye varaṃ tubhyaṃ saṃsārodbhavakāraṇam|| 59 ||

durlabhaṃ janmināṃ nṛṇāṃ sukṛtaṃ duḥkṛtaṃ ca yat|
tathyātathyaṃ yaduktaṃ ca saṃvicarya vilekhaya|| 60 ||

tasmāt tvāṃ pravadiṣyanti citragupta iti śrutaḥ|
tataḥ prāṇina ādāya yogyaṃ tāñchāśitān kuru|| 61 ||

dharmādharmau vicāryādau svarge vā narake kṣipa|
lokāstvāṃ ca vadiṣyanti kāla ityantakaḥ punaḥ|| 62 ||

imaṃ daṇḍaṃ ca pāśaṃ ca gṛhāṇa manasā dhruvam|
pāpīyasāṃ narāṇāṃ ca śāsanāya ca śāsakaḥ|| 63 ||

manmāyāhārdrarajjūvārrdapāśenābadhya jīvinaḥ|
anteśa vasam āhvānam ākṛṣyanti tam ekataḥ|| 64 ||

ekatastava pāśena sambadhvā taṃ punastataḥ|
daṇḍenānena kāla tvaṃ samākṛṣyasi tarjayan|| 65 ||

yāvanto jīvino loke garbhasthā niḥsṛtāstvayi|
tāvanto yātanāṃ kuryā madbhaktāṃśca vinā punaḥ|| 66 ||

bhasmarudrākṣadehāṃstāṃstulasīmālinastathā|
madbhaktān viṣṇubhaktāṃśca prekṣya cakṣurnimīlaya|| 67 ||

bhūyo dāsyāmyahaṃ tubhyam anuttamavaraṃ yama|
devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ pitṛṇāṃ tvaṃ patirbhava|| 68 ||

skanda uvāca |

dattveti pravaraṃ tasmai bhaktāya bhaktavatsalaḥ|
lokaniyamaparyāyaṃ tvantardhānaṃ yayau haraḥ|| 69 ||

tato brahmādayo devā harṣaṃ cakrustadā bhṛśam|
samāgatya nirīkṣyāryaṃ labdhavaraṃ tapasvinam|| 70 ||

dattvā śaktiṃ tatastasmai abhiṣekaṃ daduḥ punaḥ|
tattīrthajalasampūrṇairhiraṇyakalaśaiḥ surāḥ|| 71 ||

tato brahmā suraiḥ sārdhaṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ yayau diśi|
purodhāya yamaṃ merorvādyotsavaiḥ stavottamaiḥ|
tatra saṃsthāpya dikpālam apūpujadyamaṃ tadā|| 72 ||

tato brahmā yayau vyomnastvantardhānaṃ yayuḥ surāḥ|
adyaprabhṛti cāryo 'asau dikpālaścābhavadyamaḥ|| 73 ||

himavati mahāśaile labdhavaraḥ kapālinaḥ|
yamatīrthe tridhā snātaḥ sarvapāpairvivarjitaḥ|| 74 ||

siddhakūṭaṃ giriṃ dhīra ārohati sakṛnmune|
śakraloke sukhaṃ bhuktvā dikpālo 'asau bhavet tataḥ|| 75 ||

bhūyaśca vipreśa mahāmanāsau ādāya cājñāṃ ca pitustapaśca|
cakāra nūnaṃ varanairṛto 'api śrutvā ca labdhaṃ suvaraṃ yamena|| 76 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe yamadikpālasiddhirnāma caturdaśo adhyāyaḥ|| 14 ||

agastya uvāca |

kaścāsau nairṛto deva tapastepe mahābalaḥ|
kasmāllabdhavaro 'abhūdvai kasmiṃstīrthottame śubhe|| 1 ||

mayi yadyanukampā cet sarvavārtāviśārada|
etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ tanme 'anukampaya dhruvam|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

nikhilena ghaṭodbhūta tasya yaccaritaṃ purā|
tvaddhārdena pravakṣyāmi tat sarvaṃ śṛṇu sāmpratam|| 3 ||

kaśyapasya suto dhīmān nairṛto nāma nāmataḥ|
vīro 'asau sarvajantūnāṃ sarvonnataparākramaḥ|| 4 ||

nakhāyudho mahātejā mahābalonnato 'agraṇīḥ|
rātriṃcaraśca hiṃsātmā māṃsāhārī ca raktapaḥ|| 5 ||

kaścitkāle mahābāhuḥ prapraccha pitaraṃ munim|
upāgamya sthitaṃ yatra kaśyapaḥ sa dvijottamaḥ|| 6 ||

triḥ parikramya karbūro bhaktipūrvaṃ nanāma ca|
vidhāya cāñjaliṃ mūrdhni stutiṃ cakāra bhāvataḥ|| 7 ||

nairṛta uvāca |

namo janakadevāya prāṇināṃ janakāya ca|
sṛṣṭisthitivināśānāṃ kartre ca munaye namaḥ|| 8 ||

brahmaṇe viśvarūpāya namo vai brahmatejase|
yogīśvarāya pūtātman namaste brahmavarcase|| 9 ||

tāta icchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ tvatto brahmavidāṃ vara|
vaivasvatena yat taptaṃ kasmiṃstīrthe 'adriśekhare|| 10 ||

kaśyapa uvāca |

śṛṇu putra pravakṣyāmi yat pṛṣṭaṃ mayi tat khalu|
vaivasvatena yat taptaṃ yacca labdhaṃ ca śūlinaḥ|| 11 ||

āsīt sūryasuto dhīmān vaivasvato 'abhidhānataḥ|
sarvajantūdayātmāsau lokadharmapramāṇataḥ|| 12 ||

saṃtoṣya pitaraṃ tena upadiṣṭo hi tena ca|
harṣapūrṇayuto nemī taptum iyeṣa sūrajaḥ|| 13 ||

bhādrasya pūrṇimāyāṃ sa pūrvabhādreṇa saṃyute|
anuśiṣṭaṃ samādāya himavantaṃ giriṃ yayau|| 14 ||

siddhatīrthajale snātvā siddhakūṭaṃ samāśritaḥ|
jajāpa caikacittena saṃsthāpya vidhivadvibhum|| 15 ||

tatastasmai mahādevo dadau varam anuttamam|
labdhavaro maheśānāddikpālo 'abhūnna saṃśayaḥ|| 16 ||

dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśo meroḥ sarvakartā sa eva ca|
sa eva pitṛbhartā ca jantūnāṃ śāsakaḥ kramāt|| 17 ||

gantavyo jīvibhistasya lokaścānte na saṃśayaḥ|
asti vāñchā ca te vatsa cetasi tapyatāṃ tapaḥ|
ṣaḍvargāt sa samutsṛjya niścalaḥ sujitendriyaḥ|| 18 ||

nairṛta uvāca |

gantavyaṃ śekhare kasmiṃstīrthe cāplāvanaṃ kutaḥ|
anuṣṭheyaṃ kathaṃ tāta samārādhyaśca kaḥ punaḥ|| 19 ||

upadeśo dhruvaṃ mahyaṃ dīyatāṃ munisattama|
gurorvinopadeśaṃ hi akarma iti naḥ śrutam|| 20 ||

kaśyapa uvāca |

himavato vare sānau māno nāma sarovaraḥ|
pūrvaṃ sasarja dhātā vai sarvalokahitāya ca|| 21 ||

havyakavyārcanaṃ tatra yat kurvanti narottamāḥ|
tat sarvam akṣayaṃ prāpya svacchandaṃ mānasaṃ labhet|| 22 ||

tasmāt tvam api ca snānaṃ kuryāt tasmāt subhaktitaḥ|
tapastapasi karbūra vidhānaṃ śṛṇu vistaram|| 23 ||

kṛtvā snānaṃ jalaistīrthe vibhūtyā lepanaṃ caret|
vidhāyāṅgeṣu rudrākṣān dhiyā mantraṃ japan mudā|| 24 ||

saṃsthāpya vidhivadrudraṃ trividhaiḥ stotrayet suta|
evaṃ saṃcara karbūra tataḥ siddhirbhaviṣyati|| 25 ||

agastya uvāca |

bhagavañchrotum icchāmi sarvajñe bhavati dhruvam|
kathaṃ sasarja dhātā vai divyaṃ sarovaraṃ purā|| 26 ||

mānaḥsara iti khyātaṃ snānasaṃsāratārakam|
tasyāṃ tuhinasaṃhatyāṃ ko mukto 'abhūdvada prabho|| 27 ||

skanda uvāca |

sasarja manasā brahmā mudā yat tena śekhare|
triṃśadyojanavistāraṃ tadevāgādhavistṛtam|| 28 ||

gaṅgām āvāhya dhātāsau dadhyau paraṃ śivaṃ hṛdā|
prādurbabhūva gaṅgā sā ākhāte svacchajīvanā|| 29 ||

dhātālokya śivaṃ toyaṃ harṣavāṃstatra kumbhaja|
avocadāśiṣaṃ tasmai lokamokṣahitāya ca|| 30 ||

brahmovāca |

tiṣṭha devi hrade 'ajasraṃ jalamūrte namo 'astu te|
mokṣārthimokṣade mātarbhaktyā varaprade śubhe|| 31 ||

yaḥ snāyate naro bhaktyā tvanmūrtyarṇahrade sakṛt|
na punarjanyatāṃ yonau api janturnaraḥ kim u|| 32 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ dattvāśiṣaṃ tasmai tatra prajāpatirmudā|
divyavarṣaśataṃ tepe sarvabhūtodbhavāya ca|| 33 ||

tataḥ sasarja dhātādau saptarṣīn manasā tataḥ|
jantūṃścaturvidhān devā/llabdhaśaktiśca śūlinaḥ|| 34 ||

kvacit kālāntare 'agastya brahmaṇi tapasi sthite|
vimarṣya tapasaḥ kartuṃ te mano dadhire purā|| 35 ||

saptarṣayo mudā tatra dṛḍhaṃ tapaḥ sutepire|
samyak pṛthak sthitā rudraṃ samārādhya ca bhaktibhiḥ|| 36 ||

gaṅgām āpāhanaṃ cakruryugapat te maharṣayaḥ|
samāplavārcakāṃstatra pāśāyudhāḥ śivātmanaḥ|| 37 ||

tato gaṅgā mahāpuṇyā kasmā adya vrajāmyaham|
śāpaṃ dāsyanti me te vai iti cintākulā satī|| 38 ||

vepamānā muhurgaṅgā kṛtvaikāṃśaṃ ca saptadhā|
yatra yatra sthitā āryāstatra vavāha sā pṛthak|| 39 ||

śailānāṃ śekharebhyastā avatārya pṛthak tadā|
ṛṣyantikaṃ samuddiśya ātmānaṃ viviśurhrade|| 40 ||

tataḥ prekṣya mahātmānaḥ saptadhārāṃ samāvahām|
mumuduste bhṛśaṃ tasyai āśiṣaḥ pradaduḥ punaḥ|| 41 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

snānakāryārtham uddiśya naḥ prativāhitā satī|
adyaprabhṛti cārye tvaṃ saptanāṃ phaladā bhava|| 42 ||

tasmāt tvaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣasaubhāgyam eva ca|
hṛdyaṃ parākramaṃ rājyaṃ saptaite phaladā sadā|| 43 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti dattvāśiṣo 'agastya tābhyo maharṣayo mudā|
āsaṃstatra tapoyuktāḥ śivārcanaratāḥ sadā|| 44 ||

śatābdānte hradasyārya abhūdyuktābhidhānakam|
kṛpayā śūlino devyā hitāyāsubhṛtāṃ purā|| 45 ||

śukraśukladaśamyāṃ taddhrade hyajījanacchivaḥ|
haṃsarūpaṃ samāsthāya saumyaḥ supattrasundaraḥ|| 46 ||

raktacañcūśca raktāṅghriḥ pītalohitalocanaḥ|
mahārajanasaṃkāśaḥ sugrīvaḥ suravo 'acarat|| 47 ||

tata āryodbhavā tatra haṃsī cacāra sundarī|
tadākṛtiḥ samaṃ devī haṃsarūpeṇa śūlinā|| 48 ||

haṃsadehena deveśo haṃsīdevyāniśaṃ saha|
cacāra taddhrade nūnaṃ divyavarṣasahasrakam|| 49 ||

brahmā prekṣyāśu haṃsau dvau nirbharaṃ mumude hṛdā|
carantau svacchatoyeṣu bhakṣayantau bisāni vai|| 50 ||

mene kamalajo haṃsau śivaśaktyātmakau tadā|
kāvanyau tau vinā cātra carantau ceti mānase|| 51 ||

kṛto manoharaḥ pūto haṃsarūpeṇa śūlinā|
maddhradam iti kṛtvājo haṃsarūpaṃ dadhāra vai|| 52 ||

viṣṇurdadhāra haṃsāṅgaṃ haṃsān prekṣya mudā punaḥ|
tadākṛtirmahāsaumyaḥ sundaro 'abhicacāra vai|| 53 ||

samprekṣya tatsaro divyaṃ dharmo hāṃsaṃ dadhāra ca|
suravaḥ saumyarūpo 'asau śuklastatra galottamaḥ|| 54 ||

vyāpya divyasahasrābdaṃ cikrīḍustaddhrade hi te|
mṛṇālaṃ khādayan nūnaṃ cañcunā kaṇḍuyat punaḥ|| 55 ||

acīkriḍaddhrade rudro bhavānyā saha vai sukham|
kumbhaja haṃsarūpeṇa taiḥ parivārayan muhuḥ|| 56 ||

bibheda parvataḥ kūṭaṃ haṃsarūpeṇa viśvasṛk|
vikramairutpapātārṇo mahattaraṅgasaṃkulam|| 57 ||

bibheda yāmyataḥ kūṭaṃ haṃsarūpeṇa śaṃkaraḥ|
līlāsaktā nadī divyā utpapāta jalottamā|| 58 ||

bibhedottarataḥ kūṭaṃ haṃsarūpeṇa keśavaḥ|
jalapūrṇā suvistīrṇā śekharāllaghugāminī|| 59 ||

avācīkūṭato dharmaḥ svayaṃ bibheda vai tadā|
utpapāta nadī divyā taraṅgaiḥ saṃkulā mune|| 60 ||

tato viniryayustasmājjaladhārāścaturthakam|
prapeturgiriśṛṅgāt tā vasordhārā ivojjvalāḥ|| 61 ||

prapatitāṃ samālokya brahmā harṣitavān bhṛśam|
nāmadheyāni tāsāṃ ca cakāra sadṛśāni vai|| 62 ||

brahmovāca |

sudhīreṇa taraṅgena utpapātādriśekharāt|
puṃbhāvena yatastvaṃ me putro bhavāniśaṃ nada|| 63 ||

sarveṣāṃ janmināṃ putra snātakānāṃ tvayi dhruvam|
caturvargaphalaṃ vīra deyaṃ kilbiṣanāśakṛt|| 64 ||

saumyena līlayā putri pravavāha saridvare|
rudrayatnodbhavā yasmācchatarudrā bhavāniśam|| 65 ||

tretāyuge mahāsaumye surasaridbhaviṣyati|
raghūṇāṃ mānasaṃ karma sādhasyiṣyasi saṃtatam|| 66 ||

jalapūrṇena vistīrṇā pravavāha saridvarā|
viṣṇuyatnodbhave putri viṣṇumatī bhavādyataḥ|| 67 ||

tvajjalasparśakānāṃ tvaṃ bhuktimuktihṛdīpsitam|
deyā devi prabhutvaṃ ca snātakānāṃ viśeṣataḥ|| 68 ||

ādyodbhave saricchreṣṭhe svacchakallolamālinī|
pravavāhitha cādyā tvaṃ dharmapriyacikīrṣayā|| 69 ||

mumukṣūṇāṃ phalaṃ deyaṃ matsāyujyaṃ ca bālike|
paṅkānyapanayaṃsteṣāṃ purā kṛtānyapi dhruvam|| 70 ||

matkuṇḍe snāyate yo 'atra sarvamakhodbhavaṃ phalam|
labhitā matpriye putri vihāya sarvakilbiṣam|| 71 ||

nirmuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo giryārohaṇamātrataḥ|
prekṣya saro budho divyaṃ manaḥkāmaṃ dhruvaṃ labhet|| 72 ||

kadāciddaivayogena bhaktyātra snāyate hi yaḥ|
tasyārcanaṃ japāśaktastasya puṇyaphalaṃ mahat|| 73 ||

uttīrya duḥkhasaṃsāraṃ sarvajanma vihāya ca|
garbhavāsaṃ mahatkaṣṭaṃ vrajet tu paramaṃ padam|| 74 ||

caturāśītilakṣeṣu yoniṣu yātanāṃ ca yat|
dehānāṃ vidyate taddhi vihāya paramaṃ vrajet|| 75 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ dattvā varaṃ brahmā tābhyo 'akrīḍayaddhradāntare|
haṃsarūpo 'aniśaṃ nityaṃ haṃsadevaiḥ samaṃ mune|| 76 ||

tatra kālāntare devāḥ svargādāgatya tepire|
gandharvā guhyakāḥ siddhā daityāścāpsarasastathā|| 77 ||

vihaṃgarūpibhirdevairna mokṣate hradaḥ kalau|
medinīkucahemādrau jambūdvīpamanassaraḥ|| 78 ||

vimuktā bahavastatra duḥkhasaṃsāraniḥsṛtāḥ|
tajjalasparśanāt sadyo januṃ vihāya bhāgyataḥ|| 79 ||

āsīt kaścit purā mleccho vyādho vihaṃganāśakṛt|
jyeṣṭhaśukladaśamyāṃ sa haṃsaṃ hantuṃ gato hrade|| 80 ||

praskhalito hrade haṃsairjalāntare vyaloḍayat|
kaṣṭāduttīrya toyāt sa niṣpāpastajjalaspṛśat|| 81 ||

tato raudrā vimāne vai tam āsthāya savigraham|
ninyuḥ śivapuraṃ śreṣṭhaṃ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca|| 82 ||

daśakalpaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā papāta ca śivālayāt|
tato rājābhavadbhūmau sārvabhaumaḥ śivārcakaḥ|| 83 ||

ajñānato 'api sa mleccho labdhavāṃstat phalaṃ mune|
jñānayukto naraḥ snānānmuktiṃ lapsyati kiṃ na ca|| 84 ||

tataḥ piturvacaḥ pathyaṃ niśamya rākṣasottamaḥ|
ekacittaṃ samādhāya śīghraṃ mānasaro yayau|| 85 ||

tasmiṃstīrthe samāgatya sasnau suvimale jale|
yathoktavidhinā pitrā ekacitto mahāmanāḥ|| 86 ||

tato bhūtyā viliptāṅgo rudrākṣāṃśca dadhau tanau|
dadau dānāni viprebhya āruhadbrahmaśekharam|| 87 ||

tatra niṣadhaśṛṅgo 'asau agamye sarvajīvinām|
bahudhātusamāyukte bahuratnasumiśrite|| 88 ||

kṛṣṇāyasamayaṃ liṅgaṃ saṃsthāpya vidhivat punaḥ|
tīrthodakena cāplāvya pūjāṃ cakre 'arhaṇaistataḥ|| 89 ||

divyāsane samāsīnaḥ prāṅmukha ṛjuvigrahaḥ|
tato nirīkṣya nāsāgram īṣatsamprekṣyalocanaḥ|| 90 ||

tato jajāpa vīro 'asau ekacitto dhiyā tadā|
divyavarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ dhyātvā dhyātvā punaḥ punaḥ|| 91 ||

tato varṣāvasāne vai āvirbhūto maheśvaraḥ|
āśvinaśuklasaptamyāṃ varadānāya bhaktine|| 92 ||

karbūro 'api mahātejā rudrabhaktiparāyaṇaḥ|
samprekṣya taṃ mahādevaṃ stotraṃ cakre mahāmanāḥ|| 93 ||

naikaṣeya uvāca |

śivaṃ śāntarūpaṃ śivākāradehaṃ śivārdhapraveśaṃ śivāṃśodbhavantam|
śivādyaṃ śivāṅgaṃ kṛpāsāgaraṃ taṃ mahānīlakaṇṭhaṃ bhaje 'ahaṃ bhaje 'aham|| 94 ||

.o namo jñānarūpāya sūkṣmarūpāya vai namaḥ|
jñānajñānāya śuddhāya sthūlatarāya te namaḥ|| 95 ||

devānām api devāya divyarūpāya te namaḥ|
parāya parameśāya pūjyatamāya te namaḥ|| 96 ||

parāparavimuktāya sarvapūjyāya te namaḥ|
nityāya nityarūpāya dīptāṅgāya namo namaḥ|| 97 ||

pūjyānām api pūjyāya pūjyapūjyātmane namaḥ|
dīptāya dīptanetrāya divyabhāvāya te namaḥ|| 98 ||

śaktirūpāya śāntāya śuddhyaikahetave namaḥ|
śuddhāya śuddharūpāya śuddhatamāya te namaḥ|| 99 ||

kālarūpāya kālāya kāntadehāya śambhave|
vyomāsthāya pramāṇāya vyomarūpāya vai namaḥ|| 100 ||

sarvamantraśarīrāya kālakālāya te namaḥ|
ajāya mantrarūpāya śuddhadehāya te namaḥ|| 101 ||

apramāṇāya devāya śaṃkarāya namo namaḥ|
dīptanetrāya sārāya sārarūpāya te namaḥ|| 102 ||

ādyāya sarvarūpāya anantāya namo namaḥ|
aghorāya ca ghorāya tatpuruṣāya namo namaḥ|| 103 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ nanāma ca punaḥ punaḥ|
lomāñcano mahāvīro vāṅmanovacanaistadā|| 104 ||

stotraṃ niśamya deveśo nairṛtasya ghaṭodbhava|
mumoda ca tadā rudro varaṃ ca dattavān vibhuḥ|| 105 ||

śarva uvāca |

varaṃ varaya dharmajña sarvavaram anuttamam|
dāsye tubhyam idānīṃ vai yat tvaṃ vāñchasi rākṣasa|| 106 ||

ekacittaṃ samādhāya pratapasi tapo varam|
suniścalaśca me bhakto 'ahiṃsaśca jitendriyaḥ|| 107 ||

tuṣṭo 'ahaṃ tapasā vatsa stotraiḥ sarvamanoharaiḥ|
māṃ kāmadaṃ ca jānīhi matvā varaya mām iti|| 108 ||

nairṛta uvāca |

yadi tuṣṭo 'asi sarvajña mayi kṣudre ca sāmpratam|
kṛpāsāgara śambho mām anukampayasi dhruvam|| 109 ||

dīyatāṃ bhagavan mahyaṃ dikpālatvaṃ tathāvidham|
yathaiva daṇḍine dattaṃ bhavatā ca purā vibho|| 110 ||

śarva uvāca |

dadāmi te mahābāho yaduktaṃ tat tvayā dhruvam|
tapasā te kaṭhoreṇa tuṣṭo 'ahaṃ ca stavaistathā|| 111 ||

tathāstu te mahāvīra yat te manasi vidyate|
vidigīśo bhavādyādi pālayaṃśca tadudbhavān|| 112 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ dattvā varaṃ tasmai bhaktāya ca mahātmane|
bhaktānāṃ vatsalo devaścāntardhānaṃ tato yayau|| 113 ||

tatrāgatya surāḥ sarve bṛhaspatimukhāstadā|
brahmā ca nāradaścaiva saptarṣayastathāpare|| 114 ||

abhiṣekaṃ dadustasmai hiraṇyakalaśaiḥ śubhaiḥ|
tīrthodakasusampūrṇairdevahastoddhṛtairmune|| 115 ||

nedurdundubhayastatra jayaśabdastathāvidhaḥ|
vavarṣuḥ sumanaḥsārā/llājāsārāṃśca nākataḥ|| 116 ||

abhiṣiñcya tato devā meroḥ sānuṃ yayurmudā|
kṛtvāgre nairṛtaṃ tatra brahmā ca tam arūrupat|| 117 ||

surāstam āropya yayuryathāgatā viriñcamukhyā vidigīśa ādṛtāḥ|
tataḥ samākarṇya tapaḥ kṛtaṃ tadā sa nairṛtenāpyakarojjaleśvaraḥ|| 118 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe mānassaromāhātmye nairṛtatapaḥsiddhirnāma pañcadaśo adhyāyaḥ|| 15 ||

agastya uvāca |

trikālajña mahāsena sarvajño 'asi na saṃśayaḥ|
varuṇena tapastaptaṃ kaṭhoraṃ ca mahātmanā|| 1 ||

ityuktaṃ bhavatā mahyaṃ śrotum icchāmyahaṃ ca tat|
ko 'asau devaḥ pracetāśca kenopadeśitaḥ prabho|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

śṛṇu bhakta pravakṣyāmi sarvaṃ taccaritaṃ mayi|
bhakto 'asi me mahāprājña nāradenopadeśitaḥ|| 3 ||

āsīt kaśyapaputro 'asau varuṇo nāma viśrutaḥ|
mahātmā ca mahātejā mahābalaparākramaḥ|| 4 ||

sarvadharmarato nityaṃ sarvavidyāviśāradaḥ|
viṣṇubhaktaḥ sadā dāntaḥ śivapūjanatatparaḥ|| 5 ||

sarvabhūtadayāśīlaścātithyārhaṇatatparaḥ|
satyavādī ca dharmiṣṭho jitendriyo mahāmuniḥ|| 6 ||

kadāciddivase pāśī sabhāmadhye sthito mune|
dadarśa nāradaṃ tatra ākāśādāgataṃ munim|| 7 ||

paryaṭan brahmalokādvai jaṭākalāpinaṃ kavim|
vīṇāvādyamahollāsaṃ vādayantaṃ muhurmuhuḥ|| 8 ||

saptasvarasadābhyāsaṃ navabhiśca rasairyutam|
gītatālamahollāsaṃ hiraṇyayajñasūtrakam|| 9 ||

rudrayaśaḥ pragāyantaṃ sūcakaṃ kalahapriyam|
samadṛṣṭiṃ ca lokeṣu kathyākathyasusūcakam|| 10 ||

udatiṣṭhat tam ālokya pāśī samāgataṃ mune|
sampūjyārghyaiḥ stavairarghyaṃ tam āsane nyaveśayat|| 11 ||

kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ pāśī nanāma ca muhurmuhuḥ|
bhaktyā ca kuśalaṃ praśnaṃ cakāra bhūriśo yatim|| 12 ||

varuṇa uvāca |

aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyam anāthasya sanāthatā|
bhavedadyāryamahatī yato bhavānihāgataḥ|| 13 ||

adya pūtaṃ mamāṅgaṃ yadadyaiva pitaro mudā|
bhuñjanti dattam adyaiva prākkṛtaṃ saphalaṃ bhavet|| 14 ||

bhavataḥ kiṃkaro 'ahaṃ vai yatkāryārtham ihāgataḥ|
