vārtāṃ prabodhitaṃ cārya kiṃ karomi vidhīyatām|| 15 ||

nārada uvāca |

na vaktavyaṃ tvayaivaṃ me śreṣṭha kaśyapasūnunā|
satyasandhaśca dharmātmā dānto 'asi sarvajantuṣu|| 16 ||

viṣṇubhaktaḥ śivātmā tvaṃ mama tulyo na saṃśayaḥ|
yo hi dharmarato nityaṃ śivapūjanatatparaḥ|| 17 ||

sampūjyaḥ sarvalokaiśca sa eva hi narottamaḥ|
sa mānyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tayormūrtiḥ sa eva hi|| 18 ||

viṣṇunā me purā proktaṃ rudreṇa ca tathāvidham|
mama bhaktaśca me mūrtiḥ syānnārada na saṃśayaḥ|| 19 ||

yat kiṃcicchraddhayā dattaṃ bhojanaṃ vā vasūni ca|
madbhaktāya sudharmiṣṭhairgṛhṇāmi tanmune dhruvam|| 20 ||

ityevaṃ varṇitaṃ mahyaṃ tathā rudreṇa viṣṇunā|
tadādi varuṇa prājña tadbhaktabhaktivānaham|| 21 ||

mamāgamanakāryaṃ te vakṣyāmi śṛṇu vistaram|
himavacchikhare ramye nairṛtena tapaḥ kṛtam|| 22 ||

ekacittaṃ samādhāya kaṭhoraṃ sumahattapaḥ|
divyavarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ prataptaṃ ca mahātmanā|| 23 ||

babhūva bhagavāṃstuṣṭastatrāgatya jalādhipa|
dadau mahāvaraṃ tasmai bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ|| 24 ||

dikpālatvaṃ tathānyacca mahābalaṃ parākramam|
vidigīśo bhava merau hartā kartā sa eva hi|| 25 ||

iti vārtāṃ samādāya āgato 'ahaṃ tavāntike|
dharmiṣṭhāya hi bhaktāya tubhyaṃ vaktuṃ ca nānyathā|| 26 ||

varuṇa uvāca |

aho citraṃ mahānatra yato labdhaṃ ca rakṣasā|
vidikpālyaṃ muniśreṣṭha sarvonnatabalaṃ tathā|| 27 ||

svātmoddhāraṇahetukyaṃ tapobalaṃ tapasvinām|
svārthena tapasā proktaṃ bhagavāṃstuṣṭavān katham|| 28 ||

nārada uvāca |

tapasā labhyate dharmaṃ tapasā nṛkalevaram|
tapasā prāpyate bhūtirdevadehastathā punaḥ|| 29 ||

tapasā labhyate mokṣam akāmena yadā caret|
tapasā labhyate svargo lakṣmīśca tapasā tathā|| 30 ||

medinīśastathā putra tapasā labhyate jagat|
tapasā prāpyate sarvaṃ sudurlabhaṃ na vidyate|| 31 ||

tapasā bhagavān rudro vaśyo viṣṇustathāvidhaḥ|
jagacca tapasā vaśyaṃ kiṃ punaḥ kṣudramānuṣāḥ|| 32 ||

kāṅkṣā cedbhavato vatsa kriyatāṃ duścaraṃ tapaḥ|
himavacchikhare divye kṛtvā vāñchāṃ pralabhyate|| 33 ||

varuṇa uvāca |

mamāpi vidyate kāmastapastaptuṃ ca nārada|
kasmin sthāne mahākṣetre kasmiṃstīrthe punarvibho|| 34 ||

kathyatāṃ me mahāprājña añjasā pūrvakaṃ ca yat|
tapasaśca vidhiḥ sarvastapasvin sarvavinmune|| 35 ||

nārada uvāca |

himavatpaścime śṛṅge trikūṭākhye suśobhane|
gaṅgāsudhātaraṅgiṇyormadhye tīrthe ca kāmade|| 36 ||

tatra snānāddivaṃ yānti sadehā nātra saṃśayaḥ|
pūjayanti surāḥ svarge snātakam arhaṇaiśca tam|| 37 ||

dhanyo 'asi kṛtakṛtyo 'asi sudhātīrthe mahātapāḥ|
āplutya vidhivadvatsa sadeho 'atra samāgataḥ|| 38 ||

evaṃ vadanti devā vai svarge ca varuṇāniśam|
yadi vāñchasi he pāśiṃstatra cārādhayeśvaram|| 39 ||

tvam api tasmin āplutya trikūṭaparvate tataḥ|
sthāpanaṃ kuru vai liṅgaṃ yadṛcchayā prajapyatām|| 40 ||

skanda uvāca |

ityuktvā nārado dhīrastatraivāntaradhīyata|
varuṇo 'api yayau tatra sudhātīrthe dhruvaṃ mudā|| 41 ||

sasnau tatra mahātīrthe vimale pāpahāriṇi|
sattvānāṃ durlabhe pūte sarvatīrthottamottame|| 42 ||

vidhivacca mahāprājño vibhūtibhūṣitastanuḥ|
rudrākṣāṃśca dadhau mantrī rudraṃ smaran dhiyā punaḥ|| 43 ||

tato dāyān dadau dhīmān viprebhyo hi ghaṭodbhava|
tato 'aruhadgiriṃ pāśī trikūṭākhyaṃ mahācalam|| 44 ||

tatra kūṭe mahāśṛṅge abhraṃlihisthalottame|
sphāṭikyaṃ nirmitaṃ liṅgaṃ cakre saṃsthāpanaṃ mudā|| 45 ||

divyāsane samāsīno bhūtvā ca prāṅmukhastataḥ|
apūpujanmudā liṅgaṃ tīrthodakaiḥ samarhaṇaiḥ|| 46 ||

divyavarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ tato jajāpa niścitaḥ|
varṣānte bhagavān rudra āvirbhūtaśca ambarāt|| 47 ||

saṃdṛśya śaṃkaraṃ pāśī jyotirūpaṃ vibhūtidam|
lomaharṣatanustasmai stavaṃ cakre tadā mune|| 48 ||

varuṇa uvāca |

.o, |

namo rudrāya devāya raudrāṇāṃ pataye namaḥ|
śakrotsavavidhātre ca kṛpīṭamūrtaye namaḥ|| 49 ||

namo harāya cogrāya kṛtāntecchāphalaprada|
kāleśvarāya kālāya kālātītāya vai namaḥ|| 50 ||

namastryakṣāya bhīmāya vyomakeśāya vai namaḥ|
karbūreśvaradevāya kauṇapavāñchitaprada|| 51 ||

namo 'ajāya ca devāya sthāṇvīśvarāya śambhave|
īśānāya śivāṅgāya śāśvate vai namo namaḥ|| 52 ||

arghyāya pūjyadehāya saṃsāradāya vai namaḥ|
sarvajñāya ca sarvāya lokānāṃ pataye namaḥ|| 53 ||

sarvavyādhihareśāna niḥśreyasāya te namaḥ|
bhadrāya bhadradehāya bhūteśvarāya te namaḥ|| 54 ||

namaḥ śivāya bhargāya jātavedaḥphalaprada|
kṛpīṭayonidevāya śakreśvarāya vai namaḥ|| 55 ||

namo maṅgalarūpāya akālamṛtyunāśine|
mṛtyuṃjayāya rudrāya śūlahastāya vai namaḥ|| 56 ||

divyarūpāya devāya divyānāṃ pataye namaḥ|
varābhayapradātre ca śāntadehāya vai namaḥ|| 57 ||

namaḥ śivapradattāya śivamārgapradeśine|
saṃsārasāradevāya śambho te satataṃ namaḥ|| 58 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya mahādevaḥ stavaṃ stavottamaṃ param|
varuṇena stutaṃ dhīman harṣaṃ cakre svabhaktine|| 59 ||

varadānāya deveśo bhaktāya bhaktavatsalaḥ|
uvāca vacanaṃ tasmai sarvabhūtaguhāviśaḥ|| 60 ||

śarva uvāca |

varaṃ varaya dharmajña varuṇa mama bhaktivit|
jñātvā māṃ sarvadaṃ vatsa mayi subhaktavatsale|| 61 ||

te bhaktyāhaṃ samāhūtaḥ preritastapasātra ca|
dadāmyahaṃ varaṃ tubhyaṃ yat tvaṃ vāñchasi sāmpratam|| 62 ||

varuṇa uvāca |

aho bhāgyam anāthasya mamaivādya phalaṃ bhavet|
yataḥ prākāśayat tejo jyotirūpakalevaraḥ|| 63 ||

yadi bhavenmayi snehaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛta|
nairṛtena ca yallabdhaṃ tanme dehi mahāvibho|| 64 ||

śarva uvāca |

bhavatā vāñchitaṃ karma tapasā bhāvitātmanā|
tat tathāstu varaṃ tubhyaṃ sarvavaram anuttamam|| 65 ||

adyaprabhṛti cārya tvaṃ prācye merorhi tiṣṭhasi|
hartā kartā tathā pālo bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ|| 66 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti dattvā varaṃ tasmai bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ|
antardhānaṃ yayau śīghraṃ yathāgato 'ambarāt tathā|| 67 ||

tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ śakrāgniśamanāstathā|
āyayustatra sabrahmā rākṣasā cāpsarogaṇāḥ|| 68 ||

munayo dadṛśustatra varuṇaṃ vai tapasvinam|
labdhavaraṃ mahātmānaṃ cintayantaṃ mahāvibhum|| 69 ||

tīrthodakaṃ samānīya sudhātīrthodbhavaṃ tataḥ|
abhiṣiñcita āryaiḥ sa hiraṇyakalaśaiḥ śubhaiḥ|| 70 ||

devaiḥ stavairjayaśabdairdevadvijamukhodbhavaiḥ|
nānāvādyodbhavairnādairvaṃśatālaghanasvanaiḥ|| 71 ||

tato brahmā paṭhan vedānabhiṣekaṃ dadau punaḥ|
saptarṣayo guruḥ siddhāḥ smarantaste mudā manum|| 72 ||

tato bhūyo 'antarīkṣādvai uvāca vacanaṃ vibhuḥ|
apāṃ patirbhavādyādi varuṇa madvaco yathā|| 73 ||

śrutveti vacanaṃ devā vyomasthatejasastanoḥ|
jayaśabdaṃ punaścakruḥ sādhu sādhviti vādinaḥ|| 74 ||

vavarṣuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi lājāsārāṃstathāpsarāḥ|
nanṛtuśca jagurdevyo mumudustatra devatāḥ|| 75 ||

tato yayuḥ surāḥ sarve purodhāya tapasvinam|
paścime diśi viprendra varuṇaṃ ca sumaṅgalaiḥ|| 76 ||

meroḥ sānau tam āsthāya cādhikāraṃ dadau vidhiḥ|
antardadhe tato brahmā devarṣayastathaiva ca|| 77 ||

tadādi pāśī diśi paścime vai bhavecca kartā hyavitā ca hartā|
tathāvidhaṃ gandhavaho 'api cakre tapaḥ kaṭhoraṃ sa suduścaraṃ yat|| 78 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe sudhātīrthamāhātmye varuṇatapaḥsiddhirnāma ṣoḍaśo adhyāyaḥ|| 16 ||

agastya uvāca |

tvanmukhāmbhojasambhūtaṃ skanda śabdasudhārasam|
pītvā karṇaputeṇāpi na tṛpyāmi tṛṣārtitaḥ|| 1 ||

vijṛmbhate mano me 'adya pānāya śaktidhṛk punaḥ|
tvanmukhānniḥsṛtasyārya gharmārtaḥ salilaṃ yathā|| 2 ||

ko 'asau vāyurmahātejāḥ kasya putro mahābalī|
tapastepe kaṭhoraṃ vai pralabdhavān varottamam|| 3 ||

kasmin sthāne mahāsena tīrthe bahuphalaprade|
idānīṃ śrotum icchāmi vada me tvaṃ yathāvidhi|| 4 ||

skanda uvāca |

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ mahābhāga vāyorvṛttāntam eva ca|
idānīṃ saṃvidhāsyāmi mayi yathā tvayādhunā|| 5 ||

āsīdditirmahāsādhvī kaśyapasya mahāmuneḥ|
bhāryā tapasvinī dhīra bahuputravatī sukhī|| 6 ||

devāsure mahāyuddhe tasyāḥ putrāñchacīpatiḥ|
jaghāna sakalān vīrāṃstataḥ śokāturābhavat|| 7 ||

tataḥ sā īrṣayā sādhvī putrahantuḥ śacīpateḥ|
satīvrataṃ tapaścakre śakranāśāya hetukī|| 8 ||

tataḥ sā toṣayāmāsa kaśyapaṃ snātakaṃ patim|
varaṃ vavre tataḥ sādhvī putranidhanakarṣiṇī|| 9 ||

ditiruvāca |

bhagavan vipra dharmajña yadi sneho 'asti me vibho|
yāce 'ahaṃ tvāṃ varaṃ śubhraṃ śakranāśasya hetukam|| 10 ||

dehi me vipra taṃ putram sarvonnataparākramam|
haniṣyati ca yaḥ śakraṃ mama putranisūdanam|| 11 ||

kaśyapa uvāca |

tathāstu te priye sādhvī yat tvaṃ vāñchasi sāmpratam|
tapaso durlabhaṃ nāsti hṛdvāñchā tapasodbhavā|| 12 ||

bhaviṣyati suto devi tava sādhvyā pativrate|
śakraṃ putro nihantā vai yadyevaṃ vratam ācareḥ|| 13 ||

śaucāddhārayase devi garbhaṃ ca śaradaḥ śatam|
prasūyasi tataḥ putraṃ trailokyonmathane kṣamam|| 14 ||

skanda uvāca |

upagamya tato dityāṃ garbham ādhāya kaśyapaḥ|
rocayan vai suraśreṣṭhaṃ devānāṃ gaṇahetukam|| 15 ||

jagāma parvataśreṣṭhaṃ himavantaṃ mahācalam|
tapase ca muniśreṣṭhaḥ sarvabhūtapitāmahaḥ|| 16 ||

tato ditirmahāsādhvī dhārayāmāsa retasam|
garbhaṃ tejaḥ sudurdharṣam avadhyaṃ prāṇibhiḥ suraiḥ|| 17 ||

sā śuciḥ sarvakāleṣu sarvadharmaratā śubhā|
vrateṣu tatparā strīṇāṃ satyasandhā jitendriyā|| 18 ||

tasmin kāle ghaṭodbhūta jagāma nārado divam|
ādāya sarvavārtāṃ ca tasyā yaccaritaṃ muniḥ|| 19 ||

gāyan rudrayaśo dhīmān saṃvādya ballakīṃ muhuḥ|
gītavādye rato dhīraḥ sarvalokābhisūcakaḥ|| 20 ||

tato 'adarśat sunāsīraḥ samāyāntaṃ ca nāradam|
ballakīṃ vādayante vai rudrayaśaḥ pragāyanam|| 21 ||

udatiṣṭhat tadā śakraḥ siṃhāsanāt puro gataḥ|
tam āsane samānīya vidhivadupaveśayat|| 22 ||

apūpujat tataḥ sādhum arhaṇaiḥ susamāhitaiḥ|
sampūjya vidhivacchakraḥ praśnaṃ cakre mahāmunim|| 23 ||

śakra uvāca |

svāgataṃ te muniśreṣṭha kuśalaṃ te kalevaram|
lokeṣu sarvabhūteṣu kuśalaṃ vidyate kvacit|| 24 ||

brahmaputra dvijaśreṣṭha pavitrāya tanośca vā|
samāgato 'atra devarṣirmamopajīvino yataḥ|| 25 ||

kalpata iti bhadrāya mahātmanāṃ samāgamaḥ|
bhadrāya gamanaṃ kāryaṃ vada me munisattama|| 26 ||

nārada uvāca |

śṛṇu śakra dhruvaṃ tattvaṃ mamāgamanakāraṇam|
vimātuścaritaṃ dityāstavādbhutakṛtaṃ tapaḥ|| 27 ||

nānādharmopavāsaiśca bahuniyamasaṃyutaiḥ|
saṃtoṣitaḥ pitā te vai yācito 'asau varaṃ tayā|| 28 ||

yo haniṣyati śakraṃ vai bahubalaparākramaḥ|
hantāraṃ mama putrāṇāṃ taṃ putraṃ dehi me prabho|| 29 ||

kaśyapo 'api dadau tasyai varaṃ varamahādbhutam|
ditirdadhāra garbhaṃ sā niyamasthā tadutsukā|| 30 ||

upāyaṃ kuru devendra yadi cedātmanaḥ śubham|
yāvacca nāgato vighnastāvacca yatnavān sudhīḥ|| 31 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ saṃvarṇya śakrāya antardhānaṃ yayau muniḥ|
devendro 'api tadākarṇya vacanaṃ munibhāṣitam|
kṣemāya hi ātmano dhīra śatrūṇāṃ nidhanāya ca|| 32 ||

ādāya vai mahadvajraṃ yayau yatra ditiḥ sthitā|
śakro dharmacyutiṃ tasyāṃ chidrānveṣaṇatatparaḥ|| 33 ||

babhūvāharniśaṃ tatra channātmā saṃcaran mune|
upāgamya śanaistāṃ vai channātmā darśayan rahaḥ|| 34 ||

kadā dharmacyutiḥ syācca etasyā iti tatparaḥ|
nityam evaṃ carañchakro 'amarṣapūritaḥ sadā|| 35 ||

ekasaṃvatsare nyūne śatābde 'apaśyadantaram|
akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucaṃ salilaṃ nopasaṃspṛśan|| 36 ||

bhrāntacittena śayyāyāṃ tataḥ śete ditistadā|
nidrāvaśaṃ gatā sādhvī gurviṇī sā priyaṃvadā|| 37 ||

tato dadarśa vajrī tām aśaucacaraṇāśayām|
tasyāḥ kukṣiṃ samāviśya garbhaṃ śakro mahābalaḥ|| 38 ||

ciccheda kuliśenāśu saptadhā kṛtavāṃstataḥ|
vidāritaḥ sa vajreṇa garbho ruroda nirbharam|| 39 ||

tato 'avadadvṛṣā tasmai mā rodīcca bhavān vṛthā|
tadaṃśaṃ ca vṛṣā bhūyaḥ saptadhā saptadhācchinat|| 40 ||

tato 'abravīcca taṃ śakraḥ sakhā bhavedbhavān hi me|
yadi tvaṃ mucyate no cejjīvitaṃ tvaṃ na mucyate|| 41 ||

garbha āha ca yasmai vai yathā vadasi tat tathā|
tataḥ śakro vinirgatya saṃtuṣṭavān manorathaiḥ|
vijvaro 'asau yayau dhīro lalitām amarāvatīm|| 42 ||

tato garbhāt samudbhūto vāyurnāma mahābalī|
sarveṣām ojasaḥ sāraḥ sarvalokaprakampanaḥ|| 43 ||

ūnapañcāśadātmāsau sarvatejomayastanuḥ|
sarvabhūtaguhāśāyī sarvonnataparākramaḥ|| 44 ||

tataḥ prasannāḥ kakubho bhaveyustadīyasambhūtidine nikāmam|
surāśca mandā hṛdayena cāsaṃstadā yayau tatra muniḥ saharṣam|| 45 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe vāyorutpattirnāma saptadaśo adhyāyaḥ|| 17 ||

skanda uvāca |

sabhāmadhye sthite vāyau kasmiṃściddivase mune|
yadṛcchayāgataṃ tatra nāradaṃ munisattamam|| 1 ||

dadarśa sa mahābhāgo vīṇāhastaṃ kalāpinam|
gāyantaṃ susvaraṃ gītaṃ vādayantaṃ muhurmuhuḥ|| 2 ||

tato vāyurmahātejā udatiṣṭhat sabhātalāt|
pratyudyayau muniṃ mānyaṃ parivāraiśca mantribhiḥ|| 3 ||

sampūjya vidhivat pūjyam arghyam arghyārhaṇairmudā|
nanāma cāsane dhīmān samupāveśayanmunim|| 4 ||

tataḥ pracetaso vārtāṃ tena pṛṣṭaśca nāradaḥ|
sarvāṃ tāṃ varṇayāmāsa vāyave munisattamaḥ|| 5 ||

vāyuruvāca |

hiraṇyagarbhasambhūta sarvavārtāviśārada|
kasmin sthāne mahākṣetre tapaḥsiddhirbhaveddhruvam|| 6 ||

mamāpi vartate vāñchā tapastaptuṃ suniścitam|
adya brahmannanāthāya mahyaṃ hi copadiśyatām|| 7 ||

nārada uvāca |

aho dhanyatamo vāyo vata ceto mahādbhutam|
īdṛśī buddhirāryasya durlabhaḥ kiṃ vidhīyate|| 8 ||

himavati nagaśreṣṭhe paścimottaramadhyataḥ|
sphāṭikādrirmahātuṅgo yasmādbrahmanadījanuḥ|| 9 ||

tayośca saṃgame tīrthe sarvatīrthottamottame|| 10 ||

tatra snātvā divaṃ yāti sarvapāpairvivarjitaḥ|
brahmahatyādipāpebhyaḥ sa mukto nātra saṃśayaḥ|| 11 ||

yadyadicchati taṃ taṃ vai kāmaṃ prāpnoti niścitam|
brahmatīrthe mahāvīra snānaṃ tatra karoti yaḥ|| 12 ||

brahmaṇā ca kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ snānaṃ bhūtodbhavāya ca|
sampūjya śaṃkaraṃ tatra tataḥ sṛṣṭiṃ cakāra saḥ|| 13 ||

tasmiṃstīrthe mahāpuṇye snānaṃ karoti yaḥ punaḥ|
pravihāyodbhavaṃ sadyo brahmatvaṃ yāti bhaktibhiḥ|| 14 ||

tatra snātvā mahātīrthe sphaṭikādrau tapaḥ kuru|
bhūtyā pralepito deho rudrākṣān dhārayānila|| 15 ||

saṃsthāpya vidhivalliṅgaṃ sarvadaṃ taṃ maheśvaram|
jitendriyo jitakrodhaḥ prajapyatāṃ yadṛcchayā|| 16 ||

skanda uvāca |

evam uktvā tatastasmai cāntardhānaṃ yayau muniḥ|
nārado devavandyo 'asau sarvavārtāprasūcakaḥ|| 17 ||

tato vāyuryayau vipra himālayaṃ nagottamam|
brahmatīrthaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ bhūyaḥ pāpapraṇāśakam|| 18 ||

prāpaśyaddharṣito vāyuryaduktaṃ nāradena tam|
tatra sasnau sukhaṃ vīraḥ pronmajjya salile mudā|| 19 ||

tataḥ sasnau punarbhūtyā sarvāṅgeṣu ca mantravit|
rudrākṣāṃśca dadhārāṅge dadau dānāni bhūriśaḥ|| 20 ||

tataḥ sphaṭikaśailendraṃ śuddhaṃ sunirmalaṃ mune|
samāruhadameyātmā rājatābhaṃ mahācalam|| 21 ||

saṃsthāpya vidhivalliṅgaṃ tatra pittalasambhavam|
apūpujat tadā devaṃ sarvāsuranamaskṛtam|| 22 ||

gandhaiḥ puṣpaistathā dīpaistīrthodakaiśca mantravit|
ṛjukāyaḥ samāsīnaḥ sarvadvandvavivarjitaḥ|| 23 ||

tato jajāpe sarvātmā ekacitto mahābalaḥ|
divyavarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ ṣaḍvargaiḥ saṃvivarjitaḥ|| 24 ||

tataśca bhagavān rudra āvirbhūtastadantike|
taṃ pradarśitavān vāyuḥ stotraṃ cakāra mahātmane|| 25 ||

vāyuruvāca |

namo bhavāya bhavyāya virūpāya surūpiṇe|
kālātītāya kālāya karmarūpa namo 'astu te|| 26 ||

tejasāṃ puñjadehāya sarvatejomayātmane|
jyotiṣāṃ jyotiraṃśāya jyotirūpa namo 'astu te|| 27 ||

sarvapraṇatadevāya svayam apraṇatāya vai|
sarvadāya ca śarvāya sarveśvara namo 'astu te|| 28 ||

bahurūpāya rudrāya muktasaṃśaya te namaḥ|
buddhātmane maheśāya śuddhadeha namo 'astu te|| 29 ||

ekasmai ca dvirūpāya bahudehāya te namaḥ|
ekānanāya devāya dvivaktrāya namo namaḥ|| 30 ||

bahuvaktrāya bhargāya nakṣatreśalalāṭine|
śūline brahmarūpāya viṣṇurūpāya te namaḥ|| 31 ||

namaḥ sthūlāya sūkṣmāya sthūlasūkṣmasudehine|
lakṣyāya samalakṣyāya lakṣyālakṣasvarūpiṇe|| 32 ||

kāmeśvarāya kāmāya kāmadāya ca kāmine|
kālarātrikalāṃśāya kāmakānta namo 'astu te|| 33 ||

īśānāya maheśāya tatpuruṣāya śāśvate|
harāya vāmadevāya vyomakeśāya vai namaḥ|| 34 ||

sadyojātāya raudrāya mahādevāya vai namaḥ|
aghorāya ca ghorāya ghoradeha namo 'astu te|| 35 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti stutiṃ samākarṇya devadeva umāpatiḥ|
saṃtuṣṭavāṃstato dhīra vāyunā varayoginā|| 36 ||

uvāca śaṃkaro devo vāyave sutapasvine|
bhaktāya bhaktyatisneho varaṃ dātuṃ samāgataḥ|| 37 ||

śarva uvāca |

aho vatsa tvayā taptaṃ kaṭhoraṃ sumahat tapaḥ|
dhanyo 'ataḥ kṛtakṛtyo 'asi sarvalokaiḥ suduścaram|| 38 ||

atrāgatastavāhūtaḥ preritaste tapo hṛdā|
dāsye 'adhunā varaṃ tubhyaṃ sarvadevasudurlabham|| 39 ||

māṃ kāmadaṃ mahābāho jñātvedānīṃ na saṃśayaḥ|
sarvade mayi yadvāyo yācyatāṃ te yadīpsitam|| 40 ||

vāyuruvāca |

aho bhāgyaṃ mamedānīṃ yatastuṣṭo bhavān bhṛśam|
mayi kṣudre bhaveddāse kiṃ vidheyam ataḥ param|| 41 ||

agocaro mahādevaḥ sarvatejomayo vibhuḥ|
bhavedadya ca netrasya kṣudrasya mama gocaraḥ|| 42 ||

ābhāṣaṇo viśeṣeṇa bhaveddevasya sāmpratam|
sarvadevapravandyasya kiṃ vidheyam ataḥ param|| 43 ||

yadi dadāsi me deva lokabhūtānukampaka|
tvayi bhaktirato nityaṃ tvatpūjane ca tatparaḥ|| 44 ||

tvatpādasmaraṇaṃ nityaṃ te nāmagrahaṇaṃ tathā|
tvadvandane ca tātparyaṃ saṃśravaṇe ca te kathā|| 45 ||

iti bhaktirmahādeva nānyaṃ tattvaṃ ca yācyase|
dadasva jagadīśāna bhaktijña bhaktavatsala|| 46 ||

śarva uvāca |

naḥ kāmaścet tavedānīṃ bhavedvāyo 'atra niścayaḥ|
tathāpi te pradāsye 'ahaṃ varaṃ loke sudurlabham|| 47 ||

tapobhii ropitā vṛkṣā dṛḍhamūlāḥ phalanti yat|
tatphalāni ca dāsyanti kartṛbhyaḥ śākhinaḥ sukham|| 48 ||

adāne ca samarthāste bhavanti śākhino 'api kim|
tapo mūlaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ tapasyā tu garīyasī|| 49 ||

tapobhiśca bhavet svāmī hartā kartā ca pālakaḥ|
tasmāt taporjitaṃ karma anyathā kiṃ prakurvate|| 50 ||

yasmāt tvayā prataptaṃ hi sarvadevasuduścaram|
adyaprabhṛti cāryastvaṃ jagatprāṇo bhavāniśam|| 51 ||

tvāṃ vinā sarvalokāśca śavā eva bhavantu te|
tvayā pradhāryatāṃ lokā jagacca sacarācaram|| 52 ||

alakṣo bhava martyānāṃ manmūrtistvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ|
sarvagandhavaho 'ajasraṃ sarvonnatabalo vahaḥ|| 53 ||

saṃvartake jagat sarvaṃ salokaṃ sacarācaram|
saṃhariṣyāmyahaṃ vāyo tava mūrtyā na saṃśayaḥ|| 54 ||

ato lokā vadanti ārya tvāṃ sarvatra prabhañjanam|
mama ca te na bhedo 'asti eka eva parākramaḥ|| 55 ||

paścimottaradigbhāge tiṣṭha meroḥ sadāgatiḥ|
tataḥ pālaya samyak tvaṃ tatrasthān sacarācarān|| 56 ||

tatra hartā bhavārya tvaṃ rakṣakaśca viśeṣataḥ|
sraṣṭā ca bhava nityaṃ tvaṃ gacchānila yathāsukham|| 57 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ sambhāṣyamāṇo 'ajo varaṃ dattvā ca vāyave|
antardhānaṃ yayau śīghraṃ bahutejoyuto vibhuḥ|| 58 ||

tato devāḥ sagandharvā nārado bṛhatāṃ patiḥ|
saptarṣayastathā siddhā hāhā hūhūstathāpare|| 59 ||

brahmā ca vibudhaśreṣṭha indravahnī tathā yamaḥ|
rākṣaso varuṇo dhīra tatrāyayurmudānvitāḥ|| 60 ||

tato dadṛśurvāyuṃ te labdhavaraṃ mahādbhutam|
tejasvinaṃ tapasthaṃ vai rudrabhaktaṃ śivātmakam|| 61 ||

dṛṣṭavāṃśca tato brahmā sarvabhūtāśrayo dvija|
uvāca vacanaṃ tebhyo 'abhiṣekāya tapasvine|| 62 ||

ānīyadhvaṃ mahātmāno brahmatīrthodbhavaṃ jalam|
abhiṣekaṃ pradāsyāmi yathājñayā śivasya ca|| 63 ||

tato devāḥ samānīya tīrthodakaṃ pavitrakam|
brahmaṇe ca dadurvipra cādāya kalaśairmudā|| 64 ||

samuddhṛtya paṭhan vedānudaṅmukhastha ātmabhūḥ|
abhiṣekaṃ dadau tasmai hiraṇyakalaśairmudā|| 65 ||

divi devagaṇāḥ sarve vādyaṃ cakrurmahādbhutam|
jayaśabdaṃ tathā cāsīdvavarṣuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭayaḥ|| 66 ||

nanṛtuścāpsarovṛndā gītairmṛdaṅgavādyakaiḥ|
guruḥ sucandanaiścārya tam apūjat samarhaṇaiḥ|| 67 ||

tato devagaṇā vipra harṣotphullāḥ suhṛdgaṇāḥ|
samānīya tam āśugaṃ vidiśi sthāpayituṃ yayuḥ|| 68 ||

svaṃ svaṃ diśaṃ tadā vipra cādhikāraṃ tapasvine|
dattvā brahmā yayau tasmai tirohito mahāprabhuḥ|| 69 ||

tataḥ kubero 'api cakāra nūnaṃ tapo mukhādviśravaso himādrau|
hiraṇyarājyaṃ pravisarjya laṅkāṃ vidhāya kāmaṃ hṛdi rudrabhaktim|| 70 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe brahmatīrthamāhātmye vāyutapaḥsiddhirnāmāṣṭādaśo adhyāyaḥ|| 18 ||

agastya uvāca |

kasmiñchṛṅge tapaścakre kubera iti naḥ śrutaḥ|
ko 'asau kasyājñayā skanda kasya putro mahābalī|| 1 ||

ityetacchrotum icchāmi tvatto brahmavidāṃ vara|
karma ca yat kṛtaṃ tena tat sarvaṃ vada me prabho|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

brahmaṇo mānasodbhūtaḥ pulastyo nāma viśrutaḥ|
tatputro viśravāḥ khyātaḥ kuberaḥ syāt tadātmajaḥ|| 3 ||

guhyakakanyakājāto mahābalaparākramaḥ|
patis sa eva yakṣāṇām ekākṣapiṅgalo mune|| 4 ||

rudrabhaktirato nityaṃ śivapūjanatatparaḥ|
rudrākṣī bhasmasusnāyī rudramantraparāyaṇaḥ|| 5 ||

kvacit kālāntare 'atīte tyaktvā laṅkāṃ samāgataḥ|
uttare himavatpāde yatra gokarṇaśūlabhṛt|| 6 ||

bhrātrākrānte pure yakṣo balīyasā tapoyujā|
rāvaṇenānujenāśu audāsīnyaḥ sucintanaḥ|| 7 ||

praṇamya śirasā tātaṃ bahuvidyāsupāragam|
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā parikramya punaḥ punaḥ|| 8 ||

pitaraṃ tatra cāpṛcchadviśravasaṃ tapaḥphalam|
pūjayantaṃ mahārudraṃ dhyāyamānaṃ suniścalam|| 9 ||

kubera uvāca |

tāta sarvajña bhakto 'asi sarvavārtāviśārada|
sarvadharmarato nityaṃ sarvaprāṇyanukampaka|| 10 ||

ko dharmaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ śreṣṭhaścātra vidhīyatām|
yadanuṣṭhānamātreṇa labhyate paramā gatiḥ|| 11 ||

balenākrāntitā laṅkā rāvaṇena balīyasā|
tasyāṃ sthātuṃ samartho no bhavet tāta parākramaḥ|| 12 ||

ataścātrāgato 'ahaṃ vai kariṣyāmi kadārya kim|
atha vā śaraṇaṃ dehi tvaṃ rudraśca prasevyate|| 13 ||

viśravā uvāca |

śṛṇu putra pravakṣyāmi bhrāturyaccaritaṃ tava|
puṣpakena rathenaiva tvam āgato 'atra vai yadā|| 14 ||

ālokya rāvaṇastvāṃ ca rathasthaṃ samahotsavam|
tato duḥkhāturo 'abhūt sa apṛcchanmātaraṃ tadā|| 15 ||

namaste 'astu satī mātaḥ kaḥ puruṣa ihāgataḥ|
puṣpakena ca tejasvī devakanyāsamāyutaḥ|| 16 ||

iti vacaḥ samākarṇya putrasya nikaṣā punaḥ|
putrāya kathayāmāsa putrasnehavatī ca sā|| 17 ||

jyeṣṭhabhrātā tavāsau vai kubero nāma viśrutaḥ|
purā rudraṃ samārādhya gokarṇeśam apūpujat|| 18 ||

tataḥ saṃtuṣṭavān rudro dadau tasmai mudātmaja|
puṣpakaṃ nāma divyaṃ vai yānaṃ ca kāmagaṃ śivam|| 19 ||

tadyānena samāyātaḥ kubero nātra saṃśayaḥ|
yadi putra tavecchograṃ tvam ārādhaya śaṃkaram|| 20 ||

tato māturvacaḥ śrutvā rāvaṇo 'api prahṛṣṭavān|
gokarṇeśaṃ samārādhya apūpujanmudā punaḥ|| 21 ||

tato bhūyo mahātmāsau prayajñe ca mahāmakham|
chittvā chittvā svamūrdhānaṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti saḥ|| 22 ||

āvirbhūtastato rudraḥ pūrvaṃ gatvā daśānanam|
uvāca vacanaṃ tasmai varaṃ gṛhāṇa vatsa te|| 23 ||

rāvaṇena varo vavre vavre ca kalahaṃ mithaḥ|
tvaṃ vṛṇu tvaṃ vṛṇu procya ceti mānī daśānanaiḥ|| 24 ||

bhūya uvāca bhūteśaḥ sarvabhaktiṣu vatsalaḥ|
varaṃ gṛhāṇa he vatsa yat tvaṃ vāñchasi sāmpratam|| 25 ||

rāvaṇa uvāca |

bhavatā dīyate ceddhi mahyaṃ varam anuttamam|
bhaktavatsala mahādeva sarvaduḥkhavimocaka|| 26 ||

yāce 'adyāhaṃ ca te bhaktiṃ pūrvaṃ tataḥ paraṃ punaḥ|
avadhyatvaṃ varaṃ bhadraṃ divyaujasaṃ sadā ca me|| 27 ||

vibudhairasuraiścaiva gandharvaiḥ kiṃnaraistathā|
yakṣāṇāṃ ca gaṇairdeva vidyādharairviśeṣataḥ|| 28 ||

avadhyatvaṃ sadā śambho sarvonnataparākramam|
grahāḥ sarve ca me dāsā bhavantu ca sadā vibho|| 29 ||

kṛpayasi yadi tvaṃ mām idānīṃ sarvada prabho|
etānyeva varānyevaṃ dadasva me hi śaṃkara|| 30 ||

narakṣudraiścāvadhyatvaṃ na yāce 'ahaṃ mahāprabho|
kīṭatulyabalaiḥ kiṃ tu tārkṣyeṇa caṭakairiva|| 31 ||

śarva uvāca |

tathāstu te mahāvīra yat tvaṃ kāṅkṣasi suvrata|
bhūyo dadāmi te bhakta devadānavadurlabham|| 32 ||

caturadhikam eva ca pañcāśadyugamedhatām|
bhavāṃśca tāvantīṃ saṃkhyāṃ rājyaṃ karotu nirbharam|| 33 ||

viśravā uvāca |

iti dattvā varaṃ tasmai antardadhe mudā vibhuḥ|
tadādi rāvaṇo mānī lokān no 'agaṇayadbhṛśam|| 34 ||

gaccha putra mahābāho tapastaptuṃ yadṛcchayā|
himālaye nagaśreṣṭhe uttare śikhare gireḥ|| 35 ||

hiraṇyāḍhye mahākūṭe hiraṇyavṛkṣasaṃyute|
jāmbūnadalatāpūrṇe jāmbūnadarasodbhave|| 36 ||

agamye sarvasattvānāṃ ṣaḍvargaiḥ suvivarjite|
mahāmanohare ramye tatra saṃsthāpayeśvaram|| 37 ||

tadadhaśca mahātīrthe vimale devapūjite|
sarvakāmaprade bhadre suvinirmuktasaṃśaye|| 38 ||

brahmaputranadaśreṣṭhaḥ svarṇarasā nadīvarā|
tayośca saṃgame putra jñānatīrtham udāhṛtam|| 39 ||

tasmiṃstīrthe mahāpuṇye saṃskṛte brahmaṇā purā|
āpasparśanamātreṇa jātisaṃsmaraṇaṃ labhet|| 40 ||

pūrvajanmakṛtaṃ yadyajjñāyate tatkṣaṇājjanaiḥ|
tatrādau samyagāplāvya japyatāṃ te yadṛcchayā|| 41 ||

vibhūtyā lepayedgātraṃ rudrākṣān dhehi mantrakaiḥ|
sampūjya vidhivalliṅgaṃ niścalaḥ sujitendriyaḥ|| 42 ||

skanda uvāca |

ākarṇya ca piturvākyaṃ kuberastvaritaṃ yayau|
jñānatīrthe tapaḥ kartuṃ himavadbrahmaśekhare|| 43 ||

tatra snātvā yathoktaṃ vai pitrā ca vidhipūrvakam|
dattvā dāyāṃstataḥ śaile liṅgaṃ sthāpitavān mune|| 44 ||

divyaṃ varṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ jajāpa sa yathāsukham|
kubero hi tato 'agastya stotraṃ cakāra niścitaḥ|| 45 ||

kubera uvāca |

yena dattaṃ purā bhadraṃ śakrāya suradurlabham|
dikpālatvaṃ ca rājatvaṃ devānāṃ ca namo namaḥ|| 46 ||

yena dattaṃ punaḥ kṣemaṃ vahnaye tīkṣṇatejase|
vidikpālyaṃ samīśatvaṃ tasmai devāya vai namaḥ|| 47 ||

yena dattaṃ mahadbhavyaṃ kālāya balam uttamam|
pitṛṇāṃ ca patitvaṃ vai tasmai devāya vai namaḥ|| 48 ||

yena dattaṃ varaṃ bhūyo nairṛtāya parākramam|
devāsuramahotkṛṣṭaṃ tasmai devāya vai namaḥ|| 49 ||

yena bhūyaḥ pradattaṃ vai varuṇāya surārhaṇam|
param apāṃpatitvaṃ ca tasmai devāya vai namaḥ|| 50 ||

yena śivaṃ pradattaṃ vai jīvaiśvaryaṃ ca vāyave|
digīśatvaṃ mahābāho tasmai devāya vai namaḥ|| 51 ||

namo bhadrāya bhargāya namaḥ śivāya śūline|
namaḥ paśupadevāya śaṃkarāya namo namaḥ|| 52 ||

namo jyotiḥsvarūpāya namo 'alakṣāya dehine|
namo 'ajāya girīśāya harāya ca namo namaḥ|| 53 ||

namo nirañjaneśāya nirlepāya ca tejase|
lokapraṇatadehāya śāśvate vai namo namaḥ|| 54 ||

dhvānte bhavārṇave magnaḥ proddhṛto yena līlayā|
janmamṛtyūddhṛto yena tasmai devāya vai namaḥ|| 55 ||

skanda uvāca |

tataḥ praharṣito vipra guhyakasya stavairbhṛśam|
samāgatya mahādeva āvirbhūtastadantike|| 56 ||

dṛṣṭvā tapasvinaṃ dāntaṃ nirmamaṃ bhaktisaṃyutam|
uvāca vacanaṃ harṣaṃ varaṃ dātuṃ svabhaktine|| 57 ||

īśvara uvāca |

aho dhanyatamo bhakta mayi bhāvo nirantaram|
trividhastapasaṃyukto vidyate guhyakeśvara|| 58 ||

varaṃ gṛhāṇa me bhakta yat te vāñchā sudurlabhā|
sarveṣām unnataṃ tejo bhavatu te parākramaḥ|| 59 ||

rājarājo bhavādyādirudīcyāṃ bhava dikpatiḥ|
tatrasthānāṃ hi kartā tvaṃ merorme hi prasādataḥ|| 60 ||

bhūyo navanidhīnāṃ ca pālako bhava me tathā|
dvipañcāśacca koṭīnāṃ mattaḥ pragṛhyatāṃ tvayā|| 61 ||

adyaprabhṛtirārya tvaṃ mama sakhā bhavāniśam|
na muñcāmi kṣaṇaṃ hi tvāṃ priyabhakta kubera vai|| 62 ||

skanda uvāca |

pradāyaivaṃ varaṃ rudro devānṛṣīn samāhvayat|
svādhyakṣapriyabhaktāyābhiṣekaṃ dātuṃ tatkṣaṇāt|| 63 ||

tataḥ samāyayurdevāḥ sabrahmāḥ sapurohitāḥ|
ṛṣayaśca tathā siddhā yakṣagandharvakiṃnarāḥ|| 64 ||

īśvarasya samādāya cājñāṃ lokapitāmahaḥ|
devān paṭhan dadau tasmai tīrthatoyaiḥ prapūrakaiḥ|| 65 ||

hiraṇyakalaśairbhavyaiḥ siddhā mantraṃ japaṃstathā|
ṛṣayo vyāhṛtiṃ smṛtya stotrairdevagaṇāstathā|| 66 ||

tataścārcya gururdivyaiścandanairvividhaistadā|
arhayāmāsa pūjābhirāśīrvādaṃ dadau punaḥ|| 67 ||

tato dundubhayo nedurjagurgandharvakiṃnarāḥ|
vavarṣuḥ kusumasārā āsījjayaravo divi|| 68 ||

udīcyāṃ diśi saṃsthāpya kuberaṃ meruśekhare|
tirodhānaṃ yayau rudro devāḥ svaṃ svaṃ diśaṃ yayuḥ|| 69 ||

mahesvaro 'api prasabhaṃ digīśo 'abhavacca viprārya yadṛcchayādau|
himādrikūṭe svayam eva cakre tapaḥ kaṭhoraṃ suradurlabhaṃ ca|| 70 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe jñānatīrthamāhātmye kuberatapaḥsiddhirnāmonaviṃśatitamo adhyāyaḥ|| 19 ||

agastya uvāca |

sarvajño 'asi mahāsena sarvavārtāviśārada|
taporūpaḥ svayaṃ rudro hartā kartā ca rakṣakaḥ|| 1 ||

lokānāṃ varado nityaṃ phaladaśca tapasvinām|
sa kathaṃ ca tapastepe bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ|| 2 ||

jyotirūpo mahādeva icchārūpo mahāvibhuḥ|
nirvikāraśca saddevastejaḥpuñjo vibhāvyate|| 3 ||

alakṣyaḥ sarvalokānāṃ yataḥ prāpyanti devatāḥ|
vāñchitāni phalāni ārya tena prāptaṃ kutaḥ phalam|| 4 ||

bhoktā sa eva bhojyaṃ ca yajñarūpaḥ sa eva hi|
havirghṛtaṃ tathā dravyaṃ yajamānaḥ sa eva hi|| 5 ||

hotā vahnistathā mantro vedā japyaḥ sa eva ca|
lokasākṣī sa evāryaḥ sarvadevāśrayo vibhuḥ|| 6 ||

iti me saṃśayo jātaḥ śrutvāścaryaṃ tvayi prabho|
chindhi tanmama senānī tvaṃ suvaco 'asi no dhruvam|| 7 ||

skanda uvāca |

tejasvināṃ ca devānāṃ caritaṃ paramādbhutam|
na kṛto 'atra ca saṃdeho munibhiśca purā dvija|| 8 ||

dharmarakṣāya lokānāṃ lokasaṃsthāpanāya ca|
satapo dharmarūpo 'asi dharmaṃ samācaredvibhuḥ|| 9 ||

dharmeṇa saṃsthitā pṛthvī saparvatā sasāgarā|
satyavatī ca dharmeṇa dharmājjīvanado ghanaḥ|| 10 ||

dharmeṇa bhāgyam āpnoti dharmeṇa saṃtatiṃ labhet|
ciraṃ jīvati dharmeṇa puruṣāyuśca labhyate|| 11 ||

dharmeṇānandayeccetaḥ sukhaṃ dharmeṇa labhyate|
yadvāñchā vidyate svānte dharmeṇa tat pralabhyate|| 12 ||

lobhamohau tathā krodho madamātsarya eva ca|
duḥkhakleṣau ca dāridryam adharmeṇa pralabhyate|| 13 ||

tasmāt sadasatīṃ kartuṃ sthitiḥ sadasadātmakaḥ|
sarvalokahitātmāsau tapaścakāra bhaktivit|| 14 ||

agastya uvāca |

kasmin sthāne ca tīrthe 'asau tapaścakre svayaṃ vibhuḥ|
kam ārādhya mahātejāḥ sarvadevamayo haraḥ|| 15 ||

etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ tvattaḥ sarvajñaputrataḥ|
śrīmatām anukampā cenmayi ca vada me vibho|| 16 ||

skanda uvāca |

āsannekādaśa rudrā aṃśā jyotirmayasya ca|
teṣāṃ madhye varaikāṃśa īśānaḥ prākarot tapaḥ|| 17 ||

pūrvottaradiśormadhye tejocalasuśobhanaḥ|
tadadhaśca mahātīrthaḥ sarvatīrthottamottamaḥ|| 18 ||

citrā nadī mahāpuṇyā vahnitejāstathāparā|
bhasmapaṅkā tathā puṇyā tāsāṃ susaṃgame mune|| 19 ||

bhasmatīrtha iti khyātaḥ sarvatīrthaphalapradaḥ|
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti sadehā nātra saṃśayaḥ|| 20 ||

snātvā prajapitā rudraṃ rudraloke mahīyate|
paśyati bhasmatīrthaṃ yaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate|| 21 ||

jambūdvīpodbhaveṣvu ārya tisraḥ koṭyardhakoṭiṣu|
tīrtheṣu yat phalaṃ snātvā martyo 'api labhate mune|| 22 ||

tat phalaṃ labhyate martyaḥ sarvatīrthaphalaprade|
sakṛdāplavamātreṇa bhasmatīrthe susaṃgame|| 23 ||

agastya uvāca |

bhasmatīrthaṃ mahāpūtaṃ sarvatīrthaphalodbhavam|
tvayā proktaṃ mahāsena bhasmatīrthaṃ kathaṃ bhavet|| 24 ||

cakāra tapa īśānaḥ kathaṃ sa bhagavān guha|
tridevātmāpi tejasvī bhūtasvāntasthito 'aniśam|| 25 ||

skanda uvāca |

bhasmanā ca yadeśānaḥ snānaṃ cakre śiloccaye|
tadaṅgabhasmano jātā nadī puṇyavatī varā|| 26 ||

tataḥ śiloccayāddhīra prapatitā sunirmalā|
bhasmapaṅketi vikhyātā tayoḥ saṃgamagāminī|| 27 ||

yatra sasnau maheśānaḥ sarvadevābhikāṅkṣite|
tatastejocalaṃ vipra ruroha sa mahāmanāḥ|| 28 ||

tasya kūṭe mahāpūte sarvaratnasusambhave|
hiraṇyamayabhūmau ca sarvadevamanohare|| 29 ||

agamye devasattvānāṃ bahutuṣārabhūṣite|
maṇimayasthalotsedhe candrārkayoḥ samojjvale|| 30 ||

tatra divyāsanāsīno bhūtvā codaṅmukho vibhuḥ|
dadhyau parāparām adyāṃ brahmaparāparāṃ śivām|| 31 ||

divyavarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ jajāpa sa mahāvibhuḥ|
tato japāvasāne ca devāścintākulā mune|| 32 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

yaṃ vinā ca purā śakraḥ prāptaṃ mahat susaṃkaṭam|
jñātvedānīm iha sthāne nāsti rudra iti dhruvam|| 33 ||

ihāgatya ca daityāste harṣanirbharamānasāḥ|
kariṣyanti punaryuddhaṃ luṇṭhanti cāmarāvatīm|| 34 ||

indra uvāca |

gamyatāṃ bho 'amarāḥ sarve yatra tiṣṭhati mādhavaḥ|
tasmai nivedyatāṃ vārtāṃ śambhośca tapasaśca naḥ|| 35 ||

samākarṇya ca tadvārtām asmābhiryāṃ niveditām|
vadiṣyati yathā viṣṇuḥ kurvāmo hi tathāvidham|| 36 ||

bṛhaspatiruvāca |

sādhu śakra tvayoktaṃ naḥ pathyaṃ ca tanna saṃśayaḥ|
asmābhiḥ saṃtataṃ pūrvaṃ hṛdi me tacca vartate|| 37 ||

gacchadhvaṃ ca mahātmāno yatrāsau garuḍadhvajaḥ|
tatra saṃmantrayāmo vai sthātavyam atra mā ciram|| 38 ||

skanda uvāca |

evaṃ sambhāṣitaṃ śrutvā teṣāṃ ca vacanaṃ mudā|
matvā ca svātmanāṃ pathyaṃ jagmuryatra harirmune|| 39 ||

tato nemuḥ surāḥ sarve viṣṇuṃ brahma sanātanam|
parikramya yathāyogyaṃ stotrārhaṇairapūjayan|| 40 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

kuśalaṃ svāgatā devā bhadrāṇi santi vo 'aniśam|
rājyeṣu ca śarīreṣu tathā vitteṣu sāmpratam|| 41 ||

kāryam āgamanaṃ kiṃ vaḥ sambhūya gurupūrvakam|
vadatātra yathātathyaṃ mamāgre bho havirbhujaḥ|| 42 ||

bṛhaspatiruvāca |

svāgatāśca vayaṃ viṣṇo tava prasādato 'adhunā|
asmākam atibhītānāṃ vārtāṃ ca te vadāmyaham|| 43 ||

himālaye nagaśreṣṭhe rudro japati sa ciram|
ākramiṣyanti matveti dānavāste 'amarāvatīm|| 44 ||

rudraṃ vinā kathaṃ tatra sthātavyam iti niścayaḥ|
ihāgatā mahāviṣṇo rudram utthāpaya prabho|| 45 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya vaco viṣṇurāṅgirasamukhāccyutam|
sammataṃ caiva devānāṃ sarvalokahitaṃ tathā|| 46 ||

tat kāryaṃ cintya vai viṣṇurbrahmāṇam āhvayat tadā|
tataḥ sammantrayaddhīra brahmaṇā saha sāmpratam|| 47 ||

āhūya sarvadevāṃśca candrārkau nāradaṃ tathā|
devarṣyaṅgirasairyukto yayau viṣṇurhimālayam|| 48 ||

yatra tapati rudro 'asau sarvadevamayo vibhuḥ|
tato dadarśa maheśaṃ tapasthitaṃ vibhuṃ mune|| 49 ||

sarvajyotirmayaṃ devaṃ sūryakoṭiprabhāyutam|
candrakoṭisamudyotaṃ bhāsayantaṃ diśo daśa|| 50 ||

saṃdṛśya cātmabhūrbhūyo mantrayāmāsa daivataiḥ|
bhayaṃ kiṃcit samāviṣṭa uvāca vacanaṃ mune|| 51 ||

brahmovāca |

aho 'ajasya tapasthasya vrajāmaścāntikaṃ katham|
satyam uktaṃ mayā viṣṇo tasyaivānugrahaṃ vinā|| 52 ||

tejaḥpuñjasya vaikuṇṭha mahogratejasaḥ surāḥ|
vilīnāsmo vayaṃ satyaṃ gantāraścet tadantikam|| 53 ||

yathā ca vahnikīlāyāṃ śalabhā naiva saṃśayaḥ|
saṃdehasthā vayaṃ sarve kiṃ vidheyam ataḥ param|| 54 ||

skanda uvāca |

samākarṇya vaco devā brahmaṇo hitabhāṣitam|
babhūvuste ca niryatnā gantum api tadantikam|| 55 ||

ravirapi samagantuṃ tatsamīpe na śaktaḥ kharatarakiraṇo 'asau kampadeho muhurvai|
suravarakathito 'ajo devasammantrya vipra kamalajavacanairvai śaṃkarasyāntikaṃ ca|| 56 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe rudratapasotthāne devamantraṇaṃ nāma viṃśatitamo adhyāyaḥ|| 20 ||

agastya uvāca |

aṃśo 'ayam īśvarasyādyastvayoktaṃ me śivātmaja|
raudratejā mahādevo lokasākṣīti naḥ śrutam|| 1 ||

kathaṃ sūryo mahātejāḥ pragantuṃ ca tadantike|
aśaktavān bhavaddevo 'asahyatejasātmakaḥ|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

brahmaṇo vacanaṃ śrutvā bṛhaspatimukhāḥ surāḥ|
harṣayantastadā dhīra sādhu sādhviti vādinaḥ|| 3 ||

āhūya pūṣaṇaṃ devaṃ kathayāmāsurādritam|
vimṛṣya sarvadevaiśca harotthānāya sāmpratam|| 4 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

ādideva mahātejaḥ sarvasattvānukampaka|
tvaṃ sraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ rudratejo na saṃśayaḥ|| 5 ||

gaccha sūrya mahādeva rudrasya cāntikaṃ tataḥ|
gatvā tapasthito devo vandyatāṃ taṃ yadṛcchayā|| 6 ||

sūrya uvāca |

aho mama vināśāya yūyaṃ samudyatā dhruvam|
ko 'anuyāsyati nāśāya svātmano 'ajñaṃ vinā surāḥ|| 7 ||

yasya tejo 'atisahyaṃ yadyasya ghorekṣaṇo 'analaḥ|
tejomayasya cāṃśo 'ahaṃ yasya koṭyaṃśasambhavaḥ|| 8 ||

yasyonmeṣanimeṣeṇa lokasya pralayodbhavaḥ|
tapasthasyāntikaṃ gantuṃ śakyate na mayā vibho|| 9 ||

aṅgirasa uvāca |

bho himāṃśo mahāvīra asmabhyam anukampaya|
devānāṃ ca hitārthāya rakṣāyai surasadmanaḥ|| 10 ||

nāśāyāsmadbhayānāṃ ca gatvā candra tadantike|
tava svakiraṇaiḥ śītai raudratāṃ ca praśāmyatām|| 11 ||

candra uvāca |

na śakyate mayā tatra gantuṃ namo 'astu te guro|
rudrasyaivāntike tīkṣṇatapasthasya mahātmanaḥ|| 12 ||

krodhino 'akrodhino vāpi ko gacchati tadantikam|
vinā cājñāṃ maheśasya prathamaṃ samudāhṛtam|| 13 ||

gacchati cet tadājñāṃ yo vinā śambhostadantikam|
avimarṣya tathā bhaktaḥ prāpnoti sa mahāpadam|| 14 ||

indra uvāca |

bho bho dahana tejasvī rudrāṃśastvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ|
bhadraṃ kuru ca devānāṃ rājyānāṃ hi viśeṣataḥ|| 15 ||

dehaḥ paropakārāya dharmarakṣāya caiva ca|
sarvakāmadughaścātmā kṣaṇaṃ tiṣṭhatyasaṃśayaḥ|| 16 ||

ata evopakāryante trilokānāṃ manīṣibhiḥ|
gatvā rudrāntikaṃ caitadvārtāṃ tasmai vidhīyatām|| 17 ||

agniruvāca |

devarāja mahāvijña lokānugrahakāraka|
yaduktaṃ bhavatā mahyaṃ tat sarvaṃ tathyam eva ca|| 18 ||

śakyāśakyaṃ vicāryādau kāryaṃ ca kurvate budhāḥ|
aśakyaṃ śakra yat kāryaṃ kurvate na hi sajjanāḥ|| 19 ||

sṛjyate viśvam icchābhiḥ pālyate ca tathāvidham|
saṃharanti jagat sarvaṃ niḥśeṣaṃ sacarācaram|| 20 ||

yasya netrāgninā viśvaṃ kriyate bhasmasāddhruvam|
kariṣyati tathā māṃ ca na śakto 'ahaṃ ca te namaḥ|| 21 ||

nārada uvāca |

dāntaśīlaḥ śuciḥ sādhuḥ sarvadharmarataḥ sadā|
paropakārako devaḥ satyavādī jitendriyaḥ|| 22 ||

varuṇa tvaṃ hi samarthaḥ sarvaguṇarasātmakaḥ|
bhavān gacchatu toyeśa rudrasya cāntikaṃ dhruvam|| 23 ||

tavāṃśairjīvanaiḥ pāśin praśāmaya ca tejasam|
tīkṣṇam asahyam īśasya gatvā tadantikaṃ vibho|| 24 ||

kulīnaḥ śīlasaṃyukto dānadharmarataḥ sadā|
gaccha drutaṃ manojñastvaṃ rudrabhakto 'asi saṃtatam|| 25 ||

varuṇa uvāca |

na śakyaṃ vidyate brahman mamāpi ca tadantikam|
gantuṃ praśamanāyārya raudratejastapasvinaḥ|| 26 ||

aśakto yaḥ pratiśrutya kāryaṃ na śakyate janaḥ|
viḍambanāya lokasya syāddvija tasya jīvanam|| 27 ||

gaganasthaṃ vidhorbimbaṃ labdhum icchuryathārbhakaḥ|
tathāvidhā ca me śaktistaddhāsāya bhaviṣyati|| 28 ||

tasmānna kurute dhīmañchakyaṃ kāryam anātmanaḥ|
upālambhaiśca bhītātmā vivekastho munīśvara|| 29 ||

skanda uvāca |

tato devāḥ saśakrāśca samākarṇya yathoditam|
caturbhiramarairvipra yatra dhātā yayurdrutam|| 30 ||

kātaroktaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ teṣāṃ divaukasāṃ tadā|
vidhātre kathayanti sma ceṣṭāṃ caiva ghaṭodbhava|| 31 ||

lokeśo 'api tato gatvā varṇayāmāsa viṣṇave|
vṛttāntaṃ sarvarūpāya trikālajñāya sāmpratam|| 32 ||

brahmovāca |

bhavanti cātra te 'aśaktā gantum api tadantike|
dṛṣṭvā rudraujasaṃ devā bhīṣmagrastāḥ prakampitāḥ|| 33 ||

yatrasthā api niryatnā babhūvuste surā vibho|
yatnaṃ ca kriyatāṃ viṣṇo kiṃ vidheyam ataḥ param|| 34 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

stotraṃ ca kriyate 'asmābhiḥ saha devaiḥ pitāmaha|
gatvā ca yugapat tatra rudrāntike mahātmanaḥ|| 35 ||

śrutvā stotraṃ mahādevastataḥ praśāmyati dhruvam|
stotraiḥ śāmyanti lokeśā mahātmānastathā stavaiḥ|| 36 ||

stutibhirlabhyate dharmaḥ stavenaiva phalaṃ labhet|
tasmācca kriyate stotraṃ yasmādbhayaṃ vinaśyati|| 37 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya vaco viṣṇorjīvasya sarvajīvinaḥ|
brahmādayaḥ surāḥ sarve sādhu sādhviti vādinaḥ|| 38 ||

pūrvaṃ nemurupendraṃ te parikramya yathāvidhi|
ādhāya svāñjaliṃ mūrdhni stotrayantaśca harṣitāḥ|| 39 ||

tuṣṭuvuśca tato rudraṃ brahmādayaḥ surottamāḥ|
kiṃcidbhayaṃ samāviṣṭāḥ śanairgatvā tadantikam|| 40 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

.o, |

namo rudrāya raudrāya raudrarūpāya te namaḥ|
raudratejasvine 'ajāya raudradehāya te namaḥ|| 41 ||

nirguṇāya guṇāṃśāya nirvikārāya tejase|
ātmane pañcabhūtānāṃ satyāṃśāya namo namaḥ|| 42 ||

vyaktāvyaktasvarūpāya caitanyāya ca cetase|
vyomāya vyomadehāya candrārkāgnyakṣiṇe namaḥ|| 43 ||

aurvamukhāya devāya dyauśīrṣāya namo 'astu te|
bhūpade dikṣukarṇāya samudrajaṭharāya vai|| 44 ||

bhujaṃgāya pratītāya ahaṃkārātmane namaḥ|
meghakeśāya bhīmāya kamalaretase namaḥ|| 45 ||

vṛkṣaromaśarīrāya sumerunābhaye namaḥ|
pitāmahavisargāya sarvabhūtāśine namaḥ|| 46 ||

hṛddharmo yasya devāya pradhānapuruṣāya vai|
advitīyāpratītāya cādyāya hetave namaḥ|| 47 ||

dhyātavyāya sucintyāya cintyācintyātmane namaḥ|
bhūmaṃste tīkṣṇatejobhirdagdhānasmānabhiplutān|| 48 ||

bhavān māyārṇave 'agādhe saṃsāre 'apārake 'avatu|
bhaktavatsala te dāsān bhaktiṣvajñān vibho 'aniśam|
chāyayā chāditānasmānajñānasthān prarakṣatu|| 49 ||

skanda uvāca |

tataḥ stavaṃ samākarṇya sarvadevamukhāccyutam|
tutoṣa stutibhirdivyairāśutoṣaśca śaktibhiḥ|| 50 ||

uvāca śaṃkarastebhyo harṣagadgadayā girā|
ātmatejāṃsi saṃhṛtya prasannavadano 'abhavat|| 51 ||

īśāna uvāca |

bho devā ṛṣayo bhaktā yūyaṃ cātra madantike|
āgatya ca kṛtaṃ stotraṃ yathārthaṃ me mudā bhṛśam|| 52 ||

ataḥ saṃtuṣṭavān vatsā bhavāni stutibhiśca vaḥ|
kiṃ karomi ca yuṣmākaṃ kāryaṃ vadantu me 'adhunā|| 53 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

sarvo datto varo vai no na kiṃcidatra śiṣyate|
abhūma devatāḥ sarve bhavatprasādato vayam|| 54 ||

bhavantaṃ ca vinā svarge na śaktāḥ sthātum īśvara|
jñātvā caitadrahasyaṃ te virahitaṃ surālayam|| 55 ||

ākramiṣyanti daiteyā ato bhītā ihāgatāḥ|
ato vayaṃ bhavantaṃ hi svabhiṣicyāma adya vai|| 56 ||

skanda uvāca |

ānīya tīrthakīlālairhiraṇyakalaśoddhṛtaiḥ|
dadau viṣṇurmudā vipra abhiṣekaṃ parātmane|| 57 ||

dadau brahmā paṭhan vedānabhiṣekaṃ mudā punaḥ|
dadau sūryo mahātejāstejojjvalaiśca tejase|| 58 ||

dadau candro 'amṛtāḍhyairvai kalaśairoṣadhīyutaiḥ|
dadau śakro 'abhiṣekaṃ ca ratnaghaṭoddhṛtodakaiḥ|| 59 ||

dadau vahnirmaheśāya tejaḥpūrṇaghaṭodakaiḥ|
dadau pāśī punastasmai sarvatīrthajalaistathā|| 60 ||

dadau vāyuḥ punastasmai sugandhaśītalairjalaiḥ|
saptarṣayo daduḥ snānaṃ gāyatrīsmaraṇādṛtaiḥ|| 61 ||

nārado 'api dadau tasmai jayaśabdaṃ paṭhan mudā|
mantrāñjapanto duḥ siddhā abhiṣekaṃ pavitrakaiḥ|| 62 ||

kāmadhenurdadau snānaṃ dugdhaiḥ prasravaṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ|
devāśca pradadustasmai gandharvāśca tathāparāḥ|| 63 ||

tato gandhaiḥ samaṃ puṣpairdivyavāsobhirīśvaram|
pūjayāmāsa tanmantrāñjapan gururmudā vibhum|| 64 ||

tato vavarṣa puṣpāṇāṃ lājānāṃ saṃhatirbhṛśam|
divo devāṅganādorbhiḥ prakṣiptā divi sambhavāḥ|| 65 ||

adbhuto jayaśabdaśca nedurdundubhayo bhṛśam|
jagurdivyastriyastatra rudrayaśastadātmanā|| 66 ||

nanṛtuścāpsarāstatra mṛdaṅgatālanisvanaiḥ|
tato viṣṇuruvāceśaṃ sarvalokahitāya ca|| 67 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

bhūteśa meruśṛṅge ca tvaṃ pūrvottarayordiśaḥ|
madhye tiṣṭha tato lokāṃstatrasthān rakṣayāniśam|| 68 ||

adyaprabhṛti sarvajña dikpālo bhava sarvadā|
tato lokās vadiṣyanti īśānaṃ ca nirantaram|| 69 ||

skanda uvāca |

.o pratiśrutya tasmai sa yayau yatra ca viṣṇunā|
upariṣṭhaṃ diśormadhye jagatsaṃrakṣaṇāya vai|| 70 ||

adyāpi sa jagat sarvaṃ rakṣati sma sukhaṃ haraḥ|
tasmādviśvaṃ dvijeśānaṃ vadanti prāṇino 'aniśam|| 71 ||

tadādi pālāśca diśāṃ bhaveyurdhruvo 'api cakre hi tapaḥ kaṭhoram|
viṣṇuśca dhātā naranāmadānto bhagīratho rāṭ prasabhaṃ tadātmā|| 72 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe īśānābhiṣeko nāmaikaviṃśatitamo adhyāyaḥ|| 21 ||

agastya uvāca |

ko 'asau dhruvo mahāvīraḥ sarvonnatamanorathaḥ|
tapastepe kathaṃ skanda mānuṣo vā suro 'api vā|| 1 ||

kasmin sthāne ca tīrthe sa kenopadeśito vibho|
śrotum icchāmyahaṃ caitadvada me śaṃkarātmaja|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

āsīduttānapādo hi sarvavarṇapravandanaḥ|
tasya putro mahābāhurdhruvo nāma ca viśrutaḥ|| 3 ||

pitrā cottānapādena bhrātaraṃ pūrvajaṃ priyam|
aṅke cāropya dṛṣṭvā taṃ dhruvaḥ sadasi saṃsthitam|| 4 ||

udāsīno 'abhavat tatra māturgatvāntikaṃ dhruvaḥ|
svānādaraṃ ca tadvārtāṃ tadā mātre nyavedayat|| 5 ||

tataḥ papraccha tadvārtāṃ mātaraṃ prati tadvacaḥ|
udāsīnamanā bhūtvā smṛtya svānādaraṃ muhuḥ|| 6 ||

dhruva uvāca |

āropya bhrātaraṃ svāṅke sabhāmadhye pitā sthitaḥ|
paśyannapi ca māṃ tyaktvā harṣaṃ tena samaṃ babhau|| 7 ||

mātaḥ kathaṃ bhavedbhrātā mama pituḥ priyo vada|
na karoti mayi snehaṃ pitā kadāpi dharmavit|| 8 ||

skanda uvāca |

vaco niśamya tanmātā avamānātmakasya vai|
putrasya sāntvayāmāsa suvacanā tadātmajam|| 9 ||

sunītiruvāca |

putra mā kuru duḥkhaṃ tvaṃ pūrvajanmani yat kṛtam|
duḥkhaṃ vā ca sukhaṃ vatsa sarvaṃ tadiha labhyate|| 10 ||

daivāt prāpnoti tat sarvaṃ rājāṅgaṃ vipravigraham|
naradehaṃ ca devāṅgaṃ caturvidhaṃ kalevaram|| 11 ||

prāgjanmani kṛtaṃ karma taddaivaṃ hi na saṃśayaḥ|
jñātvātmaneha cittena dhīrastatra na muhyati|| 12 ||

tasmādapi tapo mūlaṃ tapa eva garīyasam|
tapasā labhyate sarvaṃ yadyadvāñchati tatkṣaṇāt|| 13 ||

skanda uvāca |

śrutvā māturvaco vipra taponiṣṭho babhūva saḥ|
pituranādaro 'api āśu harṣapūrṇasamāyutaḥ|| 14 ||

tato 'auttānapādirvai tapaḥ kartuṃ vanaṃ yayau|
kṣutpipāsāṃ parityajya ekākī nirjanaṃ mune|| 15 ||

tatra vṛkṣaghane 'araṇye siṃhavyāghraiśca sevite|
dhruvo dadarśa saptarṣīn sarvasattvaniṣevite|| 16 ||

vandayāmāsa tān viprān kṛtāñjalipuṭo dhruvaḥ|
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ samyak stutibhiśca punaḥ punaḥ|| 17 ||

saptarṣaya ūcuḥ |

kastvaṃ bālaka gāḍhātmā nūnam ihāgato vane|
agamye mānuṣāṇāṃ ca nānājantuniṣevite|| 18 ||

bhayaṃ na vidyate kiṃcidātmanaḥ komalārbhaka|
vyāghreṇa hariṇā drutya bāla tvam ihāgato vada|| 19 ||

dhruva uvāca |

nāhaṃ druto dvijaśreṣṭha vyāghraiḥ siṃhaiśca jantubhiḥ|
yadṛcchayāgataścātra pitṛparibhavādaham|| 20 ||

vibhoruttānapādasya putro 'ahaṃ ca prajāpateḥ|
ihāgata udāsīno dhruvo nāmeti viśrutaḥ|| 21 ||

māṃ tyaktvā pūrvajaṃ kroḍe nidhāya ca pitā mama|
sabhāmadhye sthito harṣaṃ tasmādvairāgyavānaham|| 22 ||

ataḥ samāgatastaptuṃ tapaḥ kaṭhoram icchayā|
jīvitum iha necchāmi satyam etanmaharṣayaḥ|| 23 ||

bhagavatpādukaṣoṃbhojanivaṇāya me manaḥ|
bhavatām anukampā cedupadeśaḥ pradīyatām|| 24 ||

kṣaṇaṃ tiṣṭhati kāyo 'ayaṃ sukhaduḥkhasamākulaḥ|
yasmāt saṃlabhyate mokṣaṃ duḥkhārṇavapraṇāśakam|| 25 ||

saptarṣaya ūcuḥ |

aho 'adbhutaṃ mahānatra bālakasyāsya ceṣṭitam|
yasyedṛśī mahābuddhistasya kiṃ durlabhaṃ bhavet|| 26 ||

vatsātibālako 'asi tvaṃ tapaḥ kartuṃ samudyataḥ|
śaktaśceddhi tapastaptum agnimadhye yathā tanuḥ|| 27 ||

himālaye mahāśṛṅge sarvonnate suśekhare|
ekacittaṃ samādhāya rudramantraḥ prajapyatām|| 28 ||

kāmatīrthe mahāpūte bahutīrthottamottame|
snātvādau vidhivadvatsa sarvonnate ca gamyatām|| 29 ||

skanda uvāca |

vaco niśamya munīnām ṛṣibhirupadeśitaḥ|
yayau dhruvo mahāyogī himālaye nagottame|| 30 ||

tapaḥ kartuṃ mudāyuktaḥ parityajya priyāpriyam|
mohakañcukanirmukto jñānakañcukasaṃvṛtaḥ|| 31 ||

himavadāgneyāśāyāṃ kandarairbahuśobhane|
brahmaputranadaśreṣṭhaḥ kāmadhārā nadīvarā|| 32 ||

tayośca saṃgame dhīra kāmatīrtham udāhṛtam|
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti pātakairapi varjitāḥ|| 33 ||

tasmiṃstīrthe mahāpuṇye varade brahmaṇodite|
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ snānāt kṣaṇāt praṇaśyati|| 34 ||

tatra sasnau dhruvaḥ samyak kāmatīrthe svakāmade|
bhasmanā lepayedgātraṃ rudrākṣāṃśca dadhāra vai|| 35 ||

tato yayau dhruvo nūnaṃ sarvonnataśiloccaye|
agamyaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ bahutuṣārabhūṣitam|| 36 ||

ṛjukāyaḥ samāsīnastatra kūṭe suniścalaḥ|
martyavarṣasahasrāṇi niścalaḥ sañjajāpa saḥ|| 37 ||

tuṣṭāva ca maheśānaṃ rudraṃ nāmapadairmune|
lomāñcano mahātmāsau bhāvāḍhyo gadgadoditaiḥ|| 38 ||

dhruva uvāca |

.o, |

namaḥ śivāya bhavyāya bhadrarūpāya tejase|
tejasāṃ puñjadehāya jyotiṣāṃ pataye namaḥ|| 39 ||

saṃsāradāya devāya sārarūpāya śūline|
nirañjanāya rudrāya bhūteśāya namo namaḥ|| 40 ||

vyomadehāya cādyāya anādyāya kapardine|
bhūtakṛtāya rudrāya śaṃkarāya namo namaḥ|| 41 ||

tvageva sparśarūpāya raktāṃśāya namo namaḥ|
māṃsarūpāya jīvāya medorūpāya vai namaḥ|| 42 ||

snāyuṣe cāsthirūpāya trināḍīrūpiṇe namaḥ|
ghrāṇasthāya ca gandhāya rasajñāya rasāya ca|| 43 ||

cākṣuṣāya ca netrāya śrotrāya śrutaye namaḥ|
jīvināṃ jīvarūpāya jīvasaṃjñātmane namaḥ|| 44 ||

pṛthvīrūpāya bhīmāya pānīyamūrtaye namaḥ|
tejorūpāya cogrāya samīramūrtaye namaḥ|| 45 ||

antasthāya ca devāya buddhirūpāya te namaḥ|
manorūpāya cittāya mānarūpāya vai namaḥ|| 46 ||

caitanyāya vivekāya jñānarūpāya śambhave|
śaktirūpāya bhargāya kartre ca jagatāṃ namaḥ|| 47 ||

trāhi māṃ deva bhūteśa saṃsāraduḥkhasāgarāt|
ajñānātitamonimnakūpāndhapatitaṃ vibho|| 48 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti ākarṇya stutiṃ devo dhruvasya bhaktito mune|
tutoṣātitarāṃ rudraḥ stutibhaktitapovaraiḥ|| 49 ||

tato japāvasāne ca āvirbhūto mahāvibhuḥ|
hṛṣyamāṇo hi taṃ prekṣya uvāca vacanaṃ mune|| 50 ||

īśvara uvāca |

aho 'adbhutaṃ tapastaptaṃ kaṭhoraṃ bālaka tvayā|
dvandvabhāvaṃ parityajya sarvabhogyavivarjitaḥ|| 51 ||

īdṛśo bālakaḥ śṛṅge samārādhitavān dhruvaḥ||
bhūtvā tvaṃ niścalo vatsa nirjane brahmaśekhare|| 52 ||

tasmādvaram idānīṃ te dadāmi dhruva niścalam|
ākarṇaya dhruvaṃ matta ekacittaḥ samāvṛtaḥ|| 53 ||

yasmāt pituravajñānādihāgatya tapaḥ kṛtam|
tasmāt sarvopari śrīmān bhava tvaṃ me prasādataḥ|| 54 ||

adyaprabhṛti cāryastvaṃ sarvalokopari plute|
merukūṭe mahāsthāne tatra tiṣṭha suniścalaḥ|| 55 ||

tato lokā vadiṣyanti dhruvaloka iti śrutaḥ|
sarvalokāścalanti āśu dhruva tvaṃ niścalo bhava|| 56 ||

skanda uvāca |

iti dattvā varaṃ rudro 'antardhānaṃ yayau tadā|
tasmai brahmā samāgatya abhiṣekaṃ dadau mudā|| 57 ||

tato dhruvaṃ samānīya kāmagena rathena tam|
gītavādyamahollāsāpsarogaṇayuto vidhiḥ|| 58 ||

sarvopari mahākūṭe sumeroḥ surasadmani|
tatra saṃsthāpayedbrahmā dhruvaṃ sarvonnataṃ tadā|| 59 ||

brahmāpi cakre sutapaḥ kaṭhoraṃ yatrāśu devyā dvijaśāpam āptāḥ|
devyā rahaḥ sthānagatāparādhaṃ prāptena vṛkṣā hi tato 'abhavaṃste|| 60 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe dhruvatapaḥsiddhirnāma dvāviṃśatitamo adhyāyaḥ|| 22 ||

agastya uvāca |

kathaṃ śāpaṃ dadau devī sarvabhūtadayāvatī|
devebhyaḥ sakalebhyaśca vṛkṣāṅgān prāpitāśca te|| 1 ||

etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ vada me śaṃkarātmaja|
kāsau devī mahātejāstasyā māhātmyam uttamam|| 2 ||

kasmin kṣetre mahāpuṇye sā tiṣṭhati nirantaram|
tasyā nāma mahāsena tattīrthasya viśeṣataḥ|| 3 ||

skanda uvāca |

śṛṇu kumbhaja vakṣyāmi caikacittaḥ samāhitaḥ|
yathā vṛttaṃ purā divyaṃ yat tvaṃ māṃ paripṛcchasi|| 4 ||

brahmaputro nadaśreṣṭhaḥ kāmadhārā nadīvarā|
tayormadhye mahāśailo nīlācalākhyaśekhare|| 5 ||

kāmakṣetram iti khyātaṃ sarvakṣetrottamottamam|
tasmin kṣetre mahāpūte sarvepsitaphalaprade|| 6 ||

āsīddhīman mahādevī kāmākhyā nāma viśrutā|
yā stutā brahmaṇā pūrvaṃ viṣṇunetrasthitā satī|| 7 ||

sā māyā yoginī nityā yoginīkoṭisevitā|
yaṃ yaṃ kāmanti bhaktyā te tasyāṃ labhanti taṃ ca tam|| 8 ||

kasmiṃciddivase dhīra gacchati sma maheśvaraḥ|
tyaktvā svargaṃ gaṇān devān kāmakṣetre rasātale|| 9 ||

harṣasthito harastatra kāmākhyayā samaṃ tadā|
rahaḥsthānam iti jñātvā devo devi mudaṃ yayau|| 10 ||

tat sthānaṃ tyaktum īśāno 'asamartho 'abhavanmune|
kāmākhyāmohito devaḥ kutracinna cacāra saḥ|| 11 ||

ekadā divase jñātvā nārado 'asau mahāmuniḥ|
rudro na vidyate svarge iti ca kalahapriyaḥ|| 12 ||

yayau yatra mudā yukto hiraṇyakaśipurlaghu|
dānavendro mahāvīraḥ sabhāmadhye sthito yadā|| 13 ||

svarṇasiṃhāsanāsīnaḥ sarvadaityaiśca saṃvṛtaḥ|
nānāvṛttāntam ākarṇya svacarāṇāṃ mukhāccyutam|| 14 ||

gītai rudrayaśobhūtairmṛdaṅgaistālanisvanaiḥ|
navarasānvitairnṛtyaiḥ satataṃ ca sa sevitaḥ|| 15 ||

tasmin kāle dadarśāryaṃ hiraṇyakaśipurmunim|
samāyāntaṃ mudā vyomno 'avatarantam ambarāt|| 16 ||

gītavādyamahollāsaṃ pragāyantaṃ vibhoryaśaḥ|
vīṇāhastaṃ svarairyuktaṃ mālinaṃ madhurasvaram|| 17 ||

dṛṣṭvā taṃ vai samāyātaṃ sabhāntikaṃ ca nāradam|
pratyudyayau samaṃ kṣipraṃ hiraṇyakaśipurgaṇaiḥ|| 18 ||

tato nanāma daityeśaḥ sampūjya pūjanairmunim|
samānīya tadā vipra svāsane saṃnyaveśayat|| 19 ||

papraccha kuśalaṃ pūrvaṃ vṛttāntaṃ nāradaṃ punaḥ|
svāgataṃ bho muniśreṣṭha kiṃ kurvāmo vadāśu me|| 20 ||

nārada uvāca |

nāhaṃ yadṛcchayā vatsa tava snehādihāgataḥ|
kiṃcidvārtāṃ samādāya svargasyeha ca sāmpratam|| 21 ||

śṛṇu daitya pravakṣyāmi yadvṛttāntaṃ divo bhuvām|
trāsavantaḥ surāḥ sarve tvatto bhayānna saṃśayaḥ|| 22 ||

mahādevo gato vatsa kāmākhyā yatra tiṣṭhati|
mumoda suciraṃ kālaṃ rahaḥsthāne mahāvibhuḥ|| 23 ||

tataḥ svarge surāḥ sarve cintayanti sma sāmpratam|
luṇṭhiṣyantyasurāḥ sarve naśceheti na saṃśayaḥ|| 24 ||

rudraṃ vinā surā nākam ākramiṣyanti niścayam|
kva gacchāmo vayaṃ devā anyathā svaśca sāmpratam|| 25 ||

evaṃ cintākulā devā bhaveyurnātra saṃśayaḥ|
iti satyaṃ hi jānīyādgacchāmi śivam astu te|| 26 ||

skanda uvāca |

tato gate munau dhīmān hiraṇyakaśipustadā|
samākarṇya ca tadvārtāṃ nāradāt sampraharṣitaḥ|| 27 ||

āhvayat sarvadaityāṃśca bālavṛddhān vayaḥsthitān|
tataḥ samāyayuḥ kṣipraṃ suradviṣastadanvayān|| 28 ||

tata āhūya tadgoṣṭhyāṃ trividhavayasastadā|
mahātmāno mahāvīrān kramāt tānupaveśayat|| 29 ||

hiraṇyakaśipurvīro mantrayāmāsa cāsuraiḥ|
sārdhaṃ vṛddhairamātyaistairmantrairnipuṇamantribhiḥ|| 30 ||

hiraṇyakaśipuruvāca |

bho bho daityā mahābhāgāḥ sarvonnataparākramāḥ|
vārtāṃ yūyaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ me chidrākhyāṃ ca divaukasām|| 31 ||

vibudhā vibhayāṃ cakrurasmākam ojasārditāḥ|
vayaṃ samākramiṣyanti svargaṃ ceti viniścitāḥ|| 32 ||

svargaṃ tyaktvā mahādevo gato 'anyatra mahītale|
yatra tiṣṭhati kāmākhyā yoginīvṛndasevitā|| 33 ||

idānīṃ svarmahotpātā bhavanti ceti śaṃsinaḥ|
kathaṃ rudraṃ vinā devāḥ sthīyante ceha vihvalāḥ|| 34 ||

evaṃ ca kathitaṃ mahyaṃ nāradena ca dhīmatā|
mama carairviśeṣeṇa kiṃ kartavyaṃ taducyatām|| 35 ||

skanda uvāca |

śrutvaitadvacanaṃ daityā hiraṇyakaśipormune|
mantrayāmāsurārāt tu pṛthak ca mantribhiḥ samam|| 36 ||

anuhrādo mahāvīraḥ sabhāmadhye mahāmanāḥ|
uvāca prathamaṃ dhīraḥ sarvanītiviśāradaḥ|| 37 ||

anuhrāda uvāca |

ātmaśaktiṃ ca na jñātvā kāryam ajñaḥ karoti yaḥ|
sa nindyo hi vijānīyāt sarvalokairviḍambitaḥ|| 38 ||

ātmaśaktiṃ vicāryādau kāryaṃ ca kurute sadā|
dhīmān yato viḍambaṃ ca na labheddaityasattamāḥ|| 39 ||

prahlāda uvāca |

anuhrādena satyoktam asmatpathyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ|
yatra tiṣṭhanti devā vai sarvaśatrubhayaṃkarāḥ|| 40 ||

yatra tiṣṭhati śakraśca sarvasainyagaṇairvṛtaḥ|
dikpālā rakṣakā yatra yatra śāpāyudhāstathā|| 41 ||

yatra bhrāmyati sūryo 'asau asahyo yasya dīdhitiḥ|
yatra bhrāmyati śubhrāṃsurasahyaṃ yasya śītalam|| 42 ||

yatra viṣṇurmahātejāḥ śatruhā garuḍadhvajaḥ|
yasyāsanena pūrvaṃ no balaṃ sainyaṃ vidīrṇitam|| 43 ||

tatra jayaḥ kathaṃ tāta asmābhirvada labhyate|
yadi tatra harirna syāllabhyate tat suniścayam|| 44 ||

saṃhrāda uvāca |

viṣṇurevāvamānyo na varīyān sa viṣṇureva|
viṣṇurudrau na bhinnau ca yathā viṣṇustathā haraḥ|| 45 ||

mānyena pāruṣenādau samau devau ca pūjitau|
tau lokānāṃ bhavetāṃ vai nāvamānyau kadācana|| 46 ||

rudro nāstīti kṛtvādyairyudhyante daivataiḥ samam|
asmābhistridive tāta saṃdeho 'atra jaye bhavet|| 47 ||

nikumbha uvāca |

abhyutthānaṃ pareṣāṃ ca sthitānāṃ ca balīyasām|
yena ca kriyate tāta svalpaśaktisamāhitaiḥ|| 48 ||

tasya paribhavaḥ prokto bahunītiviśāradaiḥ|
tasmādutthāpayecchrīmān bahuśaktisamāhitaiḥ|| 49 ||

ātmodayaṃ paricchidraṃ yo jānāti sa paṇḍitaḥ|
tasmācca nītibhiḥ svāmī sainyaṃ pareṣu yojayet|| 50 ||

ādāyeṣadguṇān dhīmāṃścaturaṅgabalānvitaḥ|
nītyā ca balibhistāta yodhayet sa paraiḥ saha|| 51 ||

baliruvāca |

kāle ca ripuṇā sandhiḥ kāle ca yuddhyate paraiḥ|
jayaṃ ca prāpyate kāle 'akāle caiva parājayaḥ|| 52 ||

kālam akālam ajñātvā yo yuddhyati paraiḥ samam|
so 'acireṇaiva kālena vipadyate mahānapi|| 53 ||

kālakarma vijānāti trilokeṣu jayaṃ labhet|
tasmāt kālaṃ vicāryādau karma saṃkriyate budhaiḥ|| 54 ||

hiraṇyākṣa uvāca |

ekasmādapi cet trāso yuṣmākaṃ hṛdi vidyate|
bahuvīraiḥ prayujyante kathaṃ daityāḥ paraiḥ saha|| 55 ||

bahubalaiḥ prayukto 'api kṣudrānapyavamanyate|
api hīnabalairvatsa yadi taiḥ śastrapāṇibhiḥ|| 56 ||

na yoddhavyam api kṣudrairbahubhiśca kadācana|
śrutaṃ pipīlikābhiśca kālasarpo nipātitaḥ|| 57 ||

bhayaṃ cedvidyate viṣṇoryuṣmākaṃ danujā dhruvam|
yodhayiṣye 'aham ājau vai tena sārdhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ|| 58 ||

vipracittiruvāca |

aho 'adbhutaṃ mahat tatra yūyaṃ manasvino yataḥ|
paraṃ randhraṃ na jānanti kiṃ sādhiṣyanti karmabhiḥ|| 59 ||

trasyanti devatāḥ sarve vinedānīṃ maheśvaram|
kathaṃ nāke hi tiṣṭhāma iti cintāsamākulāḥ|| 60 ||

rocate hṛdi cāsmākam etasmin samaye 'asurāḥ|
prasthānaṃ gamanāyādya sarvaśatruvimardakam|| 61 ||

etasmin samaye daityāḥ paracchidraṃ mahadbhavet|
suniścitena yoddhavyaṃ varabhūtyāṃ kadāpi na|| 62 ||

maya uvāca |

vipracittena daiteyāḥ satyam uktaṃ na saṃśayaḥ|
idānīm eva gamyantāṃ bhūtyai jayāya cātmanaḥ|| 63 ||

vidyate hṛdi kāṅkṣā cedyuṣmākaṃ daityasattamāḥ|
svarge 'amarāvatīrājyaṃ kartuṃ niḥkaṇṭakaṃ yadi|| 64 ||

āhūyatāṃ balānyadya hiraṇyakaśipo vibho|
saṃnahyatāṃ ca yuddhārthaṃ sarva eva ca sāmpratam|| 65 ||

na sthātavyaṃ ciraṃ kālam āhūya sarvasainikam|
caturaṅgabalopetairgamyatāṃ daityasattamāḥ|| 66 ||

skanda uvāca |

niśamyeti vaco vipra anyeṣāṃ hi mayasya ca|
matvā tathyaṃ tadā dhīmān svargarājyam iyeṣa saḥ|| 67 ||

hiraṇyakaśipuḥ sainyam āhvayāmāsa tatkṣaṇāt|
āgatebhyaśca sarvebhyo bālavṛddhebhya eva ca|| 68 ||

ājñāpayat tato dhīmān hiraṇyakaśipurmudā|
vipracittāya daityāya tathānyebhyaśca mantriṇe|| 69 ||

hiraṇyakaśipuruvāca |

bho bho daityāśca yuṣmābhirnahyantāṃ kavacottamaiḥ|
gṛhyantāṃ varaśastrāṇi tathā cāstrāṇi sāmpratam|| 70 ||

hastināṃ vājināṃ caiva mahiṣāṇāṃ tathaiva ca|
kharāṇāṃ ca tathoṣṭrāṇāṃ nahyantāṃ kavacairdhruvam|| 71 ||

sarvaśilpavidārya tvaṃ samyagrathaṃ sunirmayam|
sarvarathottamaṃ mahyaṃ kāmagaṃ bahucitrakam|| 72 ||

nānāśastrāṇi cāstrāṇi nirmāya bahuśo bahu|
māyāpāśaṃ ca śaktiṃ ca tiraskaraṇam āśugam|| 73 ||

skanda uvāca |

vaco niśamya vipreśa daityarājasya sāmpratam|
ānītavāṃstato dhātūn mayaḥ śilpāya tatra ca|| 74 ||

ādāya cājñāṃ prasabhaṃ mayastaddivyaṃ rathaṃ kāmagam agnidīptim|
nānāsyaceṣṭairhi cakāra nūnaṃ jāmbūnadaṃ prakkhacitāḍhyavarṇaiḥ|| 75 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe daityamantraṇaṃ nāma trayoviṃśo adhyāyaḥ|| 23 ||

agastya uvāca |

kathaṃ divyaṃ rathaṃ skanda kṛtavān daityasattamaḥ|
kiṃviśiṣṭaṃ mayo yānaṃ sāmparāya suradviṣām|| 1 ||

yadi kṛpā mayi skanda vidyate bhavato 'adhunā|
etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ vada me tvaṃ yathā vibho|| 2 ||

skanda uvāca |

jāmbūnadamayaṃ divyaṃ sarvāvayavaśobhitam|
māṇikyakhacitaṃ śubhraṃ saṃcakāra rathaṃ mayaḥ|| 3 ||

dṛḍhaṃ ṣoḍaśacakraṃ taṃ māyāmayasukūbaram|
meghanādaravopetaṃ sahasranāgavāhakam|| 4 ||

yojanārdhasamutsedhaṃ vistāraṃ ca tadardhakam|
upasarjanasaṃyuktaṃ bahukūṭāntare mune|| 5 ||

padmarāgapravālāḍhyaṃ vajravaidūryaśobhitam|
puṣparāgamaṇiprakhyairmarakataiḥ suśobhanam|| 6 ||

pañcaraṅgapatākābhiḥ sarvaratnamayaiḥ punaḥ|
nānājantvāsyanirmāṇasaṃveṣṭitaṃ mahojjvalam|| 7 ||

divākaraprabhāprakhyaṃ nānāraṅgasuśobhitam|
bahucitrasamāyuktam īhāceṣṭāmṛgānanam|| 8 ||

ulūkadhvajasaṃyuktaṃ puro deśe surājitam|
virājamānam ābhābhiḥ kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitam|| 9 ||

raśmihastaprayāṇajña upasarjanapaṇḍitaḥ|
kālajñaśca mahāprājñastena sārathinā yutam|| 10 ||

nānāśastrāstrasaṃyuktaṃ ripūṇāṃ bhayadaṃ mune|
bahumāyāsamāyuktaṃ kāmagaṃ sumanoharam|| 11 ||

evaṃ saṃsṛjya vipreśa rathottamaṃ tadā mayaḥ|
dadau daityeśvarāyādau sarvalokabhayapradam|| 12 ||

tam ālokya rathaṃ divyaṃ mumodāśvasuraiḥ samam|
svavalayaṃ dadau tasmai sabhāyāṃ danujeśvaraḥ|| 13 ||

bahucitraprayuktena kavacena virājatā|
saṃnanaddha tato daityo vajravaidūryasaṃyutaḥ|| 14 ||

tato rathaṃ rurohāśu hiraṇyakaśipuḥ sa tam|
prāyaścittavidhiṃ kṛtvā dānaṃ dattvā dvijātaye|| 15 ||

tata āśvāsayadvācā madhurayaṃśca sārathim|
vyācaṣṭa vacanaṃ bhūyastasmai hi vadatāṃ varaḥ|| 16 ||

hiraṇyakaśipuruvāca |

bho sārathe suvidvatsu vacanaṃ me śṛṇu dhruvam|
rakṣitavyastvayāhaṃ ca saṃkaṭastho yadā punaḥ|| 17 ||

apovāhya rathaṃ tasmāt parasparaṃ tathāvidham|
saṃkaṭastho yadā tvaṃ ca rakṣaṇīyā mayā punaḥ|| 18 ||

evaṃ jñātvā vidhiṃ yo hi yadyanyonyaṃ mahāyudhi|
jayaṃ ca labhate sadyo na prāpnoti ca saṃkaṭam|| 19 ||

skanda uvāca |

hiraṇyakaśipoḥ śrutvā vacanaṃ madhuraṃ mune|
aṅgīkṛtaṃ saharṣeṇa vandayāmāsa taṃ prabhum|| 20 ||

tata ājñāṃ samādāya prabhoḥ samyagghaṭodbhava|
sārathiścodayāmāsa hastino rathavāhakān|| 21 ||

tato bhūyaḥ sa vai samyak kṛtvā sajyaṃ rathottamam|
tathāvidhaṃ dadau divyaṃ hiraṇyākṣāya sāmpratam|| 22 ||

hiraṇmayaṃ mahājvālaṃ sarvaratnasuśobhanam|
aśvavāhaṃ mahātuṅgaṃ sarvaśastrāstrasaṃyutam|| 23 ||

ripūṇāṃ bhayadaṃ kṣipraṃ sapatākadhvajojjvalam|
prahlādāya dadau vipra mayo divyarathaṃ punaḥ|| 24 ||

raupyakāñcanasaṃyuktairnirmitaṃ bahucitrakam|
padmarāgapravālaiśca khacitaṃ bahuśobhanam|| 25 ||

patākābhiśca saṃyuktaṃ sarpayaṣṭidhvajottamam|
mṛgāsyānām ihāceṣṭaṃ saṃhrādāya dadau punaḥ|| 26 ||

raupyamayena bhūyo 'asya cakāra ratham uttamam|
nīlābhamaṇibhiścitraṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam|| 27 ||

kukkuṭāsyadhvajocchrāyaṃ bahuraṅgapatākinam|
aṣṭacakraṃ suśubhrābham anuhrādāya saṃdadau|| 28 ||

bahudhātuṃ samādāya sasarja ratham uttamam|
aṣṭacakraṃ ca lauhāḍhyaṃ nānājyotiḥsamākulam|| 29 ||

kiṅkiṇījālasaṃyuktaṃ kākadhvajapatākinam|
śastrāstrairbahubhiryuktaṃ nikumbhāya dadau mayaḥ|| 30 ||

ayomayaṃ rathaṃ divyaṃ saṃsṛjya prasabhaṃ mayaḥ|
suvarṇajālasaṃyuktaṃ śvetadhvajasamanvitam|| 31 ||

sitābhrābhaiḥ patākābhii rājitaṃ ca samucchritaiḥ|
mahiṣaṃ vāhakaṃ kālaṃ kālakāya dadau punaḥ|| 32 ||

jāmbūnadamayaṃ divyaṃ taptakāñcanasaṃnibham|
vṛṣasiṃhamukhairyuktaṃ nānāratnasunirmitam|| 33 ||

maṇijālagavākṣaṃ ca gṛdhradhvajapatākinam|
nānāśastrāstrasaṃyuktaṃ balaye ca dadau mayaḥ|| 34 ||

aṣṭadhātumayaṃ śubhraṃ rathaṃ kanakabhūṣitam|
vaidūryapadmarāgaiśca maṇḍitaṃ paramādbhutam|| 35 ||

lauhaghaṇṭāravopetaṃ mahiṣaiśca pravāhakam|
śatrubhayapradaṃ ghoraṃ pradadau vipracittaye|| 36 ||

bahucitraṃ rathaṃ divyaṃ satkṛtya paramādbhutam|
jāmbūnadamayaṃ jālaṃ kiṅkiṇīravamaṇḍitam|| 37 ||

citradhvajaṃ mahāghoraṃ bahukharaiḥ pravāhakam|
śastrāstraiśca samākīrṇaṃ bāṇāya saṃdadau mayaḥ|| 38 ||

evaṃ dattvā rathāṃstebhyaḥ śilpakartā tataḥ punaḥ|
svayaṃ cāpi rurohāsau sarvaratham anuttamam|| 39 ||

saṃnahya ratham āruhya niryayurdaityasattamāḥ|
triṃśatkoṭirathānīkāścaturaṅgabalairyutāḥ|| 40 ||

ādau śubhaṃ svastyayanaṃ ca kṛtvā dattvā hi dānāni vasūni dhīraḥ|
viprebhya āryo danujāṃśca sarvān prasthāpayat tān khalu saṃgarāya|| 41 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe daityaniryāṇaṃ nāna caturviṃśo adhyāyaḥ|| 24 ||

skanda uvāca |

nārado 'api yayau svargaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati vāsavaḥ|
vīṇāvādyamahollāso gāyaṃśca madhurasvaraiḥ|| 1 ||

harṣapūrṇo vivādajñaḥ sarvagaḥ kalahapriyaḥ|
tataḥ śakrāya tadvārtām avarṇayaddhi tatkṣaṇāt|| 2 ||

nārada uvāca |

devarāja mahāprājña śṛṇu vṛttāntam adya vai|
hitāya sarvadevānāṃ matta ekamanā vibho|| 3 ||

hiraṇyakaśipurdaityaḥ saṃnahya kavacena ca|
rathastho niryayau deśādbahusainyasamāyutaḥ|| 4 ||

triṃśatkoṭirathānīkaiḥ parivārya samantataḥ|
āgamiṣyati yuddhāya svovādya vātra paśyatām|| 5 ||

tvayā saha sahasrākṣa jñātvā nāstīti śaṃkaraḥ|
saṃnahyatāṃ bhavān sainyairbhadrāya svātmano divaḥ|| 6 ||

skanda uvāca |

śrutvaitadvacanaṃ tasya kiṃcit trāsaṃ samāgataḥ|
āhūya sarvadevāṃśca bṛhaspatipurogamān|| 7 ||

sāntvayāmāsa sūtrāmā svargarakṣāya sāmpratam|
vācā madhurayā sarvān viśvakarmāṇam āhvayat|| 8 ||

ājñāpayat tataḥ śakro rathārthaṃ viśvakarmaṇe|
samāhūya ca taṃ pūrvaṃ bahumānapuraḥsaram|| 9 ||

śakra uvāca |

viśvakarman mahāprājña sarvakarmaviśārada|
bhaviṣyati mahāyuddhaṃ devāsuramahadiha|| 10 ||

triṃśatkoṭirathānīkairhiraṇyakaśipuryutaḥ|
atrāgatya mahadyuddhaṃ kariṣyati mayā saha|| 11 ||

atastvayā vimānāni kriyantāṃ bahuśo bahu|
tumulayuddhasadmāni bahugāḍhāni sāmpratam|| 12 ||

skanda uvāca |

niśamyaitadvaco dhīmān bahumānyena bhāṣitam|
indreṇa ca vidhānajño viśvakarmā praharṣitaḥ|| 13 ||

sarvadhātūn samādāya varayānaṃ ca nirmame|
suvarṇaraupyaratnāḍhyairnānāvidhāntasundaram|| 14 ||

lauhacakraṃ mahāgāḍhaṃ vistīrṇaṃ lohakūbaram|
jāmbūnadamayacchatraṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam|| 15 ||

kāṃsyodbhavamahānādakiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitam|
pañcaraṅgapatākābhiryuktaṃ vajradhvajottamam|| 16 ||

khacitaṃ ratnajālaiśca gavākṣaṃ svarṇanirmitam|
airāvatasamāyuktaṃ vimānaṃ taṃ mahādbhutam|| 17 ||

vicitraratnakhacitaṃ śastrāstrāḍhyaṃ ca kāmagam|
pravālamauktikopetavitānasaṃyutaṃ mune|
viśvakarmā dadau yānaṃ śakrāya saṃgarojjvalam|| 18 ||

tataḥ śakraḥ samālokya vimānaṃ tam mahādbhutam|
praharṣavān dadau tasmai kaṇṭhādvimucya hārakam|| 19 ||

saṃnahya kavacenendro vimānam āruhaddhruvam|
dvijānabhojayaddāyān dattvā ca bhūriśastataḥ|| 20 ||

āśīrvādaṃ ca viprāṇāṃ pratigrṛhya namaskṛtaḥ|
prahṛṣṭavāṃstataḥ śakraḥ sāntvayan sārathiṃ punaḥ|| 21 ||

tato jāmbūnadenāśu nirmitaṃ yānam uttamam|
raupyavātāyanodyotam īhāceṣṭamṛgānanaiḥ|| 22 ||

succhatraṃ dhvajasaṃyuktaṃ bahuśastrāstrasaṃkulam|
hastibhirvāhakairdivyaṃ jayantāya dadau punaḥ|| 23 ||

sarvatejomayaṃ divyaṃ sunirmitya ca viśvakṛt|
nānāratnamayaṃ yānaṃ maṇijyotiḥsamujjvalam|| 24 ||

saptāśvavāhakaṃ dhīra raudratejomahojjvalam|
ratnacchatrasamāyuktaṃ dadau sūryāya sāmpratam|| 25 ||

rājatairbahubhirbhūyo vajravaidūryabhūṣaṇaiḥ|
kṛtavān viśvakarmāsau sarvayānottamottamam|| 26 ||

raupyābhaṃ ca tūṣārāṃśuṃ sacchatraṃ haṃsavāhakam|
kāntakāntisamāyuktaṃ dadau somāya viśvakṛt|| 27 ||

tatastāmramayaṃ yānaṃ kṛtavān viśvakṛt punaḥ|
khacitaiḥ sarvaratnānāṃ suvarṇaraupyabhūṣitam|| 28 ||

raktatejomayaṃ divyaṃ gavākṣapuṣparāgakam|
asahyaṃ sarvalokānāṃ dadau ca jātavedase|| 29 ||

tato lohamayaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ punaḥ|
cakāra viśvakarmāsau rājatasvarṇabhūṣaṇaiḥ|| 30 ||

patākādhvajasaṃyuktaṃ bhinnāñjanacayopamam|
mahiṣavāhakaṃ bhīṣmaṃ dadau vaivasvate mune|| 31 ||

hiraṇmayaṃ mahāyānaṃ cakāra viśvakṛt punaḥ|
īhāceṣṭaiśca jantūnāṃ mukhānāṃ ca suśobhanam|| 32 ||

aṣṭacakraṃ mahāgāḍhaṃ kharavāhaṃ sukūbaram|
nānāratnasamākīrṇaṃ nairṛtāya dadau dhruvam|| 33 ||

sarvaratnamayaṃ yānaṃ tvaṣṭā ca kṛtavān punaḥ|
ānanairjalajantūnām īhāceṣṭāsamākulam|| 34 ||

jāmbūnadamayairhṛdyairdivyāstraśataśo yutam|
kiṅkiṇījālasaṃyuktaṃ varuṇāya dadau mudā|| 35 ||

jātarūpamayaṃ divyaṃ saṃskṛtya yānam uttamam|
kāmagaṃ ratnasaundaryaṃ nānātejomayānvitam|| 36 ||

raupyakṛtrimabhūṣāḍhyam aṣṭacakraṃ suśobhanam|
patākādhvajasaṃyuktaṃ vāyave pradadau punaḥ|| 37 ||

jāmbūnadena saṃskṛtya rājatena mahojjvalam|
nānāratnaiśca saṃkīrṇaṃ cāparaṃ puṣpakaṃ tataḥ|| 38 ||

kāmagaṃ bahusaundaryaṃ kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitam|
patākādhvajasocchrāyaṃ kuberāya dadau punaḥ|| 39 ||

sarvadhātumayaṃ divyaṃ bahuratnasamākulam|
samāruhacca taṃ yānaṃ viśvakarmā svayaṃ punaḥ|| 40 ||

tata ājñāpayadindro devāniti diśo daśa|
rakṣadhvaṃ vibudhā yūyaṃ svapurasya yathākramam|| 41 ||

ādau guruḥ svastyayanaṃ ca kṛtvā prāsthāpayat tān prasabhaṃ tato vai|
sainyaṃ ca saṃnahya ca nirjagāma vyūhaṃ samāsthāya purādrathaiśca|| 42 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe devāsurasainyaniryāṇaṃ nāma pañcaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ|| 25 ||

skanda uvāca |

tasmin kāle 'asurāḥ sarve triviṣṭapaṃ samāyayuḥ|
samāruhya rathānaśvānuṣṭrān nāgāṃstathāparān|| 1 ||

tato dadarśa daityeśo nagarīm indrapālitām|
pārijātodbhavenārya nandanena samāyutām|| 2 ||

dikṣu vyūhaṃ samāsthāya dikpālaiśca prarakṣitām|
hiraṇyālayasampūrṇāṃ hiraṇyadrumam ākulām|| 3 ||

ājñāpayat tadā daityān hiraṇyakaśipurmudā|
āhūya rathinaḥ sarvān yathāyogyaṃ yathākramam|| 4 ||

hiraṇyakaśipuruvāca |

bho prahlāda mahābāho pūrvataḥ saha yuddhyatām|
jayantenāmarāvatyāḥ koṭīrathasamāvṛtaḥ|| 5 ||

anuhrāda tathā sārdham āgneyītaḥ prayudhyatām|
vahninā ca tvayā vatsa rathakoṭīsamāyutaḥ|| 6 ||

saṃhrāda saha kālena dakṣiṇataḥ prayudhyatām|
ādāya rathakoṭiṃ ca tatastaṃ nāvamannaya|| 7 ||

bho nikumbha samaṃ vīra nairṛtena prayuddhyatām|
balaṃ ca rathakoṭīnām ādāya sainyasaṃvṛtaḥ|| 8 ||

bho kālaka samaṃ vīra varuṇena prayuddhyatām|
rathakoṭīṃ samādāya paścimato balāvṛtaḥ|| 9 ||

bale tvayā ca vīreṇa vāyunā saha yuddhyatām|
rathakoṭīṃ samādāya bahusainyasamāvṛtaḥ|| 10 ||

nāvamanyasva taṃ vāyuṃ sarvasattvabhayapradam|
tvaṃ ca vatsa mahāvīraḥ sarvonnataparākramaḥ|| 11 ||

vipracitte tvayā sārdhaṃ kubereṇa prayuddhyatām|
rathakoṭiṃ samādāya cottarasyāṃ balairyutaḥ|| 12 ||

maya tena samaṃ vīra yudhyatāṃ viśvakarmaṇā|
rathakoṭiṃ samādāya bahusainyasamāvṛtaḥ|| 13 ||

hiraṇyākṣa vayaṃ cātra niṣṭhāmastatpradarśayan|
yadā dravanti sainyāni yotsyāmaśca tadā vayam|| 14 ||

skanda uvāca |

tataḥ samāyayurdaityā yuddhāya sāmprataṃ mune|
ādāya hi prabhorājñāṃ vandamānayo 'asureśvaram|| 15 ||

samāgatya tato daityāḥ sve sve sthāne mudānvitāḥ|
nādaṃ cakrurmahābhīṣmaṃ sarvasattvabhayaṃkaram|| 16 ||

devāścāpi tadā vipra nādaṃ cakrurmahādbhutam|
saṃdṛśya danujān sarvān siṃhanādaṃ tataḥ param|| 17 ||

prādurāsīt tato nādaḥ sainyayorubhayostadā|
yugānte ca yathā dhīra sarvasāttvograbhīṣaṇam|| 18 ||

bherīṇāṃ paṭahānāṃ ca mṛdaṅgajalajanminām|
ḍhakkānāṃ dundubhīnāṃ ca kāṃsyānāṃ ca tathā punaḥ|| 19 ||

hastināṃ vājināṃ dhīman hreṣitaṃ hi tathaiva ca|
jyāśabdarathacakrāṇāṃ vīrāṇāṃ saṃkulodbhavam|| 20 ||

tataste yuyudhurdaityā devaiḥ sārdhaṃ samantataḥ|
padātino mahāvīrā vibudhaiśca tathāvidhaiḥ|| 21 ||

jagmurmithaḥ surā daityāḥ śaraiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ|
gadābhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ pāśaiḥ parighaistomaraistathā|| 22 ||

tataḥ padātinaḥ svarge petustatra samantataḥ|
ubhayoḥ sainyayordhīman kaṭhorairiva śākhinaḥ|| 23 ||

purasya prāntaro reje rudhiraughaiḥ kṣatodbhavaiḥ|
samāchannastadā bhīma ekārṇava iva kṣaye|| 24 ||

dharādharā ivāchannāḥ kiṃciccheṣā mahormibhiḥ|
vigrahāḥ patitānāṃ ca rudhiraughaistathāvidhāḥ|| 25 ||

tato jayanta ādau ca svasya nāmāṅkitāśugaiḥ|
avākiraccharāsārān daityasainyopari dhruvam|| 26 ||

prahlādo 'api tadā vipra devasainyaṃ pramardayan|
śarajālairmahātīkṣṇaiḥ svanāmāṅkaiḥ samantataḥ|| 27 ||

jayanto 'api rathenāśu madhye suradviṣāṃ tadā|
ādāya kārmukaṃ krodhādabhidudrāva saṃgare|| 28 ||

jaghāna ca śaraistīkṣṇai rathino hi samantataḥ|
vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi padātīn rathino 'ardayan|| 29 ||

kṣuranemaistato bhallaiściccheda ca śirāṃsi vai|
vīrāṇāṃ samayodhānāṃ rathināṃ ca padātinām|| 30 ||

ākarṇaṃ ca samuddhṛtya saśaraṃ ca śarāsanam|
lakṣīkṛtya ca hṛtsthānaṃ prahlādasya jaghāna saḥ|| 31 ||

daśabhirdaśabhirbāṇairvāhāṃśca rathasārathīn|
pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ sarvān padātīṃśca jaghāna saḥ|| 32 ||

tato dhvajāṃścakarttāśu rathānāṃ purataḥ shtitān|
itastataḥ samutprekṣya jaghāna ca bhṛśaṃ śaraiḥ|| 33 ||

prahlādo na cacārājau ardyamāno bhṛśaṃ śaraiḥ|
kṣaṇaṃ vyathāṃ samuttīrya nāgendra iva cāṅkuśaiḥ|| 34 ||

tataḥ senāṃ vidīrṇāṃ tāṃ prahlādo 'api mahābalī|
dadarśāyodhanaṃ tyaktvā palāyitāṃ bhayāvahām|| 35 ||

jayantaṃ cābhisamprekṣya sainyamadhye vyavasthitam|
cūrṇayantaṃ svakaṃ sainyaṃ krodhena mūrchito 'asuraḥ|| 36 ||

āhūya sarvasainyāni idaṃ vacanam abravīt|
bho bho daityā mahāvīrā na siddhiḥ syāt palāyane|| 37 ||

daityapateśca kāryo hi yudhyavyaṃ saha vai mayā|
asmaddharmaṃ puraskṛtya labhyantāṃ suyaśo yataḥ|| 38 ||

skanda uvāca |

tato vaco niśamyāśu prahlādasya ca dānavāḥ|
harṣavantaśca yuddhāya yatrendrajo yayuḥ punaḥ|| 39 ||

ādāya kārmukān vīrā yugapadabhidudruvuḥ|
sasarja śaravarṣāṇi cāndhībhūtā diśo daśa|| 40 ||

ardayati sma gīrvāṇāñcharajālaistathāyudhaiḥ|
prahārairbahuśastrāstraiḥ parighaiḥ kṣepaṇaistadā|| 41 ||

tato vibudhasenā tacchastrāstraiḥ pīḍitābhavat|
hemantasya tamiśrāyāṃ goyūtiriva vṛṣṭibhiḥ|| 42 ||

prahlādo hi mahākrodhādādāya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ|
ākarṇaṃ ca samuddhṛtya saṃdaśyauṣṭhapuṭaṃ bhṛśam|| 43 ||

vivyādha daśabhirbāṇairlakṣīkṛtya stanāntaram|
jayantasya ca hṛddeśe samutplutya nanāda ca|| 44 ||

daśabhirdaśabhirbhūyo vivyādha ca nanāda ca|
rathīṃśca sārathīnaśvān padātīṃśca dvipāṃstathā|| 45 ||

devadhvajāni ciccheda bāṇairatha sthitāni ca|
vāhanāni vimānānāṃ padāni ca karāṃstathā|| 46 ||

tato 'abravīcca sūtāya rathaṃ sūta pravāhaya|
yatra yatra ca devānāṃ vyūhaṃ tiṣṭhati tatra ca|| 47 ||

bhūyo devān padātīṃśca ardayan rathanemibhiḥ|
jaghāna ca śaraistīkṣṇairdarśayaṃśca diśo daśa|| 48 ||

tatastā dudruvuḥ senā ardyamānāḥ purāntaram|
prahlādaṃ krodhinaṃ prekṣya mṛgayūthā hariṃ yathā|| 49 ||

tato vahnii rathenāsau gatvā madhye suradviṣām|
sasarja śarajālāni yugānte dṛṣṭibhiryathā|| 50 ||
 °nājau Y

ākarṇaṃ ca samuddhṛtya lakṣitavān stanāntaram|
nicakhāna samutplutya jātavedo nanāda ca|| 51 ||

sārathiṃ daśabhirbhittvā viṃśatibhiśca vāhanān|
dhvajaṃ ciccheda bhūyo 'asau chattraṃ caiva tribhistribhiḥ|| 52 ||

pañcabhiśca śaraistīkṣṇaiścakartta dhanuṣaṃ śubham|
jyāṃ ca śarāṃstathā nūnam anuhrādasamuddhatān|| 53 ||

aparān rathino vahnirdaśabhirdaśabhirmune|
sārathiṃ pañcabhirbhittvā nicakhāna ca hṛtsthale|| 54 ||

ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ padātīṃśca jaghāna cāvilambitam|
samālokya puro yodhān daśabhirdaśabhistathā|| 55 ||

asahyatejaso vahneḥ puraḥsthātuṃ suradviṣaḥ|
arditā bāṇajālaiste na ca śekuu rathasthitāḥ|| 56 ||

hitvā cāyodhanaṃ bhītā vahnivarcaḥpradāhitāḥ|
taccharaiścūrṇitā dehā dudruvuśca diśo daśa|| 57 ||

rathino dhvajino daityāḥ padātayastathā mune|
prakampitāstam ālokya mattadvipaṃ mṛgā iva|| 58 ||

anuhrādastadā vipra na cacāla mahāhave|
hanyamāno 'api gātreṣu tacchadmagaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak|| 59 ||

samuttīrṇaḥ kṣaṇaṃ pīḍāṃ dadarśa sa palāyitān|
yuddhaṃ tyaktvā svakaṃ sainyaṃ caturaṅgabalaṃ tadā|| 60 ||

trastamānāṃ mahāsenāṃ vahniśarairvidīrṇitām|
āhvayacca samālokya hastakṣepairanuhradaḥ|| 61 ||

uvāca vacanaṃ tebhyo 'anuhrādo mahārathī|
re re daityā mahāyodhā nivartadhvaṃ palāyanāt|| 62 ||

daityavaṃśodbhavā vīrā bhaveyuraghavāñchinaḥ|
āyodhanaṃ ca saṃtyajya yūyaṃ kathaṃ palāyitāḥ|| 63 ||

asmatsaṃjñā mahāvīrāstriṣu lokeṣu viśrutāḥ|
daityadharmaṃ puraskṛtya yudhyadhvaṃ vai mayā saha|| 64 ||

niśamyaitadvaco yodhā anuhrādasya sāmpratam|
saṃnivartya yayurdhīman yatra sthito 'asuraprabhuḥ|| 65 ||

bhūyaste yuyudhurdaityāḥ parasparaṃ mahāhave|
abhidrutya mithaḥ sainyaṃ na jānanti svakaṃ param|| 66 ||

anuhrādastato vipra krodhena ca pramūrchitaḥ|
ādāya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ sūtāyovāca satvaram|| 67 ||

bho sūta tvaṃ mahābāho tūrṇaṃ vāhān pracodaya|
rathaṃ naya dhruvaṃ tatra yatra sthito vibhāvasuḥ|| 68 ||

sūto 'api codayadvāhān ājñām ādāya satvaram|
yatra vahniratho vipra anayat tadrathaṃ tadā|| 69 ||

ākarṇaṃ ca samuddhṛtya saśaraṃ dhanuṣaṃ śubham|
oṣṭhapuṭaṃ ca saṃdaṃśya īṣadānamitastanuḥ|| 70 ||

anuhrādastataḥ krodhāt samuddiśya stanāntaram|
vakṣasi nicakhānāśu chadmagāñjātavedasaḥ|| 71 ||

daśa daśa tathā bāṇān hastayoḥ pādayoḥ punaḥ|
daśa caiva śirodeśe cakhāna jātavedasaḥ|| 72 ||

pañcabhistīkṣṇabāṇaiśca dvābhyāṃ tūṇaśarān dhanuḥ|
ciccheda ca dhvajaṃ sūtaṃ vāhān bibheda pañcabhiḥ|| 73 ||

vāruṇyāstraṃ samādāya tasyopari vavarṣa saḥ|
tato vahnirniṣprayatno vīro 'apyabhūdghaṭodbhava|| 74 ||

daśabhirdaśabhirbāṇairjaghāna rathino 'aparān|
ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ padātīṃśca caturbhiścaiva sārathīn|| 75 ||

triṃśadbhirviṃśatībhiśca hastino vājinastathā|
jaghāna laghuhastena samutplutya nanāda ca|| 76 ||

tato 'apovāhayadyānaṃ nagaraṃ prati sārathiḥ|
dṛṣṭvā yātam apovāhaṃ tatsenāścābhidudruvuḥ|| 77 ||

tataśca śakrāya nyavedayat tāṃ janaśca vārtāṃ samiterjavena|
jayantavaiśvānarayorhi yānau puryām apovāhakṛtau ca sūtau|| 78 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe devāsurayuddhe jayantāgnyoryānādapovāho nāma

ṣaḍviṃśo adhyāyaḥ|| 26 ||

skanda uvāca |

bhūyo yuddhaṃ mahān āsīt tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam|
śastrāstraiḥ kṣepaṇairvipra yugānta iva bhīṣaṇam|| 1 ||

tayoryuddhaṃ mahān āsīccitraṃ saṃhrādakālayoḥ|
śastrāstravṛṣṭibhirbhīṣmaṃ tato bhūto 'api vāsaraḥ|| 2 ||

abhūt sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ kālasaṃhrādayostayoḥ|
sainyānāṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ vipra parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥ|| 3 ||

jāmbūnadamayaiḥ puṅkhaiḥ prakṣepaiḥ samitastataḥ|
bahukoṭiśaraistīkṣṇaiḥ śilādhautaistayostadā|| 4 ||

tau rathau śuśubhāte hi yuddhamadhye gatau bhṛśam|
hiraṇyaśikharau rātrau khadyotairiva saṃyutau|| 5 ||

tato 'avocacca sūtāya prayāṇārthaṃ rathasya ca|
kālaḥ kṣipraṃ ca bho sūta rathaṃ naya tadantikam|| 6 ||

haniṣyāmi śaraistīkṣṇaiḥ saṃhrādasya suradviṣaḥ|
kālasya vacanaṃ śrutvā sārathiḥ praṇayadratham|| 7 ||

sārathiśca tato dhīra rathavāhāśca satvaram|
saṃhrādaśca sthito yatra yatnena ca pracodayat|| 8 ||

amarṣapūritaḥ kāla ākarṇam uddhṛtaiḥ śaraiḥ|
viṃśatibhirjaghānāśu saṃhrādasya ca vakṣasi|| 9 ||

pañcabhiśca tato bhūyaḥ saṃhrādasya jaghāna ca|
hastapādalalāṭāṃśca samuddiśya ca marmasu|| 10 ||

daśabhirdaśabhirvāhān sūtaṃ ca daśabhistathā|
dhvajaṃ cāpaṃ śarāṃstūṇāṃstribhistribhistato 'acchinat|| 11 ||

ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ śaraistīkṣṇairvivyādha rathino bhṛśam|
pañcabhiḥ pañcabhirbhūyaḥ padātīṃśca tathāparān|| 12 ||

dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ tathā ketūṃściccheda sapatākinaḥ|
vāhinīnāṃ purogāṃśca rathānāṃ ca puraḥsthitān|| 13 ||

bhallaiściccheda tān kālo danujānāṃ śirāṃsi ca|
yudhyamānapadātīnām ayutāni sakṛt sakṛt|| 14 ||

bhūyo jaghāna daityāṃśca yudhyamānān punaḥ punaḥ|
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇāṃ prāśaiśca tomaraistathā|| 15 ||

bhejire te diśaḥ sarvā daityasenāstato mune|
kālaśaraiḥ samākīrṇāḥ kampamānā muhurmuhuḥ|| 16 ||

saṃhrādaśca mahāvīraḥ krodhenāśu pramūrchitaḥ|
dṛṣṭvā sainyaṃ ca saṃtrastaṃ kālaśarairvidīrṇitam|| 17 ||

ṭaṅkāraṃ ca kṛtaḥ krodhī sammārjya supataṃjikām|
āhūya sarvasainyaṃ ca ājñāpayat sa sārathim|| 18 ||

bho sūta naya yatrāsau kālo rathaṃ ca sāmpratam|
tataḥ sūto rathaṃ śīghraṃ vāhāṃśca tatra codayat|| 19 ||

tato 'avocaddhi saṃhrādaḥ kālāya lokakāline|
śrāvayan sarvadevāṃśca svasainyāṃśca tato 'aparān|| 20 ||

saṃhrāda uvāca |

kālaśabdaśca te khyāto mṛtānāṃ kāla eva ca|
na tu jīvabhṛtāṃ kālaḥ kalaye tvaṃ kṣamo na hi|| 21 ||

na samartho 'asi kālastvaṃ lokānāṃ prāṇadhāriṇām|
kālaḥ kalayituṃ kālān nākāle karmavartinām|| 22 ||

yudhyasva pauruṣaṃ cet te mayā saha paretarāṭ|
idānīṃ darśayaujaste ante ca darśayāmyaham|| 23 ||

hatvā daityān bahūn ājau balavāṃstvaṃ samantataḥ|
kṣudrān hatān na dūye 'ahaṃ yudhyasvādya balī yadi|| 24 ||

yāvatīnāṃ hatānāṃ tvaṃ tāvatīnāṃ ca sāmpratam|
hatvā tvām uddhariṣyāmi gurumantreṇa cātmanaḥ|| 25 ||

kāla uvāca |

na valgase ciraṃ mūḍha darśaya te 'adya pauruṣam|
na valganti ca śūrā ye darśayanti ātmapauruṣam|| 26 ||

hatvā tvāṃ sānvayaṃ rājyaṃ kariṣyati puraṃdaraḥ|
niḥkaṇṭakaṃ trilokaṃ ca kṛtvā mūḍha suniścitam|| 27 ||

skanda uvāca |

niśamyaitadvaco dhīman kālasya sainyamadhyataḥ|
āmarṣapūrito daityo dadaṃśa cādharaṃ bhṛśam|| 28 ||

ākarṇam uddhataścāpaṃ śataṃ śaraṃ pradhāya ca|
jyāyāṃ ca kālam uddiśya preṣayāmāsa tān bahūn|| 29 ||

jaghāna prasabhaṃ bāṇaiḥ kālaṃ kālanibhairmune|
nicakhāna sahasrāṇi kālasya sarvamarmasu|| 30 ||

daśabhirdaśabhirvāhāñjaghāna laghuhastataḥ|
sārathiṃ daśabhirbhittvā dvābhyāṃ ciccheda ca dhvajam|| 31 ||

triṃśaistriṃśaistathā viṃśairākarṇairuddhṛtaiḥ śaraiḥ|
jaghāna rathino yodhān padātīn vāhanāni ca|| 32 ||

sārathīṃśca tato yānaṃ kālasya yuddhadeśataḥ|
apovāhitam ālokya pīḍitaṃ laghu cāntikam|| 33 ||

tataśca dudruvuryuddhāddevasenāpuraṃ prati|
taccharaiḥ pīḍyamānāstāḥ prekṣyāpovāhanaṃ yamam|| 34 ||

saṃhrādaśca tadā daityo valgamāna itastataḥ|
sasarja śaravarṣāṇi cakre siṃharavān punaḥ|| 35 ||

tato 'abhūt sumahadyuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam|
bhīṣmaṃ surāsurāṇāṃ ca yātudhānanikumbhayoḥ|| 36 ||

tomarairbhindipālaiśca prāśaiśca parighaistathā|
muṣṭibhiśca śaraiḥ khaḍgairjaghnatustau parasparam|| 37 ||

nairṛtaśca tato vipra sajyaṃ kṛtvā mahaddhanuḥ|
jagāmāsuramadhye ca rathenāśu mahārathī|| 38 ||

tataḥ sasarja bāṇānāṃ varṣāṇi ca samantataḥ|
tamobhūtā diśaḥ sarvāśchādyamānā nabhastalam|| 39 ||

śarāsārairmahāyuddhe niḥprayatnāśca vāhanāḥ|
kṛṣṇapakṣe ca hemante āsārai rajanī yathā|| 40 ||

bahūñcharān samādāya nicakhāna sa nairṛtaḥ|
nikumbhāṅge sadā rejurjalaukā iva varmaṣu|| 41 ||

saṃtāḍya sārathiṃ bāṇairatha vāhāṃstathāparān|
ciccheda tasya maurvīṃ ca saśaraṃ saśarāsanam|| 42 ||

padātīn rathinaḥ sarvān bāṇairāmardayat tataḥ|
aśvān nāgāṃstathoṣṭrāṃśca nairṛtaśca pṛthak pṛthak|| 43 ||

dudruvurdaityasenāśca trastamānā itastataḥ|
visṛjyāyodhanaṃ vipra nairṛteṣu gaṇārditāḥ|| 44 ||

nikumbho 'api samālokya amarṣaiḥ pūritastadā|
trastaṃ palāyitaṃ sainyaṃ bhinnasetum ivārṇavam|| 45 ||

mahārathī nikumbho 'api tataḥ sainyaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ|
jagāma tvaritaṃ dhanvī nairṛto yatra tiṣṭhati|| 46 ||

samāgato rathenājau mārjitavān patañjikām|
uvāca kauṇapaṃ krodhī śrāvayan sarvasainyakam|| 47 ||

nikumbha uvāca |

nikaṣātmaja mandātman nīcavṛttau rataḥ sadā|
prāṇināṃ raktapo nityaṃ māṃsāhārī niśācaraḥ|| 48 ||

nakhāyuddhavirūpo 'asi lokanindyakalevaraḥ|
etairnindyaiḥ samāyuktaḥ kṣudro 'asi tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ|| 49 ||

idānīṃ darśaya kṣudra asmākaṃ ca parākramam|
adya tvāṃ ca haniṣyāmi toṣaye danujeśvaram|| 50 ||

skanda uvāca |

ityuktvā ca nikumbho 'asau mahātmā ca mahābalī|
ādāya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ tatāra jyāsvanaṃ punaḥ|| 51 ||

ākarṇaṃ ca samutsārya saśaraṃ hi guṇaṃ dhruvam|
preṣayāmāsa śarāṃstīkṣṇān rakṣosṛkpānalālasān|| 52 ||

sārathiṃ ca jaghānāśu dhvajaṃ ciccheda ca tribhiḥ|
jāmbūnadaiśca bāṇaughaiśchattraṃ ca rathavāhakān|| 53 ||

rathinaśca tato bhūyaḥ padātīn yuddhadurmadān|
jaghāna bahubāṇaiśca saṃdaśya cādharaṃ laghu|| 54 ||

tato vraṇayutaṃ sūta ālokya rathinaṃ yudhi|
apovāhayadāryāśu vimānaṃ svarṇabhūṣitam|| 55 ||

apovāhaṃ samālokya vimānaṃ nairṛtaṃ sthitam|
dudruvurdevasainyāśca nagarīṃ tvamarāvatīm|| 56 ||

tataśca dūtaḥ sahasā ca gatvā nyavedayat tāṃ samiteḥ pravṛttim|
yathā hi bhaṅgaṃ yudhi nairṛtasya puraṃdarāyāsuraceṣṭitaṃ ca|| 57 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe devāsurasaṃgrāme kālanairṛtayoryānāpovāhanaṃ|

nāma saptaviṃśatitamo adhyāyaḥ|| 27 ||

skanda uvāca |

bhūyo yuddhaṃ mahaccāsīddevāsurabhayaṃkaram|
pāśikālakayorvipra anyonyaṃ hantum īpsayā|| 1 ||

sasarjatuḥ śarāsārān devāśca danujāstathā|
andhībhūtā diśaḥ sarvāstamisreva savāridā|| 2 ||

tomaraiḥ parighaistīkṣṇaiḥ prāśaiḥ paraśupaṭṭiśaiḥ|
bāṇairhiraṇyapuṅkhaiśca jaghnurmithaḥ surāsurāḥ|| 3 ||

āmarṣapūritaḥ kṣipraṃ prayāṇāya rathasya ca|
pracetāśca mahāvīraḥ sūtam ājñāpayadyudhi|| 4 ||

bho sūta tvaṃ mahābāho vāhān pracodya sāmpratam|
tatra nayāśu me yānaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati kālakaḥ|| 5 ||

tām ākarṇya tataḥ sūta ājñāṃ caiva pracetasaḥ|
yānaṃ pravāhayedārādvegena kālakāntikam|| 6 ||

tataḥ śarān samādhāya ākarṇapūritaṃ dhanuḥ|
preṣayāmāsa śīghraṃ sa jātarūpāṅkitāñcharān|| 7 ||

tataḥ pāśī samuddiśya kālakaṃ taṃ mahāsuram|
jaghāna saśaraistīkṣṇaiḥ sahasrairyugapat tadā|| 8 ||

tataḥ pāśaiḥ prabaddhvāśu pracetāścāsinā surān|
śatānāṃ ca sahasrāṇi jaghāna raṇamūrdhani|| 9 ||

rathino varayodhāṃśca tadagre yuddhalālasān|
jaghāna ca punarbaddhvā pāśaiḥ prāśaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ|| 10 ||

tataste dudruvurdaityā rathino 'api padātayaḥ|
daityasainyaprahantāraṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ kālasaṃnibham|| 11 ||

bhejire danujāḥ sarve kampamānā diśo daśa|
taccharairbhinnadehāśca yuddhaṃ tyaktvā bhayāturāḥ|| 12 ||

dṛṣṭavāṃśca tato daityaḥ kālako nāma vīryavān|
sainyān palāyamānān svān sutāyovāca sāmpratam|| 13 ||

sūta tvaṃ ca mahābāho sarvayuddhaviśārada|
idānīṃ yodhayiṣye 'ahaṃ tatra sārdhaṃ pracetasā|| 14 ||

rathaṃ naya mahāvīra pracetā yatra tiṣṭhati|
śīghraṃ pracodayāśvān me nākāryaṃ ciram utsahe|| 15 ||

niśamyaitadvaco vipra kālakena prabhāṣitam|
pracodayadrathaṃ vāhān sadhvajaṃ svarṇabhūṣitam|| 16 ||

tūrṇaṃ samānayat tatra yatra tiṣṭhati toyarāṭ|
tataśca kālakaḥ krodhī dadarśa yādasāṃ patim|| 17 ||

ākarṇaṃ ca samutsārya lakṣīkṛtya stanāntaram|
sahasraśaḥ śarairvīro jaghāna varuṇaṃ bhṛśam|| 18 ||

bhūyaḥ śarasahasrāṇi samādāya ca kālakaḥ|
nicakhāna śarīreṣu raktapeva pracetasaḥ|| 19 ||

tataḥ sūtaṃ jaghānāśu triṃśadbhiśca śaraistathā|
dhvajaṃ ciccheda ca dvābhyāṃ triṃśaistriṃśaiśca vāhanān|| 20 ||

śataiḥ śataistathā yodhān padātīn rathinaḥ punaḥ|
jaghāna ca śaraistīkṣṇaiḥ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda ca|| 21 ||

vāruṇaṃ ca tato yānam apovāhayadāśu ca|
bahubāṇavraṇaṃ prekṣya sūtaḥ prācetasaṃ mune|| 22 ||

dṛṣṭvā yānam apovāhaṃ cāyodhanāt pracetasaḥ|
devasenā bhayatrastā dudruvuścāmarāvatīm|| 23 ||

bhūyaśca yuyudhurvipra balivāyvormitho bhṛśam|
tayoramarṣiṇaḥ senāḥ parasparajayecchayā|| 24 ||

sasṛjuḥ śaravṛṣṭiṃ te vibudhāsurasainyakāḥ|
nabho māse yathāsārairandhībhūtaṃ digantaram|| 25 ||

tato vāyurmahātejā ādāya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ|
samādideśa sūtāya prayāṇārthaṃ rathasya vai|| 26 ||

bho sūta tvaṃ mahābhāga saṃcodyāśvān rathaṃ mama|
sāmprataṃ tatra yuddhāya naya yatra sthito baliḥ|| 27 ||

samyagvāhaya yānaṃ me etānaśvān prarakṣaya|
yuddhajña svapareṣāṃ ca jñātvā tatra balābalam|| 28 ||

skanda uvāca |

niśamyeti vaco vāyoḥ sūtaścāśvān pracodya ca|
