tatra samānayadyānaṃ yatrāsti daityarāḍbaliḥ|| 29 ||

tatra baliṃ dadarśājau hiraṇyarathasaṃsthitam|
kṣepayantaṃ śarāṃstīvrān bāṇān mūrdhni vyavasthitān|| 30 ||

tato vāyuu ruṣāviṣṭaścāyutaṃ śaram ādadhe|
jyāyāṃ bāṇairdhanustūrṇaṃ cakrīkṛtya jaghāna tam|| 31 ||

jāmbūnadamayān puṅkhān bhūyo bāṇān hi varṣmaṣu|
nicakhāna balervāyuste papustasya śoṇitam|| 32 ||

nicakhāna tato vāhān pañcāśadbhiḥ śarairmune|
pañcaviṃśatibhirbhūyaḥ sūtaṃ jaghāna satvaram|| 33 ||

dvābhyāṃ ciccheda ketuṃ ca sapatākaṃ samucchritam|
dvābhyāṃ ciccheda hastasthaṃ tadā bāṇaṃ śarāsanam|| 34 ||

śatena pattribhirvipra rathino hi jaghāna saḥ|
pañcāśadbhiḥ punaryodhān padātīṃśca tadardhakaiḥ|| 35 ||

kecit khaḍgaistathā kecit prāśaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ śaraiḥ|
bhindipālairgadābhiśca devā jaghnuśca dānavān|| 36 ||

tataḥ senāśca daityānāṃ dudruvuśca diśo daśa|
vraṇavantaḥ śarairvāyoḥ kampidehe bhayāturāḥ|| 37 ||

baliśca sārathiścaiva samuttīrṇau kṣaṇādvyathām|
sahyamānau śarairbhinnau bhādre gā iva vṛṣṭibhiḥ|| 38 ||

tato baliśca taṃ prekṣya palāyitaṃ svasainyakam|
trasyamānaṃ śarairbhinnaṃ bhinnasetum ivāpagām|| 39 ||

uvāca vacanaṃ bhūyo balirmahābalastadā|
sainyebhyastrastamānebhyo rājanītisamāyutaiḥ|| 40 ||

baliruvāca |

re re daityā adharmasthā yuddhavarmaparāṅmukhāḥ|
nivartadhvaṃ nivartadhvaṃ kuto vaścāgataṃ bhayam|| 41 ||

asmaddharmaṃ parityajya kātaratvaṃ samāśritāḥ|
dhigastu pauruṣaṃ vo hi yatastrastāḥ palāyitāḥ|| 42 ||

palāyane na siddhyanti kāryāṇi ca prabhoryataḥ|
katham icchāmahe tyaktuṃ hiraṇyakaśiporvayam|| 43 ||

daityadharmaṃ samāsthāya yudhyadhvaṃ hi mayā saha|
prāpnumo no yataḥ siddhim āyāntu bho mahābalāḥ|| 44 ||

skanda uvāca |

tataḥ śrutvā balervākyaṃ nītibhiḥ sa caturvidham|
samāyayustadā vipra digbhyo yatra sthitā yataḥ|| 45 ||

tataḥ praharṣitā daityāstadvākyai rājanītibhiḥ|
apūpujaṃstam ālokya sādhu sādhviti vādinaḥ|| 46 ||

tato yayau balirvipra sarvadaityasamāvṛtaḥ|
sāntvayan sārathiṃ yoddhuṃ rathena tatra sārathim|| 47 ||

yuyudhurdevadaityāśca parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥ|
tataḥ svālakṣamānāste cābhūvan svān parān mithaḥ|| 48 ||

bāṇajālaiḥ samāchādya jaghnuste ca parasparam|
pāśaiśca tomaraiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ parighaistadā|| 49 ||

tato balirmahātejāḥ sārdhaṃ yuddhaviśāradaḥ|
yuyodha vāyunā savyam akarodanilaṃ punaḥ|| 50 ||

saṃdaśya daśanairoṣṭham ākarṇam uddhṛtaiḥ śaraiḥ|
balirjaghāna vāyuṃ ca sahasraiśca śarairbhṛśam|| 51 ||

jātarūpamayaiḥ puṅkhairjaghāna sarvavarmasu|
sahasraiśca śarairvāyoḥ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda ca|| 52 ||

śatena ca rathāśvāṃśca sūtaṃ jaghāna sāmpratam|
dhvajaṃ ciccheda ca dvābhyāṃ lakṣīkṛtya pṛthak pṛthak|| 53 ||

sahasrārdhaiḥ punardhīra rathino nāyakāṃstathā|
sahasreṇa tadaṃśāṃstāñjaghāna satvaraṃ ruṣā|| 54 ||

rathaṃ cakraiḥ sugambhīraiścūrṇayāmāsa satvaram|
padātīn vibudhānāṃ ca vicaran sarvato diśaḥ|| 55 ||

tato 'apovāhayat sūto yānam āyodhanāddhruvam|
rathinaṃ vraṇasaṃyuktaṃ samprekṣya trāsamāṃstadā|| 56 ||

samprekṣya devasainyāste apovāhaṃ nabhasvataḥ|
yānaṃ ca dudruvustrastāḥ śakrarājyaṃ ca sāmpratam|| 57 ||

tataśca senāstvaritaṃ hi vārtām ūcuśca ceṣṭāṃ danujasya gatvā|
puraṃdarāyāyāntikam āśu dhīman samīrayānāya kṛtasya yacca|| 58 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe devāsurasaṃgrāme varuṇānilayoryānopavāho

nāmāṣṭāviṃśatitamo adhyāyaḥ|| 28 ||

skanda uvāca |

tato yuddhaṃ mahān āsīddevadaityabhayaṃkaram|
tumulaṃ ca mitho vipra vipracittikuberayoḥ|| 1 ||

rathino rathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ padātayaḥ padātibhiḥ|
hastino hastibhirbhūyo yuyudhuśca parasparam|| 2 ||

vavarṣuḥ śaravarṣāṇi devāsurā mitho bhṛśam|
tamobhūtā digantāśca vṛṣṭiyuktāḥ kṣapā yathā|| 3 ||

jaghnurmithaḥ surā daityān nānāśastrairbhayaṃkaraiḥ|
bāṇaiḥ khaḍgairgadāpāśaiḥ svān parāṃścāvijānataḥ|| 4 ||

tato nādaṃ samudbhūtaṃ trailokyānāṃ prakampakam|
gṛhyatāṃ hanyatāṃ caiva re re hā heti colbaṇam|| 5 ||

rathanemyudbhavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ vājināṃ hreṣitaṃ tathā|
gajānāṃ mahiṣāṇāṃ ca kharoṣṭrāṇāṃ tathaiva ca|| 6 ||

kubaro 'api tato dhīmaṃścāpam ādāya satvaram|
uvāca sārathiṃ tatra madhuraṃ ca prasāntvayan|| 7 ||

he sūta tvaṃ mahāprājña pracodyāśvān mamāniśam|
vipracittiśca yatrāsti tatra yānaṃ nayāśu ca|| 8 ||

tato niśamya yakṣasya sārathiḥ priyabhāṣitam|
pracodya ca vimānāśvān yānaṃ tatra pravāhayat|| 9 ||

kuberaśca mahātejā dadarśa dviṣatāṃ balam|
ghātayantaṃ surān sarvān bāṇajālairitastataḥ|| 10 ||

tataḥ krodhasamāviṣṭaḥ kubero guhyakeśvaraḥ|
ākarṇāntaṃ samutsārya jaghāna tīkṣṇakoṭibhiḥ|| 11 ||

jātarūpamayān puṅkhān yutān vai chadmagān mune|
nicakhāna tadaṅgeṣu uddiśya sarvamarmasu|| 12 ||

sūtaṃ śarairbibhedājau sahasrairvāhakān pṛthak|
ketuṃ ciccheda ca dvābhyāṃ vipracitterdhanādhipaḥ|| 13 ||

sahasraiśca pṛthagbhūyo rathino yuddhalālasān|
śataiḥ śataiḥ padātīṃśca jaghāna tvaritaṃ punaḥ|| 14 ||

vipracittii ruṣāviṣṭaḥ samuttīrṇo vyathāṃ kṣaṇāt|
yuddhamadhye 'avadat sūtaṃ śrāvayan svān dviṣo 'api ca|| 15 ||

vipracittiruvāca |

bho sūta yuddhavit prājña codaya rathavāhakān|
tūrṇaṃ tatra rathaṃ me tvaṃ yatra yakṣaḥ sthito naya|| 16 ||

adyāhaṃ ghātayiṣyāmi sayānaṃ sārathiṃ ca vai|
kuberaṃ devasainyāṃśca vāhanāni ca sāmpratam|| 17 ||

skanda uvāca |

tato niśamya sūtaśca valgitaṃ vipracittinā|
harṣapūrṇaprayāṇajñaḥ prāvāhayadrathaṃ tadā|| 18 ||

yatra tiṣṭhati paulastyastvaritaṃ ca rathaṃ mune|
ānayat taṃ ca yuddhajño devasainyaṃ pradarśayan|| 19 ||

tato dadarśa paulastyaṃ kṣepayantaṃ śarān bahūn|
tataḥ kopaprayuktātmā mahaddhanuḥ samādade|| 20 ||

cakrīkṛtya mahācāpaṃ daśāyutaiḥ śaraiḥ kṣaṇāt|
vipracittiḥ kuberaṃ ca vivyādha laghuhastataḥ|| 21 ||

bhūyaśca niyutaṃ gṛhya bāṇāṃstīkṣṇamukhāṃstadā|
nicakhāna hṛdi kṣipraṃ kuberasya mahātmanaḥ|| 22 ||

ayutenāyutenaiva rathino hi jaghāna saḥ|
dvisahasraiḥ pṛthagyodhān sahasrai rathavāhakān|| 23 ||

sahasraṃ vipra pañcānāṃ sūtaṃ jaghāna satvaram|
dvābhyāṃ ciccheda ketuṃ ca kuberasya dhanustathā|| 24 ||

tato devacamūstatra tapati sma samantataḥ|
vavāma rudhiraṃ tīvraṃ mukhanāsāśrutivraṇāt|| 25 ||

vavalgurdaityasenāśca saṃdṛśya devasainikān|
vipracitteḥ śarairbhinnān rudhiraughapariplutān|| 26 ||

kuberasya ca sūto vai durīkṛtya kṣaṇaṃ vyathām|
apovāhayadājau ca yānaṃ tadvraṇam īkṣya ca|| 27 ||

dṛṣṭvā ratham apovāhaṃ kuberasya tadā mune|
dudruvustrasyamānāstā devasenāḥ puraṃ prati|| 28 ||

bhūyo yuddhaṃ mahān āsīnmayasya viśvakarmaṇaḥ|
māyāyuddhaṃ tayostatra māyāvinaḥ parasparam|| 29 ||

bāṇavarṣaṃ vavarṣuste ādau mitho jighāṃsayā|
andhībhūtā diśaḥ sarvāḥ kṛṣṇapakṣe yathā kṣapāḥ|| 30 ||

tato jaghnurmithaḥ senāḥ śastrāstrairasibhiḥ parān|
bāṇairhiraṇyapuṅkhaiśca kaṅkagṛdhrasupattribhiḥ|| 31 ||

tatastvaṣṭā mahāmāyī sarvamāyāviśāradaḥ|
utpapātāntarikṣe ca sarathaḥ sāyudhastadā|| 32 ||

vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi lohamukhāni sāmpratam|
mayūrakaṅkapattrāṇi nabhastho viśvasṛk tadā|| 33 ||

tato mayasya sainyāste bhejire hi diśo daśa|
śarapātaiḥ prabhinnāṅgāstrastamānāḥ prapīḍitāḥ|| 34 ||

tato mayaḥ svakaṃ sainyaṃ māyāśaraiḥ prapīḍitam|
prekṣya viyatsthitaṃ vipra māyinaṃ ca ruroṣa saḥ|| 35 ||

utpapāta mayaḥ kṣipraṃ rathastho vyomnyalakṣitaḥ|
vavarṣa cāśmavarṣāṇi devasainyopari dhruvam|| 36 ||

bhūyo vavarṣa śṛṅgāni samādāya ca māyayā|
gaṇḍaśailān drumāṃścaiva yugapacca mayo 'asuraḥ|| 37 ||

devasainyāstadā tatra yuddhaṃ hitvā pradudruvuḥ|
śilādrumaśarāghātairvyathitāśca bhayāturāḥ|| 38 ||

tato yuyudhaturvīrau nānāmāyāviśāradau|
viśvakarmamayau tau ca nabhastale hyanekaśaḥ|| 39 ||

alakṣau tau ca sainyānāṃ vyomasthau ca viceratuḥ|
jaghnatustau mahātmānau śastrāstrairbahubhirmithaḥ|| 40 ||

tataścotplutya yānāt tau dharaṇyāṃ petaturbhuvam|
mitha āliṅgitau vīrau na muñcantau parasparam|| 41 ||

bāhuyuddhaṃ tato bhūyo yuyudhāte parasparam|
talaiśca muṣṭibhiścaiva jaghnaturvai viśan viśan|| 42 ||

yuyudhāte gadāyuddhaṃ sarvabhūtaprakampakam|
gadāprahārasaṃbhūtasphuliṅgo dyotayan diśaḥ|| 43 ||

sādṛśyaṃ ca tatastvaṣṭā kṛtvā mano hi māyayā|
tena yuddhāya yat sārdhaṃ svātmatulyaparākramaiḥ|| 44 ||

māyājaḥ puruṣo vipra yuyodha ca mayena vai|
sākaṃ tadā mahadyuddhaṃ kaṭhoraṃ medinītale|| 45 ||

viśvakarmā tataḥ svargaṃ gatvā cārūḍhavān mune|
nānāratnamayaṃ yānaṃ gaganasthaṃ mahojjvalam|| 46 ||

agnivṛṣṭiṃ vavarṣājau śilāvarṣaṃ tataḥ param|
daityasainyopari kṣipraṃ viśvakarmā samantataḥ|| 47 ||

śaravarṣaṃ vavarṣāśu śastravarṣaṃ tathāvidham|
drumavarṣaṃ punarvipra pāṃśuvarṣaṃ ca viśvasṛk|| 48 ||

tataḥ petuśca daiteyā vamannasṛṅmukhādvraṇāt|
śastrāstradṛṣadāsāraistāḍyamānāḥ samantataḥ|| 49 ||

tato mayaḥ samājñāya māyodbhavaṃ hi puruṣam|
tatyāja tena yuddhaṃ ca cintati sma samaṃ vidhim|| 50 ||

mayo 'api ca tadā vipra saṃsṛjya māyayātmanaḥ|
sādṛśyaṃ puruṣaṃ tena yodhāpayan mithaḥ samam|| 51 ||

utpapātāntarikṣaṃ ca mayo māyāmayastanuḥ|
tatra dadarśa yānasthaṃ tvaṣṭāraṃ ca nabhastale|| 52 ||

ghātayantaṃ śilāvarṣairdaityasainyān samantataḥ|
mayo 'api tvaritaṃ tatra ratham āruhya roṣavān|| 53 ||

vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi durbhikṣe śalabhāniva|
śilāsāraṃ tathā tīvraṃ pāṃsuvarṣaṃ samantataḥ|| 54 ||

devasainyopari kṣipraṃ vavarṣa sa mayastadā|
tato mayaśca māyāvī māyayā mohayadraṇe|| 55 ||

layairgītairmṛdaṅgaiśca tvaṣṭāraṃ cāpyanartayat|
nṛtyantaṃ gītavantaṃ tam tvaṣṭāraṃ prekṣya candramāḥ|
saṃdarśya māyayāviṣṭaṃ tvaṣṭāraṃ vavarṣāmṛtam|| 56 ||

tatastvaṣṭāmṛtāsāraiḥ paripluto ghaṭodbhava|
ceṣṭitavān mahadyuddhe āyayau samarāt puram|| 57 ||

tato 'avadadvṛtrahaṇe ca dūtaḥ pravṛttim āyodhanasambhavāṃ ca|
tvaṣṭuśca bhaṅgaṃ yudhi māyayā yadvimohanaṃ samprati nartayantam|| 58 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe himavatkhaṇḍe devāsurasaṃgrāme viśvakarmāpayānaṃ nāmonatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ|| 29 ||
